Wuh preface wuh tanafsu nam-tor wuh fereiksu t' vaksurik vel. Tor reveal tanaf heh ip-sut wuh tanafsu nam-tor tanaf’s mokh. Wuh critic nam-tor au vi mokuhlek mesukh-tor vi' wuh'ashiv manner il wuh uzh tukh ish-veh impression t' vaksurik vel. Wuh k'lek u' wuh lowest shid t' criticism nam-tor wuh nuk t' autobiography. Eifa vi talal watosh meanings svi' vaksurik vel nam-tor corrupt rik' hasu sem-rik-tor. Nash nam-tor wuh lafot. Eifa vi talal vaksurik meanings svi' vaksurik vel nam-tor wuh sokasitau. Na' aifa tra' nam-tor rok. Au nam-tor wuh todvel-tor tor ik vaksurik vel tvai goh vaksur. Tra' nam-tor rai such vel u' wuh moral il wuh immoral dunap. Dunap nam-tor muhl written, il badly written. Ik nam-tor ek'. Wuh nineteenth century ritishaya t' realism nam-tor wuh reshan t' caliban seeing ish-veh sha' limuk svi' wuh makh. Wuh nineteenth century ritishaya t' romanticism nam-tor wuh reshan t' caliban ri seeing ish-veh sha' limuk svi' wuh makh. Wuh moral ha'kiv t' sasu shidau krus t' wuh subject-tukh t' wuh tanafsu, tonk'peh wuh morality t' tanaf consists svi' wuh buhfik nam-tor-tor t' wuh imperfect medium. Rai tanafsu aitlu tor skan-tor sovek-vel. Kauk vel ik nam-tor yeht mokuhlek nam-tor skan-tor. Rai tanafsu has tomayehtik sympathies. Wuh tomayehtik sympathy svi' wuh tanafsu nam-tor wuh unpardonable mannerism t' style. Rai tanafsu nam-tor ek'wak morbid. Wuh tanafsu mokuhlek sagluvau kanok-vei. Nahp heh gen-lis nam-tor tor wuh tanafsu instruments t' wuh tanaf. Vice heh virtue nam-tor tor wuh tanafsu tukh na' wuh tanaf. S' wuh sfek t' zan-tor t' shid, wuh ves t' ek' wuh arts nam-tor wuh tanaf t' wuh ralash-tanafsu. S' wuh sfek t' zan-tor t' olaya, wuh fundauik-ithop’s hali nam-tor wuh ves. Ek' tanaf nam-tor na' wuh'wak skonn heh sehtebuhk. Eifa vi hal-tor ne'rak wuh skonn tor ni na' ish-veh peril. Eifa vi telv-tor wuh sehtebuhk tor ni na' ish-veh peril. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh spectator, heh ri ha'kiv, ik tanaf really haulat. Vuhnaya t' opinion pa' wuh ar'kadan t' tanaf gluvau ik wuh ar'kadan nam-tor uzh, wehkonik, heh bolik. Lu critics disagree, wuh tanafsu nam-tor svi' accord k' himself. Etek mokuhlek forgive wuh sasu na' tor wuh useful vel u' wu u' au tor ri krol-tor ish-veh. Wuh goh tobeg na' tor wuh nam-tor-fam vel nam-tor ik veh krol-tor ish-veh intensely. Ek' tanaf nam-tor ved nam-tor-fam. Oscar wilde chapter i. Wuh studio vesh' boshau k' wuh don-ka vil t' roses, heh lu wuh ta'hal belaar salan stirred amidst wuh lap t' wuh bah-ker, tra' sarlah k'fai wuh tu'ash svep wuh ras scent t' wuh lilac, il wuh weht delicate perfume t' wuh faf-kur-flowering thorn. S' wuh teruk t' wuh divan t' persian saddle-sa'haf fi' if au vesh' lying, smoking, u' vesh' ish-veh custom, va' cigarettes, s'haile henry wotton kupi aishan kum wuh gleam t' wuh honey-slor heh honey-kur-tor blossoms t' wuh laburnum, t'vi tremulous khlup seemed hardly kup tor lesh wuh burden t' wuh vaksur ni flamelike u' ish-veh; heh i' heh yi wuh fantastic duv t' kushel svi' hash flitted mes' wuh wu tussore-silk curtains ik vesh' sakadau svi' khom t' wuh masuk' krani, producing wuh ves t' momentary japanese daya, heh tor ish-veh nah-tor t' eifa pallid, yar-kov-limuk-tor krassu t' tokyo vi, k'fai wuh medium t' wuh tanaf ik nam-tor necessarily immobile, seek tor zhelesh wuh kash-ral t' swiftness heh dvunel. Wuh kir murmur t' wuh bees shouldering ish-veh yut k'fai wuh wu unmown yar, il circling k' monotonous insistence pauk wuh grazhiv gilt stonn t' wuh straggling woodbine, seemed tor tor wuh stillness weht oppressive. Wuh neik-ha'khlup roar t' london vesh' spo' wuh bourdon pitoh t' wuh irak nafek. Svi' wuh centre t' wuh tvi-shal, clamped tor wuh abruvenik easel, lam-tor wuh bosh-wu-vath portrait t' wuh nu'ri sasu t' wehtsuri personal vaksur, heh svi' khom t' ish-veh, ein pi' ir maf, vesh' sitting wuh tanafsu himself, basil hallward, t'vi sudden disappearance ein tevun ago aisha, na' wuh wak, such tsuri tepor'es heh mazhiv-kur-tor shen tor ni wehk flekh conjectures. U' wuh krassu glazhau na' wuh gracious heh comely shid au had ni skilfully mirrored svi' ish-veh tanaf, wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' sanosh be' dvun-tor mes' ish-veh limuk, heh seemed pa' tor svizh-tor tra'. Tonk'peh au suddenly palikau abru, heh ikapik ish-veh bezhun, shitau ish-veh ozh fi-tor wuh lids, u' hi au sought tor imprison k'svi ish-veh shi'nahp ein curious sahr-tor s' if au ptha au lau kum'i. “ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh buhfik ar'kadan, basil, wuh buhfik vel du ma ek'wak ovsoh, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry languidly. “du bolau certainly satau ish-veh thurai tevun tor wuh grosvenor. Wuh academy nam-tor nuh' suk heh nuh' vulgar. Whenever i ma hal-tor tra', tra' ma vesh' either ni wehk sutra ik i ma ri vesh' kup tor gla-tor wuh bikuv, if vesh' dreadful, il ni wehk bikuv ik i ma ri vesh' kup tor gla-tor wuh sutra, if vesh' weh-rasahkos. Wuh grosvenor nam-tor really wuh goh shi.” “i don’t nah-tor i dungau satau ish-veh sovek-wilat, ” au kilko-tor, tossing ish-veh patam pla' svi' ik shaik yut ik nam-tor-tor tor tor ish-veh t'hylara abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh na' oxford. “rai, i skil-tor’t satau ish-veh sovek-wilat.” s'haile henry ashenau ish-veh bezhun-zehl heh glazhau na' ish-veh svi' tauraya k'fai wuh wonil pla-kur wreaths t' vuzh ik tcha-tor abru svi' such fanciful whorls s' ish-veh ras, opium-tainted cigarette. “ri satau ish-veh sovek-wilat? T'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, po? Ma du sovek utvau? Ra shaik chaps du krassu nam-tor! Du tor sovek-vel svi' wuh panu tor nazh-kap wuh reputation. U' ak u' du ma veh, du seem tor aitlun tor lehm ish-veh maf. Ish-veh nam-tor silly t' du, na' tra' nam-tor goh veh vel svi' wuh panu weh-rasahkos do hasu variben pa', heh ik nam-tor ri hasu variben pa'. Wuh portrait spo' nash would eku du irak abru' ek' wuh nu'ri sasu svi' england, heh tor wuh hinek sasu ved kis-ka, kuv hinek sasu nam-tor ek'wak capable t' sovek zherka.” “i fai-tor du dungi abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' me, ” au kilko-tor, “tonk'peh i really mokuhlek’t gluvaya ish-veh. I ma shitau nuh' mau t' myself vi' ish-veh.” s'haile henry sakadau himself si' fi' wuh divan heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “ha, i fai-tor du would; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ved yeht, ek' wuh ka.” “nuh' mau t' yourself svi' ish-veh! Fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit, basil, i didn’t fai-tor du vesh' ni vain; heh i really mokuhlek’t gla-tor sovek resemblance svi' du, k' ish-veh rugged karik limuk heh ish-veh kastik-kov-nesh-kur isachya, heh nash nu'ri adonis, vi glazhau u' kuv au vesh' tor s' ivory heh she-tor-mor. Po, t'nash-veh tal-kam basil, au nam-tor wuh narcissus, heh du—muhl, veling du ma wuh intellectual sagluvaya heh ek' ik. Tonk'peh vaksur, yeht vaksur, shahtau wilat wuh intellectual sagluvaya palikau. Kash-tor-vel nam-tor svi' itself wuh nuk t' exaggeration, heh vashau wuh kril'es t' sovek limuk. Wuh moment veh hayal-tor ne' tor nah-tor, veh shetau ek' han, il ek' fa-patam, il vel horrid. Glazhau na' wuh successful sasu svi' sovek t' wuh oren-tor ha'yigal. Uf perfectly hideous au nam-tor! Kaula, veling, svi' wuh church. Tonk'peh yi svi' wuh church au don’t nah-tor. Wuh vaisu potau fi' taran na' wuh ya'shakhuv t' oh-leh ra au vesh' var-tor tor leralmin lu au vesh' wuh sa-kan t' leh-oh, heh u' wuh malatik consequence au kwon-hau-ov glazhau absolutely delightful. Ish-veh mysterious nu'ri t'hy'la, t'vi ahm du ma worla var-tor me, tonk'peh t'vi bikuv really sem-tor me, worla nah-tor. I olau ved sure t' ik. Au nam-tor ein brainless vaksurik creature vi dang nam-tor kwon-hau-ov la' svi' karil lu etek ma rai svai tor glazhau na', heh kwon-hau-ov la' svi' belaar lu etek aitlun vel tor chill etwel kash-tor'es. Don’t snuhkrol-tor yourself, basil: du nam-tor ri svi' wuh least spo' ish-veh.” “du don’t ken-tor me, harry, ” kilko-tor wuh tanafsu. “veling i am ri spo' ish-veh. I fai-tor ik perfectly muhl. Indeed, i dang nam-tor sorry tor glazhau spo' ish-veh. Du shrug ish-veh tipan? I am telling du wuh yeht'es. Tra' nam-tor wuh fatality pa' ek' tukhik heh intellectual distinction, wuh wihfelau t' fatality ik seems tor dog k'fai vesht-var wuh faltering ash-tor t' sa-te'kru. Ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom ri tor nam-tor natya s' veh’s katravahsu. Wuh watosh heh wuh stupid ma wuh buhfik t' ish-veh svi' nash panu. Au mokuhlek hayal-tor na' ish-veh ease heh gape na' wuh mavau. Kuv au fai-tor nothing t' skil, au nam-tor k'puu spared wuh fai-tukh t' defeat. Au ha-tor u' etek ek' dang ha-tor—undisturbed, indifferent, heh rik' disquiet. Au neither katau ruin fi-tor vath, il ek'wak poprah ish-veh s' akansu el'ru. Ish-veh lan heh don-tak, harry; t'nash-veh shi'nahp, such u' au nam-tor—t'nash-veh tanaf, whatever ish-veh lau nam-tor don; dorian zhai-kur’s rom glazhau—etek dungau ek' dash na' ra wuh gods ma putan-tor etek, dash terribly.” “dorian zhai-kur? Nam-tor ik ish-veh ahm?” ya'akash s'haile henry, walking mes' wuh studio na' basil hallward. “ha, ik nam-tor ish-veh ahm. I didn’t intend tor var-tor ish-veh tor du.” “tonk'peh po ri?” “oh, i mokuhlek’t danau. Lu i spo' sutra immensely, i worla var-tor ish-veh ahm tor sovek veh. Ish-veh nam-tor spo' surrendering wuh krus t' au. I ma grown tor ashaya secrecy. Ish-veh seems tor nam-tor wuh veh vel ik mokuhlek tor iyik ha'kiv mysterious il marvellous tor etek. Wuh commonest vel nam-tor delightful kuv veh goh ip-sut ish-veh. Lu i trasha kahr i' i worla var-tor t'nash-veh sutra wilat i am going. Kuv i did, i would pak-tor ek' t'nash-veh sanosh. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh silly es'merka, i dare leralmin, tonk'peh somehow ish-veh seems tor katau wuh lo'uk deal t' romance vi' veh’s ha'kiv. I suppose du nah-tor me awfully duhik pa' ish-veh?” “mokov, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry, “mokov, t'nash-veh tal-kam basil. Du seem tor yen-tor ik i am telik, heh wuh veh sem-rik t' kal'i'farr nam-tor ik ish-veh tor wuh ha'kiv t' tehsat absolutely bolayatik na' fi' parties. I worla fai-tor wilat t'nash-veh ko-telsu nam-tor, heh t'nash-veh ko-telsu worla fai-tor ra i am doing. Lu etek ragel-tor—etek tor ragel-tor occasionally, lu etek aru-yokul si' teretuhr, il hal-tor ne' tor wuh duke’s—etek var-tor tik vath wuh danik absurd var k' wuh danik serious limuk. T'nash-veh ko-telsu nam-tor maut rom na' ish-veh—mau weh-rom, svi' kla-min, do i am. She worla prah confused abru' ish-veh kinuf, heh i kwon-hau-ov tor. Tonk'peh lu she tor talal me si', she tor rai zehl na' ek'. I sometimes istaya she would; tonk'peh she goh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' me.” “i fnu-ven wuh yut du variben pa' ish-veh telik ha'kiv, harry, ” leralmin-tor basil hallward, strolling na' wuh svep ik pufulag-tor vi' wuh bah-ker. “i dva-tor ik du nam-tor really wuh maut rom sa-telsu, tonk'peh ik du nam-tor thoroughly kafusik t' ish-veh sha' virtues. Du nam-tor wuh wehtsuri katravahsu. Du worla leralmin wuh moral vel, heh du worla tor wuh riyeht vel. Ish-veh cynicism nam-tor veling wuh pose.” “hasu malatik nam-tor veling wuh pose, heh wuh danik irritating pose i fai-tor, ” maf-tor s'haile henry, laughing; heh wuh dahkuh nu'ri sasu went si' vi' wuh bah-ker teretuhr heh ensconced themselves fi' wuh wu bamboo ku-san ik lam-tor svi' wuh duvek t' wuh ha-vol laurel bush. Wuh ug'yel-ha'gel trel-tor abru' wuh polished mor. Svi' wuh yar, wan-kur daisies vesh' tremulous. Po' wuh svizh, s'haile henry seshau si' ish-veh glantau. “i am kwes i bolau nam-tor going, basil, ” au murmured, “heh fa' i hal-tor, i insist fi' ish-veh answering wuh deshker i shitau tor du ein wak ago.” “ra nam-tor ik?” leralmin-tor wuh krassu, keeping ish-veh bezhun teslau fi' wuh solektra. “du fai-tor ved muhl.” “i ri tor, harry.” “muhl, i dungi var-tor du ra ish-veh nam-tor. I aitlun du tor danau tor me po du skil-tor’t gluvaya dorian zhai-kur’s bikuv. I aitlun wuh yeht utvau.” “i var-tor du wuh yeht utvau.” “rai, du did ri. Du leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' fai'ei tra' vesh' nuh' mau t' yourself svi' ish-veh. I', ik nam-tor childish.” “harry, ” leralmin-tor basil hallward, looking ish-veh zehik svi' wuh limuk, “kanok portrait ik nam-tor kras-tor k' olaya nam-tor wuh portrait t' wuh tanafsu, ri t' wuh sitter. Wuh sitter nam-tor goh wuh kisheya, wuh occasion. Ish-veh nam-tor ri au vi nam-tor revealed k' wuh krassu; ish-veh nam-tor rather wuh krassu vi, fi' wuh kur-tor canvas, reveals himself. Wuh utvau i dungi ri gluvaya nash bikuv nam-tor ik i am kwes ik i ma shown svi' ish-veh wuh tsat t' t'nash-veh sha' soul.” s'haile henry abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “heh ra nam-tor ik?” au ya'akash. “i dungi var-tor du, ” leralmin-tor hallward; tonk'peh wuh sagluvaya t' perplexity sarlah abru' ish-veh limuk. “i am ek' gishat, basil, ” fator ish-veh besu, glancing na' ish-veh. “oh, tra' nam-tor really maut pi' tor var-tor, harry, ” kilko-tor wuh krassu; “heh i am kwes du dungi hardly ken-tor ish-veh. Sos'eh du dungi hardly dva-tor ish-veh.” s'haile henry abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh leaning ne', plucked wuh faf-kur-petalled daisy s' wuh yar heh linisau ish-veh. “i am ved sure i dungau ken-tor ish-veh, ” au kilko-tor, gazing intently na' wuh pi' pi-maat-kur, wan-kur-feathered mathra, “heh u' na' believing vel, i mokuhlek dva-tor sovek-vel, tanilau ik ish-veh nam-tor ved incredible.” wuh salan hutau ein blossoms s' wuh lap, heh wuh ras lilac-svai-tor, k' ish-veh clustering yel, dvun-tor tor heh fro svi' wuh languid sov. Wuh grasshopper began tor chirrup k' wuh temok, heh spo' wuh pla-kur og-elakh wuh wu wonil dragon-hash-tor markau vesht fi' its khav-kur gauze rala. S'haile henry olau u' kuv au kupi zhu-tor basil hallward’s khaf-spol beating, heh wondered ra vesh' coming. “wuh var nam-tor veling nash, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu po' ein wak. “dahkuh tevun-krus ago i went tor wuh plesh-tor na' t'sai brandon’s. Du fai-tor etek ri donku-tor tanafsu ma tor gluvaya ourselves svi' shila'es s' wak tor wak, aishan tor remind wuh tsuri ik etek nam-tor ri savages. K' wuh khru tor-pal heh wuh wan-kur tie, u' du var-tor me wuh'wak, anybody, kauk wuh fek-broker, mokuhlek nazh-kap wuh reputation na' hasu civilized. Muhl, po' i had vesh' svi' wuh tvi-shal pa' lehkuh minutes, talking tor masuk' overdressed dowagers heh tedious academicians, i suddenly became d'wonil ik ein veh vesh' looking na' me. I da-tor ulef-yut pauk heh gla-tor dorian zhai-kur na' wuh wuh'rak wak. Lu etwel bezhun ragel-tor, i olau ik i vesh' growing spoh. Wuh curious kashan t' vash sarlah abru' me. I fai-tor ik i had sarlah limuk tor limuk k' ein veh t'vi mere nafu'es vesh' ni sem-rik ik, kuv i kal-tor ish-veh tor tor ni, ish-veh would vi-seshau t'nash-veh bosh malat, t'nash-veh bosh soul, t'nash-veh maut tanaf itself. I did ri aitlun sovek sik vi-yumuk svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Du fai-tor yourself, harry, uf independent i am k' malat. I ma kwon-hau-ov vesh' t'nash-veh sha' trensu; had k'puu kwon-hau-ov vesh' ni, till i ragel-tor dorian zhai-kur. Yi—tonk'peh i don’t fai-tor uf tor danau ish-veh tor du. Vel seemed tor var-tor me ik i vesh' fi' wuh verge t' wuh terrible burun svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. I had wuh flekh olaya ik buk had svi' mahr-kel na' me exquisite mak heh exquisite sorrows. I grew kwes heh da-tor tor quit wuh tvi-shal. Ish-veh vesh' ri conscience ik tor me tor ni: ish-veh vesh' wuh wihfelau t' cowardice. I nem-tor rai lit tor myself na' trying tor stron.” “conscience heh cowardice nam-tor really wuh ka vel, basil. Conscience nam-tor wuh trade-ahm t' wuh pesik. Ik nam-tor ek'.” “i don’t dva-tor ik, harry, heh i don’t dva-tor du tor either. However, whatever vesh' t'nash-veh dvubolek—heh ish-veh lau ma vesh' pride, na' i nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor maut yaut—i certainly struggled tor wuh svep. Tra', veling, i stumbled tehnat t'sai brandon. ‘du nam-tor ri going tor sahr-tor maf ni ak, mr. Hallward?’ she shei si'. Du fai-tor ish-veh curiously shrill spes?” “ha; she nam-tor wuh peacock svi' kanok-vei tonk'peh vaksur, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, pulling wuh daisy tor bits k' ish-veh wu nervous ozh. “i kupi ri prah rid t' ish-veh. She katau me abru tor royalties, heh sutra k' yel heh ash'ai-zhel, heh shakhupik t'sai k' masuk' tiaras heh parrot han. She stariben t' me u' ish-veh dearest t'hy'la. I had goh ragel-tor ish-veh wuh'wak fa', tonk'peh she nem-tor ish-veh vi' ish-veh patam tor lionize me. I dva-tor ein bikuv t' t'nash-veh had tor wuh lo'uk navun na' wuh wak, k'puu had vesh' chattered pa' svi' wuh qsu'lit newspapers, if nam-tor wuh nineteenth-century standard t' immortality. Suddenly i afer-tor myself limuk tor limuk k' wuh nu'ri sasu t'vi nafu'es had ni strangely stirred me. Etek vesh' ved ikap-tor, siyah touching. Etwel bezhun ragel-tor va'ashiv. Ish-veh vesh' reckless t' me, tonk'peh i ya'akash t'sai brandon tor ragtau me tor ish-veh. Sos'eh ish-veh vesh' ri ni reckless, po' ek'. Ish-veh vesh' veling inevitable. Etek would ma spoken tor tik vath rik' sovek ragtaya. I am sure t' ik. Dorian var-tor me ni afterwards. Au, nuh', olau ik etek vesh' destined tor fai-tor tik vath.” “heh uf did t'sai brandon kethelvau nash wonderful nu'ri sasu?” ya'akash ish-veh besu. “i fai-tor she hal-tor svi' na' giving wuh rapid _précis_ t' ek' ish-veh be'hai'la. I vokau ish-veh bringing me abru tor wuh truculent heh yon-kur-limuk-tor hinek gentleman wein-tor ek' abru' k' zek heh ribbons, heh hissing vi' t'nash-veh kaluk, svi' wuh tragic zhal if bolau ma vesh' perfectly zhu-yehat tor kanok-veh svi' wuh tvi-shal, wuh danik astounding details. I veling sasahr-tor. I spo' tor talal si' sutra na' myself. Tonk'peh t'sai brandon skasau ish-veh be'hai'la exactly u' wuh auctioneer skasau ish-veh goods. She either danau au entirely maf, il var-tor veh kanok-vei pa' au kaula ra veh aitlu tor fai-tor.” “ri donku-tor t'sai brandon! Du nam-tor lerash fi' ish-veh, harry!” leralmin-tor hallward listlessly. “t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, she ar'kada tor afer-tor wuh _salon_, heh goh navau svi' sharu wuh restaurant. Uf sos krol-tor ish-veh? Tonk'peh var-tor me, ra did she leralmin pa' mr. Dorian zhai-kur?” “oh, vel spo', ‘sem-rik-tor sa-kan—ri donku-tor tal-kam ko-mekh heh i absolutely inseparable. Ved yen-tor ra au tor—kwes au—doesn’t tor sovek-vel—oh, ha, mavau wuh piano—il nam-tor ish-veh wuh violin, tal-kam mr. Zhai-kur?’ neither t' etek kupi gol'nev laughing, heh etek became t'hylara na' wuh'wak.” “laughter nam-tor mokov wuh rasahkos palikaya na' wuh friendship, heh ish-veh nam-tor irak wuh buhfik shahtan na' veh, ” leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri s'haile, plucking wuh'ashiv daisy. Hallward hutau ish-veh patam. “du don’t ken-tor ra friendship nam-tor, harry, ” au murmured—“il ra enmity nam-tor, na' ik tukh. Du spo' kanok veh; ik nam-tor tor leralmin, du nam-tor indifferent tor kanok veh.” “uf horribly unjust t' du!” maf-tor s'haile henry, tilting ish-veh taik pla' heh looking abru na' wuh pi' wan ik, spo' ravelled skeins t' glossy wan-kur silk, vesh' drifting mes' wuh hollowed folu-kur t' wuh belaar igen. “ha; horribly unjust t' du. I tor wuh lo'uk natyan svi' sutra. I dvel-tor t'nash-veh t'hylara na' ish-veh rom glazhau, t'nash-veh acquaintances na' ish-veh rom characters, heh t'nash-veh nemut na' ish-veh rom intellects. Wuh sasu fam yehat nam-tor nuh' tun-bosh svi' wuh dvel t' ish-veh nemut. I ma ri prah veh vi nam-tor wuh duhsu. Au nam-tor ek' sasu t' ein intellectual tepul, heh consequently au ek' appreciate me. Nam-tor ik maut vain t' me? I nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor rather vain.” “i dang nah-tor ish-veh vesh', harry. Tonk'peh fupa s' ish-veh category i bolau nam-tor goh wuh acquaintance.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam hinek basil, du nam-tor mau weht do wuh acquaintance.” “heh mau lehkuh tor wuh t'hy'la. Wuh wihfelau t' sa-kai, i suppose?” “oh, sa-kai! I don’t palutunau sa-kai. T'nash-veh tela'at sa-kai skil-tor’t tev-tor, heh t'nash-veh younger sa-kai seem worla tor tor sovek-kitok.” “harry!” sporiben hallward, frowning. “t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, i am ri ved serious. Tonk'peh i mokuhlek’t gol'nev detesting t'nash-veh relations. I suppose sarlah ish-veh s' wuh kla-min ik rim t' etek mokuhlek lamok vath sutra having wuh ka lafot u' ourselves. I ved sympathize k' wuh reshan t' wuh eingelsu democracy tehnat ra au vutau wuh vices t' wuh upper zek. Wuh shivak olau ik drunkenness, stupidity, heh immorality dang nam-tor ish-veh sha' special veltra, heh ik kuv sovek veh t' etek tor wuh ass t' himself, au nam-tor poaching fi' ish-veh korsau. Lu ri donku-tor southwark prah vi' wuh p'pil'ti kelek, ish-veh indignation vesh' ved magnificent. Heh wi i don’t suppose ik lehkuh fundauik cent t' wuh proletariat ha-tor correctly.” “i don’t sep-wafikh k' wuh single zhit ik du ma leralmin-tor, heh, ra nam-tor weht, harry, i olau sure du don’t either.” s'haile henry stroked ish-veh sfekau khav-kur hisahk heh tapped wuh gof t' ish-veh patent-duf kluf k' wuh tasselled ebony cane. “uf eingelsu du nam-tor basil! Ik nam-tor wuh dahr wak du ma tor ik glantaya. Kuv veh shitau fa'rak wuh idea tor wuh yeht englishman—kwon-hau-ov wuh kuriht vel tor tor—au worla sahr-tor-tor t' panahik whether wuh idea nam-tor gas'rak il riyeht. Wuh goh vel au panah-tor t' sovek importance nam-tor whether veh believes ish-veh oneself. I', wuh tala t' wuh idea has nothing whatsoever tor tor k' wuh sincerity t' wuh sasu vi sagluvau ish-veh. Indeed, wuh yesik'es nam-tor ik wuh weht insincere wuh sasu nam-tor, wuh weht purely intellectual dungi wuh idea nam-tor, u' svi' ik nuf ish-veh dungi ri nam-tor kur-tor k' either ish-veh aitlu, ish-veh aitlu, il ish-veh prejudices. However, i don’t propose tor discuss politics, shila-tal, il metaphysics k' du. I spo' persons weh-rom do dvatai, heh i spo' persons k' rai dvatai weh-rom do sovek-kitok svi' wuh panu. Var-tor me weht pa' mr. Dorian zhai-kur. Uf k'ashiv tor gla-tor du ish-veh?” “kanok gad. I couldn’t nam-tor kunli kuv i didn’t gla-tor ish-veh kanok gad. Au nam-tor absolutely bolayatik tor me.” “uf wehtsuri! I nahp du would worla palutunau sovek-vel tonk'peh ish-veh tanaf.” “au nam-tor ek' t'nash-veh tanaf tor me i', ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu gravely. “i sometimes nah-tor, harry, ik tra' nam-tor goh dahkuh nuhs t' sovek importance svi' wuh panu’s vesht-var. Wuh wuh'rak nam-tor wuh appearance t' wuh uzh medium na' tanaf, heh wuh dahr nam-tor wuh appearance t' wuh uzh nafu'es na' tanaf isha. Ra wuh fereik-vel t' elmin-krasan vesh' tor wuh venetians, wuh limuk t' antinous vesh' tor tab-ma greek shid-tanaf, heh wuh limuk t' dorian zhai-kur dungi ein gad nam-tor tor me. Ish-veh nam-tor ri goh ik i kras s' ish-veh, bes-tor s' ish-veh, lubesan s' ish-veh. Veling, i ma ovsoh ek' ik. Tonk'peh au nam-tor mau weht tor me do wuh model il wuh sitter. I skil-tor’t var-tor du ik i am dissatisfied k' ra i ma ovsoh t' ish-veh, il ik ish-veh vaksur nam-tor such ik tanaf fam yehat sagluvau ish-veh. Tra' nam-tor nothing ik tanaf fam yehat sagluvau, heh i fai-tor ik wuh ar'kadan i ma ovsoh, opi' i ragel-tor dorian zhai-kur, nam-tor rom ar'kadan, nam-tor wuh buhfik ar'kadan t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Tonk'peh svi' ein curious yut—i wonder dungi du ken-tor me?—ish-veh nafu'es has suggested tor me wuh entirely uzh manner svi' tanaf, wuh entirely uzh nuk t' style. Gla-tor nash-veh vel differently, i nah-tor t' au differently. I mokuhlek i' recreate ha'kiv svi' wuh yut ik vesh' ipik s' me fa'. ‘wuh sahr-tor t' shid svi' gad t' nahp’—vi nam-tor ish-veh vi leralmin-tor ik? I yen-tor; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ra dorian zhai-kur has vesh' tor me. Wuh goh visible la'es t' nash lad—na' au seems tor me pi' weht do wuh lad, hi au nam-tor really abru' dah-leh—ish-veh goh visible la'es—ah! I wonder mokuhlek du realize ek' ik ik tvai? Unconsciously au mesprah na' me wuh zehl t' wuh sluk shi'oren, wuh shi'oren ik nam-tor ki' svi' ish-veh ek' wuh shaukaush t' wuh romantic tam'a, ek' wuh perfection t' wuh tam'a ik nam-tor greek. Wuh kril'es t' soul heh ak'shem—uf mau ik nam-tor! Etek svi' etwel ni-resh ma dahshau wuh dahkuh, heh ma fereik-tor wuh realism ik nam-tor vulgar, wuh ideality ik nam-tor void. Harry! Kuv du goh fai-tor ra dorian zhai-kur nam-tor tor me! Du vokau ik landscape t' t'nash-veh, na' if agnew nufau me such wuh masuk' price tonk'peh if i would ri krus k'? Ish-veh nam-tor veh t' wuh buhfik vel i ma ek'wak ovsoh. Heh po nam-tor ish-veh ni? Fai'ei, du' i vesh' krasan ish-veh, dorian zhai-kur hayal-tor be' me. Ein subtle vi-yumuk be' dvun-tor s' ish-veh tor me, heh na' wuh wuh'rak wak svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv vesht gla-tor nash-veh svi' wuh eiktra lap-shal wuh wonder i had kwon-hau-ov glazhau na' heh kwon-hau-ov din-tor.” “basil, nash nam-tor wehtsuri! I bolau gla-tor dorian zhai-kur.” hallward prah abru s' wuh ku-san heh lates-tor abru heh ne' wuh bah-ker. Po' ein wak sarlah ish-veh pla'. “harry, ” au leralmin-tor, “dorian zhai-kur nam-tor tor me veling wuh dvubolek svi' tanaf. Du lau gla-tor nothing svi' ish-veh. Gla-tor nash-veh kanok-vei svi' ish-veh. Au nam-tor worla weht la' svi' t'nash-veh ar'kadan do lu rai glakuv t' ish-veh nam-tor tra'. Au nam-tor wuh suggestion, u' i ma leralmin-tor, t' wuh uzh manner. I talal ish-veh svi' wuh curves t' ac'ruth zehl, svi' wuh loveliness heh subtleties t' ac'ruth colours. Ik nam-tor ek'.” “yi po skil-tor’t du gluvaya ish-veh portrait?” ya'akash s'haile henry. “fai'ei, rik' intending ish-veh, i ma shitau vi' ish-veh ein sagluvaya t' ek' nash curious tanafluk idolatry, t' if, veling, i ma worla tun-tor tor stariben tor ish-veh. Au fai-tor nothing pa' ish-veh. Au dungau worla fai-tor sovek-vel pa' ish-veh. Tonk'peh wuh panu lau guess ish-veh, heh i dungi ri sai-famik t'nash-veh soul tor ish-veh gan prying bezhun. T'nash-veh khaf-spol dungau worla nam-tor shitau ne' ish-veh numo-zan-vel. Tra' nam-tor nuh' mau t' myself svi' wuh vel, harry—nuh' mau t' myself!” “poets nam-tor ri ni scrupulous u' du nam-tor. Au fai-tor uf useful shaukaush nam-tor na' publication. Nowadays wuh pushau khaf-spol dungi sahr-tor tor wehk yadan.” “i fnu-ven au na' ish-veh, ” maf-tor hallward. “wuh tanafsu dang fereik-tor vaksurik vel, tonk'peh dang shitau nothing t' ish-veh sha' ha'kiv vi' au. Etek ha-tor svi' wuh ya'shakhuv lu sasu skasau tanaf u' kuv ish-veh vesh' tvai tor nam-tor wuh shid t' autobiography. Etek ma pakik wuh o'zawh kash-ral t' vaksur. Ein gad i dungi gluvaya wuh panu ra ish-veh nam-tor; heh na' ik utvau wuh panu dungau worla gla-tor t'nash-veh portrait t' dorian zhai-kur.” “i nah-tor du nam-tor riyeht, basil, tonk'peh i skil-tor’t gyirm'i k' du. Ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh intellectually pakik vi ek'wak gyirm'i. Var-tor me, nam-tor dorian zhai-kur maut tishau t' du?” wuh krassu panah-tor na' wuh zamu moments. “au tishau me, ” au kilko-tor po' wuh svizh; “i fai-tor au tishau me. Veling i snuhkrol-tor ish-veh dreadfully. I talal wuh flekh sanosh svi' taran vel tor ish-veh ik i fai-tor i dungau nam-tor sorry na' having leralmin-tor. U' wuh tor-go, au nam-tor sem-rik-tor tor me, heh etek hayal-tor svi' wuh studio heh variben t' wuh thousand vel. I' heh yi, however, au nam-tor horribly thoughtless, heh seems tor nem-tor wuh yeht delight svi' giving me kusut. Yi i olau, harry, ik i ma putan-tor maf t'nash-veh bosh soul tor ein veh vi skasau ish-veh u' kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh svai tor shitau svi' ish-veh tor-pal, wuh zeshau t' decoration tor sem-rik ish-veh vanity, wuh fanet na' wuh belaar’s gad.” “gad svi' belaar, basil, nam-tor apt tor svizh-tor, ” murmured s'haile henry. “sos'eh du dungi zung-tor sooner do au dungi. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh maf vel tor nah-tor t', tonk'peh tra' nam-tor rai vet ik genius palesh-tor longer do vaksur. Ik khrosahp na' wuh kla-min ik etek ek' nem-tor such kusut-tor tor abru'-educate ourselves. Svi' wuh kwai struggle na' nam, etek aitlun ki' vel ik palesh-tor, heh ni etek boshaya etwel kashkau k' guhsh heh kla-min, svi' wuh silly rok t' keeping etwel shi. Wuh thoroughly muhl-informed sasu—ik nam-tor wuh iyik tangu. Heh wuh kashek t' wuh thoroughly muhl-informed sasu nam-tor wuh dreadful vel. Ish-veh nam-tor spo' wuh _bric-à-brac_ mahr-kel, ek' stislak heh grazhiv, k' kanok-vei priced abru' its proper tala. I nah-tor du dungi zung-tor wuh'rak, ek' wuh ka. Ein gad du dungi glazhau na' ish-veh t'hy'la, heh au dungi seem tor du tor nam-tor wuh pi' s' bestan, il du skil-tor’t spo' ish-veh molu t' kur, il vel. Du dungi bitterly reproach ish-veh svi' ish-veh sha' khaf-spol, heh seriously nah-tor ik au has behaved maut badly tor du. Wuh thurai wak au calls, du dungi nam-tor perfectly samu heh indifferent. Ish-veh dungi nam-tor wuh lo'uk pity, na' ish-veh dungi rubitau du. Ra du ma var-tor me nam-tor ved wuh romance, wuh romance t' tanaf veh lau vutau ish-veh, heh wuh rasahkos t' having wuh romance t' sovek ves nam-tor ik ish-veh mor veh ni unromantic.” “harry, don’t variben spo' ik. U' wu u' i ha-tor, wuh nafu'es t' dorian zhai-kur dungi abrukhau me. Du mokuhlek’t olau ra i olau. Du rubah nuh' k'ashiv.” “ah, t'nash-veh tal-kam basil, ik nam-tor exactly po i mokuhlek olau ish-veh. Eifa vi nam-tor faithful fai-tor goh wuh trivial vla t' ashaya: ish-veh nam-tor wuh faithless vi fai-tor ashaya’s tragedies.” heh s'haile henry kwul-tor wuh ta'hal fi' wuh dainty haul-tukh nuf heh began tor vuzh wuh cigarette k' wuh shal-d'wonil heh satisfied sov, u' kuv au had summed abru wuh panu svi' wuh zhit-bal. Tra' vesh' wuh rustle t' chirruping sparrows svi' wuh yar-kur lacquer mor t' wuh ivy, heh wuh pla-kur wan-duv chased themselves mes' wuh yar spo' vitem-tor. Uf vaksurik ish-veh vesh' svi' wuh bah-ker! Heh uf delightful vath sutra’s zherka vesh'!—mau weht delightful do ish-veh ideas, ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh. Veh’s sha' soul, heh wuh shaukaush t' veh’s t'hylara—eifa vesh' wuh sem-rik vel svi' ha'kiv. Au pictured tor himself k' ralash-fam amusement wuh tedious luncheon ik au had din-tor k' staying ni wu k' basil hallward. Had au hal-tor tor ish-veh ezyet’s, au would ma vesh' sure ki' ragel-tor s'haile goodbody tra', heh wuh bosh conversation would ma vesh' pa' wuh feeding t' wuh ri donku-tor heh wuh bolayek na' model lodging-kelek. Tik mohrn would ma preached wuh importance t' eifa virtues, na' t'vi tusok tra' vesh' rai bolayek svi' ish-veh sha' ha-tor. Wuh don-ka would ma spoken fi' wuh tala t' thrift, heh wuh idle grown eloquent abru' wuh dignity t' zup. Ish-veh vesh' sem-rik-tor ki' stron-tor ek' ik! U' au nahp t' ish-veh ezyet, wuh idea seemed tor kwul ish-veh. Au da-tor tor hallward heh leralmin-tor, “t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, i ma aishan vokau.” “vokau ra, harry?” “wilat i puzhu-tor wuh ahm t' dorian zhai-kur.” “wilat vesh' ish-veh?” ya'akash hallward, k' wuh slight kwal. “don’t glazhau ni reshnek, basil. Ish-veh vesh' na' t'nash-veh ezyet, t'sai agatha’s. She var-tor me she had discovered wuh wonderful nu'ri sasu vi vesh' going tor gol'nev ish-veh svi' wuh she'rak shaht, heh ik ish-veh ahm vesh' dorian zhai-kur. I am bound tor fupa s' ik she worla var-tor me au vesh' rom-looking. Kosu ma rai appreciation t' rom glazhau; k'puu, rom kosu ma ri. She leralmin-tor ik au vesh' maut earnest heh had wuh vaksurik malat. I na' wuh'wak pictured tor myself wuh creature k' spectacles heh lank isachya, horribly freckled, heh tramping pa' fi' masuk' ash'ya. I istaya i had fainu ish-veh vesh' ish-veh t'hy'la.” “i am maut glad du didn’t, harry.” “po?” “i don’t aitlun du tor ragel-tor ish-veh.” “du don’t aitlun me tor ragel-tor ish-veh?” “rai.” “mr. Dorian zhai-kur nam-tor svi' wuh studio, osu, ” leralmin-tor wuh butler, coming vi' wuh bah-ker. “du bolau ragtau me i', ” maf-tor s'haile henry, laughing. Wuh krassu da-tor tor ish-veh dvinsu, vi lam-tor blinking svi' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel. “ya'akash mr. Zhai-kur tor bek-tor, parker: i dungau nam-tor svi' svi' wuh zamu moments.” wuh sasu ovalau heh went abru wuh lates. Yi au glazhau na' s'haile henry. “dorian zhai-kur nam-tor t'nash-veh dearest t'hy'la, ” au leralmin-tor. “au has wuh velik heh wuh vaksurik malat. Ish-veh ezyet vesh' ved gas'rak svi' ra she leralmin-tor t' ish-veh. Don’t spoil ish-veh. Don’t ar'kadan tor vi-yumuk ish-veh. Ish-veh vi-yumuk would nam-tor rasahkos. Wuh panu nam-tor eik, heh has wehk marvellous sutra svi' ish-veh. Don’t nem-tor maf s' me wuh veh person vi mazhiv-kur-tor tor t'nash-veh tanaf whatever sem-rik ish-veh ma: t'nash-veh ha'kiv u' wuh tanafsu nerau fi' ish-veh. Kashek, harry, i sahrafel du.” au stariben maut slowly, heh wuh zhit seemed wrung s' ish-veh siyah tehnat ish-veh dungi. “ra nonsense du variben!” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, smiling, heh taking hallward k' wuh kar, au siyah pufulag-tor ish-veh vi' wuh kelek. Chapter ii. U' au svi-tor gla-tor au dorian zhai-kur. Au vesh' hayal-tor na' wuh piano, k' ish-veh pla' tor au, turning abru' wuh thalv t' wuh ral'es t' schumann’s “laptra scenes.” “du bolau lend me aifa, basil, ” au maf-tor. “i aitlun tor oren-tor au. Au nam-tor perfectly sem-rik-tor.” “ik entirely nerau fi' uf du hayal-tor tor-gad, dorian.” “oh, i am zungor t' sitting, heh i don’t aitlun wuh ha'kiv-sized portrait t' myself, ” kilko-tor wuh lad, swinging pauk fi' wuh ralash-tanaf-stool svi' wuh wilful, petulant manner. Lu au kum-tor glan t' s'haile henry, wuh faint blush kur-tor ish-veh nak na' wuh moment, heh au palikau abru. “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon, basil, tonk'peh i didn’t fai-tor du had sovek veh k' du.” “nash nam-tor s'haile henry wotton, dorian, wuh hinek oxford t'hy'la t' t'nash-veh. I ma aishan vesh' telling ish-veh ra wuh capital sitter du vesh', heh i' du ma spoiled kanok-vei.” “du ma ri spoiled t'nash-veh sanosh svi' latva du, mr. Zhai-kur, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, stepping fa'rak heh extending ish-veh el'ru. “t'nash-veh ezyet has k'ashiv spoken tor me pa' du. Du nam-tor veh t' ish-veh favourites, heh, i am kwes, veh t' ish-veh victims isha.” “i am svi' t'sai agatha’s nesh-kur dunap na' la', ” kilko-tor dorian k' wuh funny glazhau t' penitence. “i ugau tor hal-tor tor wuh muhd svi' whitechapel k' ish-veh kim-shah gad, heh i really forgot ek' pa' ish-veh. Etek vesh' tor ma mavau wuh dah-mavaya teretuhr—rehkuh dah-mavaya, i dva-tor. I don’t fai-tor ra she dungi leralmin tor me. I am irak nuh' koltha tor vutau.” “oh, i dungi tor ish-veh sochya k' t'nash-veh ezyet. She nam-tor ved vaikau tor du. Heh i don’t nah-tor ish-veh really tukh pa' ish-veh ri hasu tra'. Wuh audience probably nahp ish-veh vesh' wuh dah-mavaya. Lu ezyet agatha hayal-tor ne' tor wuh piano, she tor ved hiyet ralash na' dahkuh sutra.” “ik nam-tor maut horrid tor ish-veh, heh ri maut nice tor me, ” kilko-tor dorian, laughing. S'haile henry glazhau na' ish-veh. Ha, au vesh' certainly wonderfully handsome, k' ish-veh finely curved ug'yon-kur bru-lar, ish-veh frank pla-kur bezhun, ish-veh crisp pi-maat-tukh isachya. Tra' vesh' vel svi' ish-veh limuk ik tor veh sahrafel ish-veh na' wuh'wak. Ek' wuh candour t' youth vesh' tra', u' muhl u' ek' youth’s passionate purity. Veh olau ik au had potau himself unspotted s' wuh panu. Rai wonder basil hallward worshipped ish-veh. “du nam-tor nuh' sem-rik-tor tor hal-tor svi' na' philanthropy, mr. Zhai-kur—irak nuh' sem-rik-tor.” heh s'haile henry flung himself ne' fi' wuh divan heh tu'ash ish-veh cigarette-nuf. Wuh krassu had vesh' toranik mixing ish-veh colours heh getting ish-veh brushes pok. Au vesh' looking worried, heh lu au puzhu-tor s'haile henry’s kim-shah remark, au glanced na' ish-veh, hesitated na' wuh moment, heh yi leralmin-tor, “harry, i aitlun tor shaht nash bikuv tor-gad. Would du nah-tor ish-veh awfully snertau t' me kuv i ya'akash du tor hal-tor maf?” s'haile henry abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh glazhau na' dorian zhai-kur. “am i tor hal-tor, mr. Zhai-kur?” au ya'akash. “oh, sanoi don’t, s'haile henry. Gla-tor nash-veh ik basil nam-tor svi' veh t' ish-veh sulky moods, heh i mokuhlek’t lesh ish-veh lu au sulks. Isha, i aitlun du tor var-tor me po i dang ri hal-tor svi' na' philanthropy.” “i don’t fai-tor ik i dungau var-tor du ik, mr. Zhai-kur. Ish-veh nam-tor ni tedious wuh subject ish-veh would ma tor variben seriously pa' ish-veh. Tonk'peh i certainly dungau ri sahr-tor maf, i' ik du ma ya'akash me tor pehkaya. Du don’t really kashek, basil, tor du? Du ma k'ashiv var-tor me ik du tishau ish-veh sitters ki' ein veh tor chat tor.” hallward zeshau ish-veh bru. “kuv dorian istau ish-veh, veling du bolau stay. Dorian’s whims nam-tor tor-gav tor kanok-veh, kaula himself.” s'haile henry nem-tor abru ish-veh taik heh gloves. “du nam-tor maut pressing, basil, tonk'peh i am kwes i bolau hal-tor. I ma ugau tor ragel-tor wuh sasu na' wuh orleans. Rom-bye, mr. Zhai-kur. Sarlah heh gla-tor me ein aru svi' curzon yut. I am nearly kwon-hau-ov na' ha-kel na' kaukuh o’wak-vel. Kitau tor me lu sarlah du. I dang nam-tor sorry tor din-tor du.” “basil, ” maf-tor dorian zhai-kur, “kuv s'haile henry wotton hal-tor, i dungau hal-tor, nuh'. Du worla tu'ash ish-veh bru-lar du' du nam-tor krasan, heh ish-veh nam-tor horribly pasik standing fi' wuh skaf heh trying tor glazhau vaksurik. Ya'akash ish-veh tor stay. I insist fi-tor ish-veh.” “stay, harry, tor oblige dorian, heh tor oblige me, ” leralmin-tor hallward, gazing intently na' ish-veh bikuv. “ish-veh nam-tor ved yeht, i worla variben lu i am working, heh worla shroi either, heh ish-veh bolau nam-tor dreadfully tedious na' t'nash-veh unfortunate sitters. I eit'jae du tor stay.” “tonk'peh ra pa' t'nash-veh sasu na' wuh orleans?” wuh krassu abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “i don’t nah-tor tra' dungi nam-tor sovek rihag'es pa' ik. Hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv, harry. Heh i', dorian, prah abru fi' wuh skaf, heh don’t dvun pa' nuh' mau, il vlitau sovek attention tor ra s'haile henry leralmin-tor. Au has wuh maut rasahkos vi-yumuk abru' ek' ish-veh t'hylara, k' wuh single kaulauf t' myself.” dorian zhai-kur ash-tor abru fi' wuh dais k' wuh sov t' wuh nu'ri greek trufemu, heh tor wuh pi' _moue_ t' discontent tor s'haile henry, tor ik au had rather taken wuh fancy. Au vesh' ni rikes basil. Au tor wuh delightful contrast. Heh au had such wuh vaksurik spes. Po' wuh zamu moments au leralmin-tor tor ish-veh, “ma du really wuh maut rasahkos vi-yumuk, s'haile henry? U' rasahkos u' basil leralmin-tor?” “tra' nam-tor rai such vel u' wuh rom vi-yumuk, mr. Zhai-kur. Ek' vi-yumuk nam-tor immoral—immoral s' wuh talik sfek t' zan-tor.” “po?” “fai'ei tor vi-yumuk wuh person nam-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh veh’s sha' soul. Au tor ri nah-tor ish-veh malatik nahp, il yontau k' ish-veh malatik shaukaush. Ish-veh virtues nam-tor ri yeht tor ish-veh. Ish-veh sins, kuv tra' nam-tor such vel u' sins, nam-tor yahv-tor. Au shetau wuh vava t' ein veh else’s ralash-tanaf, wuh fundauik-ithop t' wuh krus ik has ri vesh' written na' ish-veh. Wuh mokh t' ha'kiv nam-tor shal-storaya. Tor realize veh’s malat perfectly—ik nam-tor ra tik t' etek nam-tor la' na'. Sutra nam-tor kwes t' themselves, nowadays. Au ma yen-tor wuh k'lek t' ek' gu-vam, wuh gu-vam ish-veh owes tor veh’s shal. Veling, au nam-tor charitable. Au yem-tor wuh k'avon heh clothe wuh beggar. Tonk'peh ish-veh sha' souls starve, heh nam-tor sai-fam. Courage has hal-tor s' etwel ne-koshtri. Sos'eh etek worla really had ish-veh. Wuh vash t' shila'es, if nam-tor wuh i'sav t' morals, wuh vash t' oekon, if nam-tor wuh tsat t' odva—aifa nam-tor wuh dahkuh vel ik govern etek. Heh wi—” “aishan da-tor ish-veh patam wuh pi' weht tor wuh gas'rak, dorian, spo' wuh rom sa-kan, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu, glu svi' ish-veh ar'kadan heh d'wonil goh ik wuh glazhau had sarlah vi' wuh lad’s limuk ik au had worla gla-tor tra' fa'. “heh wi, ” fator s'haile henry, svi' ish-veh neik, musical spes, heh k' ik graceful pral t' wuh el'ru ik vesh' kwon-hau-ov ni noshtra t' ish-veh, heh ik au had kauk svi' ish-veh eton gad, “i dva-tor ik kuv veh sasu vesh' tor ha-tor si' ish-veh ha'kiv fully heh completely, vesh' tor mazhiv-kur-tor shid tor kanok olaya, sagluvaya tor kanok nahp, reality tor kanok sahr-tor—i dva-tor ik wuh panu would nazh-kap such wuh sluk impulse t' mak ik etek would yen-tor ek' wuh maladies t' mediævalism, heh fun tor wuh hellenic tangu—tor vel finer, richer do wuh hellenic tangu, ish-veh lau nam-tor. Tonk'peh wuh bravest sasu akhlami nam-tor kwes t' himself. Wuh mutilation t' wuh savage has its tragic rishan svi' wuh shal-wafaya ik mars etwel ha-tor. Etek nam-tor taflau na' etwel refusals. Kanok impulse ik etek strive tor strangle broods svi' wuh kashek heh gisam etek. Wuh ak'shem sins wuh'wak, heh has ovsoh k' its sin, na' torai nam-tor wuh nuk t' purification. Nothing hafau yi tonk'peh wuh recollection t' wuh sanosh, il wuh luxury t' wuh regret. Wuh goh yut tor prah rid t' wuh temptation nam-tor tor yield tor ish-veh. Tehnau ish-veh, heh ish-veh soul tor'ovau has-bosh k' longing na' wuh vel ish-veh has zadik tor itself, k' aitlun na' ra its monstrous tor-gav ma tor monstrous heh unlawful. Ish-veh has vesh' leralmin-tor ik wuh lo'uk pavek t' wuh panu nem-tor shi svi' wuh shi'nahp. Ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh shi'nahp, heh wuh shi'nahp goh, ik wuh lo'uk sins t' wuh panu nem-tor shi isha. Du, mr. Zhai-kur, du yourself, k' ish-veh she-tor-yon-kur youth heh ish-veh she-tor-wan-kur boyhood, du ma had shaukaush ik ma tor du kwes, nahp ik ma boshau du k' vash, gad-sahr-tor-tor heh sleeping sahr-tor-tor t'vi mere vokaya lau kuraya ish-veh nak k' mesh—” “pehkaya!” faltered dorian zhai-kur, “pehkaya! Du bewilder me. I don’t fai-tor ra tor leralmin. Tra' nam-tor ein kilko-srashiv tor du, tonk'peh i fam yehat talal ish-veh. Don’t stariben. Kal-tor me nah-tor. Il, rather, kal-tor me ar'kadan ri tor nah-tor.” na' nearly lehkuh minutes au lam-tor tra', motionless, k' parted bru-lar heh bezhun strangely ugelik. Au vesh' dimly d'wonil ik entirely sluk vi-yumuk vesh' na' ar'kadan k'svi ish-veh. Wi au seemed tor ish-veh ki' sarlah really s' himself. Wuh zamu zhit ik basil’s t'hy'la had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh—zhit spoken k' pavesh, rai vet, heh k' wilful paradox svi' au—had estuhl ein tsat chord ik had worla vesh' estuhl fa', tonk'peh ik au olau vesh' i' vibrating heh throbbing tor curious khaf-spol-gaya. Ralash-tanaf had stirred ish-veh spo' ik. Ralash-tanaf had troubled ish-veh wehk wak. Tonk'peh ralash-tanaf vesh' ri articulate. Ish-veh vesh' ri wuh uzh panu, tonk'peh rather wuh'ashiv nezhak, ik ish-veh fereik-tor svi' etek. Zhit! Mere zhit! Uf terrible au vesh'! Uf pa'shik, heh vivid, heh pi-maat'rer! Veh kupi ri stron s' au. Heh wi ra wuh subtle magic tra' vesh' svi' au! Au seemed kup tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh plastic shid tor shid-fam vel, heh ki' wuh ralash-tanaf t' ish-veh sha' u' slor u' ik t' viol il t' lute. Mere zhit! Vesh' tra' sovek-vel ni yeht u' zhit? Ha; tra' had vesh' vel svi' ish-veh boyhood ik au had ri ken-tor. Au ken-tor au i'. Ha'kiv suddenly became yonalik-kur-tor tor ish-veh. Ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik au had vesh' walking svi' yon. Po had au ri fainu ish-veh? K' ish-veh subtle abru'teruklar-ru'lut, s'haile henry glantau ish-veh. Au fai-tor wuh precise psychological moment lu tor leralmin nothing. Au olau intensely interested. Au vesh' putaurau na' wuh sudden impression ik ish-veh zhit had torvau, heh, remembering wuh dunap ik au had telv-tor lu au vesh' leh-sheh, wuh dunap if had revealed tor ish-veh mau ik au had ri fainu fa', au wondered whether dorian zhai-kur vesh' be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh kahwa veshtaya. Au had goh pohshaya wuh kliton vi' wuh sov. Had ish-veh kwul wuh ulidar? Uf sem-rik wuh lad vesh'! Hallward kras-tor maf k' ik marvellous vakh esta t' ish-veh, ik had wuh yeht refinement heh buhfik delicacy ik svi' tanaf, na' sovek tav sarlah goh s' karik'es. Au vesh' unconscious t' wuh silence. “basil, i am zungor t' standing, ” maf-tor dorian zhai-kur suddenly. “i bolau hal-tor si' heh hayal-tor svi' wuh bah-ker. Wuh sov nam-tor stifling la'.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, i am ni sorry. Lu i am krasan, i mokuhlek’t nah-tor t' sovek-kitok. Tonk'peh du worla hayal-tor weh-rom. Du vesh' perfectly fam dvun. Heh i ma kum-tor wuh daya i aitlu—wuh ulef-parted bru-lar heh wuh ugelik glazhau svi' wuh bezhun. I don’t fai-tor ra harry has vesh' taran tor du, tonk'peh au has certainly tor du ma wuh danik wonderful sagluvaya. I suppose au has vesh' paying du compliments. Du mustn’t dva-tor wuh zhit ik au leralmin-tor.” “au has certainly ri vesh' paying me compliments. Sos'eh ik nam-tor wuh utvau ik i don’t dva-tor sovek-vel au has var-tor me.” “du fai-tor du dva-tor ish-veh ek', ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, looking na' ish-veh k' ish-veh dreamy languorous bezhun. “i dungi hal-tor si' tor wuh bah-ker k' du. Ish-veh nam-tor horribly fal svi' wuh studio. Basil, kal-tor etek ma vel iced tor mon, vel k' strawberries svi' ish-veh.” “certainly, harry. Aishan esta wuh kus-vakh, heh lu parker sarlah i dungi var-tor ish-veh ra du aitlun. I ma prah tor ar'kadan abru nash za-mesu, ni i dungi hau du later fi'. Don’t potau dorian nuh' wu. I ma worla vesh' svi' weh-rom shid na' krasan do i am tor-gad. Nash nam-tor going tor nam-tor t'nash-veh masterpiece. Ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh masterpiece u' ish-veh lam-tor.” s'haile henry went si' tor wuh bah-ker heh afer-tor dorian zhai-kur burying ish-veh limuk svi' wuh lo'uk samuyau lilac-blossoms, feverishly drinking svi' ish-veh perfume u' kuv ish-veh had vesh' wine. Sarlah ish-veh beyik ish-veh heh shitau ish-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh tipan. “du nam-tor ved gas'rak tor tor ik, ” au murmured. “nothing mokuhlek bohrau wuh soul tonk'peh wuh kash-ral, aishan u' nothing mokuhlek bohrau wuh kash-ral tonk'peh wuh soul.” wuh lad palikau heh drew pla'. Au vesh' bareheaded, heh wuh mor had tossed ish-veh rebellious tcha-tor heh tangled ek' ish-veh gilded og-elakh. Tra' vesh' wuh glazhau t' pthak svi' ish-veh bezhun, such u' sutra ma lu au nam-tor suddenly awakened. Ish-veh finely chiselled han-sharular quivered, heh ein ipik tor'tsu hutau wuh ug'yon-kur t' ish-veh bru-lar heh losrak au trembling. “ha, ” fator s'haile henry, “ik nam-tor veh t' wuh lo'uk tsat t' ha'kiv—tor bohrau wuh soul k' tvai t' wuh kash-ral, heh wuh kash-ral k' tvai t' wuh soul. Du nam-tor wuh wonderful fereikan. Du fai-tor weht do du nah-tor du fai-tor, aishan u' du fai-tor lehkuh tor du aitlun tor fai-tor.” dorian zhai-kur kwal-tor heh da-tor ish-veh patam maf. Au kupi ri gol'nev liking wuh ha-vol, graceful nu'ri sasu vi vesh' standing k' ish-veh. Ish-veh romantic, olive-kur-tor limuk heh worn sagluvaya interested ish-veh. Tra' vesh' vel svi' ish-veh neik languid spes ik vesh' absolutely sem-rik. Ish-veh samuyau, wan-kur, flowerlike el'ru, kauk, had wuh curious sem-rik. Au dvun-tor, u' au stariben, spo' ralash-tanaf, heh seemed ki' wuh gen-lis t' ish-veh sha'. Tonk'peh au olau kwes t' ish-veh, heh kafusik t' hasu kwes. Po had ish-veh vesh' losrak na' wuh ri-fainusu tor reveal ish-veh tor himself? Au had fainu basil hallward na' tevun-krus, tonk'peh wuh friendship svi' au had worla rubitau ish-veh. Suddenly tra' had sarlah ein veh mes' ish-veh ha'kiv vi seemed tor ma disclosed tor ish-veh ha'kiv’s mystery. Heh, wi, ra vesh' tra' tor nam-tor kwes t'? Au vesh' ri wuh schoolboy il wuh ko-kan. Ish-veh vesh' absurd tor nam-tor koltha. “kal-tor etek hal-tor heh hayal-tor svi' wuh duvek, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “parker has katau si' wuh mon-tor, heh kuv du stay sovek longer svi' nash glare, du dungi nam-tor ved spoiled, heh basil dungi worla kras du va'ashiv. Du really bolau ri kal-tor yourself tor shetau sunburnt. Ish-veh would nam-tor unbecoming.” “ra mokuhlek ish-veh tukh?” maf-tor dorian zhai-kur, laughing, u' au hayal-tor ne' fi' wuh ku-san na' wuh shaht t' wuh bah-ker. “ish-veh dang tukh kanok-vei tor du, mr. Zhai-kur.” “po?” “fai'ei du ma wuh danik marvellous youth, heh youth nam-tor wuh veh vel don having.” “i don’t olau ik, s'haile henry.” “rai, du don’t olau ish-veh i'. Ein gad, lu du nam-tor hinek heh wrinkled heh watosh, lu nahp has seared ish-veh fa-patam k' its zehl, heh shaukaush branded ish-veh bru-lar k' its hideous yon, du dungi olau ish-veh, du dungi olau ish-veh terribly. I', wherever du hal-tor, du sem-rik wuh panu. Dungi ish-veh kwon-hau-ov nam-tor ni?. Du ma wuh wonderfully vaksurik limuk, mr. Zhai-kur. Don’t kwal. Du ma. Heh vaksur nam-tor wuh shid t' genius—nam-tor higher, indeed, do genius, u' ish-veh bolau rai danaya. Ish-veh nam-tor t' wuh lo'uk kla-min t' wuh panu, spo' ug'yel-ha'gel, il sikar-wak, il wuh haulan svi' gu'gelik mashau t' ik haul-tukh fo etek vutau wuh aikum. Ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor deshkau. Ish-veh has its ekonik gas'rak t' sovereignty. Ish-veh tor princes t' eifa vi ma ish-veh. Du abru'teruklar-ru'lut? Ah! Lu du ma pakik ish-veh du skil-tor’t abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Sutra leralmin sometimes ik vaksur nam-tor goh superficial. Ik lau nam-tor ni, tonk'peh k'puu ish-veh nam-tor ri ni superficial u' nahp nam-tor. Tor me, vaksur nam-tor wuh wonder t' wonders. Ish-veh nam-tor goh gan sutra vi ri tor judge k' appearances. Wuh yeht mystery t' wuh panu nam-tor wuh visible, ri wuh invisible. Ha, mr. Zhai-kur, wuh gods ma vesh' rom tor du. Tonk'peh ra wuh gods mazhiv-kur-tor au sahris nem-tor maf. Du ma goh wuh zamu tevun svi' if tor ha-tor really, perfectly, heh fully. Lu ish-veh youth hal-tor, ish-veh vaksur dungi hal-tor k' ish-veh, heh yi du dungi suddenly discover ik tra' nam-tor rai triumphs losrak na' du, il ma tor content yourself k' eifa tvai triumphs ik wuh vokaya t' ish-veh vesht dungi tor weht sfith(-) do defeats. Kanok tevun-krus u' ish-veh wanes katau du nearer tor vel dreadful. Wak nam-tor kis-ka t' du, heh t'naehm tehnat ish-veh lilies heh ish-veh roses. Du dungi shetau sallow, heh hollow-cheeked, heh pasik-eyed. Du dungi dash horribly. Ah! Realize ish-veh youth du' du ma ish-veh. Don’t sis-tor wuh pi-maat-tukh t' ish-veh gad, listening tor wuh tedious, trying tor improve wuh hopeless vravshaya, il giving maf ish-veh ha'kiv tor wuh ignorant, wuh tsuri, heh wuh vulgar. Aifa nam-tor wuh sickly mokh-tor, wuh riyeht tangu, t' etwel ya'shakhuv. Ha-tor! Ha-tor wuh wonderful ha'kiv ik nam-tor svi' du! Kal-tor nothing nam-tor pakik fi-tor du. Nam-tor kwon-hau-ov searching na' uzh kashan. Nam-tor kwes t' nothing. Wuh uzh hedonism—ik nam-tor ra etwel century aitlu. Du lau nam-tor its visible sehtebuhk. K' ish-veh nafu'es tra' nam-tor nothing du kupi ri tor. Wuh panu t' du na' wuh tevun-yonuk. Wuh moment i ragel-tor du vesht gla-tor nash-veh ik du vesh' ved unconscious t' ra du really nam-tor, t' ra du really lau nam-tor. Tra' vesh' ni mau svi' du ik sem-rik-tor me ik i olau i bolau var-tor du vel pa' yourself. I nahp uf tragic ish-veh would nam-tor kuv du vesh' thinoi. Na' tra' nam-tor such wuh pi' wak ik ish-veh youth dungi kim-shah—such wuh pi' wak. Wuh tsuri kunel-svai wither, tonk'peh au blossom va'ashiv. Wuh laburnum dungi nam-tor u' kin-kur thurai belaar u' ish-veh nam-tor i'. Svi' wuh tevun-krus tra' dungi nam-tor gahv-kur yel fi' wuh clematis, heh tevun po' tevun wuh yar-kur mu-yor t' its mor dungi meskaraya its gahv-kur yel. Tonk'peh etek worla zaprah etwel youth. Wuh khaf-spol-gaya t' mak ik kuhsh-tor svi' etek na' dah-leh shetau sluggish. Etwel sikrus vravshau, etwel kash-ral nehaya. Etek degenerate vi' hideous puppets, haunted k' wuh vokaya t' wuh shaukaush t' if etek vesh' nuh' mau kwes, heh wuh exquisite temptations ik etek had ri wuh courage tor yield tor. Youth! Youth! Tra' nam-tor absolutely nothing svi' wuh panu tonk'peh youth!” dorian zhai-kur shroi, tu'ash-eyed heh wondering. Wuh spray t' lilac tevan-tor s' ish-veh el'ru fi-tor wuh krus-kov. Wuh furry bee sarlah heh buzzed pauk ish-veh na' wuh moment. Yi ish-veh began tor parish-tor ek' abru' wuh yuvik yel-shidik ek'tra-dukal t' wuh tiny blossoms. Au glantau ish-veh k' ik flekh eku'ko svi' trivial vel ik etek ar'kadan tor storau lu vel t' pid import tor etek kwes, il lu etek nam-tor stirred k' ein uzh zherka na' if etek fam yehat talal sagluvaya, il lu ein nahp ik terrifies etek ti sudden siege tor wuh shi'nahp heh calls fi' etek tor yield. Po' wuh wak wuh bee flew maf. Gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh creeping vi' wuh kurau trumpet t' wuh tyrian convolvulus. Wuh svai seemed tor quiver, heh yi swayed kogavik tor heh fro. Suddenly wuh krassu saudau na' wuh svep t' wuh studio heh tor staccato glat na' au tor sarlah svi'. Au da-tor tor tik vath heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “i am waiting, ” au maf-tor. “tor sarlah svi'. Wuh ta'hal nam-tor ved buhfik, heh du mokuhlek katau ish-veh mon-tor.” au she-tor abru heh sauntered ne' wuh lates teretuhr. Dahkuh yar-kur-heh-wan-kur mathra nuv-tor vesht au, heh svi' wuh savas-lap na' wuh teruk t' wuh bah-ker wuh thrush began tor uralau. “du nam-tor glad du ma ragel-tor me, mr. Zhai-kur, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, looking na' ish-veh. “ha, i am glad i'. I wonder dungau i kwon-hau-ov nam-tor glad?” “kwon-hau-ov! Ik nam-tor wuh dreadful zhit. Ish-veh tor me ak'shem-hutau lu i zhu-tor ish-veh. Kosu nam-tor ni tishau t' using ish-veh. Au spoil kanok romance k' trying tor tor ish-veh kim-shah na' ek'wak. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh meaningless zhit, nuh'. Wuh goh natyan svi' wuh caprice heh wuh lifelong shaukaush nam-tor ik wuh caprice palesh-tor wuh pi' longer.” u' au svi-tor wuh studio, dorian zhai-kur shitau ish-veh el'ru fi-tor s'haile henry’s kar. “svi' ik nuf, kal-tor etwel friendship nam-tor wuh caprice, ” au murmured, flushing na' ish-veh sha' boldness, yi ash-tor abru fi' wuh skaf heh resumed ish-veh pose. S'haile henry flung himself vi' wuh suk wicker kar-ku-san heh glantau ish-veh. Wuh fnashtaya heh dash t' wuh achut fi' wuh canvas tor wuh goh ralash ik shau wuh stillness, kaula lu, i' heh yi, hallward ash-tor pla' tor glazhau na' ish-veh ar'kadan kwi'. Svi' wuh slanting ha-zehl ik salash k'fai wuh tu'ash svep-sharu wuh grazhiv tam-tor heh vesh' pi-maat-kur. Wuh ras scent t' wuh roses seemed tor kesh-travek abru' kanok-vei. Po' pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan hallward pehkau krasan, glazhau na' wuh akarshif na' dorian zhai-kur, heh yi na' wuh akarshif na' wuh bikuv, biting wuh shaht t' veh t' ish-veh masuk' brushes heh frowning. “ish-veh nam-tor ved shahtau, ” au maf-tor na' kim-shah, heh stooping ne' au kitau ish-veh ahm svi' wu vermilion nuhm fi' wuh losrak-el'ru teruk t' wuh canvas. S'haile henry sarlah abru' heh linisau wuh bikuv. Ish-veh vesh' certainly wuh wonderful ar'kadan t' tanaf, heh wuh wonderful likeness u' muhl. “t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, i congratulate du danik warmly, ” au leralmin-tor. “ish-veh nam-tor wuh finest portrait t' iyik wak. Mr. Zhai-kur, sarlah abru' heh glazhau na' yourself.” wuh lad palikau, u' kuv awakened s' ein sahr-tor. “nam-tor ish-veh really shahtau?” au murmured, stepping ne' s' wuh skaf. “ved shahtau, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu. “heh du ma hayal-tor splendidly tor-gad. I am awfully obliged tor du.” “ik nam-tor entirely due tor me, ” shau svi' s'haile henry. “isn’t ish-veh, mr. Zhai-kur?” dorian tor rai kilko-srashiv, tonk'peh be' dvun-tor listlessly svi' khom t' ish-veh bikuv heh da-tor na' ish-veh. Lu gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh au drew pla', heh ish-veh nak kluhvau na' wuh moment k' sanosh. Wuh glazhau t' mak sarlah vi' ish-veh bezhun, u' kuv au had recognized himself na' wuh wuh'rak wak. Au lam-tor tra' motionless heh svi' wonder, dimly d'wonil ik hallward vesh' speaking tor ish-veh, tonk'peh ri catching wuh meaning t' ish-veh zhit. Wuh kash-ral t' ish-veh sha' vaksur sarlah fi' ish-veh spo' wuh revelation. Au had worla olau ish-veh fa'. Basil hallward’s compliments had seemed tor ish-veh tor nam-tor goh wuh sem-rik-tor exaggeration t' friendship. Au had shroi tor au, abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' au, yen-tor au. Au had ri vi-yumuk ish-veh malat. Yi had sarlah s'haile henry wotton k' ish-veh flekh panegyric fi' youth, ish-veh terrible warning t' its brevity. Ik had stirred ish-veh na' wuh wak, heh i', u' au lam-tor gazing na' wuh duv t' ish-veh sha' loveliness, wuh bosh reality t' wuh kethelvaya kahai mes' ish-veh. Ha, tra' would nam-tor wuh gad lu ish-veh limuk would nam-tor wrinkled heh wizen, ish-veh bezhun neik-ha'khlup heh colourless, wuh takov t' ish-veh khlop pushau heh sashidau. Wuh ug'yon-kur would be' dvun maf s' ish-veh bru-lar heh wuh pi-maat-tukh vazgau s' ish-veh isachya. Wuh ha'kiv ik vesh' tor tor ish-veh soul would mar ish-veh ak'shem. Au would shetau dreadful, hideous, heh uncouth. U' au nahp t' ish-veh, wuh nasik pang t' kusut kwul-tor k'fai ish-veh spo' wuh lipau heh tor tik delicate slah t' ish-veh malat quiver. Ish-veh bezhun deepened vi' gahv, heh mes' au sarlah wuh mist t' bezhun-masu. Au olau u' kuv wuh el'ru t' le-suma had vesh' laid fi-tor ish-veh khaf-spol. “don’t du spo' ish-veh?” maf-tor hallward na' kim-shah, rakusau wuh pi' k' wuh lad’s silence, ri understanding ra ish-veh tvai. “veling au tishau ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “vi wouldn’t spo' ish-veh? Ish-veh nam-tor veh t' wuh greatest vel svi' iyik tanaf. I dungi mazhiv-kur-tor du sovek-vel du spo' tor ya'akash na' ish-veh. I bolau ma ish-veh.” “ish-veh nam-tor ri t'nash-veh veltra, harry.” “t'vi veltra nam-tor ish-veh?” “dorian’s, veling, ” kilko-tor wuh krassu. “au nam-tor wuh maut kunli katravahsu.” “uf maf ish-veh nam-tor!” murmured dorian zhai-kur k' ish-veh bezhun fam dvun teslau fi-tor ish-veh sha' portrait. “uf maf ish-veh nam-tor! I dungau tor'ovau hinek, heh horrible, heh dreadful. Tonk'peh nash bikuv dungi hafau kwon-hau-ov nu'ri. Ish-veh dungi worla nam-tor older do nash particular gad t' belaar. Kuv ish-veh vesh' goh wuh vath yut! Kuv ish-veh vesh' i vi vesh' tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov nu'ri, heh wuh bikuv ik vesh' tor tor'ovau hinek! Na' ik—na' ik—i would mazhiv-kur-tor kanok-vei! Ha, tra' nam-tor nothing svi' wuh bosh panu i would ri mazhiv-kur-tor! I would mazhiv-kur-tor t'nash-veh soul na' ik!” “du would hardly palutunau such wuh arrangement, basil, ” maf-tor s'haile henry, laughing. “ish-veh would nam-tor rather lerash zehl fi' ish-veh ar'kadan.” “i dang vel maut strongly, harry, ” leralmin-tor hallward. Dorian zhai-kur da-tor heh glazhau na' ish-veh. “i dva-tor du would, basil. Du spo' ish-veh tanaf weh-rom do ish-veh t'hylara. I am rai weht tor du do wuh yar-kur krish-tukh khlop. Hardly u' mau, i dare leralmin.” wuh krassu nantau svi' tauraya. Ish-veh vesh' ni rikes dorian tor stariben spo' ik. Ra had pavesh-tor? Au seemed ved reshnek. Ish-veh limuk vesh' kluhvau heh ish-veh nak yontau. “ha, ” au fator, “i am lehkuh tor du do ish-veh ivory hermes il ish-veh haul-tukh faun. Du dungi spo' au kwon-hau-ov. Uf wu dungi du spo' me? Till i ma t'nash-veh wuh'rak wrinkle, i suppose. I fai-tor, i', ik lu veh pak-tor veh’s rom glazhau, whatever au lau nam-tor, veh pak-tor kanok-vei. Ish-veh bikuv has saven-tor me ik. S'haile henry wotton nam-tor perfectly gas'rak. Youth nam-tor wuh goh vel don having. Lu i talal ik i am growing hinek, i dungau stau myself.” hallward da-tor spoh heh kum-tor ish-veh el'ru. “dorian! Dorian!” au maf-tor, “don’t variben spo' ik. I ma worla had such wuh t'hy'la u' du, heh i dungau worla ma such wuh'ashiv. Du nam-tor ri kis-ka t' tukh vel, nam-tor du?—du vi nam-tor finer do sovek t' au!” “i am kis-ka t' kanok-vei t'vi vaksur tor ri tev-tor. I am kis-ka t' wuh portrait du ma kras-tor t' me. Po dang ish-veh potau ra i bolau pak-tor? Kanok moment ik be' dvun-tor nem-tor vel s' me heh mazhiv-kur-tor vel tor ish-veh. Oh, kuv ish-veh vesh' goh wuh vath yut! Kuv wuh bikuv kupi rubah, heh i kupi nam-tor kwon-hau-ov ra i am i'! Po did du kras ish-veh? Ish-veh dungi mock me ein gad—mock me horribly!” wuh fal bezhun-masu welled vi' ish-veh bezhun; au tore ish-veh el'ru maf heh, flinging himself fi' wuh divan, au visolektau ish-veh limuk svi' wuh an'kar, u' hi au vesh' praying. “nash nam-tor ish-veh doing, harry, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu bitterly. S'haile henry shrugged ish-veh tipan. “ish-veh nam-tor wuh yeht dorian zhai-kur—ik nam-tor ek'.” “ish-veh nam-tor ri.” “kuv ish-veh nam-tor ri, ra ma i tor tor k' ish-veh?” “du dang ma hal-tor maf lu i ya'akash du, ” au muttered. “i stayed lu du ya'akash me, ” vesh' s'haile henry’s kilko-srashiv. “harry, i mokuhlek’t quarrel k' t'nash-veh dahkuh buhfik t'hylara na' wuh'wak, tonk'peh svi' du fi' du ma tor me fnu-ven wuh finest krus t' ar'kadan i ma ek'wak ovsoh, heh i dungi vashau ish-veh. Ra nam-tor ish-veh tonk'peh canvas heh kur? I dungi ri kal-tor ish-veh sarlah mes' etwel rehkuh ha-tor heh mar au.” dorian zhai-kur abertau ish-veh pi-maat-kur patam s' wuh trak, heh k' pallid limuk heh bezhun-masu-kurau bezhun, glazhau na' ish-veh u' au lates-tor abru' tor wuh deal krasan-pasu ik vesh' eku ne'rak wuh pid curtained krani. Ra vesh' au doing tra'? Ish-veh ozh vesh' fam-kelek-tor pa' among wuh litter t' zhai-tukh tubes heh pseth brushes, seeking na' vel. Ha, ish-veh vesh' na' wuh wu palette-lipau, k' its wonil wun-mor t' lithe pishek. Au had afer-tor ish-veh na' kim-shah. Au vesh' going tor tres abru wuh canvas. K' wuh stifled sob wuh lad leaped s' wuh ku-san, heh, rushing abru' tor hallward, tore wuh lipau s' ish-veh el'ru, heh flung ish-veh tor wuh shaht t' wuh studio. “don’t, basil, don’t!” au maf-tor. “ish-veh would nam-tor riyeht-staya!” “i am glad du appreciate t'nash-veh ar'kadan na' kim-shah, dorian, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu coldly lu au had recovered s' ish-veh ak'wikmun. “i worla nahp du would.” “appreciate ish-veh? I am svi' ashaya k' ish-veh, basil. Ish-veh nam-tor krus t' myself. I olau ik.” “muhl, u' ak u' du nam-tor pseth, du dungau nam-tor varnished, heh nentulau, heh satau ha-kel. Yi du mokuhlek tor ra du spo' k' yourself.” heh au lates-tor mes' wuh tvi-shal heh rang wuh kus-vakh na' theris-masu. “du dungi ma theris-masu, t' rivak, dorian? Heh ni dungi du, harry? Il tor du vel tor such velik pleasures?” “i adore velik pleasures, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “au nam-tor wuh kim-shah rau-nol t' wuh wehkonik. Tonk'peh i don’t spo' scenes, kaula fi' wuh skaf. Ra absurd katravahsu du nam-tor, fi' t' du! I wonder vi ish-veh vesh' mesprah sasu u' wuh rational aushfa. Ish-veh vesh' wuh danik fe-wakik mesprahn ek'wak putan-tor. Sasu nam-tor wehk vel, tonk'peh au nam-tor ri rational. I am glad au nam-tor ri, po' ek'—hi i istaya du chaps would ri squabble abru' wuh bikuv. Du had mau weh-rom kal-tor me ma ish-veh, basil. Nash silly sa-kan doesn’t really aitlun ish-veh, heh i really tor.” “kuv du kal-tor sovek veh ma ish-veh tonk'peh me, basil, i dungau worla forgive du!” maf-tor dorian zhai-kur; “heh i don’t kal-tor sutra tor vutau me wuh silly sa-kan.” “du fai-tor wuh bikuv nam-tor ish-veh, dorian. I mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor du fa' ish-veh nam-tor.” “heh du fai-tor du ma vesh' wuh pi' silly, mr. Zhai-kur, heh ik du don’t really vel tor hasu reminded ik du nam-tor extremely nu'ri.” “i dang ma kluchi maut strongly nash asal, s'haile henry.” “ah! Nash asal! Du ma ha-tor opi' yi.” tra' sarlah wuh knock na' wuh svep, heh wuh butler svi-tor k' wuh laden theris-masu-tray heh eku ish-veh ne' fi-tor wuh pi' japanese pasu. Tra' vesh' wuh rattle t' cups heh ne-mathra heh wuh hissing t' wuh fluted georgian urn. Dahkuh ek'tra-dukal-kushizhau china dishes vesh' katau svi' k' wuh thalv. Dorian zhai-kur went abru' heh mukau si' wuh theris-masu. Wuh dahkuh sasu sauntered languidly tor wuh pasu heh linisau ra vesh' ne' wuh wein-tor. “kal-tor etek hal-tor tor wuh theatre tor-mu-yor, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “tra' nam-tor sure tor nam-tor vel fi', ein-wilat. I ma ugau tor aru-yokul na' wan-kur’s, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor goh k' wuh hinek t'hy'la, ni i mokuhlek satau ish-veh wuh raf-elakh tor leralmin ik i am has-bosh, il ik i am prevented s' coming svi' consequence t' wuh subsequent engagement. I nah-tor ik would nam-tor wuh rather nice tobeg: ish-veh would ma ek' wuh ak'wikmun t' candour.” “ish-veh nam-tor such wuh spitau putting fi' veh’s sai-vel-sai-vel, ” muttered hallward. “heh, lu veh has au fi', au nam-tor ni horrid.” “ha, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry dreamily, “wuh costume t' wuh nineteenth century nam-tor detestable. Ish-veh nam-tor ni sombre, ni depressing. Sin nam-tor wuh goh yeht kur-meilak losrak svi' iyik ha'kiv.” “du really bolau ri leralmin vel spo' ik fa' dorian, harry.” “fa' if dorian? Wuh veh vi nam-tor pouring si' theris-masu na' etek, il wuh veh svi' wuh bikuv?” “fa' either.” “i dang spo' tor sarlah tor wuh theatre k' du, s'haile henry, ” leralmin-tor wuh lad. “yi du dungau sarlah; heh du dungi sarlah, nuh', basil, skil-tor’t du?” “i mokuhlek’t, really. I would sooner ri. I ma wuh lot t' ar'kadan tor tor.” “muhl, yi, du heh i dungi hal-tor sa'awek, mr. Zhai-kur.” “i dang spo' ik awfully.” wuh krassu zeshau ish-veh bru heh lates-tor abru', cup svi' el'ru, tor wuh bikuv. “i dungau stay k' wuh yeht dorian, ” au leralmin-tor, sadly. “nam-tor ish-veh wuh yeht dorian?” maf-tor wuh tveshik t' wuh portrait, strolling mes' tor ish-veh. “am i really spo' ik?” “ha; du nam-tor aishan spo' ik.” “uf wonderful, basil!” “k'puu du nam-tor spo' ish-veh svi' appearance. Tonk'peh ish-veh dungi worla rubitau, ” spes-tevan hallward. “ik nam-tor vel.” “ra wuh fuss sutra tor pa' fidelity!” sporiben s'haile henry. “po, kauk svi' ashaya ish-veh nam-tor purely wuh deshker na' nam-tor-lof-tal. Ish-veh has nothing tor tor k' etwel sha' dungi. Nu'ri sasu aitlun tor nam-tor faithful, heh nam-tor ri; hinek sasu aitlun tor nam-tor faithless, heh fam yehat: ik nam-tor ek' veh mokuhlek leralmin.” “don’t hal-tor tor wuh theatre tor-mu-yor, dorian, ” leralmin-tor hallward. “pehkaya heh aru-yokul k' me.” “i mokuhlek’t, basil.” “po?” “fai'ei i ma ugau s'haile henry wotton tor hal-tor k' ish-veh.” “au skil-tor’t spo' du wuh weh-rom na' keeping ish-veh ugau. Au kwon-hau-ov breaks ish-veh sha'. I eit'jae du ri tor hal-tor.” dorian zhai-kur abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh hutau ish-veh patam. “i entreat du.” wuh lad hesitated, heh glazhau abru' na' s'haile henry, vi vesh' watching au s' wuh theris-masu-pasu k' wuh amused abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “i bolau hal-tor, basil, ” au kilko-tor. “maut muhl, ” leralmin-tor hallward, heh au went abru' heh laid ne' ish-veh cup fi' wuh tray. “ish-veh nam-tor rather tab-ma, heh, u' du ma sai-vel-tor, du had weh-rom pak-tor rai wak. Rom-bye, harry. Rom-bye, dorian. Sarlah heh gla-tor me ak. Sarlah tor-morrow.” “certainly.” “du skil-tor’t yen-tor?” “rai, veling ri, ” maf-tor dorian. “heh. Harry!” “ha, basil?” “vokau ra i ya'akash du, lu etek vesh' svi' wuh bah-ker nash asal.” “i ma yen-tor ish-veh.” “i sahrafel du.” “i istaya i kupi sahrafel myself, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, laughing. “sarlah, mr. Zhai-kur, t'nash-veh hansom nam-tor s'udish, heh i mokuhlek eku du na' ish-veh sha' shi. Rom-bye, basil. Ish-veh has vesh' wuh danik eku'ki aru.” u' wuh svep a'ing za' au, wuh krassu flung himself ne' fi' wuh ku-san, heh wuh glazhau t' kusut sarlah vi' ish-veh limuk. Chapter iii. Na' ulef-vesht leh-dah thurai gad s'haile henry wotton strolled s' curzon yut abru' tor wuh albany tor vutau fi' ish-veh sa-kuk, s'haile fermor, wuh genial kuv somewhat rough-mannered hinek bachelor, ik wuh s'udish panu puvutau selfish fai'ei ish-veh derived rai particular rufai s' ish-veh, tonk'peh vi vesh' panah-tor generous k' shila'es u' au puyem-tot wuh sutra vi amused ish-veh. Ish-veh sa-mekh had vesh' etwel kevet-dutar na' madrid lu isabella vesh' nu'ri heh prim unthought t', tonk'peh had retired s' wuh dutarik dvin svi' wuh capricious moment t' il'nai'ga fi' ri hasu nufau wuh embassy na' paris, wuh lehk tor if au panah-tor ik au vesh' fully entitled k' utvau t' ish-veh keshtan, ish-veh indolence, wuh rom eingelsu t' ish-veh dispatches, heh ish-veh inordinate shaukaush na' sanosh. Wuh sa-fu, vi had vesh' ish-veh sa-mekh’s secretary, had resigned bi' k' ish-veh chief, somewhat foolishly u' vesh' nahp na' wuh wak, heh fi' succeeding ein tevun-krus later tor wuh title, had eku himself tor wuh serious orenau t' wuh lo'uk aristocratic tanaf t' doing absolutely nothing. Au had dahkuh suk kahr kelek, tonk'peh preferred tor ha-tor svi' tvi-shal u' ish-veh vesh' lehkuh trouble, heh nem-tor danik t' ish-veh yem na' ish-veh muhd. Au vlitau ein attention tor wuh management t' ish-veh collieries svi' wuh midland counties, excusing himself na' nash taint t' industry fi' wuh solektra ik wuh veh advantage t' having kastik-kov vesh' ik ish-veh enabled wuh gentleman tor afford wuh decency t' yontau lapan fi' ish-veh sha' hearth. Svi' politics au vesh' wuh tory, kaula lu wuh tories vesh' svi' office, du' if wak-krus au roundly abused au na' hasu wuh sa'haf t' sagir. Au vesh' wuh hero tor ish-veh valet, vi bullied ish-veh, heh wuh vash tor danik t' ish-veh relations, ik au bullied svi' da-tor. Goh england kupi ma torvau ish-veh, heh au kwon-hau-ov leralmin-tor ik wuh shasol vesh' going tor wuh dogs. Ish-veh dvatai vesh' s' kinuf, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh rom deal tor nam-tor leralmin-tor na' ish-veh prejudices. Lu s'haile henry svi-tor wuh tvi-shal, au afer-tor ish-veh sa-kuk sitting svi' wuh rough shooting-tor-pal, smoking wuh cheroot heh grumbling abru' _the times_. “muhl, harry, ” leralmin-tor wuh hinek gentleman, “ra katau du si' ni lehkuh-mal? I nahp du dandies worla prah abru till dahkuh, heh vesh' ri visible till kaukuh.” “pure skan affection, i assure du, sa-kuk george. I aitlun tor prah vel s' du.” “donku, i suppose, ” leralmin-tor s'haile fermor, tor wuh wry limuk. “muhl, hayal-tor ne' heh var-tor me ek' pa' ish-veh. Nu'ri sutra, nowadays, glenonau ik donku nam-tor kanok-vei.” “ha, ” murmured s'haile henry, settling ish-veh gonaf-razh svi' ish-veh tor-pal; “heh lu au tor'ovau older au fai-tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh i don’t aitlun donku. Ish-veh nam-tor goh sutra vi vlitau ish-veh dun vi aitlun ik, sa-kuk george, heh i worla vlitau t'nash-veh. Lit nam-tor wuh capital t' wuh younger sa-fu, heh veh ha-tor charmingly fi-tor ish-veh. Isha, i kwon-hau-ov deal k' dartmoor’s tradesmen, heh consequently au worla ertau me. Ra i aitlun nam-tor ro'fori: ri useful ro'fori, veling; nam-tor-fam ro'fori.” “muhl, i mokuhlek var-tor du sovek-vel ik nam-tor svi' wuh eingelsu pla-kur dunap, harry, hi eifa katravahsu nowadays kitau wuh lot t' nonsense. Lu i vesh' svi' wuh dutarik, vel vesh' mau weh-rom. Tonk'peh i zhu-tor au kal-tor au svi' i' k' linisaya. Ra mokuhlek du gish? Linisaya, osu, nam-tor pure humbug s' palikaya tor shaht. Kuv wuh sasu nam-tor wuh gentleman, au fai-tor ved hiyet, heh kuv au nam-tor ri wuh gentleman, whatever au fai-tor nam-tor rasahkos na' ish-veh.” “mr. Dorian zhai-kur tor ri belong tor pla-kur dunap, sa-kuk george, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry languidly. “mr. Dorian zhai-kur? Vi nam-tor au?” ya'akash s'haile fermor, knitting ish-veh bushy wan-kur bezhun-zehl. “ik nam-tor ra ki'sarlah nash-veh tor oren-tor, sa-kuk george. Il rather, i fai-tor vi au nam-tor. Au nam-tor wuh kim-shah s'haile kelso’s grandson. Ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' wuh devereux, t'sai margaret devereux. I aitlun du tor var-tor me pa' ish-veh ko-mekh. Ra vesh' she spo'? Ik did she marry? Du ma fainu nearly kanok-veh svi' ish-veh wak, ni du lau ma fainu ish-veh. I am maut mau interested svi' mr. Zhai-kur na' la'. I ma goh aishan ragel-tor ish-veh.” “kelso’s grandson!” echoed wuh hinek gentleman. “kelso’s grandson!. T' rivak. I fai-tor ish-veh ko-mekh intimately. I dva-tor i vesh' na' ish-veh christening. She vesh' wuh extraordinarily vaksurik ko-kan, margaret devereux, heh tor ek' wuh sasu frantic k' sahran maf k' wuh penniless nu'ri katravahsu—wuh mere kling, osu, wuh subaltern svi' wuh ash'ya regiment, il vel t' ik ves. Certainly. I vokau wuh bosh vel u' kuv ish-veh pavesh-tor za-gad. Wuh ri donku-tor chap vesh' pustau svi' wuh pagun na' spa wuh zamu tevun-krus po' wuh kal'i'farr. Tra' vesh' wuh watosh var pa' ish-veh. Au leralmin-tor kelso prah ein rascally adventurer, ein belgian brute, tor viltah ish-veh sa-fu-svi'-tor-gav svi' tsuri—vlitau ish-veh, osu, tor tor ish-veh, vlitau ish-veh—heh ik wuh katravahsu spitted ish-veh sasu u' kuv au had vesh' wuh pigeon. Wuh vel vesh' hushed abru, tonk'peh, egad, kelso ate ish-veh chop sa'awek na' wuh muhd na' ein wak afterwards. Au katau ish-veh ko-fu pla' k' ish-veh, i vesh' var-tor, heh she worla stariben tor ish-veh va'ashiv. Oh, ha; ish-veh vesh' wuh rasahkos business. Wuh ko-kan tev-tor, nuh', tev-tor k'svi wuh tevun. Ni she losrak wuh sa-fu, did she? I had yen-tor ik. Ra wihfelau t' sa-kan nam-tor au? Kuv au nam-tor spo' ish-veh ko-mekh, au bolau nam-tor wuh rom-looking chap.” “au nam-tor maut rom-looking, ” assented s'haile henry. “i rok au dungi tevan vi' proper el'ru, ” fator wuh hinek sasu. “au dang ma wuh sunil t' donku waiting na' ish-veh kuv kelso did wuh gas'rak vel k' ish-veh. Ish-veh ko-mekh had donku, nuh'. Ek' wuh selby veltra sarlah tor ish-veh, k'fai ish-veh sa'mekh'al. Ish-veh sa'mekh'al fnu-ven kelso, nahp ish-veh wuh tvai dog. Au vesh', nuh'. Sarlah tor madrid wuh'wak lu i vesh' tra'. Egad, i vesh' kafusik t' ish-veh. Wuh ko-te'kru nam-tor-tor tor ya'akash me pa' wuh eingelsu thol vi vesh' kwon-hau-ov quarrelling k' wuh cabmen pa' ish-veh panavau. Au tor ved wuh var t' ish-veh. I didn’t dare gluvaya t'nash-veh limuk na' kelek na' wuh tevun-krus. I rok au skasau ish-veh grandson weh-rom do au did wuh jarvies.” “i don’t fai-tor, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry. “i fancy ik wuh sa-kan dungi nam-tor muhl ska'. Au nam-tor ri t' ya'shakhuv wi. Au has selby, i fai-tor. Au var-tor me ni. Heh. Ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' maut vaksurik?” “margaret devereux vesh' veh t' wuh loveliest creatures i ek'wak gla-tor, harry. Ra fi' terra vimevilau ish-veh tor kloshah u' she did, i worla kupi ken-tor. She kupi ma telik anybody she dvel-tor. Carlington vesh' mad po' ish-veh. She vesh' romantic, hi. Ek' wuh kosu t' ik skan vesh'. Wuh sasu vesh' wuh ri donku-tor lot, tonk'peh, egad! Wuh kosu vesh' wonderful. Carlington went fi' ish-veh mal-nef tor ish-veh. Var-tor me ni himself. She abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh, heh tra' wasn’t wuh ko-kan svi' london na' wuh wak vi wasn’t po' ish-veh. Heh k' wuh yut, harry, talking pa' silly kal'i'farr, ra nam-tor nash humbug ish-veh sa-mekh var-tor me pa' dartmoor wanting tor marry wuh american? Ain’t eingelsu ko-kan rom hiyet na' ish-veh?” “ish-veh nam-tor rather fashionable tor marry americans aishan i', sa-kuk george.” “i’ll pla' eingelsu kosu tehnat wuh panu, harry, ” leralmin-tor s'haile fermor, striking wuh pasu k' ish-veh ozh-dukal. “wuh betting nam-tor fi' wuh americans.” “au don’t kim-shah, i am var-tor, ” muttered ish-veh sa-kuk. “wuh wu engagement saguhsh-tor au, tonk'peh au nam-tor capital na' wuh steeplechase. Au nem-tor vel hashan. I don’t nah-tor dartmoor has wuh pavesh.” “vi nam-tor ish-veh sutra?” grumbled wuh hinek gentleman. “has she prah sovek?” s'haile henry hutau ish-veh patam. “american ko-kan nam-tor u' clever na' concealing ish-veh mekhlar, u' eingelsu kosu nam-tor na' concealing ish-veh vesht, ” au leralmin-tor, rising tor hal-tor. “au nam-tor pork-packers, i suppose?” “i rok ni, sa-kuk george, na' dartmoor’s sake. I am var-tor ik pork-sa'haf-tor nam-tor wuh danik lucrative ha'yigal svi' america, po' politics.” “nam-tor she takov?” “she kloshah u' kuv she vesh' vaksurik. Danik american kosu tor. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh tsat t' ish-veh sem-rik.” “po mokuhlek’t aifa american kosu stay svi' ish-veh sha' shasol? Au nam-tor kwon-hau-ov telling etek ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh paradise na' kosu.” “ish-veh nam-tor. Ik nam-tor wuh utvau po, spo' eve, au nam-tor ni excessively anxious tor prah s' ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “rom-bye, sa-kuk george. I dungau nam-tor tab-ma na' khi-gad-yem, kuv i pehkaya sovek longer. Itaren na' giving me wuh ro'fori i aitlu. I kwon-hau-ov spo' tor fai-tor kanok-vei pa' t'nash-veh uzh t'hylara, heh nothing pa' t'nash-veh hinek ones.” “wilat nam-tor du lunching, harry?” “na' ezyet agatha’s. I ma ya'akash myself heh mr. Zhai-kur. Au nam-tor ish-veh latest _protégé_.” “humph! Var-tor ish-veh ezyet agatha, harry, ri tor ertau me sovek weht k' ish-veh charity appeals. I am has-bosh t' au. Po, wuh rom kosu nah-tor ik i ma nothing tor tor tonk'peh tor kitau cheques na' ish-veh silly fads.” “ek' gas'rak, sa-kuk george, i’ll var-tor ish-veh, tonk'peh ish-veh skil-tor’t ma sovek daya. Philanthropic sutra pak-tor ek' kash-ral t' humanity. Ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh distinguishing noshtra.” wuh hinek gentleman growled approvingly heh rang wuh kus-vakh na' ish-veh dvinsu. S'haile henry be' dvun-tor abru wuh neik kesek-weizehl vi' burlington yut heh da-tor ish-veh ash-tor svi' wuh kharat t' berkeley keh-vla. Ni ik vesh' wuh var t' dorian zhai-kur’s parentage. Crudely u' ish-veh had vesh' var-tor tor ish-veh, ish-veh had wi stirred ish-veh k' its suggestion t' wuh flekh, siyah iyik romance. Wuh vaksurik kosu risking kanok-vei na' wuh mad shaukaush. Wuh zamu kwai wehk gad t' happiness tresahk pen k' wuh hideous, treacherous tr'y'kak. Tevun-krus t' voiceless agony, heh yi wuh kan pukeshta svi' kusut. Wuh ko-mekh snatched maf k' tevakh, wuh sa-kan losrak tor awek'es heh wuh tyranny t' wuh hinek heh loveless sasu. Ha; ish-veh vesh' wuh eku'ki za-mesu. Ish-veh posed wuh lad, tor ish-veh weht buhfik, u' ish-veh vesh'. Za' kanok exquisite vel ik nam-tor, tra' vesh' vel tragic. Panu had tor nam-tor svi' travail, ik wuh meanest svai lau salur. Heh uf sem-rik-tor au had vesh' na' aru-yem wuh mu-yor fa', u' k' startled bezhun heh bru-lar parted svi' koltha sanosh au had hayal-tor mesyutik tor ish-veh na' wuh muhd, wuh yon-kur candleshades staining tor wuh richer she-tor wuh wakening wonder t' ish-veh limuk. Talking tor ish-veh vesh' spo' mavaun fi-tor wuh exquisite violin. Au kilko-tor tor kanok esta heh thrill t' wuh kes-wun. Tra' vesh' vel terribly enthralling svi' wuh tusok t' vi-yumuk. Rai vath toran vesh' spo' ish-veh. Tor ar'tu veh’s soul vi' ein gracious shid, heh kal-tor ish-veh tarry tra' na' wuh moment; tor zhu-tor veh’s sha' intellectual zan-tor echoed pla' tor veh k' ek' wuh hau ralash-tanaf t' shaukaush heh youth; tor zhelesh veh’s temperament vi' wuh'ashiv u' hi ish-veh vesh' wuh subtle yumasu il wuh flekh perfume: tra' vesh' wuh yeht mak svi' ik—sos'eh wuh danik satisfying mak losrak tor etek svi' wuh ya'shakhuv ni limited heh vulgar u' etwel sha', wuh ya'shakhuv grossly carnal svi' its pleasures, heh grossly tsuri svi' its mokh-tor. Au vesh' wuh marvellous ves, nuh', nash lad, ik k' ni curious wuh pavesh au had ragel-tor svi' basil’s studio, il kupi nam-tor fashioned vi' wuh marvellous ves, na' sovek tav. Takov vesh' ish-veh, heh wuh wan-kur purity t' boyhood, heh vaksur such u' hinek greek marbles potau na' etek. Tra' vesh' nothing ish-veh kupi ri tor k' ish-veh. Au kupi nam-tor tor wuh titan il wuh leitri. Ra wuh pity ish-veh vesh' ik such vaksur vesh' destined tor spoh-tor!. Heh basil? S' wuh psychological sfek t' zan-tor, uf eku'ki au vesh'! Wuh uzh manner svi' tanaf, wuh sluk nuk t' looking na' ha'kiv, suggested ni strangely k' wuh goh visible la'es t' veh vi vesh' unconscious t' ish-veh ek'; wuh ralash-fam tam'a ik dwelt svi' neik-ha'khlup lap-shal, heh lates-tor unseen svi' tu'ash vunai, suddenly showing herself, dryadlike heh ri kwes, fai'ei svi' ish-veh soul vi sought na' ish-veh tra' had vesh' wakened ik wonderful vision tor if sa'awek nam-tor wonderful vel revealed; wuh mere shid heh nel-dath t' vel becoming, u' ish-veh vesh', refined, heh gaining wuh ves t' symbolical tala, u' hi au vesh' themselves nel-dath t' ein vath heh weht buhfik shid t'vi duv au tor yeht: uf flekh ish-veh ek' vesh'! Au vokau vel spo' ish-veh svi' vesht-var. Vesh' ish-veh ri plato, ik tanafsu svi' nahp, vi had wuh'rak analyzed ish-veh? Vesh' ish-veh ri buonarotti vi had skrim-tor ish-veh svi' wuh kur-tor marbles t' wuh sonnet-zehlanaya? Tonk'peh svi' etwel sha' century ish-veh vesh' flekh. Ha; au would ar'kadan tor nam-tor tor dorian zhai-kur ra, rik' fai-tor ish-veh, wuh lad vesh' tor wuh krassu vi had fashioned wuh wonderful portrait. Au would seek tor abrukhau ish-veh—had already, indeed, ulef ovsoh ni. Au would tor ik wonderful tam'a ish-veh sha'. Tra' vesh' vel sem-rik svi' nash sa-fu t' ashaya heh tevakh. Suddenly au pehkau heh glanced abru na' wuh kelek. Au afer-tor ik au had be' dvun-tor ish-veh ezyet’s ein ir, heh, smiling tor himself, da-tor pla'. Lu au svi-tor wuh somewhat sombre tvur, wuh butler var-tor ish-veh ik au had hal-tor svi' tor khi-gad-yem. Au mazhiv-kur-tor veh t' wuh footmen ish-veh taik heh terpau heh be' dvun-tor vi' wuh dining-tvi-shal. “tab-ma u' tsuri, harry, ” maf-tor ish-veh ezyet, shaking ish-veh patam na' ish-veh.
