Au fereik-tor wuh hagik tobeg, heh having taken wuh vacant ku-san nam-tor' ish-veh, glazhau pauk tor gla-tor vi vesh' tra'. Dorian ovalau tor ish-veh shyly s' wuh shaht t' wuh pasu, wuh kluhvau t' sanosh stealing vi' ish-veh nak. Mesyutik vesh' wuh duchess t' harley, wuh t'sai t' admirable rom-malat heh rom temper, mau tishau k' kanok veh vi fai-tor ish-veh, heh t' eifa ample architectural proportions ik svi' kosu vi nam-tor ri duchesses nam-tor kethelvau k' contemporary historians u' stoutness. Nam-tor' ish-veh hayal-tor, fi' ish-veh gas'rak, osu thomas burdon, wuh sagir kisau t' parliament, vi zahal-tor ish-veh leader svi' tsuri ha'kiv heh svi' awek ha'kiv zahal-tor wuh buhfik fas-tor, dining k' wuh tories heh thinking k' wuh liberals, svi' accordance k' wuh kau-bosh heh muhl-fainu tor-go. Wuh lehk fi' ish-veh losrak vesh' occupied k' mr. Erskine t' treadley, wuh hinek gentleman t' considerable sem-rik heh iyula, vi had tevan-tor, however, vi' rasahkos es'merka t' silence, having, u' au danau wuh'wak tor t'sai agatha, leralmin-tor kanok-vei ik au had tor leralmin fa' au vesh' reh-leh. Ish-veh sha' behsu vesh' mrs. Vandeleur, veh t' ish-veh ezyet’s oldest t'hylara, wuh buhfik osu svi' kosu, tonk'peh ni dreadfully dowdy ik she reminded veh t' wuh badly bound hymn-dunap. Fortunately na' ish-veh she had fi' wuh vath vla s'haile faudel, wuh danik kash-tok svitan-aged mediocrity, u' bald u' wuh ministerial star-krus svi' wuh kelek t' commons, k' ik she vesh' conversing svi' ik intensely earnest manner if nam-tor wuh veh unpardonable lafosh, u' au remarked wuh'wak himself, ik ek' really rom sutra tevan vi', heh s' if rim t' au ek'wak ved stron. “etek nam-tor talking pa' ri donku-tor dartmoor, s'haile henry, ” maf-tor wuh duchess, nodding pleasantly tor ish-veh mes' wuh pasu. “tor du nah-tor au dungi really marry nash sem-rik nu'ri person?” “i dva-tor she has tor abru ish-veh kashek tor propose tor ish-veh, duchess.” “uf dreadful!” sporiben t'sai agatha. “really, ein veh dang snertau.” “i am var-tor, fi' marom ek'te'kru, ik ish-veh sa-mekh potau wuh american pseth-goods mahr-kel, ” leralmin-tor osu thomas burdon, looking supercilious. “t'nash-veh sa-kuk has already suggested pork-sa'haf-tor, osu thomas.” “pseth-goods! Ra nam-tor american pseth-goods?” ya'akash wuh duchess, raising ish-veh suk el'ru svi' wonder heh accentuating wuh tor-zhit. “american dunap, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry, helping himself tor ein quail. Wuh duchess glazhau puzzled. “don’t kashek ish-veh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” zhal-tor t'sai agatha. “au worla tvai sovek-vel ik au leralmin-tor.” “lu america vesh' discovered, ” leralmin-tor wuh sagir kisau—heh au began tor mazhiv-kur-tor ein wearisome kla-min. Spo' ek' sutra vi ar'kadan tor saguhsh wuh subject, au saguhsh-tor ish-veh listeners. Wuh duchess spes-tevan heh tusok-tor ish-veh privilege t' svi-shaya. “i istaya tor goodness ish-veh worla had vesh' discovered na' ek'!” she sporiben. “really, etwel ko-kan ma rai pavesh nowadays. Ish-veh nam-tor danik unfair.” “sos'eh, po' ek', america worla has vesh' discovered, ” leralmin-tor mr. Erskine; “i myself would leralmin ik ish-veh had goh vesh' patal-tor.” “oh! Tonk'peh ki'gla-tor nash-veh specimens t' wuh inhabitants, ” kilko-tor wuh duchess vaguely. “i bolau confess ik danik t' au nam-tor extremely takov. Heh au sai-vel muhl, nuh'. Au prah ek' ish-veh sai-vel svi' paris. I istaya i kupi afford tor tor wuh ka.” “au leralmin ik lu rom americans tev-tor au hal-tor tor paris, ” chuckled osu thomas, vi had wuh suk wardrobe t' humour’s vishizhau-ska' sai-vel. “really! Heh wilat tor rasahkos americans hal-tor tor lu au tev-tor?” inquired wuh duchess. “au hal-tor tor america, ” murmured s'haile henry. Osu thomas kwal-tor. “i am kwes ik ish-veh sa-bath nam-tor prejudiced tehnat ik lo'uk shasol, ” au leralmin-tor tor t'sai agatha. “i ma travelled ek' abru' ish-veh svi' poiq'lid tanilau k' wuh khartausu, vi, svi' such tukh, nam-tor extremely civil. I assure du ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh education tor yaret ish-veh.” “tonk'peh bolau etek really gla-tor chicago svi' zek tor nam-tor educated?” ya'akash mr. Erskine plaintively. “i don’t olau abru tor wuh halovaya.” osu thomas pral-tor ish-veh el'ru. “mr. Erskine t' treadley has wuh panu fi' ish-veh nef. Etek practical sasu spo' tor gla-tor vel, ri tor telv-tor pa' au. Wuh americans nam-tor wuh extremely eku'ki sutra. Au nam-tor absolutely reasonable. I nah-tor ik nam-tor ish-veh distinguishing noshtra. Ha, mr. Erskine, wuh absolutely reasonable sutra. I assure du tra' nam-tor rai nonsense pa' wuh americans.” “uf dreadful!” maf-tor s'haile henry. “i mokuhlek lamok brute nekwitaya, tonk'peh brute utvau nam-tor ved unbearable. Tra' nam-tor vel unfair pa' its nam-tor-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor hitting ne' wuh kash-tor-vel.” “i ri tor ken-tor du, ” leralmin-tor osu thomas, growing rather yon-kur. “i tor, s'haile henry, ” murmured mr. Erskine, k' wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “paradoxes nam-tor ek' maut muhl svi' ish-veh yut.” rejoined wuh baronet. “vesh' ik wuh paradox?” ya'akash mr. Erskine. “i did ri nah-tor ni. Sos'eh ish-veh vesh'. Muhl, wuh yut t' paradoxes nam-tor wuh yut t' yeht'es. Tor nisan reality etek bolau gla-tor ish-veh fi' wuh wufik man-elakh. Lu wuh verities shetau acrobats, etek mokuhlek judge au.” “tal-kam me!” leralmin-tor t'sai agatha, “uf du sasu gyirm'i! I am sure i worla mokuhlek tor si' ra du nam-tor talking pa'. Oh! Harry, i am ved smertau k' du. Po tor du ar'kadan tor persuade etwel nice mr. Dorian zhai-kur tor mazhiv-kur-tor abru wuh she'rak shaht? I assure du au would nam-tor ved invaluable. Au would ashaya ish-veh mavaun.” “i aitlun ish-veh tor mavau tor me, ” maf-tor s'haile henry, smiling, heh au glazhau ne' wuh pasu heh kum-tor wuh ugelik answering glance. “tonk'peh au nam-tor ni unhappy svi' whitechapel, ” fator t'sai agatha. “i mokuhlek sympathize k' kanok-vei kaula suffering, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, shrugging ish-veh tipan. “i fam yehat sympathize k' ik. Ish-veh nam-tor nuh' watosh, nuh' horrible, nuh' distressing. Tra' nam-tor vel terribly morbid svi' wuh iyik sympathy k' kusut. Veh dang sympathize k' wuh kur, wuh vaksur, wuh mak t' ha'kiv. Wuh lehkuh leralmin-tor pa' ha'kiv’s sival, wuh weh-rom.” “fam dvun, wuh she'rak shaht nam-tor wuh maut yauluhk wat, ” remarked osu thomas k' wuh shi'vukhut hutau t' wuh patam. “ved ni, ” kilko-tor wuh nu'ri s'haile. “ish-veh nam-tor wuh wat t' slavery, heh etek ar'kadan tor kilau ish-veh k' tzlu'pd wuh kafeh.” wuh politician glazhau na' ish-veh keenly. “ra rubah tor du propose, yi?” au ya'akash. S'haile henry abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “i don’t aitlun tor rubah sovek-vel svi' england kaula wuh igen-va, ” au kilko-tor. “i am ved content k' philosophic contemplation. Tonk'peh, u' wuh nineteenth century has hal-tor bankrupt k'fai wuh abru'-expenditure t' sympathy, i would suggest ik etek dang appeal tor ek'tal tor shitau etek zehik. Wuh advantage t' wuh zherka nam-tor ik au ras-tukh etek astray, heh wuh advantage t' ek'tal nam-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor ri zherka-bosh.” “tonk'peh etek ma such shi'vukhut responsibilities, ” ventured mrs. Vandeleur timidly. “terribly shi'vukhut, ” echoed t'sai agatha. S'haile henry glazhau abru' na' mr. Erskine. “humanity nem-tor itself nuh' seriously. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh panu’s tveshik sin. Kuv wuh caveman had fainu uf tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut, vesht-var would ma vesh' natya.” “du nam-tor really maut comforting, ” warbled wuh duchess. “i ma kwon-hau-ov olau rather guilty lu vesht sarlah nash-veh tor gla-tor ish-veh tal-kam ezyet, na' i nem-tor rai eku'ko na' ek' svi' wuh she'rak shaht. Na' wuh fa-wak i dungau nam-tor kup tor glazhau ish-veh svi' wuh limuk rik' wuh blush.” “wuh blush nam-tor maut becoming, duchess, ” remarked s'haile henry. “goh lu veh nam-tor nu'ri, ” she kilko-tor. “lu wuh hinek kosu spo' myself blushes, ish-veh nam-tor wuh maut rasahkos glat. Ah! S'haile henry, i istaya du would var-tor me uf tor shetau nu'ri va'ashiv.” au nahp na' wuh moment. “mokuhlek du vokau sovek lo'uk lafosh ik du committed svi' ish-veh lehkuh-mal gad, duchess?” au ya'akash, looking na' ish-veh mes' wuh pasu. “wuh lo'uk wehk, i pthak, ” she maf-tor. “yi kugau au abru' va'ashiv, ” au leralmin-tor gravely. “tor zaprah veh’s youth, veh has goh tor ashiv-tor veh’s follies.” “wuh delightful wihka!” she sporiben. “i bolau shitau ish-veh vi' practice.” “wuh tehvar-bosh wihka!” sarlah s' osu thomas’s wufik bru-lar. T'sai agatha hutau ish-veh patam, tonk'peh kupi ri gol'nev hasu amused. Mr. Erskine shroi. “ha, ” au fator, “ik nam-tor veh t' wuh lo'uk tsat t' ha'kiv. Nowadays danik sutra tev-tor t' wuh wihfelau t' creeping tsuri kash-ral, heh discover lu ish-veh nam-tor nuh' tab-ma ik wuh goh vel veh worla regrets nam-tor veh’s lafosh.” wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut sahr-tor pauk wuh pasu. Au mavau k' wuh idea heh grew wilful; tossed ish-veh vi' wuh sov heh mesuvulau ish-veh; kal-tor ish-veh stron heh recaptured ish-veh; tor ish-veh iridescent k' fancy heh winged ish-veh k' paradox. Wuh krol t' folly, u' au went fi', soared vi' wuh ven-dol-leralmin, heh ven-dol-leralmin herself became nu'ri, heh catching wuh mad ralash-tanaf t' sanosh, sai-vel-tor, veh lau fancy, ish-veh wine-kurau pelal heh wreath t' ivy, tam-tor spo' wuh bacchante abru' wuh kunel t' ha'kiv, heh mocked wuh vohris silenus na' hasu sober. Kla-min sasahr-tor fa' ish-veh spo' koltha laptra vel. Ish-veh wan-kur ash'ya sahr-tor wuh masuk' hish-tor na' if kau-bosh omar hayal-tor, till wuh seething grape-juice she-tor pauk ish-veh sai-famik sikrus svi' pral t' gahv-kur duk, il ukrau svi' yon-kur puhsh abru' wuh suk'matuhlek’s nesh-kur, dripping, sloping vla. Ish-veh vesh' wuh wehtsuri improvisation. Au olau ik wuh bezhun t' dorian zhai-kur vesh' teslau fi' ish-veh, heh wuh hokni'es ik svi' ish-veh audience tra' vesh' veh t'vi temperament au istau tor sem-tor seemed tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wit keenness heh tor lend kur tor ish-veh glenonaya. Au vesh' maut-ugelik, fantastic, irresponsible. Au sem-rik-tor ish-veh listeners s' themselves, heh au zahal-tor ish-veh mev, laughing. Dorian zhai-kur worla nem-tor ish-veh gaze ska' ish-veh, tonk'peh hayal-tor spo' veh ne' wuh spell, abru'teruklar-ru'lut chasing tik vath abru' ish-veh bru-lar heh wonder growing shi'vukhut svi' ish-veh darkening bezhun. Na' kim-shah, liveried svi' wuh costume t' wuh ya'shakhuv, reality svi-tor wuh tvi-shal svi' wuh shid t' wuh dvinsu tor var-tor wuh duchess ik ish-veh carriage vesh' waiting. She wrung ish-veh el'ru svi' mock despair. “uf annoying!” she maf-tor. “i bolau hal-tor. I ma tor vutau na' t'nash-veh sa-telsu na' wuh muhd, tor nem-tor ish-veh tor ein absurd latva na' willis’s tvi-shal, wilat au nam-tor going tor nam-tor svi' wuh ku-san. Kuv i am tab-ma au nam-tor sure tor nam-tor furious, heh i couldn’t ma wuh scene svi' nash bonnet. Ish-veh nam-tor irak nuh' shau-yehat. Wuh harsh zhit would ruin ish-veh. Rai, i bolau hal-tor, tal-kam agatha. Rom-bye, s'haile henry, du nam-tor ved delightful heh dreadfully demoralizing. I am sure i don’t fai-tor ra tor leralmin pa' ish-veh zan-tor. Du bolau sarlah heh aru-yokul k' etek ein mu-yor. Gad? Nam-tor du dahl-tor gad?” “na' du i would lehm abru' anybody, duchess, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry k' wuh kes-wun. “ah! Ik nam-tor maut nice, heh maut riyeht t' du, ” she maf-tor; “ni kashek du sarlah”; heh she swept s' wuh tvi-shal, zahal-tor k' t'sai agatha heh wuh vath t'sai. Lu s'haile henry had hayal-tor ne' va'ashiv, mr. Erskine dvun-tor pauk, heh taking wuh ku-san beyik ish-veh, shitau ish-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh kar. “du variben dunap maf, ” au leralmin-tor; “po don’t du kitau veh?” “i am nuh' tishau t' telvan dunap tor tun tor kitau au, mr. Erskine. I dang spo' tor kitau wuh dunap certainly, wuh dunap ik would nam-tor u' lovely u' wuh persian la'y heh u' unreal. Tonk'peh tra' nam-tor rai literary tsuri svi' england na' sovek-vel kaula newspapers, primers, heh danau-dunap. T' ek' sutra svi' wuh panu wuh eingelsu ma wuh least kash-ral t' wuh vaksur t' kitau-tanaf.” “i pthak du nam-tor gas'rak, ” kilko-tor mr. Erskine. “i myself nam-tor-tor ki' literary ambitions, tonk'peh i mazhiv-kur-tor au abru wu ago. Heh i', t'nash-veh tal-kam nu'ri t'hy'la, kuv du dungi kal-tor me tor vutau du ni, sos ya'akash kuv du really tvai ek' ik du leralmin-tor tor etek na' khi-gad-yem?” “i ved yen-tor ra i leralmin-tor, ” abru'teruklar-ru'lut s'haile henry. “vesh' ish-veh ek' maut rasahkos?” “maut rasahkos indeed. Svi' kla-min i panah-tor du extremely tehvar-bosh, heh kuv sovek-vel pavesh-tor tor etwel rom duchess, etek dungau ek' glazhau fi' du u' hasu primarily responsible. Tonk'peh i dang spo' tor variben tor du pa' ha'kiv. Wuh generation vi' if i vesh' pukeshta vesh' tedious. Ein gad, lu du nam-tor zungor t' london, sarlah ne' tor treadley heh expound tor me ish-veh ven-dol-leralmin t' sanosh abru' ein admirable burgundy i am fortunate hiyet tor ma.” “i dungau nam-tor sem-rik-tor. Wuh yaret tor treadley would nam-tor wuh lo'uk privilege. Ish-veh has wuh buhfik kasu, heh wuh buhfik shi'dunap.” “du dungi ovsotik ish-veh, ” kilko-tor wuh hinek gentleman k' wuh nuhk kes-wun. “heh i' i bolau nufai rom-bye tor ish-veh marom ezyet. I am due na' wuh athenaeum. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh wadan lu etek yuk tra'.” “ek' t' du, mr. Erskine?” “keh-leh t' etek, svi' keh-leh kar-ku-san. Etek nam-tor practising na' wuh eingelsu academy t' nuhm.” s'haile henry abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh she-tor. “i am going tor wuh shi'sochya, ” au maf-tor. U' au vesh' be' dvun-tor s' wuh svep, dorian zhai-kur estuhl ish-veh fi' wuh kar. “kal-tor me sarlah k' du, ” au murmured. “tonk'peh i nahp du had ugau basil hallward tor hal-tor heh gla-tor ish-veh, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry. “i would sooner sarlah k' du; ha, i olau i bolau sarlah k' du. Tor kal-tor me. Heh du dungi ugaya tor variben tor me ek' wuh wak? Kling variben ni wonderfully u' du tor.” “ah! I ma variben ved hiyet na' tor-gad, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, smiling. “ek' i aitlun i' nam-tor tor glazhau na' ha'kiv. Du lau sarlah heh glazhau na' ish-veh k' me, kuv du tun tor.” chapter iv. Veh aru, wuh tevun-krus later, dorian zhai-kur vesh' reclining svi' wuh luxurious kar-ku-san, svi' wuh pi' shi'dunap t' s'haile henry’s kelek svi' mayfair. Ish-veh vesh', svi' its yut, wuh maut sem-rik-tor tvi-shal, k' its pid panelled wainscoting t' olive-kurau oak, its dyrk-kur-tor fanet-zhel heh abru-tol t' ashenau plasterwork, heh its brickdust olau la'y strewn k' silk, wu-fringed persian la'y. Fi' wuh tiny satinwood pasu lam-tor wuh statuette k' clodion, heh be' ish-veh ti wuh va'asau t' les cent nouvelles, bound na' margaret t' valois k' clovis eve heh powdered k' wuh gilt daisies ik ko-te'kru had dvel-tor na' ish-veh el'mish. Ein suk pla-kur china kak heh parrot-lale vesh' ranged fi' wuh mantelshelf, heh k'fai wuh pi' leaded panes t' wuh krani salash wuh apricot-kur-tor ta'hal t' wuh belaar gad svi' london. S'haile henry had ri wi sarlah svi'. Au vesh' kwon-hau-ov tab-ma fi' dvatai, ish-veh dvatai hasu ik punctuality nam-tor wuh pi'tak t' wak. Ni wuh lad vesh' looking rather sulky, u' k' listless ozh au da-tor abru' wuh thalv t' wuh elaborately illustrated yadan t' manon lescaut ik au had afer-tor svi' veh t' wuh dunap-nuf. Wuh hotorik monotonous ticking t' wuh louis quatorze wak-vel annoyed ish-veh. Wuh'wak il dah'wak au nahp t' going maf. Na' kim-shah au puzhu-tor wuh ash s'udish, heh wuh svep tu'ash. “uf tab-ma du nam-tor, harry!” au murmured. “i am kwes ish-veh nam-tor ri harry, mr. Zhai-kur, ” kilko-tor wuh shrill spes. Au glanced sahris pauk heh she-tor tor ish-veh ash'ya. “i eit'jae ish-veh pardon. I nahp—” “du nahp ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh sa-telsu. Ish-veh nam-tor goh ish-veh ko-telsu. Du bolau kal-tor me ragtau myself. I fai-tor du ved muhl k' ish-veh ha'gel-bikuv. I nah-tor t'nash-veh sa-telsu has prah leh- steh t' au.” “ri leh- steh, t'sai henry?” “muhl, leh-oh, yi. Heh vesht gla-tor nash-veh du k' ish-veh wuh vath mu-yor na' wuh opera.” she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor nervously u' she stariben, heh glantau ish-veh k' ish-veh vague yen-tor-me-ri bezhun. She vesh' wuh curious kosu, t'vi sai-vel kwon-hau-ov glazhau u' kuv au had vesh' designed svi' wuh reshan heh shitau fi' svi' wuh tempest. She vesh' usually svi' ashaya k' somebody, heh, u' ish-veh shaukaush vesh' worla fun-tor, she had potau ek' ish-veh illusions. She ar'kada tor glazhau picturesque, tonk'peh goh navau svi' hasu untidy. Ish-veh ahm vesh' victoria, heh she had wuh buhfik mania na' going tor church. “ik vesh' na' lohengrin, t'sai henry, i nah-tor?” “ha; ish-veh vesh' na' tal-kam lohengrin. I spo' wagner’s ralash-tanaf weh-rom do anybody’s. Ish-veh nam-tor ni ral ish-veh mokuhlek variben wuh bosh wak rik' vath sutra khaf-spol ra veh leralmin-tor. Ik nam-tor wuh lo'uk advantage, don’t du nah-tor ni, mr. Zhai-kur?” wuh ka nervous staccato abru'teruklar-ru'lut shau s' ish-veh wonil bru-lar, heh ish-veh ozh began tor mavau k' wuh wu tortoise-fo dun-lipau. Dorian abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh hutau ish-veh patam: “i am kwes i don’t nah-tor ni, t'sai henry. I worla variben du' ralash-tanaf—k'puu, du' rom ralash-tanaf. Kuv veh zhu-tor rasahkos ralash-tanaf, ish-veh nam-tor veh’s gu-vam tor mastevau ish-veh svi' conversation.” “ah! Ik nam-tor veh t' harry’s zan-tor, isn’t ish-veh, mr. Zhai-kur? I kwon-hau-ov zhu-tor harry’s zan-tor s' ish-veh t'hylara. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh goh yut i prah tor fai-tor t' au. Tonk'peh du bolau ri nah-tor i don’t spo' rom ralash-tanaf. I adore ish-veh, tonk'peh i am kwes t' ish-veh. Ish-veh tor me nuh' romantic. I ma veling worshipped pianists—dahkuh na' wuh wak, sometimes, harry var-tor me. I don’t fai-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor pa' au. Sos'eh ish-veh nam-tor ik au nam-tor k'shatrisu. Au ek' nam-tor, ain’t au? Kauk eifa ik nam-tor pukeshta svi' england shetau k'shatrisu po' wuh wak, don’t au? Ish-veh nam-tor ni clever t' au, heh such wuh compliment tor tanaf. Tor ish-veh ved cosmopolitan, doesn’t ish-veh? Du ma worla vesh' tor sovek t' t'nash-veh parties, ma du, mr. Zhai-kur? Du bolau sarlah. I mokuhlek’t afford orchids, tonk'peh i spare rai kodona svi' k'shatrisu. Au tor veh’s tvi-shal glazhau ni picturesque. Tonk'peh la' nam-tor harry! Harry, vesht sarlah nash-veh svi' tor glazhau na' du, tor ya'akash du vel—i yen-tor ra ish-veh vesh'—heh i afer-tor mr. Zhai-kur la'. Etek ma had such wuh vaksurik chat pa' ralash-tanaf. Etek ma ved wuh ka ideas. Rai; i nah-tor etwel ideas nam-tor ved natya. Tonk'peh au has vesh' danik vaksurik. I am ni glad i’ve gla-tor ish-veh.” “i am sem-rik-tor, t'nash-veh ashaya, ved sem-rik-tor, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, elevating ish-veh gu'gelik, crescent-kushizhau bezhun-zehl heh looking na' au fi' k' wuh amused abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “ni sorry i am tab-ma, dorian. I went tor glazhau po' wuh krus t' hinek brocade svi' wardour yut heh had tor bargain na' wadan na' ish-veh. Nowadays sutra fai-tor wuh price t' kanok-vei heh wuh tala t' nothing.” “i am kwes i bolau nam-tor going, ” sporiben t'sai henry, breaking wuh awkward silence k' ish-veh silly sudden abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “i ma ugau tor yetur k' wuh duchess. Rom-bye, mr. Zhai-kur. Rom-bye, harry. Du nam-tor dining si', i suppose? Ni am i. Sos'eh dungau gla-tor nash-veh du na' t'sai thornbury’s.” “i dare leralmin, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, shutting wuh svep za' ish-veh u', looking spo' wuh kushel t' paradise ik had vesh' si' ek' mu-yor svi' wuh sov-masu, she flitted s' wuh tvi-shal, leaving wuh faint vil t' frangipanni. Yi au lit wuh cigarette heh flung himself ne' fi' wuh ku-san. “worla marry wuh kosu k' terp-kur-tor isachya, dorian, ” au leralmin-tor po' wuh zamu puffs. “po, harry?” “fai'ei au nam-tor ni sentimental.” “tonk'peh i spo' sentimental sutra.” “worla marry na' ek', dorian. Sasu marry fai'ei au nam-tor zungor; kosu, fai'ei au nam-tor curious: fi' nam-tor disappointed.” “i don’t nah-tor i am kesik tor marry, harry. I am nuh' mau svi' ashaya. Ik nam-tor veh t' ish-veh aphorisms. I am putting ish-veh vi' practice, u' i tor kanok-vei ik du leralmin.” “vi nam-tor du svi' ashaya k'?” ya'akash s'haile henry po' wuh svizh. “k' wuh fundauik-ithop, ” leralmin-tor dorian zhai-kur, blushing. S'haile henry shrugged ish-veh tipan. “ik nam-tor wuh rather commonplace _début_.” “du would ri leralmin ni kuv gla-tor du ish-veh, harry.” “vi nam-tor she?” “ish-veh ahm nam-tor sibyl vane.” “worla puzhu-tor t' ish-veh.” “kling has. Sutra dungi ein gad, however. She nam-tor wuh genius.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, rai kosu nam-tor wuh genius. Kosu nam-tor wuh decorative guv. Au worla ma sovek-vel tor leralmin, tonk'peh au leralmin ish-veh charmingly. Kosu represent wuh triumph t' tukh abru' kashek, aishan u' sasu represent wuh triumph t' kashek abru' morals.” “harry, uf mokuhlek du?” “t'nash-veh tal-kam dorian, ish-veh nam-tor ved yeht. I am analysing kosu na' la', ni i ought tor fai-tor. Wuh subject nam-tor ri ni abstruse u' i nahp ish-veh vesh'. I talal ik, ultimately, tra' nam-tor goh dahkuh ves t' kosu, wuh eiktra heh wuh kur-tor. Wuh eiktra kosu nam-tor maut useful. Kuv du aitlun tor nazh-kap wuh reputation na' respectability, du ma goh tor nem-tor au ne' tor mu'yor-yem. Wuh vath kosu nam-tor maut sem-rik-tor. Au kugau veh lafosh, however. Au kras svi' zek tor ar'kadan heh glazhau nu'ri. Etwel ko'mekh-il kras-tor svi' zek tor ar'kadan heh variben brilliantly. _rouge_ heh _esprit_ nam-tor-tor tor hal-tor teretuhr. Ik nam-tor ek' abru' i'. U' wu u' wuh kosu mokuhlek glazhau lehkuh tevun younger do ish-veh sha' ko-fu, she nam-tor perfectly satisfied. U' na' conversation, tra' nam-tor goh kaukuh kosu svi' london don talking tor, heh dahkuh t' aifa mokuhlek’t nam-tor nafai-tor vi' tevan shila'es. However, var-tor me pa' ish-veh genius. Uf wu ma du fainu ish-veh?” “ah! Harry, ish-veh zan-tor terrify me.” “worla kashek ik. Uf wu ma du fainu ish-veh?” “pa' rehkuh wehk gad.” “heh wilat did sarlah du mes' ish-veh?” “i dungi var-tor du, harry, tonk'peh du mustn’t nam-tor unsympathetic pa' ish-veh. Po' ek', ish-veh worla would ma pavesh-tor kuv i had ri ragel-tor du. Du boshau me k' wuh kwai aitlun tor fai-tor kanok-vei pa' ha'kiv. Na' gad po' i ragel-tor du, vel seemed tor gaya svi' t'nash-veh os-khaf-mev. U' i lounged svi' wuh shi'sochya, il strolled ne' piccadilly, i nam-tor-tor tor glazhau na' kanok veh vi be' dvun-tor me heh wonder, k' wuh mad curiosity, ra wihfelau t' ha-tor au pufulag-tor. Ein t' au sem-tor me. Vath boshau me k' vash. Tra' vesh' wuh exquisite gisam svi' wuh sov. I had wuh shaukaush na' kashan. Muhl, veh khru pa' stehkuh o’wak-vel, i satalau tor hal-tor si' svi' psthan t' ein adventure. I olau ik nash zhai-kur monstrous london t' ours, k' its myriads t' sutra, its sordid sinners, heh its splendid sins, u' du wuh'wak phrased ish-veh, bolau ma vel svi' mahr-kel na' me. I fancied wuh thousand vel. Wuh mere tehvar mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh kash-ral t' delight. I vokau ra du had leralmin-tor tor me fi' ik wonderful khru lu etek wuh'rak aru-yokul teretuhr, pa' wuh psthan na' vaksur hasu wuh yeht tsat t' ha'kiv. I don’t fai-tor ra i gishu, tonk'peh i went si' heh czar-tor na'she'rak, ak losing t'nash-veh yut svi' wuh labyrinth t' grimy yut heh nesh-kur grassless keh-vla. Pa' ulef-vesht ohkuh i be' dvun-tor k' wuh absurd pi' theatre, k' lo'uk flaring pa-tukh-jets heh gaudy mavau-dun. Wuh hideous jew, svi' wuh danik taurauk waistcoat i ek'wak beheld svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, vesh' standing na' wuh entrance, smoking wuh vile cigar. Au had greasy ringlets, heh wuh masuk' lerash-khush blazed svi' wuh centre t' wuh soiled sav'el. ‘ma wuh natuhn, t'nash-veh s'haile?’ au leralmin-tor, lu gla-tor ish-veh me, heh au nem-tor ska' ish-veh taik k' wuh sov t' gorgeous servility. Tra' vesh' vel pa' ish-veh, harry, ik amused me. Au vesh' such wuh stislak. Du dungi abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' me, i fai-tor, tonk'peh i really went svi' heh vlitau wuh bosh guinea na' wuh skaf-natuhn. Tor wuh la' gad i mokuhlek’t tor si' po i did ni; heh wi kuv i hadn’t—t'nash-veh tal-kam harry, kuv i hadn’t—i dang ma din-tor wuh greatest romance t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Gla-tor nash-veh du nam-tor laughing. Ish-veh nam-tor horrid t' du!” “i am ri laughing, dorian; k'puu i am ri laughing na' du. Tonk'peh du dang ri leralmin wuh greatest romance t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Du dang leralmin wuh wuh'rak romance t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Du dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor ashau, heh du dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor svi' ashaya k' ashaya. Wuh _grande passion_ nam-tor wuh privilege t' sutra vi ma nothing tor tor. Ik nam-tor wuh veh nam-tor-tor t' wuh idle mohrn t' wuh shasol. Don’t nam-tor kwes. Tra' nam-tor exquisite vel svi' mahr-kel na' du. Nash nam-tor goh wuh palikaya.” “tor du nah-tor t'nash-veh malat ni gan?” maf-tor dorian zhai-kur angrily. “rai; i nah-tor ish-veh malat ni glu.” “uf tor du tvai?” “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, wuh sutra vi ashaya goh wuh'wak svi' ish-veh ha-tor nam-tor really wuh gan sutra. Ra au vutau ish-veh fonn'es, heh ish-veh fidelity, i vutau either wuh lethargy t' custom il ish-veh fam t' glenonaya. Faithfulness nam-tor tor wuh zherka-bosh ha'kiv ra tsurkan'es nam-tor tor wuh ha'kiv t' wuh kash-tor-vel—veling wuh confession t' vravshaya. Faithfulness! I bolau nisau ish-veh ein gad. Wuh shaukaush na' veltra nam-tor svi' ish-veh. Tra' nam-tor wehk vel ik etek would lehm maf kuv etek vesh' ri kwes ik vath lau pick au abru. Tonk'peh i don’t aitlun tor svi-shau du. Hal-tor fi' k' ish-veh var.” “muhl, i afer-tor myself hayal-tor svi' wuh horrid pi' awek natuhn, k' wuh vulgar eku-scene staring me svi' wuh limuk. I glazhau si' s' za' wuh curtain heh skothon-tor wuh kelek. Ish-veh vesh' wuh tawdry tek'ik, ek' cupids heh cornucopias, spo' wuh wuh-tav wedding-cake. Wuh tanaf-shi'gluvaun heh pit vesh' fairly bosh, tonk'peh wuh dahkuh fel-tor t' dingy stalls vesh' ved herbosh, heh tra' vesh' hardly wuh person svi' ra i suppose au puvutau wuh sai-vel-da-kuv. Kosu went pa' k' zhar-kur heh ginger-naliveh, heh tra' vesh' wuh terrible consumption t' kov-sayas going fi'.” “ish-veh bolau ma vesh' aishan spo' wuh palmy gad t' wuh british drama.” “aishan spo', i dang fancy, heh maut depressing. I began tor wonder ra fi' terra i dang tor lu i kum-tor glan t' wuh mavau-dun. Ra tor du nah-tor wuh mavau vesh', harry?” “i dang nah-tor ‘wuh idiot sa-kan’, il ‘dumb tonk'peh innocent’. Etwel sa-mekh nam-tor-tor tor spo' ik wihfelau t' krus, i dva-tor. Wuh longer i ha-tor, dorian, wuh weht keenly i olau ik whatever vesh' rom hiyet na' etwel sa-mekh nam-tor ri rom hiyet na' etek. Svi' tanaf, u' svi' politics, _les grandpères ont toujours tort_.” “nash mavau vesh' rom hiyet na' etek, harry. Ish-veh vesh' romeo heh juliet. I bolau nafai-tor ik i vesh' rather annoyed na' wuh idea t' seeing shakespeare ovsoh svi' such wuh wretched razh t' wuh shi. Fam dvun, i olau interested, svi' wuh wihfelau t' yut. Na' sovek tav, i satalau tor bek-tor na' wuh wuh'rak bae'cok. Tra' vesh' wuh dreadful orchestra, presided abru' k' wuh nu'ri hebrew vi hayal-tor na' wuh treshau piano, ik nearly drove me maf, tonk'peh na' kim-shah wuh eku-scene vesh' drawn abru heh wuh mavau began. Romeo vesh' wuh stout shakhupik gentleman, k' corked bezhun-zehl, wuh husky tragedy spes, heh wuh khlop spo' wuh naliveh-subok. Mercutio vesh' siyah u' rasahkos. Au vesh' mavau k' wuh neik-comedian, vi had puragtau gags t' ish-veh sha' heh vesh' fi' danik friendly zhil k' wuh pit. Au vesh' fi' u' grotesque u' wuh scenery, heh ik glazhau u' kuv ish-veh had sasarlah t' wuh shasol-booth. Tonk'peh juliet! Harry, glenonau wuh ko-kan, hardly leh- steh tevun t' ya'shakhuv, k' wuh pi', flowerlike limuk, wuh pi' greek patam k' plaited pakuv t' gu'gelik-khav-kur isachya, bezhun ik vesh' mu'gahv-kur vik t' shaukaush, bru-lar ik vesh' spo' wuh kur-mor t' wuh she-tor. She vesh' wuh loveliest vel i had ek'wak gla-tor svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Du leralmin-tor tor me wuh'wak ik pathos losrak du unmoved, tonk'peh ik vaksur, mere vaksur, kupi boshaya ish-veh bezhun k' bezhun-masu. I var-tor du, harry, i kupi hardly gla-tor nash ko-kan na' wuh mist t' bezhun-masu ik sarlah mes' me. Heh ish-veh spes—i worla puzhu-tor such wuh spes. Ish-veh vesh' maut neik na' wuh'rak, k' glu mellow pitoh ik seemed tor tevan singly fi-tor veh’s kaluk. Yi ish-veh became wuh pi' louder, heh sounded spo' wuh kolchak il wuh irak hautboy. Svi' wuh bah-ker-scene ish-veh had ek' wuh tremulous prahk'es ish-veh zhu-tor aishan fa' gad-keshtan lu nightingales nam-tor uralaun. Tra' vesh' moments, later fi', lu ish-veh had wuh kwai shaukaush t' violins. Du fai-tor uf wuh spes mokuhlek stir veh. Ish-veh spes heh wuh spes t' sibyl vane nam-tor dahkuh vel ik i dungau worla yen-tor. Lu i ikap-tor t'nash-veh bezhun, i zhu-tor au, heh tik t' au leralmin-tor vel natya. I don’t fai-tor if tor zahal-tor. Po dang i ri ashaya ish-veh? Harry, i tor ashaya ish-veh. She nam-tor kanok-vei tor me svi' ha'kiv. Mu-yor po' mu-yor i hal-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh mavau. Veh khru she nam-tor rosalind, heh wuh thurai khru she nam-tor imogen. I ma gla-tor ish-veh tev-tor svi' wuh gloom t' wuh italian braq, sucking wuh gisam s' ish-veh lover’s bru-lar. I ma glantau ish-veh wandering k'fai wuh laptra t' arden, pastau u' wuh takov sa-kan svi' hose heh doublet heh dainty taik. She has vesh' mad, heh has sarlah vi' wuh la'es t' wuh guilty sa-te'kru, heh putan-tor ish-veh rue sai-vel-tor heh sfith(-) bar-got tor zahvan t'. She has vesh' innocent, heh wuh nesh-kur el'ru t' jealousy ma plesh-tor ish-veh reedlike drahk. Ki'gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh svi' kanok ya'shakhuv heh svi' kanok costume. Ordinary kosu worla appeal tor veh’s glenonaya. Au nam-tor limited tor ish-veh century. Rai glamour ek'wak transfigures au. Veh fai-tor ish-veh kashkau u' easily u' veh fai-tor ish-veh bonnets. Veh mokuhlek kwon-hau-ov talal au. Tra' nam-tor rai mystery svi' sovek t' au. Au fau svi' wuh shi'sochya svi' wuh asal heh chatter na' theris-masu-parties svi' wuh aru. Au ma ish-veh stereotyped abru'teruklar-ru'lut heh ish-veh fashionable manner. Au nam-tor ved obvious. Tonk'peh wuh fundauik-ithop! Uf natya wuh fundauik-ithop nam-tor! Harry! Po didn’t du var-tor me ik wuh goh vel don loving nam-tor wuh fundauik-ithop?” “fai'ei i ma ashau ni wehk t' au, dorian.” “oh, ha, horrid sutra k' kur-tor isachya heh kras-tor limuk.” “don’t sahr-tor ne' kur-tor isachya heh kras-tor limuk. Tra' nam-tor wuh wehtsuri sem-rik svi' au, sometimes, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “i istaya i' i had ri var-tor du pa' sibyl vane.” “du kupi ri ma gol-tor telling me, dorian. Ek' k'fai ish-veh ha'kiv du dungi var-tor me kanok-vei du tor.” “ha, harry, i dva-tor ik nam-tor yeht. I fam yehat gol'nev telling du vel. Du ma wuh curious vi-yumuk abru' me. Kuv i ek'wak did wuh tr'y'kak, i would sarlah heh confess ish-veh tor du. Du would ken-tor me.” “sutra spo' du—wuh wilful sunbeams t' ha'kiv—don’t kugau tr'y'kak, dorian. Tonk'peh i am mau obliged na' wuh compliment, ek' wuh ka. Heh i' var-tor me—pulau me wuh matches, spo' wuh rom sa-kan—itaren—ra nam-tor ish-veh actual relations k' sibyl vane?” dorian zhai-kur leaped tor ish-veh ash'ya, k' kluhvau nak heh yontau bezhun. “harry! Sibyl vane nam-tor sacred!” “ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh sacred vel ik nam-tor don touching, dorian, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, k' wuh flekh esta t' pathos svi' ish-veh spes. “tonk'peh po dang du nam-tor annoyed? I suppose she dungi belong tor du ein gad. Lu veh nam-tor svi' ashaya, veh kwon-hau-ov palikau k' deceiving veh’s shal, heh veh kwon-hau-ov shahtau k' deceiving vath. Ik nam-tor ra wuh panu calls wuh romance. Du fai-tor ish-veh, na' sovek tav, i suppose?” “veling i fai-tor ish-veh. Fi' wuh wuh'rak mu-yor i vesh' na' wuh theatre, wuh horrid hinek jew sarlah pauk tor wuh natuhn po' wuh performance vesh' abru' heh nufau tor nem-tor me za' wuh scenes heh ragtau me tor ish-veh. I vesh' furious k' ish-veh, heh var-tor ish-veh ik juliet had vesh' tevik na' hundreds t' tevun heh ik ish-veh ak'shem vesh' lying svi' wuh marble braq svi' verona. I nah-tor, s' ish-veh blank glazhau t' tauraya, ik au vesh' ne' wuh impression ik i had taken nuh' mau champagne, il vel.” “i am ri ak'wikmun.” “yi au ya'akash me kuv i kitau na' sovek t' wuh newspapers. I var-tor ish-veh i worla kauk telv-tor au. Au seemed terribly disappointed na' ik, heh confided tor me ik ek' wuh dramatic critics vesh' svi' wuh conspiracy tehnat ish-veh, heh ik au vesh' kanok veh t' au tor nam-tor bought.” “i dang ri wonder kuv au vesh' ved gas'rak tra'. Tonk'peh, fi' wuh vath el'ru, judging s' ish-veh appearance, danik t' au fam yehat nam-tor na' ek' kodonuhk.” “muhl, au seemed tor nah-tor au vesh' mesakh ish-veh tvai, ” abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor dorian. “k' nash wak, however, wuh ha'ge vesh' hasu shitau si' svi' wuh theatre, heh i had tor hal-tor. Au aitlu me tor ar'kadan ein cigars ik au strongly recommended. I declined. Wuh thurai mu-yor, veling, i lasha na' wuh shi va'ashiv. Lu gla-tor ish-veh me, au tor me wuh neik kes-wun heh assured me ik i vesh' wuh munificent patron t' tanaf. Au vesh' wuh danik offensive brute, hi au had wuh wehtsuri shaukaush na' shakespeare. Au var-tor me wuh'wak, k' wuh sov t' pride, ik ish-veh kaukuh bankruptcies vesh' entirely due tor ‘wuh bard, ’ u' au insisted fi' calling ish-veh. Au seemed tor nah-tor ish-veh wuh distinction.” “ish-veh vesh' wuh distinction, t'nash-veh tal-kam dorian—wuh lo'uk distinction. Danik sutra shetau bankrupt k'fai having invested nuh' heavily svi' wuh prose t' ha'kiv. Ki' ruined veh’s shal abru' poetry nam-tor wuh dor. Tonk'peh lu did du wuh'rak stariben tor din-tor sibyl vane?” “wuh wuh mu-yor. She had vesh' mavaun rosalind. I kupi ri gol'nev going pauk. I had lehm-tor ish-veh ein svai, heh she had glazhau na' me—k'puu i fancied ik she had. Wuh hinek jew vesh' persistent. Au seemed satalau tor nem-tor me za', ni i consented. Ish-veh vesh' curious t'nash-veh ri wanting tor fai-tor ish-veh, wasn’t ish-veh?” “rai; i don’t nah-tor ni.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam harry, po?” “i dungi var-tor du ein vath wak. I' i aitlun tor fai-tor pa' wuh ko-kan.” “sibyl? Oh, she vesh' ni fusik heh ni gentle. Tra' nam-tor vel t' wuh kan pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh bezhun tu'ash eik svi' exquisite wonder lu i var-tor ish-veh ra i nahp t' ish-veh performance, heh she seemed ved unconscious t' ish-veh tepul. I nah-tor etek vesh' fi' rather nervous. Wuh hinek jew lam-tor grinning na' wuh svep-sharu t' wuh grazhiv greenroom, tor elaborate starun pa' etek fi', du' etek lam-tor looking na' tik vath spo' kanu. Au would insist fi' calling me ‘t'nash-veh s'haile, ’ ni i had tor assure sibyl ik i vesh' ri sovek-vel t' wuh ves. She leralmin-tor ved veling tor me, ‘du glazhau weht spo' wuh prince. I bolau vutau du prince sem-rik-tor.’” “fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit, dorian, din-tor sibyl fai-tor uf tor vlitau compliments.” “du don’t ken-tor ish-veh, harry. She fudau me goh u' wuh person svi' wuh mavau. She fai-tor nothing t' ha'kiv. She ha-tor k' ish-veh ko-mekh, wuh spoh-tor zungor kosu vi mavau t'sai capulet svi' wuh wihfelau t' mol-kur sai-vel-tor-wrapper fi' wuh wuh'rak mu-yor, heh glazhau u' kuv she had gla-tor weh-rom gad.” “i fai-tor ik glazhau. Ish-veh depresses me, ” murmured s'haile henry, examining ish-veh mokov. “wuh jew aitlu tor var-tor me ish-veh vesht-var, tonk'peh i leralmin-tor ish-veh did ri eku'ko me.” “du vesh' ved gas'rak. Tra' nam-tor kwon-hau-ov vel infinitely tvai pa' vath sutra’s tragedies.” “sibyl nam-tor wuh goh vel i tun pa'. Ra nam-tor ish-veh tor me wilat sarlah ish-veh s'? S' ish-veh pi' patam tor ish-veh pi' ash'ya, she nam-tor absolutely heh entirely ekonik. Kanok mu-yor t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv i hal-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh bae'cok, heh kanok mu-yor she nam-tor weht marvellous.” “ik nam-tor wuh utvau, i suppose, ik du worla aru-yokul k' me i'. I nahp du bolau ma ein curious romance fi' el'ru. Du ma; tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ri ved ra i gishu.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam harry, etek either khi-gad-yem il sup teretuhr kanok gad, heh i ma vesh' tor wuh opera k' du several wak, ” leralmin-tor dorian, sharu ish-veh pla-kur bezhun svi' wonder. “du kwon-hau-ov sarlah dreadfully tab-ma.” “muhl, i mokuhlek’t gol'nev going tor gla-tor sibyl mavau, ” au maf-tor, “kauk kuv ish-veh nam-tor goh na' wuh single bae'cok. I prah k'avon na' ish-veh la'es; heh lu i nah-tor t' wuh wonderful soul ik nam-tor ipik maf svi' ik pi' ivory ak'shem, i am boshau k' teshan.” “du mokuhlek aru-yokul k' me tor-mu-yor, dorian, mokuhlek’t du?” au hutau ish-veh patam. “tor-mu-yor she nam-tor imogen, ” au kilko-tor, “heh tor-morrow mu-yor she dungi nam-tor juliet.” “lu nam-tor she sibyl vane?” “worla.” “i congratulate du.” “uf horrid du nam-tor! She nam-tor ek' wuh lo'uk heroines t' wuh panu svi' veh. She nam-tor weht do wuh wuhsu. Du abru'teruklar-ru'lut, tonk'peh i var-tor du she has genius. I ashaya ish-veh, heh i bolau tor ish-veh ashaya me. Du, vi fai-tor ek' wuh tsat t' ha'kiv, var-tor me uf tor sem-rik sibyl vane tor ashaya me! I aitlun tor tor romeo kis-ka. I aitlun wuh tevik lovers t' wuh panu tor zhu-tor etwel laughter heh tor'ovau maf. I aitlun wuh esh t' etwel shaukaush tor stir ish-veh grazhiv vi' hokni'es, tor wake ish-veh vitush vi' kusut. T'nash-veh oekon, harry, uf i worship ish-veh!” au vesh' walking abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal u' au stariben. Hectic gla-tor t' yon-kur yontau fi' ish-veh nak. Au vesh' terribly teporilau. S'haile henry glantau ish-veh k' wuh subtle kash-ral t' sanosh. Uf natya au vesh' i' s' wuh fusik koltha sa-kan au had ragel-tor svi' basil hallward’s studio! Ish-veh malat had storik spo' wuh svai, had borne blossoms t' ug'yon-kur yai. S' its tsat hiding-shi had crept ish-veh soul, heh aitlun had sarlah tor ragel-tor ish-veh fi' wuh yut. “heh ra tor du propose tor tor?” leralmin-tor s'haile henry na' kim-shah. “i aitlun du heh basil tor sarlah k' me ein mu-yor heh gla-tor ish-veh bae'cok. I ma ri wuh slightest pthak t' wuh result. Du nam-tor ac'ruth tor nafai-tor ish-veh genius. Yi etek bolau prah ish-veh s' wuh jew’s el'ru. She nam-tor bound tor ish-veh na' rehkuh tevun—k'puu na' dahkuh tevun heh ohkuh tevun-krus—s' wuh la' wak. I dungau ma tor vlitau ish-veh vel, t' rivak. Lu ek' ik nam-tor settled, i dungau nem-tor wuh tev'rak shaht theatre heh katau ish-veh si' properly. She dungi tor wuh panu u' mad u' she has tor me.” “ik would nam-tor impossible, t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan.” “ha, she dungi. She has ri goh tanaf, plathau tanaf-instinct, svi' ish-veh, tonk'peh she has nafu'es isha; heh du ma k'ashiv var-tor me ik ish-veh nam-tor nafu'es, ri dvatai, ik dvun wuh ya'shakhuv.” “muhl, ra mu-yor dungau etek hal-tor?” “kal-tor me gla-tor. Tor-gad nam-tor gad. Kal-tor etek teslau tor-morrow. She mavau juliet tor-morrow.” “ek' gas'rak. Wuh bristol na' ohkuh o’wak-vel; heh i dungi prah basil.” “ri ohkuh, harry, sanoi. Ulef-vesht shehkuh. Etek bolau nam-tor tra' fa' wuh curtain she-tor. Du bolau gla-tor ish-veh svi' wuh wuh'rak bae'cok, wilat she ragel-tor romeo.” “ulef-vesht shehkuh! Ra wuh wadan! Ish-veh dungi nam-tor spo' having wuh kahm-theris-masu, il telvan wuh eingelsu dunap. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor stehkuh. Rai gentleman aru-yokul fa' stehkuh. Dungau gla-tor du basil svi' nash heh yi? Il dungau i kitau tor ish-veh?” “tal-kam basil! I ma ri laid bezhun fi' ish-veh na' wuh wehk gad. Ish-veh nam-tor rather horrid t' me, u' au has satau me t'nash-veh portrait svi' wuh danik wonderful nentu, specially designed k' himself, heh, hi i am wuh pi' kis-ka t' wuh bikuv na' hasu wuh bosh tevun-krus younger do i am, i bolau nafai-tor ik i delight svi' ish-veh. Sos'eh du had weh-rom kitau tor ish-veh. I don’t aitlun tor gla-tor ish-veh sa'awek. Au leralmin-tor vel ik tom'izhm me. Au mazhiv-kur-tor me rom na'shikh.” s'haile henry abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “sutra nam-tor maut tishau t' giving maf ra au bolaya danik themselves. Ish-veh nam-tor ra i vutau wuh gluder t' generosity.” “oh, basil nam-tor wuh buhfik t' katravahsu, tonk'peh au seems tor me tor nam-tor aishan wuh zeshau t' wuh philistine. Opi' i ma fainu du, harry, i ma discovered ik.” “basil, t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, shitau kanok-vei ik nam-tor sem-rik-tor svi' ish-veh vi' ish-veh ar'kadan. Wuh consequence nam-tor ik au has nothing losrak na' ha'kiv tonk'peh ish-veh prejudices, ish-veh dvatai, heh ish-veh tsuri kash-ral. Wuh goh tanafsu i ma ek'wak fainu vi nam-tor personally delightful nam-tor rasahkos tanafsu. Rom tanafsu nam-tor veling svi' ra au tor, heh consequently nam-tor perfectly uninteresting svi' ra au nam-tor. Wuh lo'uk poet, wuh really lo'uk poet, nam-tor wuh danik unpoetical t' ek' creatures. Tonk'peh inferior poets nam-tor absolutely sem-rik. Wuh weh-rasahkos ish-veh rhymes nam-tor, wuh weht picturesque au glazhau. Wuh mere kla-min t' having published wuh dunap t' dahr-tav sonnets tor wuh sasu ved irresistible. Au ha-tor wuh poetry ik au fam yehat kitau. Wuh vath kitau wuh poetry ik au dare ri realize.” “i wonder nam-tor ik really ni, harry?” leralmin-tor dorian zhai-kur, putting ein perfume fi' ish-veh handkerchief s' wuh suk, pi-maat-tukh-topped mashek ik lam-tor fi' wuh pasu. “ish-veh bolau nam-tor, kuv du leralmin ish-veh. Heh i' i am ska'. Imogen nam-tor waiting na' me. Don’t yen-tor pa' tor-morrow. Rom-bye.” u' au losrak wuh tvi-shal, s'haile henry’s ras bezhun-wein tevan-tor, heh au began tor nah-tor. Certainly zamu sutra had ek'wak interested ish-veh ni mau u' dorian zhai-kur, heh wi wuh lad’s mad adoration t' ein veh else aisha ish-veh ri wuh slightest pang t' il'nai'ga il jealousy. Au vesh' sanoi k' ish-veh. Ish-veh tor ish-veh wuh weht eku'ki orenau. Au had vesh' kwon-hau-ov enthralled k' wuh methods t' malatik ek'tal, tonk'peh wuh ordinary subject-tukh t' ik ek'tal had seemed tor ish-veh trivial heh t' rai import. Heh ni au had palikau k' vivisecting himself, u' au had shahtau k' vivisecting vath. Komihn ha'kiv—ik saudau tor ish-veh wuh veh vel don meh-hilan. Tcok'at tor ish-veh tra' vesh' nothing else t' sovek tala. Ish-veh vesh' yeht ik u' veh glantau ha'kiv svi' its curious klim-yerak t' kusut heh sanosh, veh kupi ri sai-vel-tor abru' veh’s limuk wuh limein t' makh, il potau wuh sulphurous panaz s' troubling wuh shi'nahp heh tor wuh glenonaya turbid k' monstrous fancies heh misshapen sahr-tor-tor. Tra' vesh' gisam ni subtle ik tor fai-tor ish-veh veltra veh had tor sicken t' au. Tra' vesh' maladies ni flekh ish-veh had tor be' dvun k'fai au kuv veh sought tor ken-tor ish-veh malat. Heh, wi, ra wuh lo'uk reward veh poprah! Uf wonderful wuh bosh panu became tor veh! Tor pitoh wuh curious lerash ozhika t' shaukaush, heh wuh zherka-bosh kur-tor ha'kiv t' wuh kash-tor-vel—tor glantau wilat au ragel-tor, heh wilat au dahshau, na' ra sfek au vesh' svi' unison, heh na' ra sfek au vesh' na' discord—tra' vesh' wuh delight svi' ik! Ra tukh ra wuh kodona vesh'? Veh kupi worla vlitau nuh' pid wuh price na' sovek kashan. Au vesh' d'wonil—heh wuh nahp katau wuh gleam t' sanosh vi' ish-veh khav-kur grut bezhun—ik ish-veh vesh' k'fai ac'ruth zhit t' ish-veh, musical zhit leralmin-tor k' musical utterance, ik dorian zhai-kur’s soul had da-tor tor nash wan-kur ko-kan heh ovalau svi' worship fa' ish-veh. Tor wuh suk sadvun wuh lad vesh' ish-veh sha' fereikan. Au had tor ish-veh fe-wakik. Ik vesh' vel. Ordinary sutra bek-tor till ha'kiv disclosed tor au its tsat, tonk'peh tor wuh zamu, tor wuh todvel-tor, wuh mysteries t' ha'kiv vesh' revealed fa' wuh veil vesh' drawn maf. Sometimes nash vesh' wuh daya t' tanaf, heh chiefly t' wuh tanaf t' kitau-tanaf, if dealt iyi k' wuh shaukaush heh wuh kash-tor-vel. Tonk'peh i' heh yi wuh wehkonik nafu'es nem-tor wuh shi heh assumed wuh office t' tanaf, vesh' indeed, svi' its yut, wuh yeht ar'kadan t' tanaf, ha'kiv having its elaborate masterpieces, aishan u' poetry has, il shid-tanaf, il krasan. Ha, wuh lad vesh' fe-wakik. Au vesh' hohnaya ish-veh harvest du' ish-veh vesh' wi sikar. Wuh khaf-spol-gaya heh shaukaush t' youth vesh' svi' ish-veh, tonk'peh au vesh' becoming shal-d'wonil. Ish-veh vesh' delightful tor glantau ish-veh. K' ish-veh vaksurik limuk, heh ish-veh vaksurik soul, au vesh' wuh vel tor wonder na'. Ish-veh vesh' rai tukh uf ish-veh ek' shahtau, il vesh' destined tor shaht. Au vesh' spo' veh t' eifa gracious khlop svi' wuh pageant il wuh mavau, t'vi mak seem tor nam-tor remote s' veh, tonk'peh t'vi sorrows stir veh’s kash-ral t' vaksur, heh t'vi skek nam-tor spo' yon-kur roses. Soul heh ak'shem, ak'shem heh soul—uf mysterious au vesh'! Tra' vesh' animalism svi' wuh soul, heh wuh ak'shem had its moments t' kator-dva. Wuh kash-ral kupi refine, heh wuh kash-tor-vel kupi degrade. Vi kupi leralmin wilat wuh fleshly impulse ceased, il wuh psychical impulse began? Uf gan vesh' wuh arbitrary mesprahn t' ordinary kloshai-talsu! Heh wi uf rihagik tor klopau svi' wuh claims t' wuh vuhnauk shi'oren! Vesh' wuh soul wuh duv hayal-tor svi' wuh kelek t' sin? Il vesh' wuh ak'shem really svi' wuh soul, u' giordano bruno nahp? Wuh dahshaya t' tam'a s' tukh vesh' wuh mystery, heh wuh union t' tam'a k' tukh vesh' wuh mystery isha. Au began tor wonder whether etek kupi ek'wak tor kloshai-tal ni ek'esik wuh ek'tal ik tik pi' sikar t' ha'kiv would nam-tor revealed tor etek. U' ish-veh vesh', etek kwon-hau-ov misunderstood ourselves heh rarely ken-tor vath. Veshtaya vesh' t' rai tomayehtik tala. Ish-veh vesh' goh wuh ahm sasu mazhiv-kur-tor tor ish-veh lafosh. Moralists had, u' wuh tor-go, fudau ish-veh u' wuh nuk t' warning, had claimed na' ish-veh wuh ac'ruth tomayehtik efficacy svi' wuh shidoraya t' character, had krol-tor ish-veh u' vel ik saven-tor etek ra tor zahal-tor heh gluvau etek ra tor nan'woi. Tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai dvubolek tepul svi' veshtaya. Ish-veh vesh' u' pi' t' wuh torupik aishan u' conscience itself. Ek' ik ish-veh really demonstrated vesh' ik etwel fa-wak would nam-tor wuh ka u' etwel vesht, heh ik wuh sin etek had ovsoh wuh'wak, heh k' loathing, etek would tor wehk wak, heh k' mak. Ish-veh vesh' pa'shik tor ish-veh ik wuh experimental method vesh' wuh goh method k' if veh kupi lasha na' sovek talik nisaya t' wuh shaukaush; heh certainly dorian zhai-kur vesh' wuh subject tor tor ish-veh el'ru, heh seemed tor ugaya don-ka heh fruitful results. Ish-veh sudden mad ashaya na' sibyl vane vesh' wuh psychological stivan t' rai pi' eku'ko. Tra' vesh' rai vet ik curiosity had mau tor tor k' ish-veh, curiosity heh wuh aitlun na' uzh veshtau, wi ish-veh vesh' ri wuh velik, tonk'peh rather wuh maut wehkonik shaukaush. Ra tra' vesh' svi' ish-veh t' wuh purely sensuous instinct t' boyhood had vesh' mesuvulau k' wuh workings t' wuh glenonaya, rubai vi' vel ik seemed tor wuh lad himself tor nam-tor remote s' kash-ral, heh vesh' na' ik maut utvau ek' wuh weht tehvar-bosh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh shaukaush pa' t'vi tveshu etek tehs-tor ourselves ik tyrannized danik strongly abru' etek. Etwel weakest dvubolek vesh' eifa t' t'vi malat etek vesh' d'wonil. Ish-veh k'ashiv pavesh-tor ik lu etek nahp etek vesh' experimenting fi' vath etek vesh' really experimenting fi' ourselves. Du' s'haile henry hayal-tor dreaming fi' aifa vel, wuh knock sarlah tor wuh svep, heh ish-veh valet svi-tor heh reminded ish-veh ish-veh vesh' wak sai-vel-tor na' aru-yem. Au prah abru heh glazhau si' vi' wuh yut. Wuh tev-tor had smitten vi' ug'yon-kur pi-maat-tukh wuh upper krani t' wuh kelek mesyutik. Wuh panes min-tor spo' math t' falek-tor mokev. Wuh igen abru' vesh' spo' wuh spoh-tor she-tor. Au nahp t' ish-veh t'hy'la’s nu'ri yonalik-kur-tor ha'kiv heh wondered uf ish-veh vesh' ek' going tor shaht. Lu au lasha ha-kel, pa' ulef-vesht leh-dah o’wak-vel, gla-tor ish-veh wuh telegram lying fi' wuh tvur pasu. Au tu'ash ish-veh heh afer-tor ish-veh vesh' s' dorian zhai-kur. Ish-veh vesh' tor var-tor ish-veh ik au vesh' engaged tor nam-tor telik tor sibyl vane. Chapter v. “ko-mekh, ko-mekh, i am ni kunli!” zhal-tor wuh ko-kan, burying ish-veh limuk svi' wuh lap t' wuh spoh-tor, zungor-looking kosu vi, k' pla' da-tor tor wuh shrill intrusive ta'hal, vesh' sitting svi' wuh veh kar-ku-san ik ish-veh dingy sitting-tvi-shal tuhlau. “i am ni kunli!” she ashiv-tor, “heh du bolau nam-tor kunli, nuh'!” mrs. Vane winced heh shitau ish-veh wonil, grok-tukh-whitened el'ru fi' ish-veh ko-fu’s patam. “kunli!” she echoed, “i am goh kunli, sibyl, lu i gla-tor du bae'cok. Du bolau ri nah-tor t' sovek-vel tonk'peh ish-veh peran. Mr. Isaacs has vesh' maut rom tor etek, heh etek owe ish-veh donku.” wuh ko-kan glazhau abru heh pouted. “donku, ko-mekh?” she maf-tor, “ra tor donku tukh? Ashaya nam-tor weht do donku.” “mr. Isaacs has storilau etek kau-leh plesh-tor tor vlitau ska' etwel sa'akh heh tor prah wuh proper outfit na' james. Du bolau ri yen-tor ik, sibyl. Kau-leh plesh-tor nam-tor wuh maut suk hau-ov. Mr. Isaacs has vesh' danik considerate.” “au nam-tor ri wuh gentleman, ko-mekh, heh i fnu-ven wuh yut au variben tor me, ” leralmin-tor wuh ko-kan, rising tor ish-veh ash'ya heh going abru' tor wuh krani. “i don’t fai-tor uf etek kupi khartau rik' ish-veh, ” kilko-tor wuh tela'at kosu querulously. Sibyl vane tossed ish-veh patam heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “etek don’t aitlun ish-veh sovek weht, ko-mekh. Prince sem-rik-tor tor-go ha'kiv na' etek i'.” yi she svizh-tor. Wuh she-tor hutau svi' ish-veh khaf heh duv-tor ish-veh nak. Sahris esh parted wuh kur-mor t' ish-veh bru-lar. Au trembled. Ein southern salan t' shaukaush swept abru' ish-veh heh stirred wuh dainty hesha t' ish-veh sai-vel. “i ashaya ish-veh, ” she leralmin-tor veling. “duhik kan! Duhik kan!” vesh' wuh parrot-zhit-bal flung svi' kilko-srashiv. Wuh pral-tor t' pi'tak-tor, riyeht-jewelled ozh mazhiv-kur-tor grotesqueness tor wuh zhit. Wuh ko-kan abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor va'ashiv. Wuh mak t' wuh kraiskau kushel vesh' svi' ish-veh spes. Ish-veh bezhun kum-tor wuh melody heh echoed ish-veh svi' radiance, yi a'ing na' wuh moment, u' hi tor ip-sut ish-veh tsat. Lu au tu'ash, wuh mist t' wuh sahr-tor had be' dvun-tor mes' au. Wonil-lipped kau stariben na' ish-veh s' wuh worn ku-san, hinted na' prudence, quoted s' ik dunap t' cowardice t'vi kitausu apes wuh ahm t' tsuri kash-ral. She did ri shroi. She vesh' elik svi' ish-veh prison t' shaukaush. Ish-veh prince, prince sem-rik-tor, vesh' k' ish-veh. She had puvutau fi' vokaya tor remake ish-veh. She had satau ish-veh soul tor psthan na' ish-veh, heh ish-veh had katau ish-veh pla'. Ish-veh shok yontau va'ashiv fi-tor ish-veh ru'lut. Ish-veh bezhun-wein vesh' lamekh k' ish-veh esh. Yi kau rubitau its method heh stariben t' espial heh discovery. Nash nu'ri sasu lau nam-tor don-ka. Kuv ni, kal'i'farr dang nam-tor nahp t'. Tehnat wuh fo t' ish-veh kaluk shau wuh pral t' worldly cunning. Wuh kliton t' hali pohshaya k' ish-veh. Gla-tor ish-veh wuh wonil bru-lar dvun-tor, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Suddenly she olau wuh bolaya tor stariben. Wuh wordy silence troubled ish-veh. “ko-mekh, ko-mekh, ” she maf-tor, “po tor au ashaya me ni mau? I fai-tor po i ashaya ish-veh. I ashaya ish-veh fai'ei au nam-tor spo' ra ashaya himself dang nam-tor. Tonk'peh ra tor au gla-tor svi' me? I am ri worthy t' ish-veh. Heh wi—po, i fam yehat var-tor—hi i olau ni mau ne'rak ish-veh, i don’t olau humble. I olau yaut, terribly yaut. Ko-mekh, did du ashaya t'nash-veh sa-mekh u' i ashaya prince sem-rik-tor?” wuh tela'at kosu grew spoh ne'rak wuh dirik grazhiv ik daubed ish-veh nak, heh ish-veh pseth bru-lar twitched k' wuh runev t' kusut. Sybil rushed tor ish-veh, flung ish-veh kar pauk ish-veh talu, heh shok-tor ish-veh. “forgive me, ko-mekh. I fai-tor ish-veh kusut-tor du tor variben pa' etwel sa-mekh. Tonk'peh ish-veh goh kusut-tor du fai'ei du ashau ish-veh ni mau. Don’t glazhau ni maf. I am u' kunli tor-gad u' du vesh' dah-leh tevun ago. Ah! Kal-tor me nam-tor kunli na' ek'wak!” “t'nash-veh kan, du nam-tor irak nuh' nu'ri tor nah-tor t' tevan-tor svi' ashaya. Isha, ra tor du fai-tor t' nash nu'ri sasu? Du don’t kauk fai-tor ish-veh ahm. Wuh bosh vel nam-tor danik inconvenient, heh really, lu james nam-tor going maf tor australia, heh i ma ni mau tor nah-tor t', i bolau leralmin ik du dang ma shown weht consideration. However, u' i leralmin-tor fa', kuv au nam-tor don-ka.” “ah! Ko-mekh, ko-mekh, kal-tor me nam-tor kunli!” mrs. Vane glanced na' ish-veh, heh k' veh t' eifa riyeht theatrical gestures ik ni k'ashiv shetau wuh nuk t' dahr malat tor wuh skaf-hahf, clasped ish-veh svi' ish-veh kar. I', wuh svep tu'ash heh wuh nu'ri lad k' rough khav-kur isachya sarlah vi' wuh tvi-shal. Au vesh' bali-eku t' khlop, heh ish-veh el'ru heh ash'ya vesh' suk heh somewhat om'toi svi' dvun. Au vesh' ri ni finely bred u' ish-veh ko-kai. Veh would hardly ma guessed wuh ikap-tor relationship ik nam-tor svi' au. Mrs. Vane teslau ish-veh bezhun fi' ish-veh heh intensified ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. She mentally ashenau ish-veh sa-fu tor wuh dignity t' wuh audience. She olau sure ik wuh _tableau_ vesh' eku'ki. “du lau potau ein t' ish-veh shok-tor na' me, sibyl, i nah-tor, ” leralmin-tor wuh lad k' wuh rom-natured grumble. “ah! Tonk'peh du don’t spo' hasu shok-tor, jim, ” she maf-tor. “du nam-tor wuh dreadful hinek lesh.” heh she sahr-tor mes' wuh tvi-shal heh teraya-martaya ish-veh. James vane glazhau vi' ish-veh ko-kai’s limuk k' tenderness. “i aitlun du tor sasarlah k' me na' wuh lates, sibyl. I don’t suppose i dungau ek'wak gla-tor nash horrid london va'ashiv. I am sure i don’t aitlun tor.” “t'nash-veh sa-fu, don’t leralmin such dreadful vel, ” murmured mrs. Vane, taking abru wuh tawdry theatrical sai-vel, k' wuh spes-tevan, heh palikaya tor patch ish-veh. She olau wuh pi' disappointed ik au had ri hau wuh travek. Ish-veh would ma increased wuh theatrical picturesqueness t' wuh situation. “po ri, ko-mekh? I tvai ish-veh.” “du kusut me, t'nash-veh sa-fu. I sahrafel du dungi fun s' australia svi' wuh shul t' affluence. I dva-tor tra' nam-tor rai shila'es t' sovek ves svi' wuh sashila—nothing ik i would vutau shila'es—ni lu du ma tor ish-veh fortune, du bolau sarlah pla' heh seo'a yourself svi' london.” “shila'es!” muttered wuh lad. “i don’t aitlun tor fai-tor sovek-vel pa' ik. I dang spo' tor tor ein donku tor nem-tor du heh sibyl ska' wuh skaf. I fnu-ven ish-veh.” “oh, jim!” leralmin-tor sibyl, laughing, “uf unkind t' du! Tonk'peh nam-tor du really going na' wuh lates k' me? Ik dungi nam-tor nice! I vesh' kwes du vesh' going tor leralmin rom-bye tor ein t' ish-veh t'hylara—tor tom hardy, vi mazhiv-kur-tor du ik hideous mev, il ned langton, vi tor mihrsh t' du na' smoking ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor maut slor t' du tor kal-tor me ma ish-veh kim-shah aru. Wilat dungau etek hal-tor? Kal-tor etek hal-tor tor wuh shi'sochya.” “i am nuh' shabby, ” au kilko-tor, frowning. “goh puv-tor sutra hal-tor tor wuh shi'sochya.” “nonsense, jim, ” she zhal-tor, stroking wuh sleeve t' ish-veh tor-pal. Au hesitated na' wuh moment. “maut muhl, ” au leralmin-tor na' kim-shah, “tonk'peh don’t nam-tor nuh' wu sai-vel-tor.” she tam-tor s' wuh svep. Veh kupi zhu-tor ish-veh uralaun u' she sahr-tor upstairs. Ish-veh pi' ash'ya lates-tor overhead. Au lates-tor abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal dahkuh il rehkuh wak. Yi au da-tor tor wuh fam dvun khlop svi' wuh ku-san. “ko-mekh, nam-tor t'nash-veh vel pok?” au ya'akash. “ved pok, james, ” she kilko-tor, keeping ish-veh bezhun fi' ish-veh ar'kadan. Na' ein tevun-krus vesht she had olau has-bosh na' ease lu she vesh' sa'awek k' nash rough harr-krus sa-fu t' ish-veh. Ish-veh gan tsat malat vesh' troubled lu ish-veh bezhun ragel-tor. She nam-tor-tor tor wonder kuv au suspected sovek-vel. Wuh silence, na' au tor rai vath glantaya, became intolerable tor ish-veh. She began tor complain. Kosu fosh-tor themselves k' attacking, aishan u' au nashiv-tor k' sudden heh flekh surrenders. “i rok du dungi nam-tor contented, james, k' ish-veh masutra-faring ha'kiv, ” she leralmin-tor. “du bolau vokau ik ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh sha' dvel. Du lau ma svi-tor wuh solicitor’s office. Solicitors nam-tor wuh maut respectable mohrn, heh svi' wuh shasol k'ashiv aru-yokul k' wuh buhfik skan.” “i fnu-ven offices, heh i fnu-ven clerks, ” au kilko-tor. “tonk'peh du nam-tor ved gas'rak. I ma pudvel-tor t'nash-veh sha' ha'kiv. Ek' i leralmin nam-tor, paluntunau sibyl. Don’t kal-tor ish-veh sarlah tor sovek klau. Ko-mekh, du bolau paluntunau ish-veh.” “james, du really variben maut strangely. Veling i paluntunau sibyl.” “i zhu-tor wuh gentleman sarlah kanok mu-yor tor wuh theatre heh hal-tor za' tor variben tor ish-veh. Nam-tor ik gas'rak? Ra pa' ik?” “du nam-tor speaking pa' vel du don’t ken-tor, james. Svi' wuh ha'yigal etek nam-tor accustomed tor poprah wuh lo'uk deal t' danik gratifying attention. I myself nam-tor-tor tor poprah wehk bouquets na' veh wak. Ik vesh' lu peran vesh' really ken-tor. U' na' sibyl, i ri tor fai-tor na' la' whether ish-veh attachment nam-tor serious il ri. Tonk'peh tra' nam-tor rai vet ik wuh nu'ri sasu svi' deshker nam-tor wuh buhfik gentleman. Au nam-tor kwon-hau-ov danik polite tor me. Isha, au has wuh appearance t' hasu don-ka, heh wuh svai au satau nam-tor lovely.” “du don’t fai-tor ish-veh ahm, hi, ” leralmin-tor wuh lad harshly. “rai, ” kilko-tor ish-veh ko-mekh k' wuh placid sagluvaya svi' ish-veh limuk. “au has ri wi revealed ish-veh yeht ahm. I nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor ved romantic t' ish-veh. Au nam-tor probably wuh kisau t' wuh aristocracy.” james vane zeshau ish-veh bru. “paluntunau sibyl, ko-mekh, ” au maf-tor, “glantau abru' ish-veh.” “t'nash-veh sa-fu, du flakosh me maut mau. Sibyl nam-tor kwon-hau-ov ne' t'nash-veh special tun. Veling, kuv nash gentleman nam-tor wealthy, tra' nam-tor rai utvau po she dang ri contract wuh alliance k' ish-veh. I sahrafel au nam-tor veh t' wuh aristocracy. Au has ek' wuh appearance t' ish-veh, i bolau leralmin. Ish-veh lau nam-tor wuh danik maut-ugelik kal'i'farr na' sibyl. Au would tor wuh sem-rik-tor couple. Ish-veh rom glazhau nam-tor really ved remarkable; kanok-veh beglanau au.” wuh lad muttered vel tor himself heh vluhn-tor fi' wuh krani-pane k' ish-veh dirik ozh. Au had aishan da-tor pauk tor leralmin vel lu wuh svep tu'ash heh sibyl sahr-tor svi'. “uf serious du fi' nam-tor!” she maf-tor. “ra nam-tor wuh tukh?” “nothing, ” au kilko-tor. “i suppose veh bolau nam-tor serious sometimes. Rom-bye, ko-mekh; i dungi ma t'nash-veh aru-yem na' kaukuh o’wak-vel. Kanok-vei nam-tor sa'haf-tor, kaula t'nash-veh sav'el, ni du bolaya ri trouble.” “rom-bye, t'nash-veh sa-fu, ” she kilko-tor k' wuh kes-wun t' ish-veh-tor stateliness. She vesh' extremely annoyed na' wuh molu au had thanai k' ish-veh, heh tra' vesh' vel svi' ish-veh glazhau ik had tor ish-veh olau kwes. “shok me, ko-mekh, ” leralmin-tor wuh ko-kan. Ish-veh flowerlike bru-lar estuhl wuh withered nak heh warmed its le-su. “t'nash-veh kan! T'nash-veh kan!” maf-tor mrs. Vane, looking abru tor wuh abru-tol svi' psthan t' wuh glenonik tanaf-shi'gluvaun. “sarlah, sibyl, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh sa-kai impatiently. Au fnu-ven ish-veh ko-mekh’s affectations. Au went si' vi' wuh flickering, salan-blown ug'yel-ha'gel heh strolled ne' wuh dreary euston fau-yut. Wuh passersby glanced svi' wonder na' wuh kir ras youth vi, svi' dirik, has-bosh-fitting sai-vel, vesh' svi' wuh apc'koik t' such wuh graceful, refined-looking ko-kan. Au vesh' spo' wuh tsuri bahsu walking k' wuh she-tor. Jim kwal-tor s' wak tor wak lu au kum-tor wuh inquisitive glance t' ein ri-fainusu. Au had ik ritishaya t' hasu nantau na', if sarlah fi' geniuses tab-ma svi' ha'kiv heh worla mor wuh commonplace. Sibyl, however, vesh' ved unconscious t' wuh daya she vesh' producing. Ish-veh ashaya vesh' trembling svi' laughter fi' ish-veh bru-lar. She vesh' thinking t' prince sem-rik-tor, heh, ik she lau nah-tor t' ish-veh ek' wuh weht, she did ri variben t' ish-veh, tonk'peh prattled fi' pa' wuh hali svi' if jim vesh' going tor mashalo-thalv, pa' wuh pi-maat-tukh au vesh' ac'ruth tor talal, pa' wuh wonderful heiress t'vi ha'kiv au vesh' tor korsau s' wuh wicked, yon-kur-shirted bushrangers. Na' au vesh' ri tor hafau wuh masusu, il wuh supercargo, il whatever au vesh' going tor nam-tor. Oh, rai! Wuh masusu’s nam vesh' dreadful. Fancy hasu cooped abru svi' wuh horrid hali, k' wuh hoarse, hump-backed pral trying tor prah svi', heh wuh nesh-kur salan blowing wuh mashalo-thalv-lap ne' heh tearing wuh masu-halovau vi' wu screaming ribands! Au vesh' tor trasha wuh hali na' melbourne, nufai wuh polite rom-bye tor wuh khart-lan, heh hal-tor ska' na' wuh'wak tor wuh pi-maat-tukh-vunai. Fa' wuh wehk gad vesh' abru' au vesh' tor sarlah mes' wuh suk nugget t' pure pi-maat-tukh, wuh largest nugget ik had ek'wak vesh' discovered, heh katau ish-veh ne' tor wuh gef svi' wuh waggon klashau k' shehkuh mounted policemen. Wuh bushrangers vesh' tor nashiv-tor au rehkuh wak, heh nam-tor defeated k' immense slaughter. Il, rai. Au vesh' ri tor hal-tor tor wuh pi-maat-tukh-vunai na' ek'. Au vesh' horrid shitau, wilat sasu prah intoxicated, heh pohshaya tik vath svi' mofek-tvi-shal, heh nam-tor-tor rasahkos gen-lis. Au vesh' tor nam-tor wuh nice sheep-uroshitausu, heh veh khru, u' au vesh' riding ha-kel, au vesh' tor gla-tor wuh vaksurik heiress hasu lesh ska' k' wuh robber fi' wuh nesh-kur jarel, heh mazhiv-kur-tor a'vesh', heh rescue ish-veh. Veling, she would tevan svi' ashaya k' ish-veh, heh au k' ish-veh, heh au would prah telik, heh sarlah ha-kel, heh ha-tor svi' wuh immense kelek svi' london. Ha, tra' vesh' delightful vel svi' mahr-kel na' ish-veh. Tonk'peh au bolau nam-tor maut rom, heh ri pak-tor ish-veh temper, il spend ish-veh donku foolishly. She vesh' goh wuh tevun older do au vesh', tonk'peh she fai-tor ni mau weht t' ha'kiv. Au bolau nam-tor sure, isha, tor kitau tor ish-veh k' kanok sakat, heh tor leralmin ish-veh prayers tik mu-yor fa' au went tor yuk. Oekon vesh' maut rom, heh would paluntunau ish-veh. She would pray na' ish-veh, nuh', heh svi' wuh zamu tevun au would sarlah pla' ved don-ka heh kunli. Wuh lad shroi sulkily tor ish-veh heh tor rai kilko-srashiv. Au vesh' khaf-spol-has-bosh na' leaving ha-kel. Wi ish-veh vesh' ri nash sa'awek ik tor ish-veh gloomy heh morose. Inexperienced hi au vesh', au had fam dvun wuh karik kash-ral t' wuh tehvar t' sibyl’s shul. Nash nu'ri dandy vi vesh' tor ashaya tor ish-veh kupi tvai ish-veh rai rom. Au vesh' wuh gentleman, heh au fnu-ven ish-veh na' ik, fnu-ven ish-veh k'fai ein curious ne-koshtri-instinct na' if au kupi ri khrosahp, heh if na' ik utvau vesh' ek' wuh weht abrupik k'svi ish-veh. Au vesh' d'wonil isha t' wuh shallowness heh vanity t' ish-veh ko-mekh’s malat, heh svi' ik gla-tor vaik peril na' sibyl heh sibyl’s happiness. Kanu palikau k' loving ish-veh mekhlar; u' au tor'ovau older au judge au; sometimes au forgive au. Ish-veh ko-mekh! Au had vel fi' ish-veh kashek tor ya'akash t' ish-veh, vel ik au had brooded fi' na' wehk tevun-krus t' silence. Wuh pavesh zhit-bal ik au had puzhu-tor na' wuh theatre, wuh zhal-tor sneer ik had pulau ish-veh kaluk veh mu-yor u' au bek-tor na' wuh skaf-svep, had eku thal wuh ranau t' horrible nahp. Au vokau ish-veh u' kuv ish-veh had vesh' wuh lash t' wuh hunting-urozh mes' ish-veh limuk. Ish-veh meix'tem knit teretuhr vi' wuh shihvek-spo' furrow, heh k' wuh twitch t' kusut au zeshau ish-veh underlip. “du nam-tor ri listening tor wuh zhit i am taran, jim, ” maf-tor sibyl, “heh i am tor wuh danik delightful dotoran na' ish-veh fa-wak. Tor leralmin vel.” “ra tor du aitlun me tor leralmin?” “oh! Ik du dungi nam-tor wuh rom sa-kan heh ri yen-tor etek, ” she kilko-tor, smiling na' ish-veh. Au shrugged ish-veh tipan. “du nam-tor weht kesik tor yen-tor me do i am tor yen-tor du, sibyl.” she kluhvau. “ra tor du tvai, jim?” she ya'akash. “du ma wuh uzh t'hy'la, i zhu-tor. Vi nam-tor au? Po ma du ri var-tor me pa' ish-veh? Au tvai du rai rom.” “pehkaya, jim!” she sporiben. “du bolau ri leralmin sovek-vel tehnat ish-veh. I ashaya ish-veh.” “po, du don’t kauk fai-tor ish-veh ahm, ” kilko-tor wuh lad. “vi nam-tor au? I ma wuh gas'rak tor fai-tor.” “au nam-tor puvutau prince sem-rik-tor. Don’t du spo' wuh ahm. Oh! Du silly sa-kan! Du dang worla yen-tor ish-veh. Kuv du goh gla-tor ish-veh, du would nah-tor ish-veh wuh danik wonderful person svi' wuh panu. Ein gad du dungi ragel-tor ish-veh—lu sarlah du pla' s' australia. Du dungi spo' ish-veh ni mau. Kanok-veh tishau ish-veh, heh i. Ashaya ish-veh. I istaya du kupi sarlah tor wuh theatre tor-mu-yor. Au nam-tor going tor nam-tor tra', heh i am tor mavau juliet. Oh! Uf i dungau mavau ish-veh! Fancy, jim, tor nam-tor svi' ashaya heh mavau juliet! Ki' ish-veh sitting tra'! Tor mavau na' ish-veh delight! I am kwes i lau koltha wuh apc'koik, koltha il enthrall au. Tor nam-tor svi' ashaya nam-tor tor namautau veh’s shal. Ri donku-tor dreadful mr. Isaacs dungi nam-tor shouting ‘genius’ tor ish-veh loafers na' wuh mofek. Au has preached me u' wuh dogma; tor-mu-yor au dungi tor'pra me u' wuh revelation. I olau ish-veh. Heh ish-veh nam-tor ek' ish-veh, ish-veh goh, prince sem-rik-tor, t'nash-veh wonderful lover, t'nash-veh oekon t' takov-tor. Tonk'peh i am ri donku-tor be' ish-veh. Ri donku-tor? Ra tor ik tukh? Lu poverty creeps svi' na' wuh svep, ashaya hash-tor svi' k'fai wuh krani. Etwel proverbs aitlun rewriting. Au vesh' tor svi' karil, heh ish-veh nam-tor belaar i'; sikar-wak na' me, i nah-tor, wuh maut tam t' blossoms svi' pla-kur igen.” “au nam-tor wuh gentleman, ” leralmin-tor wuh lad sullenly. “wuh prince!” she maf-tor musically. “ra weht tor du aitlun?” “au aitlu tor enslave du.” “i ak'shem-hutau na' wuh nahp t' hasu elik.” “i aitlun du tor beware t' ish-veh.” “tor gla-tor ish-veh nam-tor tor worship ish-veh; tor fai-tor ish-veh nam-tor tor sahrafel ish-veh.” “sibyl, du nam-tor mad pa' ish-veh.” she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh nem-tor ish-veh kar. “du tal-kam hinek jim, du variben u' kuv du vesh' wuh hundred. Ein gad du dungi nam-tor svi' ashaya yourself. Yi du dungi fai-tor ra ish-veh nam-tor. Don’t glazhau ni sulky. Surely du dang nam-tor glad tor nah-tor ik, hi du nam-tor going maf, du trasha me happier do i ma ek'wak vesh' fa'. Ha'kiv has vesh' lerash na' etek fi', terribly lerash heh rihagik. Tonk'peh ish-veh dungi nam-tor natya i'. Du nam-tor going tor wuh uzh panu, heh i ma afer-tor veh. La' nam-tor dahkuh ku-san; kal-tor etek hayal-tor ne' heh gla-tor wuh klon sutra hal-tor k'.” au nem-tor ish-veh ku-san amidst wuh patreitan t' watchers. Wuh lale-sar-tak mes' wuh fau-yut flamed spo' throbbing mokov t' yon. Wuh wan-kur grazhiv—tremulous wan t' orris-gir ish-veh seemed—geldau svi' wuh panting sov. Wuh brightly kur-tor parasols tam-tor heh spis-tor spo' monstrous mathra. She tor ish-veh sa-kai variben t' himself, ish-veh rok-tor, ish-veh prospects. Au stariben slowly heh k' urgam. Au be' dvun-tor zhit tor tik vath u' hahf na' wuh zhagra be' dvun tumek. Sibyl olau oppressed. She kupi ri sviribau ish-veh mak. Wuh faint abru'teruklar-ru'lut curving ik kir ru'lut vesh' ek' wuh vava she kupi skil. Po' ein wak she became ralash-fam. Suddenly she kum-tor wuh glimpse t' pi-maat-kur isachya heh laughing bru-lar, heh svi' wuh tu'ash carriage k' dahkuh t'sai dorian zhai-kur drove vesht. She palikau tor ish-veh ash'ya. “tra' au nam-tor!” she maf-tor. “vi?” leralmin-tor jim vane. “prince sem-rik-tor, ” she kilko-tor, looking po' wuh victoria. Au spen-tor abru heh seized ish-veh roughly k' wuh kar. “gluvaya ish-veh tor me. If nam-tor au? Sfek ish-veh si'. I bolau gla-tor ish-veh!” au sporiben; tonk'peh na' ik moment wuh duke t' berwick’s kehkuh-svi'-el'ru sarlah svi', heh lu ish-veh had losrak wuh ret pa'shik, wuh carriage had swept s' wuh shi'sochya. “au nam-tor hal-tor, ” murmured sibyl sadly. “i istaya du had gla-tor ish-veh.” “i istaya i had, na' u' sure u' tra' nam-tor wuh oekon svi' sha-ka-ri, kuv au ek'wak tor du sovek riyeht, i dungau stau ish-veh.” she glazhau na' ish-veh svi' horror. Au ashiv-tor ish-veh zhit. Au tresahk wuh sov spo' wuh lipitah. Wuh sutra pauk began tor gape. Wuh t'sai standing beyik ish-veh tittered. “sarlah maf, jim; sarlah maf, ” she zhal-tor. Au zahal-tor ish-veh doggedly u' she be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh patreitan. Au olau glad na' ra au had leralmin-tor. Lu au pulau wuh achilles sukhlop, she da-tor pauk. Tra' vesh' pity svi' ish-veh bezhun ik became laughter fi' ish-veh bru-lar. She hutau ish-veh patam na' ish-veh. “du nam-tor duhik, jim, utterly duhik; wuh rasahkos-tempered sa-kan, ik nam-tor ek'. Uf mokuhlek du leralmin such horrible vel? Du don’t fai-tor ra du nam-tor talking pa'. Du nam-tor veling kis-ka heh unkind. Ah! I istaya du would tevan svi' ashaya. Ashaya tor sutra rom, heh ra du leralmin-tor vesh' wicked.” “i am leh-sheh, ” au kilko-tor, “heh i fai-tor ra i am pa'. Ko-mekh nam-tor rai gol'nev tor du. She doesn’t ken-tor uf tor glazhau po' du. I istaya i' ik i vesh' ri going tor australia na' ek'. I ma wuh lo'uk kashek tor chuck wuh bosh vel abru. I would, kuv t'nash-veh ua'mrki hadn’t vesh' signed.” “oh, don’t nam-tor ni serious, jim. Du nam-tor spo' veh t' wuh heroes t' eifa silly melodramas ko-mekh nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor ni tishau t' peran svi'. I am ri going tor quarrel k' du. Ki'gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh, heh oh! Tor gla-tor ish-veh nam-tor buhfik happiness. Etek skil-tor’t quarrel. I fai-tor du would worla klau sovek veh i ashaya, would du?” “ri u' wu u' du ashaya ish-veh, i suppose, ” vesh' wuh kir kilko-srashiv. “i dungau ashaya ish-veh na' ek'wak!” she maf-tor. “heh au?” “na' ek'wak, nuh'!” “au had weh-rom.” she shrank s' ish-veh. Yi she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh shitau ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh kar. Au vesh' goh wuh sa-kan. Na' wuh marble kesek au hailed wuh omnibus, if losrak au beyik ish-veh shabby ha-kel svi' wuh euston fau-yut. Ish-veh vesh' po' kaukuh o’wak-vel, heh sibyl had tor ti ne' na' wuh couple t' wadan fa' peran. Jim insisted ik she dang tor ni. Au leralmin-tor ik au would sooner krus k' ish-veh lu ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' ri la'. She would nam-tor sure tor tor wuh scene, heh au detested scenes t' kanok ves. Svi' sybil’s sha' tvi-shal au parted. Tra' vesh' jealousy svi' wuh lad’s khaf-spol, heh wuh kei murderous hatred t' wuh ri-fainusu vi, u' ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh, had sarlah svi' au. Wi, lu ish-veh kar vesh' flung pauk ish-veh talu, heh ish-veh ozh fam-kelek-tor k'fai ish-veh isachya, au softened heh shok-tor ish-veh k' yeht affection. Tra' vesh' bezhun-masu svi' ish-veh bezhun u' au went downstairs. Ish-veh ko-mekh vesh' waiting na' ish-veh ne'. She grumbled na' ish-veh unpunctuality, u' au svi-tor. Au tor rai kilko-srashiv, tonk'peh hayal-tor ne' tor ish-veh meagre yem. Wuh hash-tor buzzed pauk wuh pasu heh ukrau abru' wuh kurau sai. K'fai wuh rumble t' omnibuses, heh wuh clatter t' yut-cabs, au kupi zhu-tor wuh droning spes devouring tik minute ik vesh' losrak tor ish-veh. Po' ein wak, au kwit maf ish-veh math heh shitau ish-veh patam svi' ish-veh el'ru. Au olau ik au had wuh gas'rak tor fai-tor. Ish-veh dang ma vesh' var-tor tor ish-veh fa', kuv ish-veh vesh' u' au suspected. Leaden k' pthak, ish-veh ko-mekh glantau ish-veh. Zhit eku-tor mechanically s' ish-veh bru-lar. Wuh tattered lace handkerchief twitched svi' ish-veh ozh. Lu wuh wak-vel kwul-tor shehkuh, au prah abru heh went tor wuh svep. Yi au da-tor pla' heh glazhau na' ish-veh. Ish-veh bezhun ragel-tor. Svi' ish-veh gla-tor ish-veh wuh kwai appeal na' mercy. Ish-veh enraged ish-veh. “ko-mekh, i ma vel tor ya'akash du, ” au leralmin-tor. Ish-veh bezhun czar-tor vaguely pa' wuh tvi-shal. She tor rai kilko-srashiv. “var-tor me wuh yeht'es. I ma wuh gas'rak tor fai-tor. Vesh' du telik tor t'nash-veh sa-mekh?” she heaved wuh glu spes-tevan. Ish-veh vesh' wuh spes-tevan t' vas. Wuh terrible moment, wuh moment ik mu-yor heh gad, na' wehk gad heh tevun-krus, she had dreaded, had sarlah na' kim-shah, heh wi she olau rai vash. Indeed, svi' ein thon-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh disappointment tor ish-veh. Wuh vulgar directness t' wuh deshker puvutau na' wuh kharik kilko-srashiv. Wuh situation had ri vesh' gradually pufulag-tor abru tor. Ish-veh vesh' crude. Ish-veh reminded ish-veh t' wuh rasahkos rehearsal. “rai, ” she kilko-tor, wondering na' wuh harsh simplicity t' ha'kiv. “t'nash-veh sa-mekh vesh' wuh scoundrel yi!” maf-tor wuh lad, clenching ish-veh ozh-dukal. She hutau ish-veh patam. “i fai-tor au vesh' ri elik. Etek ashau tik vath maut mau. Kuv au had ha-tor, au would ma tor provision na' etek. Don’t stariben tehnat ish-veh, t'nash-veh sa-fu. Au vesh' ish-veh sa-mekh, heh wuh gentleman. Indeed, au vesh' highly tersau.” wuh oath shau s' ish-veh bru-lar. “i don’t palutunau myself, ” au sporiben, “tonk'peh don’t kal-tor sibyl. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh gentleman, isn’t ish-veh, vi nam-tor svi' ashaya k' ish-veh, il leralmin-tor au nam-tor? Highly tersau, nuh', i suppose.” na' wuh moment wuh hideous kash-ral t' humiliation sarlah abru' wuh kosu. Ish-veh patam tevan-tor. She psethau ish-veh bezhun k' shaking el'ru. “sibyl has wuh ko-mekh, ” she murmured; “i had rim.” wuh lad vesh' estuhl. Au went na' ish-veh, heh stooping ne', au shok-tor ish-veh. “ni'droi'ik nar-tor kuv i ma kusut-tor du k' asking pa' t'nash-veh sa-mekh, ” au leralmin-tor, “tonk'peh i kupi ri gol'nev ish-veh. I bolau hal-tor i'. Rom-bye. Don’t yen-tor ik du dungi ma goh veh kan i' tor glazhau po', heh dva-tor me ik kuv nash sasu wrongs t'nash-veh ko-kai, i dungi talal si' vi au nam-tor, yut ish-veh ne', heh stau ish-veh spo' wuh dog. I swear ish-veh.” wuh exaggerated folly t' wuh nan, wuh passionate gesture ik accompanied ish-veh, wuh mad melodramatic zhit, tor ha'kiv seem weht vivid tor ish-veh. She vesh' familiar k' wuh igen-tukh. She breathed weht freely, heh na' wuh wuh'rak wak na' wehk tevun-krus she really krol-tor ish-veh sa-fu. She would ma tishau ki' fator wuh scene fi' wuh ka zherka-bosh wef, tonk'peh au tresahk ish-veh pen. Lap-fek had tor nam-tor lesh ne' heh mufflers glazhau na'. Wuh lodging-kelek drudge bustled svi' heh si'. Tra' vesh' wuh bargaining k' wuh cabman. Wuh moment vesh' pakik svi' vulgar details. Ish-veh vesh' k' wuh uzhau olaya t' disappointment ik she pral-tor wuh tattered lace handkerchief s' wuh krani, u' ish-veh sa-fu drove maf. She vesh' d'wonil ik wuh lo'uk opportunity had vesh' thinoi. She consoled herself k' telling sibyl uf desolate she olau ish-veh ha'kiv would nam-tor, i' ik she had goh veh kan tor glazhau po'. She vokau wuh zhit-bal. Ish-veh had sanoi ish-veh. T' wuh nan she leralmin-tor nothing. Ish-veh vesh' vividly heh dramatically sagluvau. She olau ik au would ek' abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' ish-veh ein gad. Chapter vi. “i suppose du ma puzhu-tor wuh ro'fori, basil?” leralmin-tor s'haile henry ik khru u' hallward vesh' shown vi' wuh pi' awek tvi-shal na' wuh bristol wilat aru-yem had vesh' laid na' rehkuh. “rai, harry, ” kilko-tor wuh tanafsu, giving ish-veh taik heh tor-pal tor wuh bowing waiter. “ra nam-tor ish-veh? Nothing pa' politics, i rok! Au don’t eku'ko me. Tra' nam-tor hardly wuh single person svi' wuh kelek t' commons don krasan, hi wehk t' au would nam-tor wuh weh-rom na' wuh pi' whitewashing.” “dorian zhai-kur nam-tor engaged tor nam-tor telik, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, watching ish-veh u' au stariben. Hallward palikau heh yi kwal-tor. “dorian engaged tor nam-tor telik!” au maf-tor. “impossible!” “ish-veh nam-tor perfectly yeht.” “tor ik?” “tor ein pi' fundauik-ithop il vath.” “i mokuhlek’t dva-tor ish-veh. Dorian nam-tor irak nuh' sensible.” “dorian nam-tor irak nuh' kau-bosh ri tor tor duhik vel i' heh yi, t'nash-veh tal-kam basil.” “kal'i'farr nam-tor hardly wuh vel ish-veh mokuhlek tor i' heh yi, harry.” “kaula svi' america, ” rejoined s'haile henry languidly. “tonk'peh i didn’t leralmin au vesh' telik. I leralmin-tor au vesh' engaged tor nam-tor telik. Tra' nam-tor wuh lo'uk natyan. I ma wuh natya remembrance t' hasu telik, tonk'peh i ma rai recollection na' ek' t' hasu engaged. I am vul-tor tor nah-tor ik i worla vesh' engaged.” “tonk'peh nah-tor t' dorian’s keshtan, heh shul, heh don-tak. Ish-veh would nam-tor absurd na' ish-veh tor marry ni mau ne'rak ish-veh.” “kuv du aitlun tor tor ish-veh marry nash ko-kan, var-tor ish-veh ik, basil. Au nam-tor sure tor tor ish-veh, yi. Whenever wuh sasu tor wuh thoroughly stupid vel, ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov s' wuh noblest dvubolek.” “i rok wuh ko-kan nam-tor rom, harry. I don’t aitlun tor gla-tor dorian tied tor ein vile creature, vi lau degrade ish-veh malat heh ruin ish-veh kash-tor-vel.” “oh, she nam-tor weh-rom do rom—she nam-tor vaksurik, ” murmured s'haile henry, mon-tor wuh makh t' vermouth heh zhar-kur-bitters. “dorian leralmin-tor she nam-tor vaksurik, heh au nam-tor ri k'ashiv riyeht pa' vel t' ik ves. Ish-veh portrait t' ish-veh has quickened ish-veh appreciation t' wuh personal appearance t' vath sutra. Ish-veh has had ik marom daya, svi' vath. Etek nam-tor tor gla-tor ish-veh tor-mu-yor, kuv ik sa-kan doesn’t yen-tor ish-veh latva.” “nam-tor du serious?” “ved serious, basil. I dang nam-tor miserable kuv i nahp i dang ek'wak nam-tor weht serious do i am na' wuh la' moment.” “tonk'peh tor du messau t' ish-veh, harry?” ya'akash wuh krassu, walking abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal heh biting ish-veh bru. “du mokuhlek’t messau t' ish-veh, possibly. Ish-veh nam-tor ein silly infatuation.” “i worla messau, il disapprove, t' sovek-vel i'. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh absurd attitude tor nem-tor na' ha'kiv. Etek nam-tor ri satau vi' wuh panu tor sov etwel moral prejudices. I worla nem-tor sovek beglanau t' ra tsuri sutra leralmin, heh i worla snertau k' ra sem-rik-tor sutra tor. Kuv wuh nafu'es sem-tor me, whatever nuk t' sagluvaya ik nafu'es dvel-tor nam-tor absolutely delightful tor me. Dorian zhai-kur tevan-tor svi' ashaya k' wuh vaksurik ko-kan vi fundauik-tor juliet, heh proposes tor marry ish-veh. Po ri? Kuv au wedded messalina, au would nam-tor rim wuh lehkuh eku'ki. Du fai-tor i am ri wuh skilamu t' kal'i'farr. Wuh yeht drawback tor kal'i'farr nam-tor ik ish-veh tor veh unselfish. Heh unselfish sutra nam-tor colourless. Au fam individuality. Fam dvun, tra' nam-tor ac'ruth temperaments ik kal'i'farr tor weht wehkonik. Au retain ish-veh ritsuri-shai'es, heh hau tor ish-veh wehk vath shayuf. Au nam-tor punekwitau ki' weht do veh ha'kiv. Au shetau weht highly organized, heh tor nam-tor highly organized nam-tor, i dang fancy, wuh vel t' sasu’s nam. Isha, kanok veshtaya nam-tor t' tala, heh whatever veh lau leralmin tehnat kal'i'farr, ish-veh nam-tor certainly wuh veshtaya. I rok ik dorian zhai-kur dungi tor nash ko-kan ish-veh ko-telsu, passionately adore ish-veh na' shehkuh tevun-krus, heh yi suddenly shetau sem-tor k' ein veh else. Au would nam-tor wuh wonderful orenau.” “du don’t tvai wuh single zhit t' ek' ik, harry; du fai-tor du don’t. Kuv dorian zhai-kur’s ha'kiv vesh' spoiled, kling would nam-tor sorrier do yourself. Du nam-tor mau weh-rom do du pretend tor nam-tor.” s'haile henry abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “wuh utvau etek ek' spo' tor nah-tor ni muhl t' vath nam-tor ik etek nam-tor ek' kwes na' ourselves. Wuh i'sav t' optimism nam-tor sheer vash. Etek nah-tor ik etek nam-tor generous fai'ei etek lit etwel behsu k' wuh mat t' eifa virtues ik nam-tor kesik tor nam-tor wuh rufai tor etek. Etek krol wuh banker ik etek lau overdraw etwel khrosahp, heh talal rom qualities svi' wuh highwayman svi' wuh rok ik au lau spare etwel abru'lik. I tvai kanok-vei ik i ma leralmin-tor. I ma wuh greatest contempt na' optimism. U' na' wuh spoiled ha'kiv, rai ha'kiv nam-tor spoiled tonk'peh veh t'vi tor'ovak nam-tor pehkau. Kuv du aitlun tor mar wuh malat, du ma goh tor reform ish-veh. U' na' kal'i'farr, veling ik would nam-tor silly, tonk'peh tra' nam-tor vath heh weht eku'ki tel svi' sasu heh kosu. I dungi certainly kastorau au. Au ma wuh sem-rik t' hasu fashionable. Tonk'peh la' nam-tor dorian himself. Au dungi var-tor du weht do i mokuhlek.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam harry, t'nash-veh tal-kam basil, du bolau fi' congratulate me!” leralmin-tor wuh lad, throwing ska' ish-veh khru cape k' its satin-zehl-tor rala heh shaking tik t' ish-veh t'hylara k' wuh el'ru svi' da-tor. “i ma worla vesh' ni kunli.
