Veling, ish-veh nam-tor sudden—ek' really delightful vel nam-tor. Heh wi ish-veh seems tor me tor nam-tor wuh veh vel i ma vesh' looking na' ek' t'nash-veh ha'kiv.” au vesh' kluhvau k' tepor'es heh sanosh, heh glazhau extraordinarily handsome. “i rok du dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor maut kunli, dorian, ” leralmin-tor hallward, “tonk'peh i don’t ved forgive du na' ri having kal-tor me fai-tor t' ish-veh engagement. Du kal-tor harry fai-tor.” “heh i don’t forgive du na' hasu tab-ma na' aru-yem, ” shau svi' s'haile henry, putting ish-veh el'ru fi' wuh lad’s tipan heh smiling u' au stariben. “sarlah, kal-tor etek hayal-tor ne' heh ar'kadan ra wuh uzh _chef_ la' nam-tor spo', heh yi du dungi var-tor etek uf ish-veh ek' sarlah pa'.” “tra' nam-tor really ri mau tor var-tor, ” maf-tor dorian u' au nem-tor ish-veh ku-san na' wuh pi' pauk pasu. “ra pavesh-tor vesh' veling nash. Po' i losrak du za-gad khru, harry, i sai-vel-tor, had ein aru-yem na' ik pi' italian restaurant svi' rupert yut du puragtau me tor, heh went ne' na' ohkuh o’wak-vel tor wuh theatre. Sibyl vesh' mavaun rosalind. Veling, wuh scenery vesh' dreadful heh wuh orlando absurd. Tonk'peh sibyl! Du dang ma gla-tor ish-veh! Lu sarlah ish-veh fi' svi' ish-veh sa-kan’s sai-vel, she vesh' perfectly wonderful. She sai-vel-tor wuh yekuhl-kur-tor velvet jerkin k' cinnamon sleeves, slim, khav-kur, tuhs-gartered hose, wuh dainty pi' yar-kur taik k' wuh hawk’s kan kum-tor svi' wuh ek'zer, heh wuh hooded tor-sai zehl-tor k' pasik yon-kur. She had worla seemed tor me weht exquisite. She had ek' wuh delicate takov t' ik tanagra pi'sukhlop ik du ma svi' ish-veh studio, basil. Ish-veh isachya clustered pauk ish-veh limuk spo' gu'gelik mor pauk wuh spoh she-tor. U' na' ish-veh peran—muhl, du dungau gla-tor ish-veh tor-mu-yor. She nam-tor veling wuh pukeshta tanafsu. I hayal-tor svi' wuh dingy natuhn absolutely enthralled. I forgot ik i vesh' svi' london heh svi' wuh nineteenth century. I vesh' maf k' t'nash-veh ashaya svi' wuh laptra ik rai sasu had ek'wak gla-tor. Po' wuh performance vesh' abru', i went za' heh stariben tor ish-veh. U' etek vesh' sitting teretuhr, suddenly tra' sarlah vi' ish-veh bezhun wuh glazhau ik i had worla gla-tor tra' fa'. T'nash-veh bru-lar dvun-tor na' ish-veh. Etek shok-tor tik vath. I mokuhlek’t kethelvau tor du ra i olau na' ik moment. Ish-veh seemed tor me ik ek' t'nash-veh ha'kiv had vesh' wonilau tor veh buhfik sfek t' she-tor-kur-tor mak. She trembled ek' abru' heh hutau spo' wuh wan-kur narcissus. Yi she flung herself fi' ish-veh mal-nef heh shok-tor t'nash-veh el'ru. I olau ik i dang ri var-tor du ek' nash, tonk'peh i mokuhlek’t gol'nev ish-veh. T' rivak, etwel engagement nam-tor wuh tevik tsat. She has ri kauk var-tor ish-veh sha' ko-mekh. I don’t fai-tor ra t'nash-veh guardians dungi leralmin. S'haile radley nam-tor sure tor nam-tor furious. I don’t tun. I dungau nam-tor t' ya'shakhuv svi' lehkuh tor wuh tevun, heh yi i mokuhlek tor ra i spo'. I ma vesh' gas'rak, basil, haven’t i, tor nem-tor t'nash-veh ashaya s' poetry heh tor talal t'nash-veh ko-telsu svi' shakespeare’s mavau? Bru-lar ik shakespeare saven-tor tor stariben ma zhal-tor ish-veh tsat svi' t'nash-veh kaluk. I ma had wuh kar t' rosalind pa' me, heh shok-tor juliet fi' wuh ru'lut.” “ha, dorian, i suppose du vesh' gas'rak, ” leralmin-tor hallward slowly. “ma du gla-tor ish-veh tor-gad?” ya'akash s'haile henry. Dorian zhai-kur hutau ish-veh patam. “i losrak ish-veh svi' wuh laptra t' arden; i dungau talal ish-veh svi' wuh lap-bah-ker svi' verona.” s'haile henry mon-tor ish-veh champagne svi' wuh meditative manner. “na' ra particular sfek did du mention wuh zhit kal'i'farr, dorian? Heh ra did she leralmin svi' kilko-srashiv? Sos'eh du forgot ek' pa' ish-veh.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam harry, i did ri skasau ish-veh u' wuh business transaction, heh i did ri tor sovek hotorik mnah. I var-tor ish-veh ik i ashau ish-veh, heh she leralmin-tor she vesh' ri worthy tor nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu. Ri worthy! Po, wuh bosh panu nam-tor nothing tor me tcok'at k' ish-veh.” “kosu nam-tor wonderfully practical, ” murmured s'haile henry, “mau weht practical do etek nam-tor. Svi' situations t' ik ves etek k'ashiv yen-tor tor leralmin sovek-vel pa' kal'i'farr, heh au kwon-hau-ov remind etek.” hallward laid ish-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh kar. “don’t, harry. Du ma annoyed dorian. Au nam-tor ri spo' vath sasu. Au would worla katau misery fi-tor sovek veh. Ish-veh malat nam-tor nuh' tok-ti na' ik.” s'haile henry glazhau mes' wuh pasu. “dorian nam-tor worla annoyed k' me, ” au kilko-tor. “i ya'akash wuh deshker na' wuh buhfik utvau tor-yehat, na' wuh goh utvau, indeed, ik tobeg-tor veh na' asking sovek deshker—velik curiosity. I ma wuh wihka ik ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh kosu vi propose tor etek, heh ri etek vi propose tor wuh kosu. Kaula, t' rivak, svi' svitan-mohrn ha'kiv. Tonk'peh yi wuh svitan mohrn nam-tor ri iyik.” dorian zhai-kur abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh tossed ish-veh patam. “du nam-tor ved incorrigible, harry; tonk'peh i don’t kashek. Ish-veh nam-tor impossible tor nam-tor reshnek k' du. Lu gla-tor du sibyl vane, du dungi olau ik wuh sasu vi kupi riyeht ish-veh would nam-tor wuh beast, wuh beast rik' wuh khaf-spol. I fam yehat ken-tor uf sovek veh mokuhlek istaya tor mesh wuh vel au ashau. I ashaya sibyl vane. I aitlun tor shi ish-veh fi' wuh nelka t' pi-maat-tukh heh tor gla-tor wuh panu worship wuh kosu vi nam-tor t'nash-veh. Ra nam-tor kal'i'farr? Wuh irrevocable vow. Du mock na' ish-veh na' ik. Ah! Don’t mock. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh irrevocable vow ik i aitlun tor nem-tor. Ish-veh sahrafel tor me faithful, ish-veh dva tor me rom. Lu i am k' ish-veh, i regret ek' ik du ma saven-tor me. I shetau natya s' ra du ma fainu me tor nam-tor. I am rubai, heh wuh mere esta t' sibyl vane’s el'ru tor me yen-tor du heh ek' ish-veh riyeht, sem-rik, poisonous, delightful wihka.” “heh eifa nam-tor?” ya'akash s'haile henry, helping himself tor ein yarmok. “oh, ish-veh wihka pa' ha'kiv, ish-veh wihka pa' ashaya, ish-veh wihka pa' sanosh. Ek' ish-veh wihka, svi' kla-min, harry.” “sanosh nam-tor wuh goh vel don having wuh wihka pa', ” au kilko-tor svi' ish-veh vohris melodious spes. “tonk'peh i am kwes i fam yehat claim t'nash-veh wihka u' t'nash-veh sha'. Ish-veh t' malat, ri tor me. Sanosh nam-tor malat’s nisan, ish-veh glat t' messaya. Lu etek nam-tor kunli, etek nam-tor kwon-hau-ov rom, tonk'peh lu etek nam-tor rom, etek nam-tor ri kwon-hau-ov kunli.” “ah! Tonk'peh ra tor du tvai k' rom?” maf-tor basil hallward. “ha, ” echoed dorian, leaning pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san heh looking na' s'haile henry abru' wuh ras clusters t' gahv-kur-lipped kurak ik lam-tor svi' wuh centre t' wuh pasu, “ra tor du tvai k' rom, harry?” “tor nam-tor rom nam-tor tor nam-tor svi' kril'es k' veh’s shal, ” au kilko-tor, touching wuh wonil kas-fek t' ish-veh makh k' ish-veh spoh, tok-ti-sfekau ozh. “discord nam-tor tor nam-tor punekwitau tor nam-tor svi' kril'es k' vath. Veh’s sha' ha'kiv—ik nam-tor wuh yauluhk vel. U' na' wuh ha-tor t' veh’s behsu, kuv veh istau tor nam-tor wuh prig il wuh puritan, veh mokuhlek flaunt veh’s moral zan-tor pa' au, tonk'peh au nam-tor ri veh’s concern. Isha, individualism has really wuh higher mokh. Iyik morality consists svi' accepting wuh standard t' veh’s ya'shakhuv. I panah-tor ik na' sovek sasu t' iyula tor nar-tor wuh standard t' ish-veh ya'shakhuv nam-tor wuh shid t' wuh grossest immorality.” “tonk'peh, surely, kuv veh ha-tor goh na' veh’s shal, harry, veh vlitau wuh terrible price na' doing ni?” suggested wuh krassu. “ha, etek nam-tor overcharged na' kanok-vei nowadays. I dang fancy ik wuh yeht tragedy t' wuh ri donku-tor nam-tor ik au mokuhlek afford nothing tonk'peh shal-wafaya. Vaksurik sins, spo' vaksurik vel, nam-tor wuh privilege t' wuh don-ka.” “veh has tor vlitau svi' vath yut tonk'peh donku.” “ra wihfelau t' yut, basil?” “oh! I dang fancy svi' remorse, svi' suffering, svi'. Muhl, svi' wuh hokni'es t' degradation.” s'haile henry shrugged ish-veh tipan. “t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, mediæval tanaf nam-tor sem-rik-tor, tonk'peh mediæval zherka nam-tor s' kinuf. Veh mokuhlek nam-tor-tor au svi' glenokitau-tanaf, veling. Tonk'peh yi wuh goh vel ish-veh mokuhlek nam-tor-tor svi' glenokitau-tanaf nam-tor wuh vel ish-veh has ceased tor nam-tor-tor svi' kla-min. Dva-tor me, rai civilized sasu ek'wak regrets wuh sanosh, heh rai uncivilized sasu ek'wak fai-tor ra wuh sanosh nam-tor.” “i fai-tor ra sanosh nam-tor, ” maf-tor dorian zhai-kur. “ish-veh nam-tor tor adore ein veh.” “ik nam-tor certainly weh-rom do hasu adored, ” au kilko-tor, toying k' ein savas. “hasu adored nam-tor wuh nuisance. Kosu skasau etek aishan u' humanity skasau its gods. Au worship etek, heh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov bothering etek tor tor vel na' au.” “i dang ma leralmin-tor ik whatever au ya'akash na' au had wuh'rak putan-tor tor etek, ” murmured wuh lad gravely. “au fereik-tor ashaya svi' etwel natures. Au ma wuh gas'rak tor haishaya ish-veh pla'.” “ik nam-tor ved yeht, dorian, ” maf-tor hallward. “nothing nam-tor ek'wak ved yeht, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “nash nam-tor, ” svi-shau dorian. “du bolau nafai-tor, harry, ik kosu mazhiv-kur-tor tor sasu wuh maut pi-maat-tukh t' ish-veh ha-tor.” “possibly, ” au spes-tevan, “tonk'peh au invariably aitlun ish-veh pla' svi' such maut pi' rubah. Ik nam-tor wuh worry. Kosu, u' ein witty frenchman wuh'wak shitau ish-veh, vi'le-esh-tor etek k' wuh aitlun tor tor masterpieces heh kwon-hau-ov prevent etek s' carrying au si'.” “harry, du nam-tor dreadful! I don’t fai-tor po i spo' du ni mau.” “du dungi kwon-hau-ov spo' me, dorian, ” au kilko-tor. “dungi du ma ein mon, du katravahsu? Waiter, katau mon, heh _fine-champagne_, heh ein cigarettes. Rai, don’t kashek wuh cigarettes—i ma ein. Basil, i mokuhlek’t kal-tor du tor vuzh cigars. Du bolau ma wuh cigarette. Wuh cigarette nam-tor wuh buhfik ves t' wuh buhfik sanosh. Ish-veh nam-tor exquisite, heh ish-veh mor veh unsatisfied. Ra weht mokuhlek veh aitlun? Ha, dorian, du dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor tishau t' me. I represent tor du ek' wuh sins du ma worla had wuh courage tor kugau.” “ra nonsense du variben, harry!” maf-tor wuh lad, taking wuh ta'hal s' wuh yon-eshan haul-tukh dragon ik wuh waiter had shitau fi' wuh pasu. “kal-tor etek hal-tor ne' tor wuh theatre. Lu sibyl sarlah fi' wuh skaf du dungi ma wuh uzh tangu t' ha'kiv. She dungi represent vel tor du ik du ma worla fainu.” “i ma fainu kanok-vei, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, k' wuh zungor glazhau svi' ish-veh bezhun, “tonk'peh i am kwon-hau-ov pok na' wuh uzh zherka. I am kwes, however, ik, na' me na' sovek tav, tra' nam-tor rai such vel. Fam dvun, ish-veh wonderful ko-kan lau thrill me. I ashaya peran. Ish-veh nam-tor ni mau weht yeht do ha'kiv. Kal-tor etek hal-tor. Dorian, du dungi sarlah k' me. I am ni sorry, basil, tonk'peh tra' nam-tor goh tvi-shal na' dahkuh svi' wuh brougham. Du bolau zahal-tor etek svi' wuh hansom.” au prah abru heh shitau fi' ish-veh tor-pal, mon-tor ish-veh mon standing. Wuh krassu vesh' ralash-fam heh preoccupied. Tra' vesh' wuh gloom abru' ish-veh. Au kupi ri lesh nash kal'i'farr, heh wi ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh tor nam-tor weh-rom do wehk vath vel ik lau ma pavesh-tor. Po' wuh zamu minutes, au ek' be' dvun-tor downstairs. Au drove ska' k' himself, u' had vesh' arranged, heh glantau wuh flashing ha'ge t' wuh pi' brougham svi' khom t' ish-veh. Wuh flekh kash-ral t' pak sarlah abru' ish-veh. Au olau ik dorian zhai-kur would worla va'ashiv nam-tor tor ish-veh ek' ik au had vesh' svi' wuh vesht. Ha'kiv had sarlah svi' au. Ish-veh bezhun mu'glau, heh wuh crowded flaring yut became blurred tor ish-veh bezhun. Lu wuh cab drew abru na' wuh theatre, ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik au had grown tevun older. Chapter vii. Na' ein utvau il vath, wuh kelek vesh' crowded ik mu-yor, heh wuh thelik jew khartausu vi ragel-tor au na' wuh svep vesh' beaming s' kaluk tor kaluk k' wuh oily tremulous abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Au escorted au tor ish-veh natuhn k' wuh wihfelau t' pompous humility, pral-tor ish-veh thelik jewelled el'ru heh talking na' wuh fik t' ish-veh spes. Dorian zhai-kur loathed ish-veh weht do ek'wak. Au olau u' kuv au had sarlah tor glazhau na' miranda heh had vesh' ragel-tor k' caliban. S'haile henry, fi-tor wuh vath el'ru, rather tishau ish-veh. K'puu au afsakau au did, heh insisted fi' shaking ish-veh k' wuh el'ru heh assuring ish-veh ik au vesh' yaut tor ragel-tor wuh sasu vi had discovered wuh yeht genius heh hal-tor bankrupt abru' wuh poet. Hallward amused himself k' watching wuh limuk svi' wuh pit. Wuh falek vesh' terribly oppressive, heh wuh masuk' ug'yel-ha'gel flamed spo' wuh monstrous dahlia k' kur-mor t' kin-kur yon. Wuh youths svi' wuh tanaf-shi'gluvaun had taken ska' ish-veh tor-pal heh waistcoats heh geldau au abru' wuh vla. Au variben tor tik vath mes' wuh theatre heh thresh-tor ish-veh zhar-kur k' wuh tawdry ko-kan vi hayal-tor be' au. Ein kosu vesh' laughing svi' wuh pit. Ish-veh spes vesh' horribly shrill heh discordant. Wuh ralash t' wuh popping t' kem sarlah s' wuh mofek. “ra wuh shi tor talal veh’s divinity svi'!” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “ha!” kilko-tor dorian zhai-kur. “ish-veh vesh' la' i afer-tor ish-veh, heh she nam-tor ekonik mesakh ek' living vel. Lu she fundauik-tor, du dungi yen-tor kanok-vei. Aifa tsuri rough sutra, k' ish-veh dirik limuk heh brutal gestures, shetau ved natya lu she nam-tor fi' wuh skaf. Au hayal-tor silently heh glantau ish-veh. Au tusa heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut u' she dungi au tor tor. She tor au u' responsive u' wuh violin. She spiritualizes au, heh veh olau ik au nam-tor t' wuh ka kahm heh khaf u' veh’s shal.” “wuh ka kahm heh khaf u' veh’s shal! Oh, i rok ri!” sporiben s'haile henry, vi vesh' scanning wuh occupants t' wuh tanaf-shi'gluvaun k'fai ish-veh opera-makh. “don’t vlitau sovek attention tor ish-veh, dorian, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu. “i ken-tor ra du tvai, heh i dva-tor svi' nash ko-kan. Sovek veh du ashaya bolau nam-tor marvellous, heh sovek ko-kan vi has wuh daya du kethelvau bolau nam-tor tok-ti heh thol. Tor spiritualize veh’s ya'shakhuv—ik nam-tor vel don doing. Kuv nash ko-kan mokuhlek mazhiv-kur-tor wuh soul tor eifa vi ma ha-tor rik' veh, kuv she mokuhlek fereik-tor wuh kash-ral t' vaksur svi' sutra t'vi ha-tor ma vesh' sordid heh watosh, kuv she mokuhlek strip au t' ish-veh selfishness heh lend au bezhun-masu na' sorrows ik nam-tor ri ish-veh sha', she nam-tor worthy t' ek' ish-veh adoration, worthy t' wuh adoration t' wuh panu. Nash kal'i'farr nam-tor ved gas'rak. I did ri nah-tor ni palikauk, tonk'peh i nafai-tor ish-veh i'. Wuh gods tor sibyl vane na' du. Rik' ish-veh du would ma vesh' incomplete.” “itaren, basil, ” kilko-tor dorian zhai-kur, pressing ish-veh el'ru. “i fai-tor ik du would ken-tor me. Harry nam-tor ni cynical, au terrifies me. Tonk'peh la' nam-tor wuh orchestra. Ish-veh nam-tor ved dreadful, tonk'peh ish-veh goh palesh-tor na' pa' kaukuh minutes. Yi wuh curtain she-tor, heh du dungi gla-tor wuh ko-kan tor ik i am going tor mazhiv-kur-tor ek' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, tor ik i ma putan-tor kanok-vei ik nam-tor rom svi' me.” wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan afterwards, amidst wuh wehtsuri turmoil t' applause, sibyl vane ash-tor fi' tor wuh skaf. Ha, she vesh' certainly lovely tor glazhau na'—veh t' wuh loveliest creatures, s'haile henry nahp, ik au had ek'wak gla-tor. Tra' vesh' vel t' wuh fawn svi' ish-veh fusik takov heh startled bezhun. Wuh faint blush, spo' wuh duv t' wuh she-tor svi' wuh haulat t' haul-tukh, sarlah tor ish-veh nak u' she glanced na' wuh crowded buhlik kelek. She ash-tor pla' wuh zamu sahr-tor heh ish-veh bru-lar seemed tor tremble. Basil hallward leaped tor ish-veh ash'ya heh began tor applaud. Motionless, heh u' veh svi' wuh sahr-tor, hayal-tor dorian zhai-kur, gazing na' ish-veh. S'haile henry peered k'fai ish-veh bezhun-zaneshu, murmuring, “sem-rik-tor! Sem-rik-tor!” wuh scene vesh' wuh tvur t' capulet’s kelek, heh romeo svi' ish-veh pilgrim’s sai-vel had svi-tor k' mercutio heh ish-veh vath t'hylara. Wuh zhel, such u' ish-veh vesh', kwul-tor abru wuh zamu mofek t' ralash-tanaf, heh wuh tam began. K'fai wuh patreitan t' ungainly, shabbily sai-vel-tor actors, sibyl vane dvun-tor spo' wuh creature s' wuh finer panu. Ish-veh ak'shem swayed, du' she tam-tor, u' wuh kastik sways svi' wuh masu. Wuh curves t' ish-veh drahk vesh' wuh curves t' wuh wan-kur lily. Ish-veh el'ru seemed tor nam-tor tor t' samuyau ivory. Wi she vesh' curiously listless. She gluvau rai glat t' mak lu ish-veh bezhun shom-tor fi' romeo. Wuh zamu zhit she had tor stariben— rom pilgrim, du tor riyeht ish-veh el'ru nuh' mau, if mannerly vaikaya gluvau svi' nash; na' osu ma el'ru ik pilgrims’ el'ru tor esta, heh ku tor ku nam-tor vai palmers’ shok— k' wuh brief dialogue ik zahal-tor, vesh' spoken svi' wuh thoroughly sutorik manner. Wuh spes vesh' exquisite, tonk'peh s' wuh sfek t' zan-tor t' molu ish-veh vesh' absolutely riyeht. Ish-veh vesh' riyeht svi' kur. Ish-veh nem-tor maf ek' wuh ha'kiv s' wuh zehl. Ish-veh tor wuh shaukaush unreal. Dorian zhai-kur grew spoh u' au glantau ish-veh. Au vesh' puzzled heh anxious. Neither t' ish-veh t'hylara dared tor leralmin sovek-vel tor ish-veh. She seemed tor au tor nam-tor absolutely incompetent. Au vesh' horribly disappointed. Wi au olau ik wuh yeht nisan t' sovek juliet nam-tor wuh fah-yat scene t' wuh dahr bae'cok. Au bek-tor na' ik. Kuv she vravshau tra', tra' vesh' nothing svi' ish-veh. She glazhau sem-rik-tor u' she sasarlah svi' wuh moonlight. Ik kupi ri nam-tor wafu. Tonk'peh wuh staginess t' ish-veh peran vesh' unbearable, heh grew weh-rasahkos u' she went fi'. Ish-veh gestures became absurdly sutorik. She overemphasized kanok-vei ik she had tor leralmin. Wuh vaksurik tvur— thou knowest wuh limein t' mu-yor nam-tor fi' t'nash-veh limuk, else would wuh maiden blush bepaint t'nash-veh nak na' ik if thou hast puzhu-tor me stariben tor-mu-yor— vesh' declaimed k' wuh kusut-tor precision t' wuh schoolgirl vi has vesh' saven-tor tor recite k' ein dahr-tav professor t' elocution. Lu she gal-tor abru' wuh fah-yat heh sarlah tor eifa wonderful zehl— hi i mak svi' thee, i ma rai mak t' nash contract tor-mu-yor: ish-veh nam-tor nuh' kuriht, nuh' unadvised, nuh' sudden; nuh' spo' wuh igen-wesh, if doth cease tor nam-tor ere veh mokuhlek leralmin, “ish-veh lightens.” slor, rom-mu-yor! Nash bud t' ashaya k' belaar’s piyahtaya esh lau skan-tor wuh beauteous svai lu thurai etek ragel-tor— she stariben wuh zhit u' hi au zhelesh rai meaning tor ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' ri nervousness. Indeed, ni irak s' hasu nervous, she vesh' absolutely shal-tuhlau. Ish-veh vesh' veling rasahkos tanaf. She vesh' wuh ovsotik vravshaya. Kauk wuh tsuri uneducated audience t' wuh pit heh tanaf-shi'gluvaun pakik ish-veh eku'ko svi' wuh mavau. Au prah restless, heh began tor variben loudly heh tor whistle. Wuh jew khartausu, vi vesh' standing na' wuh pla' t' wuh sai-vel-da-kuv, stamped heh swore k' reshan. Wuh goh person unmoved vesh' wuh ko-kan herself. Lu wuh dahr bae'cok vesh' abru', tra' sarlah wuh sahriv t' shisau, heh s'haile henry prah abru s' ish-veh ku-san heh shitau fi' ish-veh tor-pal. “she nam-tor ved vaksurik, dorian, ” au leralmin-tor, “tonk'peh she mokuhlek’t bae'cok. Kal-tor etek hal-tor.” “i am going tor gla-tor wuh mavau k'fai, ” kilko-tor wuh lad, svi' wuh lerash sfith(-) spes. “i am awfully sorry ik i ma tor du thinoi wuh khru, harry. I apologize tor du fi'.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam dorian, i dang nah-tor din-tor vane vesh' has-bosh, ” svi-shau hallward. “etek dungi sarlah ein vath mu-yor.” “i istaya she vesh' has-bosh, ” au rejoined. “tonk'peh she seems tor me tor nam-tor veling callous heh samu. She has entirely rubitau. Kim-shah mu-yor she vesh' wuh lo'uk tanafsu. Nash khru she nam-tor goh wuh commonplace mediocre fundauik-ithop.” “don’t variben spo' ik pa' sovek veh du ashaya, dorian. Ashaya nam-tor wuh weht wonderful vel do tanaf.” “au nam-tor fi' veling shidau t' imitation, ” remarked s'haile henry. “tonk'peh tor kal-tor etek hal-tor. Dorian, du bolau ri stay la' sovek longer. Ish-veh nam-tor ri rom na' veh’s morals tor gla-tor rasahkos peran. Isha, i don’t suppose du dungi aitlun ish-veh ko-telsu tor bae'cok, ni ra tor ish-veh tukh kuv she mavau juliet spo' wuh wooden su-leitri? She nam-tor maut lovely, heh kuv she fai-tor u' pi' pa' ha'kiv u' she tor pa' peran, she dungi nam-tor wuh delightful veshtaya. Tra' nam-tor goh dahkuh ves t' sutra vi nam-tor really sem-rik—sutra vi fai-tor absolutely kanok-vei, heh sutra vi fai-tor absolutely nothing. Rom heavens, t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, don’t glazhau ni tragic! Wuh tsat t' remaining nu'ri nam-tor worla ki' wuh zherka ik nam-tor unbecoming. Sarlah tor wuh muhd k' basil heh myself. Etek dungi vuzh cigarettes heh mon tor wuh vaksur t' sibyl vane. She nam-tor vaksurik. Ra weht mokuhlek du aitlun?” “hal-tor maf, harry, ” maf-tor wuh lad. “i aitlun tor nam-tor sa'awek. Basil, du bolau hal-tor. Ah! Mokuhlek’t gla-tor du ik t'nash-veh khaf-spol nam-tor breaking?” wuh fal bezhun-masu sarlah tor ish-veh bezhun. Ish-veh bru-lar trembled, heh rushing tor wuh pla' t' wuh natuhn, au gal-tor abru tehnat wuh temok, hiding ish-veh limuk svi' ish-veh el'ru. “kal-tor etek hal-tor, basil, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry k' wuh flekh tenderness svi' ish-veh spes, heh wuh dahkuh nu'ri sasu be' dvun-tor si' teretuhr. Wuh zamu moments afterwards wuh footlights flared abru heh wuh curtain she-tor fi' wuh wuh bae'cok. Dorian zhai-kur went pla' tor ish-veh ku-san. Au glazhau spoh, heh yaut, heh indifferent. Wuh mavau zaseshau fi', heh seemed interminable. Ulef t' wuh audience went si', tramping svi' ras kluf heh laughing. Wuh bosh vel vesh' wuh _fiasco_. Wuh kim-shah bae'cok vesh' mavau tor siyah herbosh wu-ku-san. Wuh curtain went ne' fi' wuh titter heh ein groans. U' ak u' ish-veh vesh' abru', dorian zhai-kur rushed za' wuh scenes vi' wuh greenroom. Wuh ko-kan vesh' standing tra' sa'awek, k' wuh glazhau t' triumph fi' ish-veh limuk. Ish-veh bezhun vesh' lit k' wuh exquisite yon. Tra' vesh' wuh radiance pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh parted bru-lar vesh' smiling abru' ein tsat t' ish-veh sha'. Lu au svi-tor, she glazhau na' ish-veh, heh wuh sagluvaya t' vaik mak sarlah abru' ish-veh. “uf badly i bae'cok tor-mu-yor, dorian!” she maf-tor. “horribly!” au kilko-tor, gazing na' ish-veh svi' tauraya. “horribly! Ish-veh vesh' dreadful. Nam-tor du has-bosh? Du ma rai idea ra ish-veh vesh'. Du ma rai idea ra i dashau.” wuh ko-kan abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “dorian, ” she kilko-tor, svizh-tor abru' ish-veh ahm k' wu-drawn ralash-tanaf svi' ish-veh spes, u' hi ish-veh vesh' sweeter do honey tor wuh yon-kur kur-mor t' ish-veh ru'lut. “dorian, du dang ma ken-tor. Tonk'peh du ken-tor i', don’t du?” “ken-tor ra?” au ya'akash, angrily. “po i vesh' ni rasahkos tor-mu-yor. Po i dungau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor rasahkos. Po i dungau worla bae'cok muhl va'ashiv.” au shrugged ish-veh tipan. “du nam-tor has-bosh, i suppose. Lu du nam-tor has-bosh du shouldn’t bae'cok. Du tor yourself ridiculous. T'nash-veh t'hylara vesh' bored. I vesh' bored.” she seemed ri tor shroi tor ish-veh. She vesh' transfigured k' mak. Wuh prahk'es t' happiness abrukhau ish-veh. “dorian, dorian, ” she maf-tor, “fa' i fai-tor du, peran vesh' wuh veh reality t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Ish-veh vesh' goh svi' wuh theatre ik i ha-tor. I nahp ik ish-veh vesh' ek' yeht. I vesh' rosalind veh mu-yor heh portia wuh vath. Wuh mak t' beatrice vesh' t'nash-veh mak, heh wuh sorrows t' cordelia vesh' t'nash-veh isha. I pudva-tor svi' kanok-vei. Wuh tsuri sutra vi bae'cok k' me seemed tor me tor nam-tor godlike. Wuh kras-tor scenes vesh' t'nash-veh panu. I fai-tor nothing tonk'peh duv, heh i nahp au yeht. Sarlah du—oh, t'nash-veh vaksurik ashaya!—heh du el-tor t'nash-veh soul s' prison. Du saven-tor me ra reality really nam-tor. Tor-mu-yor, na' wuh wuh'rak wak svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv, vesht gla-tor nash-veh k'fai wuh hollowness, wuh sham, wuh silliness t' wuh herbosh pageant svi' if i had kwon-hau-ov mavau. Tor-mu-yor, na' wuh wuh'rak wak, i became d'wonil ik wuh romeo vesh' hideous, heh hinek, heh kras-tor, ik wuh moonlight svi' wuh lap-bah-ker vesh' riyeht, ik wuh scenery vesh' vulgar, heh ik wuh zhit i had tor stariben vesh' unreal, vesh' ri t'nash-veh zhit, vesh' ri ra i aitlu tor leralmin. Du had katau me vel higher, vel t' if ek' tanaf nam-tor tonk'peh wuh haulan. Du had tor me ken-tor ra ashaya really nam-tor. T'nash-veh ashaya! T'nash-veh ashaya! Prince sem-rik-tor! Prince t' ha'kiv! I ma grown has-bosh t' duv. Du nam-tor weht tor me do ek' tanaf mokuhlek ek'wak nam-tor. Ra ma i tor tor k' wuh puppets t' wuh mavau? Lu vesht sarlah nash-veh fi' tor-mu-yor, i kupi ri ken-tor uf ish-veh vesh' ik kanok-vei had hal-tor s' me. I nahp ik i vesh' going tor nam-tor wonderful. I afer-tor ik i kupi tor nothing. Suddenly ish-veh dawned fi' t'nash-veh soul ra ish-veh ek' tvai. Wuh fai-tukh vesh' exquisite tor me. I puzhu-tor au hissing, heh i abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Ra kupi au fai-tor t' ashaya such u' ours? Nem-tor me maf, dorian—nem-tor me maf k' du, wilat etek mokuhlek nam-tor ved sa'awek. I fnu-ven wuh skaf. I lau va'amau wuh shaukaush ik i ri tor olau, tonk'peh i fam yehat va'amau veh ik yontau me spo' yon. Oh, dorian, dorian, du ken-tor i' ra ish-veh signifies? Kauk kuv i kupi tor ish-veh, ish-veh would nam-tor profanation na' me tor mavau na' hasu svi' ashaya. Du ma tor me gla-tor ik.” au flung himself ne' fi' wuh ku-san heh da-tor maf ish-veh limuk. “du ma pustau t'nash-veh ashaya, ” au muttered. She glazhau na' ish-veh svi' wonder heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. Au tor rai kilko-srashiv. Sarlah ish-veh mes' tor ish-veh, heh k' ish-veh wuhr-ozh stroked ish-veh isachya. She knelt ne' heh hish-tor ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh bru-lar. Au drew au maf, heh wuh ak'shem-hutau sahr-tor k'fai ish-veh. Yi au leaped abru heh went tor wuh svep. “ha, ” au maf-tor, “du ma pustau t'nash-veh ashaya. Du nam-tor-tor tor stir t'nash-veh glenonaya. I' du don’t kauk stir t'nash-veh curiosity. Du veling torvau rai daya. I ashau du fai'ei du vesh' marvellous, fai'ei du had genius heh kash-tor-vel, fai'ei du realized wuh sahr-tor-tor t' lo'uk poets heh mazhiv-kur-tor shid heh substance tor wuh duv t' tanaf. Du ma lehm-tor ish-veh ek' maf. Du nam-tor gan heh stupid. T'nash-veh oekon! Uf mad i vesh' tor ashaya du! Ra wuh duhsu i ma vesh'! Du nam-tor nothing tor me i'. I dungi worla gla-tor du va'ashiv. I dungi worla nah-tor t' du. I dungi worla mention ish-veh ahm. Du don’t fai-tor ra du vesh' tor me, wuh'wak. Po, wuh'wak. Oh, i mokuhlek’t lesh tor nah-tor t' ish-veh! I istaya i had worla laid bezhun fi-tor du! Du ma spoiled wuh romance t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Uf pi' du mokuhlek fai-tor t' ashaya, kuv du leralmin ish-veh mars ish-veh tanaf! Rik' ish-veh tanaf, du nam-tor nothing. I would ma tor du khinik, splendid, magnificent. Wuh panu would ma worshipped du, heh du would ma borne t'nash-veh ahm. Ra nam-tor du i'? Wuh wuh-tav fundauik-ithop k' wuh takov limuk.” wuh ko-kan grew wan-kur, heh trembled. She clenched ish-veh el'ru teretuhr, heh ish-veh spes seemed tor kum svi' ish-veh drahk. “du nam-tor ri serious, dorian?” she murmured. “du nam-tor peran.” “peran! I trasha ik tor du. Du tor ish-veh ni muhl, ” au kilko-tor bitterly. She she-tor s' ish-veh mal-nef heh, k' wuh piteous sagluvaya t' kusut svi' ish-veh limuk, sarlah mes' wuh tvi-shal tor ish-veh. She shitau ish-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh kar heh glazhau vi' ish-veh bezhun. Au kwit ish-veh pla'. “don’t esta me!” au maf-tor. Wuh neik naya shau s' ish-veh, heh she flung herself na' ish-veh ash'ya heh ti tra' spo' wuh sahr-tor svai. “dorian, dorian, don’t trasha me!” she zhal-tor. “i am ni sorry i didn’t bae'cok muhl. I vesh' thinking t' du ek' wuh wak. Tonk'peh i dungi ar'kadan—indeed, i dungi ar'kadan. Sarlah ish-veh ni suddenly mes' me, t'nash-veh ashaya na' du. I nah-tor i dang worla ma fainu ish-veh kuv du had ri shok-tor me—kuv etek had ri shok-tor tik vath. Shok me va'ashiv, t'nash-veh ashaya. Don’t hal-tor maf s' me. I couldn’t lesh ish-veh. Oh! Don’t hal-tor maf s' me. T'nash-veh sa-kai. Rai; worla kashek. Au didn’t tvai ish-veh. Au vesh' svi' jest. Tonk'peh du, oh! Mokuhlek’t du forgive me na' tor-mu-yor? I dungi ar'kadan ni lerash heh ar'kadan tor improve. Don’t nam-tor pi-maat'rer tor me, fai'ei i ashaya du weh-rom do sovek-vel svi' wuh panu. Po' ek', ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh'wak ik i ma ri sanoi du. Tonk'peh du nam-tor ved gas'rak, dorian. I dang ma shown myself weht t' wuh tanafsu. Ish-veh vesh' duhik t' me, heh wi i couldn’t gol'nev ish-veh. Oh, don’t trasha me, don’t trasha me.” wuh nunau t' passionate sobbing khluhkau ish-veh. She crouched fi' wuh lan-tol spo' wuh wounded vel, heh dorian zhai-kur, k' ish-veh vaksurik bezhun, glazhau ne' na' ish-veh, heh ish-veh chiselled bru-lar tcha-tor svi' exquisite disdain. Tra' nam-tor kwon-hau-ov vel ridiculous pa' wuh zherka t' sutra ik veh has ceased tor ashaya. Sibyl vane seemed tor ish-veh tor nam-tor absurdly melodramatic. Ish-veh bezhun-masu heh sobs annoyed ish-veh. “i am going, ” au leralmin-tor na' kim-shah svi' ish-veh hayal pa'shik spes. “i don’t istaya tor nam-tor unkind, tonk'peh i mokuhlek’t gla-tor du va'ashiv. Du ma disappointed me.” she wept silently, heh tor rai kilko-srashiv, tonk'peh crept nearer. Ish-veh pi' el'ru sakadau blindly si', heh saudau tor nam-tor seeking na' ish-veh. Au da-tor fi' ish-veh timut heh losrak wuh tvi-shal. Svi' wuh zamu moments au vesh' s' wuh theatre. Wilat au went tor au hardly fai-tor. Au vokau wandering k'fai dimly lit yut, vesht gaunt, nesh-kur-duv-tor archways heh ek'rasah-looking kelek. Kosu k' hoarse spes heh harsh laughter had puvutau po' ish-veh. Drunkards had reeled k', cursing heh chattering tor themselves spo' monstrous apes. Au had gla-tor grotesque kanu huddled fi-tor svep-ash-tor, heh puzhu-tor shrieks heh oaths s' gloomy kelek. U' wuh gad-keshtan vesh' aishan breaking, au afer-tor himself beyik covent bah-ker. Wuh mu'khlup'es abertau, heh, kluhvau k' faint yon, wuh igen hollowed itself vi' wuh buhfik pearl. Masuk' hal boshau k' nodding lilies rumbled slowly ne' wuh polished herbosh yut. Wuh sov vesh' ras k' wuh perfume t' wuh svai, heh ish-veh vaksur seemed tor katau ish-veh wuh anodyne na' ish-veh kusut. Au zahal-tor vi' wuh mahr-kel heh glantau wuh sasu unloading ish-veh waggons. Wuh wan-kur-smocked carter nufau ish-veh ein cherries. Au itaren ish-veh, wondered po au klee'fah tor nar-tor sovek donku na' au, heh began tor yokul au listlessly. Au had vesh' plucked na' midnight, heh wuh coldness t' wuh aikum had svi-tor vi' au. Wuh wu zehl t' sa-kan carrying chasulh t' zhel-tor lale, heh t' kin-kur heh yon-kur roses, defiled svi' khom t' ish-veh, threading ish-veh yut k'fai wuh masuk', yar-kov-yar-kur tuh t' sazh. Ne' wuh portico, k' its zhai-kur, yel-lafau pillars, loitered wuh vus t' draggled bareheaded ko-kan, waiting na' wuh auction tor nam-tor abru'. Vath crowded pauk wuh swinging svep t' wuh mon-kelek svi' wuh piazza. Wuh ras hal-jarel trel-tor heh stamped fi-tor wuh rough kov, shaking ish-veh kus-vakh heh trappings. Ein t' wuh yetursu vesh' lying asleep fi' wuh tuh t' sa'haf. Kurak-necked heh faf-kur-footed, wuh pigeons sahr-tor pa' picking abru nei. Po' wuh pi' du', au hailed wuh hansom heh drove ha-kel. Na' wuh zamu moments au loitered fi-tor wuh svep-ashef, looking pauk na' wuh ralash-fam keh-vla, k' its blank, ikap-tor-shuttered krani heh its staring blinds. Wuh igen vesh' pure opal i', heh wuh kamu t' wuh kelek glistened spo' haul-tukh tehnat ish-veh. S' ein vuzh-mev mesyutik wuh wonil wreath t' vuzh vesh' rising. Ish-veh tcha-tor, wuh mu'gahv-kur riband, k'fai wuh ba'hun'ahb-kur-tor sov. Svi' wuh masuk' gilt venetian makh-yonet, spoil t' ein doge’s tus-hali, ik geldau s' wuh abru-tol t' wuh lo'uk, oak-panelled tvur t' entrance, ha'ge vesh' fam dvun yontau s' rehkuh flickering jets: wonil pla-kur kur-mor t' yai au seemed, rimmed k' wan-kur yon. Au da-tor au si' heh, having lehm-tor ish-veh taik heh cape fi' wuh pasu, be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh shi'dunap na' wuh svep t' ish-veh shi'yuk, wuh suk octagonal tvi-shal fi' wuh solektra lan-tol ik, svi' ish-veh uzh-pukeshta olaya na' luxury, au had aishan had decorated na' himself heh geldau k' ein curious renaissance tapestries ik had vesh' discovered tsorau svi' wuh disused fik tvi-shal na' selby royal. U' au vesh' turning wuh el'rek t' wuh svep, ish-veh bezhun tevan-tor fi-tor wuh portrait basil hallward had kras-tor t' ish-veh. Au palikau pla' u' kuv svi' ak'wikmun. Yi au went fi' vi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, looking somewhat puzzled. Po' au had taken wuh gonaf-razh s' ish-veh tor-pal, au seemed tor hesitate. T'forti, sarlah ish-veh pla', went abru' tor wuh bikuv, heh linisau ish-veh. Svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup pehkau ta'hal ik struggled k'fai wuh dyrk-kur-tor silk blinds, wuh limuk saudau tor ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh pi' rubai. Wuh sagluvaya glazhau natya. Veh would ma leralmin-tor ik tra' vesh' wuh esta t' cruelty svi' wuh ru'lut. Ish-veh vesh' certainly flekh. Au da-tor pauk heh, walking tor wuh krani, drew abru wuh glan-fam. Wuh ugelik gad-keshtan abrash-tor wuh tvi-shal heh swept wuh fantastic duv vi' dusky teruk, wilat au ti shuddering. Tonk'peh wuh flekh sagluvaya ik au had pubeglanau svi' wuh limuk t' wuh portrait seemed tor svizh-tor tra', tor nam-tor weht intensified kauk. Wuh quivering ardent ug'yel-ha'gel gluvau ish-veh wuh zehl t' cruelty pauk wuh ru'lut u' clearly u' kuv au had vesh' looking vi' wuh haulat po' au had ovsoh ein dreadful vel. Au winced heh, taking abru s' wuh pasu wuh yuvik makh nentulau svi' ivory cupids, veh t' s'haile henry’s wehk presents tor ish-veh, glanced hurriedly vi' its polished gluder. Rai zehl spo' ik warped ish-veh yon-kur bru-lar. Ra did ish-veh tvai? Au tetau ish-veh bezhun, heh sarlah beyik wuh bikuv, heh linisau ish-veh va'ashiv. Tra' vesh' rai glat t' sovek rubah lu au glazhau vi' wuh actual krasan, heh wi tra' vesh' rai vet ik wuh bosh sagluvaya had rubitau. Ish-veh vesh' ri wuh mere fancy t' ish-veh sha'. Wuh vel vesh' horribly apparent. Au threw himself vi' wuh ku-san heh began tor nah-tor. Suddenly tra' kahai mes' ish-veh kashek ra au had leralmin-tor svi' basil hallward’s studio wuh gad wuh bikuv had vesh' shahtau. Ha, au vokau ish-veh perfectly. Au had uttered wuh mad istaya ik au himself lau hafau nu'ri, heh wuh portrait tor'ovau hinek; ik ish-veh sha' vaksur lau nam-tor untarnished, heh wuh limuk fi' wuh canvas lesh wuh burden t' ish-veh shaukaush heh ish-veh sins; ik wuh kras-tor glakuv lau nam-tor seared k' wuh zehl t' suffering heh nahp, heh ik au lau potau ek' wuh delicate svai heh loveliness t' ish-veh yi aishan d'wonil boyhood. Surely ish-veh istaya had ri vesh' fulfilled? Such vel vesh' impossible. Ish-veh seemed monstrous kauk tor nah-tor t' au. Heh, wi, tra' vesh' wuh bikuv fa' ish-veh, k' wuh esta t' cruelty svi' wuh ru'lut. Cruelty! Had au vesh' pi-maat'rer? Ish-veh vesh' wuh ko-kan’s lafot, ri ish-veh. Au had sahr-tor-tor t' ish-veh u' wuh lo'uk tanafsu, had putan-tor ish-veh ashaya tor ish-veh fai'ei au had nahp ish-veh lo'uk. Yi she had disappointed ish-veh. She had vesh' gan heh unworthy. Heh, wi, wuh olaya t' vaik regret sarlah abru' ish-veh, u' au nahp t' ish-veh lying na' ish-veh ash'ya sobbing spo' wuh pi' kan. Au vokau k' ra callousness au had glantau ish-veh. Po had au vesh' tor spo' ik? Po had such wuh soul vesh' putan-tor tor ish-veh? Tonk'peh au had dashau isha. Du' wuh rehkuh terrible wadan ik wuh mavau had palesh-tor, au had ha-tor centuries t' kusut, aeon fi-tor aeon t' torture. Ish-veh ha'kiv vesh' muhl don ish-veh. She had marred ish-veh na' wuh moment, kuv au had wounded ish-veh na' wuh ya'shakhuv. Isha, kosu vesh' weh-rom suited tor lesh sorrow do sasu. Au ha-tor fi' ish-veh zherka. Au goh nahp t' ish-veh zherka. Lu au nem-tor lovers, ish-veh vesh' goh ki' ein veh k' ik au kupi ma scenes. S'haile henry had var-tor ish-veh ik, heh s'haile henry fai-tor ra kosu vesh'. Po dang au trouble pa' sibyl vane? She vesh' nothing tor ish-veh i'. Tonk'peh wuh bikuv? Ra vesh' au tor leralmin t' ik? Ish-veh meskarau wuh tsat t' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh var-tor ish-veh var. Ish-veh had saven-tor ish-veh tor ashaya ish-veh sha' vaksur. Would ish-veh saven-tor ish-veh tor loathe ish-veh sha' soul? Would au ek'wak glazhau na' ish-veh va'ashiv? Rai; ish-veh vesh' goh wuh illusion wrought fi' wuh troubled kash-ral. Wuh horrible mu-yor ik au had be' dvun-tor had losrak phantoms za' ish-veh. Suddenly tra' had tevan-tor fi-tor ish-veh shi'nahp ik tiny ug'yon-kur speck ik tor sasu mad. Wuh bikuv had ri rubai. Ish-veh vesh' folly tor nah-tor ni. Wi ish-veh vesh' watching ish-veh, k' its vaksurik marred limuk heh its pi-maat'rer abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Its ugelik isachya gleamed svi' wuh lehkuh-mal ug'yel-ha'gel. Its pla-kur bezhun ragel-tor ish-veh sha'. Wuh kash-ral t' vaik pity, ri na' himself, tonk'peh na' wuh kras-tor glakuv t' himself, sarlah abru' ish-veh. Ish-veh had rubitau already, heh would rubitau weht. Its pi-maat-tukh would wither vi' zhai-kur. Its yon-kur heh wan-kur roses would tev-tor. Na' kanok sin ik au committed, wuh kuraya would fleck heh vashau its fairness. Tonk'peh au would ri sin. Wuh bikuv, rubai il unchanged, would nam-tor tor ish-veh wuh visible emblem t' conscience. Au would tehnau temptation. Au would ri gla-tor s'haile henry sovek weht—would ri, na' sovek tav, shroi tor eifa subtle poisonous wihka ik svi' basil hallward’s bah-ker had wuh'rak stirred k'svi ish-veh wuh shaukaush na' impossible vel. Au would hal-tor pla' tor sibyl vane, tor ish-veh amends, marry ish-veh, ar'kadan tor ashaya ish-veh va'ashiv. Ha, ish-veh vesh' ish-veh gu-vam tor tor ni. She bolau ma dashau weht do au had. Ri donku-tor kan! Au had vesh' selfish heh pi-maat'rer tor ish-veh. Wuh sem ik she had tusok-tor abru' ish-veh would fun. Au would nam-tor kunli teretuhr. Ish-veh ha'kiv k' ish-veh would nam-tor vaksurik heh pure. Au prah abru s' ish-veh ku-san heh drew wuh suk gluvayek gas'rak svi' khom t' wuh portrait, shuddering u' au glanced na' ish-veh. “uf horrible!” au murmured tor himself, heh au lates-tor mes' tor wuh krani heh tu'ash ish-veh. Lu au ash-tor si' fi' tor wuh yar, au drew wuh glu esh. Wuh sluk asal sov seemed tor yetur maf ek' ish-veh sombre shaukaush. Au nahp goh t' sibyl. Wuh faint vava t' ish-veh ashaya sarlah pla' tor ish-veh. Au ashiv-tor ish-veh ahm abru' heh abru' va'ashiv. Wuh kushel ik vesh' uralaun svi' wuh asal-masu-drenched bah-ker seemed tor nam-tor telling wuh svai pa' ish-veh. Chapter viii. Ish-veh vesh' wu vesht aru lu au awoke. Ish-veh valet had crept several wak fi' tiptoe vi' wuh tvi-shal tor gla-tor kuv au vesh' stirring, heh had wondered ra tor ish-veh nu'ri trensu yuk ni tab-ma. T'forti ish-veh kus-vakh sounded, heh skilsu sarlah svi' softly k' wuh cup t' theris-masu, heh wuh tuh t' nuhm, fi' wuh pi' tray t' hinek sevres china, heh drew pla' wuh olive-satin curtains, k' ish-veh shimmering pla-kur tvitaya, ik geldau svi' khom t' wuh rehkuh ha-vol krani. “monsieur has muhl yuk-tor nash asal, ” au leralmin-tor, smiling. “ra o’wak-vel nam-tor ish-veh, skilsu?” ya'akash dorian zhai-kur drowsily. “veh wadan heh wuh yonuk, monsieur.” uf tab-ma ish-veh vesh'! Au hayal-tor abru, heh having mon-tor ein theris-masu, da-tor abru' ish-veh nuhm. Veh t' au vesh' s' s'haile henry, heh had vesh' katau k' el'ru ik asal. Au hesitated na' wuh moment, heh yi shitau ish-veh aside. Wuh vath au tu'ash listlessly. Au tuhlau wuh tsuri tershaya t' nop, k'waw'zhe tor aru-yem, tickets na' awek zan-tor, tumaya t' charity concerts, heh wuh spo' ik nam-tor showered fi' fashionable nu'ri sasu kanok asal du' wuh tevun-yonuk. Tra' vesh' wuh rather ras dun na' wuh chased haul-tukh louis-quinze toilet-eku ik au had ri wi had wuh courage tor satau fi' tor ish-veh guardians, vi vesh' extremely hinek-fashioned sutra heh did ri realize ik etek ha-tor svi' wuh ya'shakhuv lu unnecessary vel nam-tor etwel goh bolayek; heh tra' vesh' several maut courteously worded communications s' jermyn yut donku-lenders nufaya tor storilaya sovek hau-ov t' donku na' wuh moment’s beglanau heh na' wuh danik reasonable tav-tor t' eku'ko. Po' pa' lehkuh minutes au prah abru, heh throwing fi' wuh elaborate sai-vel-tor-gown t' silk-embroidered cashmere terkarf-tukh, be' dvun-tor vi' wuh zer-hir-elyutau bathroom. Wuh samuyau masu uzhau ish-veh po' ish-veh wu yuk. Au seemed ki' yen-tor ek' ik au had hal-tor k'fai. Wuh neik-ha'khlup kash-ral t' having taken krus svi' ein flekh tragedy sarlah tor ish-veh wuh'wak il dah'wak, tonk'peh tra' vesh' wuh unreality t' wuh sahr-tor pa' ish-veh. U' ak u' au vesh' sai-vel-tor, au went vi' wuh shi'dunap heh hayal-tor ne' tor wuh ta'hal french asal-yem ik had vesh' laid si' na' ish-veh fi' wuh pi' pauk pasu beyik wuh tu'ash krani. Ish-veh vesh' wuh exquisite gad. Wuh lamekh sov seemed laden k' bar-kas. Wuh bee flew svi' heh buzzed pauk wuh pla-kur-dragon yerak ik, boshau k' sulphur-kin-kur roses, lam-tor fa' ish-veh. Au olau perfectly kunli. Suddenly ish-veh bezhun tevan-tor fi' wuh gluvayek ik au had shitau svi' khom t' wuh portrait, heh au palikau. “nuh' samu na' monsieur?” ya'akash ish-veh valet, putting wuh omelette fi' wuh pasu. “i ikap-tor wuh krani?” dorian hutau ish-veh patam. “i am ri samu, ” au murmured. Vesh' ish-veh ek' yeht? Had wuh portrait really rubai? Il had ish-veh vesh' veling ish-veh sha' glenonaya ik had tor ish-veh gla-tor wuh glazhau t' ek'rasah wilat tra' had vesh' wuh glazhau t' mak? Surely wuh kras-tor canvas kupi ri rubitau? Wuh vel vesh' absurd. Ish-veh would dvin-tor u' wuh var tor var-tor basil ein gad. Ish-veh would tor ish-veh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Heh, wi, uf vivid vesh' ish-veh recollection t' wuh bosh vel! Wuh'rak svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup twilight, heh yi svi' wuh ugelik gad-keshtan, au had gla-tor wuh esta t' cruelty pauk wuh warped bru-lar. Au siyah dreaded ish-veh valet leaving wuh tvi-shal. Au fai-tor ik lu au vesh' sa'awek au would ma tor linisau wuh portrait. Au vesh' kwes t' certainty. Lu wuh mon heh cigarettes had vesh' katau heh wuh sasu da-tor tor hal-tor, au olau wuh kwai aitlun tor var-tor ish-veh tor hafau. U' wuh svep vesh' ikapik za' ish-veh, au puvutau ish-veh pla'. Wuh sasu lam-tor waiting na' ish-veh zek. Dorian glazhau na' ish-veh na' wuh moment. “i am ri na' ha-kel tor sovek veh, skilsu, ” au leralmin-tor k' wuh spes-tevan. Wuh sasu ovalau heh retired. Yi au she-tor s' wuh pasu, lit wuh cigarette, heh flung himself ne' fi' wuh luxuriously cushioned ku-san ik lam-tor limuk-tor wuh gluvayek. Wuh gluvayek vesh' wuh hinek veh, t' gilt spanish duf, stamped heh wrought k' wuh rather florid louis-quatorze nel-dath. Au glashau ish-veh curiously, wondering kuv ek'wak fa' ish-veh had ip-sut wuh tsat t' wuh sasu’s ha'kiv. Dang au dvun ish-veh aside, po' ek'? Po ri kal-tor ish-veh stay tra'? Ra vesh' wuh nam-tor-tor t' fai-tor? Kuv wuh vel vesh' yeht, ish-veh vesh' terrible. Kuv ish-veh vesh' ri yeht, po trouble pa' ish-veh? Tonk'peh ra kuv, k' ein buk il deadlier pavesh, bezhun vath do ish-veh zama-tor za' heh gla-tor wuh horrible rubah? Ra dang au tor kuv basil hallward sarlah heh ya'akash tor glazhau na' ish-veh sha' bikuv? Basil would nam-tor sure tor tor ik. Rai; wuh vel had tor nam-tor linisau, heh na' wuh'wak. Sovek-vel would nam-tor weh-rom do nash dreadful fupa s' t' vet. Au prah abru heh klacha fi' svep. K'puu au would nam-tor sa'awek lu au glazhau fi-tor wuh limein t' ish-veh mesh. Yi au drew wuh gluvayek aside heh gla-tor himself limuk tor limuk. Ish-veh vesh' perfectly yeht. Wuh portrait had rubitau. U' au k'ashiv vokau afterwards, heh kwon-hau-ov k' rai pi' wonder, au afer-tor himself palikauk gazing na' wuh portrait k' wuh olaya t' siyah talik eku'ko. Ik such wuh rubah dang ma taken shi vesh' incredible tor ish-veh. Heh wi ish-veh vesh' wuh kla-min. Vesh' tra' ein subtle affinity svi' wuh meli-tukh galu ik kushizhau themselves vi' shid heh kur fi' wuh canvas heh wuh soul ik vesh' k'svi ish-veh? Kupi ish-veh nam-tor ik ra ik soul nahp, au realized?—ik ra ish-veh sahr-tor-tor, au tor yeht? Il vesh' tra' ein vath, weht terrible utvau? Au ak'shem-hutau, heh olau kwes, heh, going pla' tor wuh ku-san, ti tra', gazing na' wuh bikuv svi' sickened horror. Veh vel, however, au olau ik ish-veh had ovsoh na' ish-veh. Ish-veh had tor ish-veh d'wonil uf unjust, uf pi-maat'rer, au had vesh' tor sibyl vane. Ish-veh vesh' ri nuh' tab-ma tor tor reparation na' ik. She kupi fam dvun nam-tor ish-veh ko-telsu. Ish-veh unreal heh selfish ashaya would yield tor ein higher vi-yumuk, would nam-tor mesuvulau vi' ein nobler shaukaush, heh wuh portrait ik basil hallward had kras-tor t' ish-veh would nam-tor wuh kakhartausu tor ish-veh k'fai ha'kiv, would nam-tor tor ish-veh ra holiness nam-tor tor ein, heh conscience tor vath, heh wuh pthak t' oekon tor etek ek'. Tra' vesh' opiates na' remorse, ta'bek ik kupi lull wuh moral kash-ral tor yuk. Tonk'peh la' vesh' wuh visible sehtebuhk t' wuh degradation t' sin. La' vesh' wuh ek'wak-la' glat t' wuh ruin sasu katau fi-tor ish-veh souls. Rehkuh o’wak-vel kwul-tor, heh kehkuh, heh wuh ulef-wadan rang its dahtau kusek, tonk'peh dorian zhai-kur did ri stir. Au vesh' trying tor hoknau abru wuh ug'yon-kur og-elakh t' ha'kiv heh tor pris-tor au vi' wuh nel-dath; tor talal ish-veh yut k'fai wuh sanguine labyrinth t' shaukaush k'fai'ei au vesh' wandering. Au did ri fai-tor ra tor tor, il ra tor nah-tor. T'forti, au went abru' tor wuh pasu heh kitau wuh passionate nuhm tor wuh ko-kan au had ashau, imploring ish-veh thrap-fam'es nufau heh accusing himself t' ni-resh. Au wein-tor thalv po' thalv k' kwai zhit t' sorrow heh wilder zhit t' kusut. Tra' nam-tor wuh luxury svi' shal-reproach. Lu etek tenai ourselves, etek olau ik kling else has wuh gas'rak tor tenai etek. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh confession, ri wuh priest, ik mazhiv-kur-tor etek absolution. Lu dorian had shahtau wuh nuhm, au olau ik au had vesh' forgiven. Suddenly tra' sarlah wuh knock tor wuh svep, heh au puzhu-tor s'haile henry’s spes s'udish. “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, i bolau gla-tor du. Kal-tor me svi' na' wuh'wak. I mokuhlek’t lesh ish-veh shutting yourself abru spo' nash.” au tor rai kilko-srashiv palikauk, tonk'peh hafau ved fam dvun. Wuh knocking fam dvun fator heh grew louder. Ha, ish-veh vesh' weh-rom tor kal-tor s'haile henry svi', heh tor danau tor ish-veh wuh uzh ha'kiv au vesh' going tor ras-tukh, tor quarrel k' ish-veh kuv ish-veh became bolayatik tor quarrel, tor krus kuv parting vesh' inevitable. Au spen-tor abru, drew wuh gluvayek hastily mes' wuh bikuv, heh unlocked wuh svep. “i am ni sorry na' ish-veh ek', dorian, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry u' au svi-tor. “tonk'peh du bolau ri nah-tor nuh' mau pa' ish-veh.” “tor du tvai pa' sibyl vane?” ya'akash wuh lad. “ha, veling, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry, sinking vi' wuh ku-san heh slowly pulling ska' ish-veh kin-kur gloves. “ish-veh nam-tor dreadful, s' veh sfek t' zan-tor, tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri ish-veh lafot. Var-tor me, did du hal-tor za' heh gla-tor ish-veh, po' wuh mavau vesh' abru'?” “ha.” “i olau sure du had. Did du tor wuh scene k' ish-veh?” “i vesh' brutal, harry—perfectly brutal. Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ek' gas'rak i'. I am ri sorry na' sovek-vel ik has pavesh-tor. Ish-veh has saven-tor me tor fai-tor myself weh-rom.” “ah, dorian, i am ni glad du nem-tor ish-veh svi' ik yut! I vesh' kwes i would talal du taul-tor svi' remorse heh tearing ik nice curly isachya t' ish-veh.” “i ma prah k'fai ek' ik, ” leralmin-tor dorian, shaking ish-veh patam heh smiling. “i am perfectly kunli i'. I fai-tor ra conscience nam-tor, tor palikau k'. Ish-veh nam-tor ri ra du var-tor me ish-veh vesh'. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh divinest vel svi' etek. Don’t sneer na' ish-veh, harry, sovek weht—k'puu ri fa' me. I aitlun tor nam-tor rom. I mokuhlek’t lesh wuh idea t' t'nash-veh soul hasu hideous.” “wuh maut sem-rik-tor tanafluk i'sav na' ethics, dorian! I congratulate du fi' ish-veh. Tonk'peh uf nam-tor du going tor palikau?” “k' marrying sibyl vane.” “marrying sibyl vane!” maf-tor s'haile henry, standing abru heh looking na' ish-veh svi' perplexed tauraya. “tonk'peh, t'nash-veh tal-kam dorian—” “ha, harry, i fai-tor ra du nam-tor going tor leralmin. Vel dreadful pa' kal'i'farr. Don’t leralmin ish-veh. Don’t ek'wak leralmin vel t' ik ves tor me va'ashiv. Dahkuh gad ago i ya'akash sibyl tor marry me. I am ri going tor shaya t'nash-veh zhit tor ish-veh. She nam-tor tor nam-tor t'nash-veh ko-telsu.” “ish-veh ko-telsu! Dorian!. Didn’t du prah t'nash-veh nuhm? I kitau tor du nash asal, heh satau wuh pitoh ne' k' t'nash-veh sha' sasu.” “ish-veh nuhm? Oh, ha, i vokau. I ma ri telv-tor ish-veh wi, harry. I vesh' kwes tra' lau nam-tor vel svi' ish-veh ik i wouldn’t spo'. Du tresahk ha'kiv tor krus k' ish-veh epigrams.” “du fai-tor nothing yi?” “ra tor du tvai?” s'haile henry lates-tor mes' wuh tvi-shal, heh sitting ne' k' dorian zhai-kur, nem-tor fi' ish-veh el'ru svi' ish-veh sha' heh meskarau au tightly. “dorian, ” au leralmin-tor, “t'nash-veh nuhm—don’t nam-tor koltha—vesh' tor var-tor du ik sibyl vane nam-tor tevik.” wuh maf t' kusut shau s' wuh lad’s bru-lar, heh au leaped tor ish-veh ash'ya, tearing ish-veh el'ru maf s' s'haile henry’s ruskaraya. “tevik! Sibyl tevik! Ish-veh nam-tor ri yeht! Ish-veh nam-tor wuh horrible ti! Uf dare du leralmin ish-veh?” “ish-veh nam-tor ved yeht, dorian, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, gravely. “ish-veh nam-tor svi' ek' wuh asal dun. I kitau ne' tor du tor ya'akash du ri tor gla-tor sovek veh till vesht sarlah nash-veh. Tra' dungi ma tor nam-tor wuh inquest, veling, heh du bolau ri nam-tor rish-tor abru svi' ish-veh. Vel spo' ik tor wuh sasu fashionable svi' paris. Tonk'peh svi' london sutra nam-tor ni prejudiced. La', veh dang worla tor veh’s _début_ k' wuh scandal. Veh dang reserve ik tor mazhiv-kur-tor wuh eku'ko tor veh’s hinek ya'shakhuv. I suppose au don’t fai-tor ish-veh ahm na' wuh theatre? Kuv au don’t, ish-veh nam-tor ek' gas'rak. Did sovek veh gla-tor du going pauk tor ish-veh tvi-shal? Ik nam-tor wuh yauluhk sfek.” dorian did ri kilko-srashiv na' wuh zamu moments. Au vesh' dazed k' horror. T'forti au stammered, svi' wuh stifled spes, “harry, did du leralmin wuh inquest? Ra did du tvai k' ik? Did sibyl—? Oh, harry, i mokuhlek’t lesh ish-veh! Tonk'peh nam-tor sahris. Var-tor me kanok-vei na' wuh'wak.” “i ma rai vet ish-veh vesh' ri wuh kisheya, dorian, hi ish-veh bolau nam-tor shitau svi' ik yut tor wuh tsuri. Ish-veh seems ik u' she vesh' leaving wuh theatre k' ish-veh ko-mekh, pa' ulef-vesht leh-dah il ni, she leralmin-tor she had yen-tor vel upstairs. Au bek-tor ein wak na' ish-veh, tonk'peh she did ri sarlah ne' va'ashiv. Au ultimately afer-tor ish-veh lying tevik fi' wuh lan-tol t' ish-veh sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal. She had vitem-tor vel k' lafosh, ein dreadful vel au nam-tor-tor na' theatres. I don’t fai-tor ra ish-veh vesh', tonk'peh ish-veh had either prussic sash il wan-kur ras-tukh svi' ish-veh. I dang fancy ish-veh vesh' prussic sash, u' she seems ki' tev-tor instantaneously.” “harry, harry, ish-veh nam-tor terrible!” maf-tor wuh lad. “ha; ish-veh nam-tor maut tragic, veling, tonk'peh du bolau ri prah yourself rish-tor abru svi' ish-veh. Gla-tor nash-veh k' _the standard_ ik she vesh' leh- steh. I dang ma nahp she vesh' siyah younger do ik. She glazhau such wuh kan, heh seemed tor fai-tor ni pi' pa' peran. Dorian, du mustn’t kal-tor nash vel prah fi' ish-veh tor'tsu. Du bolau sarlah heh aru-yokul k' me, heh afterwards etek dungi glazhau svi' na' wuh opera. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh patti mu-yor, heh kanok-veh dungi nam-tor tra'. Du mokuhlek sarlah tor t'nash-veh ko-kai’s natuhn. She has prah ein klon kosu k' ish-veh.” “ni i ma riyeht-stau sibyl vane, ” leralmin-tor dorian zhai-kur, ulef tor himself, “riyeht-stau ish-veh u' surely u' kuv i had tresahk ish-veh pi' drahk k' wuh lipau. Wi wuh roses nam-tor ri lehkuh lovely na' ek' ik. Wuh kushel uralau aishan u' kunling svi' t'nash-veh bah-ker. Heh tor-mu-yor i am tor aru-yokul k' du, heh yi hal-tor fi' tor wuh opera, heh sup ein-wilat, i suppose, afterwards. Uf extraordinarily dramatic ha'kiv nam-tor! Kuv i had telv-tor ek' nash svi' wuh dunap, harry, i nah-tor i would ma wept abru' ish-veh. Somehow, i' ik ish-veh has pavesh-tor actually, heh tor me, ish-veh seems irak nuh' wonderful na' bezhun-masu. La' nam-tor wuh wuh'rak passionate ashaya-nuhm i ma ek'wak written svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Flekh, ik t'nash-veh wuh'rak passionate ashaya-nuhm dang ma vesh' addressed tor wuh tevik ko-kan. Mokuhlek au olau, i wonder, eifa wan-kur ralash-fam sutra etek vutau wuh tevik? Sibyl! Mokuhlek she olau, il fai-tor, il shroi? Oh, harry, uf i ashau ish-veh wuh'wak! Ish-veh seems tevun ago tor me i'. She vesh' kanok-vei tor me. Yi sarlah ik dreadful mu-yor—vesh' ish-veh really goh kim-shah mu-yor?—lu she mavau ni badly, heh t'nash-veh khaf-spol siyah shau. She danau ish-veh ek' tor me. Ish-veh vesh' terribly pathetic. Tonk'peh i vesh' ri dvun-tor wuh zeshau. I nahp ish-veh gan. Suddenly vel pavesh-tor ik tor me kwes. I mokuhlek’t var-tor du ra ish-veh vesh', tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' terrible. I leralmin-tor i would hal-tor pla' tor ish-veh. I olau i had ovsoh riyeht. Heh i' she nam-tor tevik. T'nash-veh oekon! T'nash-veh oekon! Harry, ra dungau i tor? Du don’t fai-tor wuh tehvar i am svi', heh tra' nam-tor nothing tor potau me zehik. She would ma ovsoh ik na' me. She had rai gas'rak tor stau herself. Ish-veh vesh' selfish t' ish-veh.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam dorian, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry, taking wuh cigarette s' ish-veh nuf heh producing wuh pi-maat-tukh-latten matchbox, “wuh goh yut wuh kosu mokuhlek ek'wak reform wuh sasu nam-tor k' guhfik ish-veh ni completely ik au pak-tor ek' tor-yehat eku'ko svi' ha'kiv. Kuv du had telik nash ko-kan, du would ma vesh' wretched. Veling, du would ma skasau ish-veh kindly. Veh mokuhlek kwon-hau-ov nam-tor ves tor sutra pa' ik veh tun-tor nothing. Tonk'peh she would ma ak afer-tor si' ik du vesh' absolutely indifferent tor ish-veh. Heh lu wuh kosu tal-tor ik si' pa' ish-veh sa-telsu, she either shetau dreadfully dowdy, il sai-vel-tor maut klon bonnets ik ein vath kosu’s sa-telsu has tor vlitau na'. I leralmin nothing pa' wuh shilaik lafosh, if would ma vesh' abject—if, veling, i would ri ma kal-tor—tonk'peh i assure du ik svi' sovek nuf wuh bosh vel would ma vesh' wuh ek'esik vravshaya.” “i suppose ish-veh would, ” muttered wuh lad, walking abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal heh looking horribly spoh. “tonk'peh i nahp ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh gu-vam. Ish-veh nam-tor ri t'nash-veh lafot ik nash terrible tragedy has prevented t'nash-veh doing ra vesh' gas'rak. I vokau ish-veh taran wuh'wak ik tra' nam-tor wuh fatality pa' rom resolutions—ik au nam-tor kwon-hau-ov tor nuh' tab-ma. T'nash-veh certainly vesh'.” “rom resolutions nam-tor nam-tor-fam attempts tor snertau k' talik tor-gav. Ish-veh tveshu nam-tor pure vanity. Ish-veh result nam-tor absolutely _nil_. Au mazhiv-kur-tor etek, i' heh yi, ein t' eifa luxurious ek'puyik zherka ik ma wuh ac'ruth sem-rik na' wuh kobat. Ik nam-tor ek' ik mokuhlek nam-tor leralmin-tor na' au. Au nam-tor veling cheques ik sasu bes-tor fi' wuh kutra wilat au ma rai khrosahp.” “harry, ” maf-tor dorian zhai-kur, coming abru' heh sitting ne' be' ish-veh, “po nam-tor ish-veh ik i fam yehat olau nash tragedy u' mau u' i aitlun tor? I don’t nah-tor i am heartless. Tor du?” “du ma ovsoh nuh' wehk duhik vel du' wuh kim-shah fortnight tor nam-tor entitled tor mazhiv-kur-tor yourself ik ahm, dorian, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry k' ish-veh slor melancholy abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Wuh lad kwal-tor. “i don’t spo' ik danaya, harry, ” au rejoined, “tonk'peh i am glad du don’t nah-tor i am heartless. I am nothing t' wuh ves. I fai-tor i am ri. Heh wi i bolau nafai-tor ik nash vel ik has pavesh-tor tor ri dau me u' ish-veh dang. Ish-veh seems tor me tor nam-tor veling spo' wuh wonderful shahtan tor wuh wonderful mavau. Ish-veh has ek' wuh terrible vaksur t' wuh greek tragedy, wuh tragedy svi' if i nem-tor wuh lo'uk krus, tonk'peh k' if i ma ri vesh' wounded.” “ish-veh nam-tor wuh eku'ki deshker, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, vi afer-tor wuh exquisite sanosh svi' mavaun fi' wuh lad’s unconscious ritsuri-shai'es, “wuh extremely eku'ki deshker. I fancy ik wuh yeht danaya nam-tor nash: ish-veh k'ashiv pavesh-tor ik wuh yeht tragedies t' ha'kiv paresh-tor svi' such wuh inartistic manner ik au dash-tor etek k' ish-veh crude khrash, ish-veh ek'esik incoherence, ish-veh absurd aitlun t' meaning, ish-veh entire fam t' style. Au dau etek aishan u' vulgarity dau etek. Au mazhiv-kur-tor etek wuh impression t' sheer brute nekwitaya, heh etek revolt tehnat ik. Sometimes, however, wuh tragedy ik ma tanafluk meilak t' vaksur tuhsau etwel ha-tor. Kuv aifa meilak t' vaksur nam-tor yeht, wuh bosh vel veling appeals tor etwel kash-ral t' dramatic daya. Suddenly etek talal ik etek nam-tor rai longer wuh actors, tonk'peh wuh spectators t' wuh mavau. Il rather etek nam-tor fi'. Etek glantau ourselves, heh wuh mere wonder t' wuh spectacle enthralls etek. Svi' wuh la' nuf, ra nam-tor ish-veh ik has really pavesh-tor? Ein veh has pustau herself na' ashaya t' du. I istaya ik i had ek'wak had such wuh veshtaya. Ish-veh would ma tor me svi' ashaya k' ashaya na' wuh shom t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. Wuh sutra vi ma adored me—tra' ma ri vesh' maut wehk, tonk'peh tra' ma vesh' ein—ma kwon-hau-ov insisted fi' living fi', wu po' i had ceased tor palutunau au, il au tor palutunau me. Au ma shetau stout heh tedious, heh lu i ragel-tor au, au hal-tor svi' na' wuh'wak na' reminiscences. Ik awful vokaya t' kosu! Ra wuh pthak-bosh vel ish-veh nam-tor! Heh ra wuh utter intellectual stagnation ish-veh reveals! Veh dang vi-seshau wuh kur t' ha'kiv, tonk'peh veh dang worla vokau its details. Details nam-tor kwon-hau-ov vulgar.” “i bolau sow poppies svi' t'nash-veh bah-ker, ” spes-tevan dorian. “tra' nam-tor rai bolayek, ” rejoined ish-veh besu. “ha'kiv has kwon-hau-ov poppies svi' ish-veh el'ru. Veling, i' heh yi vel svizh-tor. I wuh'wak sai-vel-tor nothing tonk'peh mu'gahv-kur ek' k'fai veh tevun-yonuk, u' wuh shid t' tanafluk mourning na' wuh romance ik would ri tev-tor. Ultimately, however, ish-veh did tev-tor. I yen-tor ra pustau ish-veh. I nah-tor ish-veh vesh' ish-veh proposing tor sacrifice wuh bosh panu na' me. Ik nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh dreadful moment. Ish-veh boshau veh k' wuh vash t' ek'wak'es. Muhl—would du dva-tor ish-veh?—wuh wehk gad ago, na' t'sai hampshire’s, i afer-tor myself hayal-tor na' aru-yem thurai wuh t'sai svi' deshker, heh she insisted fi' going abru' wuh bosh vel va'ashiv, heh digging abru wuh vesht, heh raking abru wuh fa-wak. I had visolektau t'nash-veh romance svi' wuh sar-tak t' asphodel. She zaseshau ish-veh si' va'ashiv heh assured me ik i had spoiled ish-veh ha'kiv. I am bound tor fupa s' ik she ate wuh masuk' aru-yem, ni i did ri olau sovek anxiety. Tonk'peh ra wuh fam t' zahvan she gluvau! Wuh veh sem-rik t' wuh vesht nam-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh vesht. Tonk'peh kosu worla fai-tor lu wuh curtain has tevan-tor. Au kwon-hau-ov aitlun wuh sixth bae'cok, heh u' ak u' wuh eku'ko t' wuh mavau nam-tor entirely abru', au propose tor fator ish-veh. Kuv au vesh' kal-tor ish-veh sha' yut, kanok comedy would ma wuh tragic shahtan, heh kanok tragedy would culminate svi' wuh farce. Au nam-tor charmingly sutorik, tonk'peh au ma rai kash-ral t' tanaf. Du nam-tor weht fortunate do i am. I assure du, dorian, ik ri veh t' wuh kosu i ma fainu would ma ovsoh na' me ra sibyl vane did na' du. Ordinary kosu kwon-hau-ov console themselves. Ein t' au tor ish-veh k' going svi' na' sentimental colours. Worla sahrafel wuh kosu vi sai-vel-tor kihsh-kur, whatever ish-veh ya'shakhuv lau nam-tor, il wuh kosu abru' reh-leh-kaukuh vi nam-tor tishau t' faf-kur ribbons. Ish-veh kwon-hau-ov tvai ik au ma wuh vesht-var. Vath talal wuh lo'uk consolation svi' suddenly discovering wuh rom qualities t' ish-veh sa-telsu. Au flaunt ish-veh conjugal felicity svi' veh’s limuk, u' kuv ish-veh vesh' wuh danik sem-rik t' sins. Odva consoles ein. Its mysteries ma ek' wuh sem-rik t' wuh flirtation, wuh kosu wuh'wak var-tor me, heh i mokuhlek ved ken-tor ish-veh. Isha, nothing tor veh ni vain u' hasu var-tor ish-veh nam-tor wuh sinner. Conscience tor egotists t' etek ek'. Ha; tra' nam-tor really rai shaht tor wuh consolations ik kosu talal svi' iyik ha'kiv. Indeed, i ma ri mentioned wuh danik yauluhk veh.” “ra nam-tor ik, harry?” leralmin-tor wuh lad listlessly. “oh, wuh obvious consolation. Taking ein veh else’s admirer lu veh pak-tor veh’s sha'. Svi' rom shila'es ik kwon-hau-ov whitewashes wuh kosu. Tonk'peh really, dorian, uf natya sibyl vane bolau ma vesh' s' ek' wuh kosu veh ragel-tor! Tra' nam-tor vel tor me ved vaksurik pa' ish-veh tevakh. I am glad i am living svi' wuh century lu such wonders pavesh-tor. Au tor veh dva-tor svi' wuh reality t' wuh vel etek ek' mavau k', such u' romance, shaukaush, heh ashaya.” “i vesh' terribly pi-maat'rer tor ish-veh. Du yen-tor ik.” “i am kwes ik kosu appreciate cruelty, downright cruelty, weht do sovek-kitok. Au ma wonderfully os-shidik instincts. Etek ma su'el-tor au, tonk'peh au hafau kafeh looking na' ish-veh trensu, ek' wuh ka. Au ashaya hasu abrukhau. I am sure du vesh' splendid. I ma worla gla-tor du really heh absolutely reshnek, tonk'peh i mokuhlek fancy uf delightful du glazhau. Heh, po' ek', du leralmin-tor vel tor me wuh gad fa' za-gad ik seemed tor me na' wuh wak tor nam-tor goh fanciful, tonk'peh ik gla-tor nash-veh i' vesh' absolutely yeht, heh ish-veh meskarau wuh tal-muv tor kanok-vei.” “ra vesh' ik, harry?” “du leralmin-tor tor me ik sibyl vane represented tor du ek' wuh heroines t' romance—ik she vesh' desdemona veh mu-yor, heh ophelia wuh vath; ik kuv she tev-tor u' juliet, sarlah ish-veh tor ha'kiv u' imogen.” “she dungi worla sarlah tor ha'kiv va'ashiv i', ” muttered wuh lad, burying ish-veh limuk svi' ish-veh el'ru. “rai, she dungi worla sarlah tor ha'kiv. She has mavau ish-veh kim-shah krus. Tonk'peh du bolau nah-tor t' ik lonely tevakh svi' wuh tawdry sai-vel-tor-tvi-shal veling u' wuh flekh lurid karf s' ein jacobean tragedy, u' wuh wonderful scene s' webster, il masmezh, il cyril tourneur. Wuh ko-kan worla really ha-tor, heh ni she has worla really tev-tor. Tor du k'puu she vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh sahr-tor, wuh phantom ik flitted k'fai shakespeare’s mavau heh losrak au lovelier na' its la'es, wuh reed k'fai'ei shakespeare’s ralash-tanaf sounded richer heh weht bosh t' mak. Wuh moment she estuhl actual ha'kiv, she marred ish-veh, heh ish-veh marred ish-veh, heh ni she be' dvun-tor maf. La'tusa na' ophelia, kuv du spo'. Shitau vitush fi' ish-veh patam fai'ei cordelia vesh' strangled. Lit'dhae tehnat sha-ka-ri fai'ei wuh ko-fu t' brabantio tev-tor. Tonk'peh don’t thinoi ish-veh bezhun-masu abru' sibyl vane. She vesh' lehkuh yeht do au nam-tor.” tra' vesh' wuh silence. Wuh khru mu'glau svi' wuh tvi-shal. Noiselessly, heh k' haul-tukh ash'ya, wuh duv crept svi' s' wuh bah-ker. Wuh colours spoh-tor wearily s' vel. Po' ein wak dorian zhai-kur glazhau abru. “du ma danau me tor myself, harry, ” au murmured k' vel t' wuh spes-tevan t' vas. “i olau ek' ik du ma leralmin-tor, tonk'peh somehow i vesh' kwes t' ish-veh, heh i kupi ri sagluvau ish-veh tor myself. Uf muhl du fai-tor me! Tonk'peh etek dungi ri variben va'ashiv t' ra has pavesh-tor. Ish-veh has vesh' wuh marvellous veshtaya. Ik nam-tor ek'. I wonder kuv ha'kiv has fam dvun svi' mahr-kel na' me sovek-vel u' marvellous.” “ha'kiv has kanok-vei svi' mahr-kel na' du, dorian. Tra' nam-tor nothing ik du, k' ish-veh wehtsuri rom glazhau, dungi ri nam-tor kup tor tor.” “tonk'peh suppose, harry, i became haggard, heh hinek, heh wrinkled? Ra yi?” “ah, yi, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, rising tor hal-tor, “yi, t'nash-veh tal-kam dorian, du would ma tor puk na' ish-veh skil. U' ish-veh nam-tor, au nam-tor katau tor du. Rai, du bolau potau ish-veh rom glazhau. Etek ha-tor svi' wuh ya'shakhuv ik telv-tor nuh' mau tor nam-tor kau-bosh, heh ik nah-tor nuh' mau tor nam-tor vaksurik. Etek fam yehat spare du. Heh i' du had weh-rom sai-vel heh yetur ne' tor wuh muhd. Etek nam-tor rather tab-ma, u' ish-veh nam-tor.” “i nah-tor i dungau hau du na' wuh opera, harry. I olau nuh' zungor tor yokul sovek-vel. Ra nam-tor wuh su'etek t' ish-veh ko-kai’s natuhn?” “dah-leh-stehkuh, i dva-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor fi' wuh grand tier. Du dungi gla-tor ish-veh ahm fi' wuh svep. Tonk'peh ni'droi'ik nar-tor du skil-tor’t sarlah heh aru-yokul.” “i don’t olau abru tor ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor dorian listlessly. “tonk'peh i am awfully obliged tor du na' ek' ik du ma leralmin-tor tor me. Du nam-tor certainly t'nash-veh buhfik t'hy'la. Kling has ek'wak ken-tor me u' du ma.” “etek nam-tor goh na' wuh palikaya t' etwel friendship, dorian, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry, shaking ish-veh k' wuh el'ru. “rom-bye. Dungau gla-tor nash-veh du fa' naukuh-reh-leh, i rok. Vokau, patti nam-tor uralaun.” u' au a'ing wuh svep za' ish-veh, dorian zhai-kur estuhl wuh kus-vakh, heh svi' wuh zamu minutes skilsu saudau k' wuh ha'gelek heh drew wuh blinds ne'. Au bek-tor impatiently na' ish-veh tor hal-tor. Wuh sasu seemed tor nem-tor wuh interminable wak abru' kanok-vei. U' ak u' au had losrak, au rushed tor wuh gluvayek heh drew ish-veh pla'. Rai; tra' vesh' rai further rubah svi' wuh bikuv. Ish-veh had poprah wuh ro'fori t' sibyl vane’s tevakh fa' au had fainu t' ish-veh himself. Ish-veh vesh' d'wonil t' wuh pavek t' ha'kiv u' au paresh-tor. Wuh vicious cruelty ik marred wuh tok-ti zehl t' wuh ru'lut had, rai vet, saudau na' wuh maut moment ik wuh ko-kan had mon-tor wuh gisam, whatever ish-veh vesh'. Il vesh' ish-veh indifferent tor results? Did ish-veh goh nem-tor cognizance t' ra be' dvun-tor k'svi wuh soul? Au wondered, heh rok-tor ik ein gad au would gla-tor wuh rubah taking shi fa' ish-veh maut bezhun, shuddering u' au rok-tor ish-veh. Ri donku-tor sibyl! Ra wuh romance ish-veh had ek' vesh'! She had k'ashiv va'amau tevakh fi' wuh skaf. Yi tevakh himself had estuhl ish-veh heh taken ish-veh k' ish-veh. Uf had she mavau ik dreadful kim-shah scene? Had she cursed ish-veh, u' she tev-tor? Rai; she had tev-tor na' ashaya t' ish-veh, heh ashaya would kwon-hau-ov nam-tor wuh sacrament tor ish-veh i'. She had atoned na' kanok-vei k' wuh sacrifice she had tor t' ish-veh ha'kiv. Au would ri nah-tor sovek weht t' ra she had tor ish-veh hal-tor k'fai, fi' ik horrible mu-yor na' wuh theatre. Lu au nahp t' ish-veh, ish-veh would nam-tor u' wuh wonderful tragic khlop satau fi' tor wuh panu’s skaf tor gluvaya wuh supreme reality t' ashaya. Wuh wonderful tragic khlop? Bezhun-masu sarlah tor ish-veh bezhun u' au vokau ish-veh childlike glazhau, heh winsome fanciful yut, heh fusik tremulous takov. Au brushed au maf hastily heh glazhau va'ashiv na' wuh bikuv. Au olau ik wuh wak had really sarlah na' tor ish-veh dvel. Il had ish-veh dvel already vesh' tor? Ha, ha'kiv had klopau ik na' ish-veh—ha'kiv, heh ish-veh sha' vaik curiosity pa' ha'kiv. Ek'wakik youth, vaik shaukaush, pleasures subtle heh tsat, kwai mak heh wilder sins—au vesh' ki' ek' aifa vel. Wuh portrait vesh' tor lesh wuh burden t' ish-veh mesh: ik vesh' ek'. Wuh olaya t' kusut crept abru' ish-veh u' au nahp t' wuh desecration ik vesh' svi' mahr-kel na' wuh rom limuk fi' wuh canvas. Wuh'wak, svi' boyish mockery t' narcissus, au had shok-tor, il vup-tor tor shok, eifa kras-tor bru-lar ik i' abru'teruklar-ru'lut ni cruelly na' ish-veh. Asal po' asal au had hayal-tor fa' wuh portrait wondering na' its vaksur, siyah enamoured t' ish-veh, u' ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh na' wak. Vesh' ish-veh tor rubitau i' k' kanok mood tor if au yielded? Vesh' ish-veh tor shetau wuh monstrous heh loathsome vel, tor nam-tor ipik maf svi' wuh klacha tvi-shal, tor nam-tor ikap-tor si' s' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel ik had ni k'ashiv estuhl tor brighter pi-maat-tukh wuh pral-tor wonder t' its isachya? Wuh pity t' ish-veh! Wuh pity t' ish-veh! Na' wuh moment, au nahp t' praying ik wuh horrible sympathy ik nam-tor svi' ish-veh heh wuh bikuv lau cease. Ish-veh had rubai svi' kilko-srashiv tor wuh prayer; sos'eh svi' kilko-srashiv tor wuh prayer ish-veh lau hafau unchanged. Heh wi, vi, ik fai-tor sovek-vel pa' ha'kiv, would surrender wuh pavesh t' remaining kwon-hau-ov nu'ri, however fantastic ik pavesh lau nam-tor, il k' ra buk-bosh consequences ish-veh lau nam-tor fraught? Isha, vesh' ish-veh really ne' ish-veh tash? Had ish-veh indeed vesh' prayer ik had torvau wuh substitution? Lau tra' ri nam-tor ein curious talik utvau na' ish-veh ek'? Kuv nahp kupi tusok its vi-yumuk fi-tor wuh living ha-vel, lau ri nahp tusok wuh vi-yumuk fi-tor tevik heh inorganic vel? Nay, rik' nahp il d'wonil aitlun, lau ri vel sik tor ourselves vibrate svi' unison k' etwel moods heh shaukaush, galu calling tor galu svi' tsat ashaya il flekh affinity? Tonk'peh wuh utvau vesh' t' rai importance. Au would worla va'ashiv tempt k' wuh prayer sovek terrible tepul. Kuv wuh bikuv vesh' tor rubitau, ish-veh vesh' tor rubitau. Ik vesh' ek'. Po inquire nuh' closely vi' ish-veh? Na' tra' would nam-tor wuh yeht sanosh svi' watching ish-veh. Au would nam-tor kup tor zahal-tor ish-veh kashek vi' its tsat shitau. Nash portrait would nam-tor tor ish-veh wuh danik magical t' haulat. U' ish-veh had revealed tor ish-veh ish-veh sha' ak'shem, ni ish-veh would reveal tor ish-veh ish-veh sha' soul. Heh lu karil sarlah fi-tor ish-veh, au would fam dvun nam-tor standing wilat sikar trembles fi' wuh verge t' belaar. Lu wuh khaf crept s' its limuk, heh losrak za' wuh pallid limein t' gav k' leaden bezhun, au would potau wuh glamour t' boyhood. Ri veh blossom t' ish-veh loveliness would ek'wak spoh-tor. Ri veh khaf-spol-gaya t' ish-veh ha'kiv would ek'wak kobatau. Spo' wuh gods t' wuh greeks, au would nam-tor karik, heh halitra, heh joyous. Ra did ish-veh tukh ra pavesh-tor tor wuh kur-tor glakuv fi' wuh canvas? Au would nam-tor safe. Ik vesh' kanok-vei. Au drew wuh gluvayek pla' vi' its former shi svi' khom t' wuh bikuv, smiling u' au did ni, heh be' dvun-tor vi' ish-veh shi'yuk, wilat ish-veh valet vesh' already waiting na' ish-veh. Wuh wadan later au vesh' na' wuh opera, heh s'haile henry vesh' leaning abru' ish-veh ku-san. Chapter ix. U' au vesh' sitting na' asal-yem thurai asal, basil hallward vesh' shown vi' wuh tvi-shal. “i am ni glad i ma afer-tor du, dorian, ” au leralmin-tor gravely. “i puvutau kim-shah mu-yor, heh au var-tor me du vesh' na' wuh opera. Veling, i fai-tor ik vesh' impossible. Tonk'peh i istaya du had losrak zhit wilat du had really hal-tor tor. I be' dvun-tor wuh dreadful khru, ulef kwes ish-veh tragedy lau nam-tor zahal-tor k' wuh'ashiv. I nah-tor du lau ma telegraphed na' me lu du puzhu-tor t' ish-veh wuh'rak. I telv-tor t' ish-veh ved k' pavesh svi' wuh tab-ma yadan t' _the globe_ ik i abrashau na' wuh muhd. Vesht sarlah nash-veh la' na' wuh'wak heh vesh' miserable na' ri finding du. I mokuhlek’t var-tor du uf khaf-spol-pushau i am pa' wuh bosh vel. I fai-tor ra du bolau dash. Tonk'peh wilat vesh' du? Did du hal-tor ne' heh gla-tor wuh ko-kan’s ko-mekh? Na' wuh moment i nahp t' zahalik du tra'. Au mazhiv-kur-tor wuh shi'yavekh svi' wuh dun. Ein-wilat svi' wuh euston fau-yut, isn’t ish-veh? Tonk'peh i vesh' kwes t' intruding fi-tor wuh sorrow ik i kupi ri lighten. Ri donku-tor kosu! Ra wuh fupa s' she bolau nam-tor svi'! Heh ish-veh goh kan, nuh'! Ra did she leralmin pa' ish-veh ek'?” “t'nash-veh tal-kam basil, uf tor i fai-tor?” murmured dorian zhai-kur, mon-tor ein spoh-kin-kur wine s' wuh delicate, pi-maat-tukh-beaded duk t' venetian makh heh looking dreadfully bored. “i vesh' na' wuh opera. Du dang ma sarlah fi' tra'. I ragel-tor t'sai gwendolen, harry’s ko-kai, na' wuh wuh'rak wak. Etek vesh' svi' ish-veh natuhn. She nam-tor perfectly sem-rik-tor; heh patti sang divinely. Don’t variben pa' horrid subjects. Kuv veh doesn’t variben pa' wuh vel, ish-veh has worla pavesh-tor. Ish-veh nam-tor veling sagluvaya, u' harry leralmin-tor, ik mazhiv-kur-tor reality tor vel. I lau mention ik she vesh' ri wuh kosu’s goh kan. Tra' nam-tor wuh sa-fu, wuh sem-rik-tor katravahsu, i dva-tor. Tonk'peh au nam-tor ri fi' wuh skaf. Au nam-tor wuh masusu, il vel. Heh i', var-tor me pa' yourself heh ra du nam-tor krasan.” “du went tor wuh opera?” leralmin-tor hallward, speaking maut slowly heh k' wuh ish-veh-tor esta t' kusut svi' ish-veh spes. “du went tor wuh opera du' sibyl vane vesh' lying tevik svi' ein sordid lodging? Du mokuhlek variben tor me t' vath kosu hasu sem-rik-tor, heh t' patti uralaun divinely, fa' wuh ko-kan du ashau has kauk wuh hizhuk t' wuh shi'vukhut tor yuk svi'? Po, sasu, tra' nam-tor horrors svi' mahr-kel na' ik pi' wan-kur ak'shem t' ish-veh!” “pehkaya, basil! I skil-tor’t zhu-tor ish-veh!” maf-tor dorian, leaping tor ish-veh ash'ya. “du bolau ri var-tor me pa' vel. Ra nam-tor ovsoh nam-tor ovsoh. Ra nam-tor vesht nam-tor vesht.” “du vutau za-gad wuh vesht?” “ra has wuh actual lapse t' wak prah tor tor k' ish-veh? Ish-veh nam-tor goh gan sutra vi require tevun tor prah rid t' wuh zherka. Wuh sasu vi nam-tor trensu t' himself mokuhlek shaht wuh sorrow u' easily u' au mokuhlek fereik-tor wuh sanosh. I don’t aitlun tor nam-tor na' wuh mercy t' t'nash-veh zherka. I aitlun tor nam-tor-tor au, tor tizh-tor au, heh tor abrukhau au.” “dorian, nash nam-tor horrible! Vel has rubai du completely. Du glazhau exactly wuh ka wonderful sa-kan vi, gad po' gad, nam-tor-tor tor sarlah ne' tor t'nash-veh studio tor hayal-tor na' ish-veh bikuv. Tonk'peh du vesh' velik, malatik, heh affectionate yi. Du vesh' wuh danik unspoiled creature svi' wuh bosh panu. I', i don’t fai-tor ra has sarlah abru' du. Du variben u' kuv du had rai khaf-spol, rai pity svi' du. Ish-veh nam-tor ek' harry’s vi-yumuk. Gla-tor nash-veh ik.” wuh lad kluhvau abru heh, going tor wuh krani, glazhau si' na' wuh zamu moments fi' wuh yar-kur, flickering, yel-lashed bah-ker. “i owe wuh lo'uk deal tor harry, basil, ” au leralmin-tor na' kim-shah, “weht do i owe tor du. Du goh saven-tor me tor nam-tor vain.” “muhl, i am taflau na' ik, dorian—il dungau nam-tor ein gad.” “i don’t fai-tor ra du tvai, basil, ” au sporiben, turning pauk. “i don’t fai-tor ra du aitlun. Ra tor du aitlun?” “i aitlun wuh dorian zhai-kur i nam-tor-tor tor kras, ” leralmin-tor wuh tanafsu sadly. “basil, ” leralmin-tor wuh lad, going abru' tor ish-veh heh putting ish-veh el'ru fi' ish-veh tipan, “du ma sarlah nuh' tab-ma. Za-gad, lu i puzhu-tor ik sibyl vane had pustau herself—” “pustau herself! Rom heavens! Nam-tor tra' rai vet pa' ik?” maf-tor hallward, looking abru na' ish-veh k' wuh sagluvaya t' horror. “t'nash-veh tal-kam basil! Surely du don’t nah-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh vulgar kisheya? T' rivak she pustau herself.” wuh tela'at sasu visolektau ish-veh limuk svi' ish-veh el'ru. “uf pthak-bosh, ” au muttered, heh wuh ak'shem-hutau sahr-tor k'fai ish-veh. “rai, ” leralmin-tor dorian zhai-kur, “tra' nam-tor nothing pthak-bosh pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor veh t' wuh lo'uk romantic tragedies t' wuh ya'shakhuv. U' wuh tor-go, sutra vi bae'cok ras-tukh wuh danik commonplace ha-tor. Au nam-tor rom sa-telsu, il faithful ko-telsu, il vel tedious. Du fai-tor ra i tvai—svitan-mohrn virtue heh ek' ik ves t' vel. Uf natya sibyl vesh'! She ha-tor ish-veh finest tragedy. She vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh heroine. Wuh kim-shah mu-yor she mavau—wuh mu-yor gla-tor du ish-veh—she bae'cok badly fai'ei she had fainu wuh reality t' ashaya. Lu she fai-tor its unreality, she tev-tor, u' juliet lau ma tev-tor. She be' dvun-tor va'ashiv vi' wuh ek'kal t' tanaf. Tra' nam-tor vel t' wuh trufemu pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh tevakh has ek' wuh pathetic uselessness t' martyrdom, ek' its thinoi vaksur. Tonk'peh, u' i vesh' taran, du bolau ri nah-tor i ma ri dashau. Kuv du had sarlah svi' za-gad na' wuh particular moment—pa' ulef-vesht kaukuh, sos'eh, il wuh yonuk tor shehkuh—du would ma afer-tor me svi' bezhun-masu. Kauk harry, vi vesh' la', vi katau me wuh ro'fori, svi' kla-min, had rai idea ra i vesh' going k'fai. I dashau immensely. Yi ish-veh be' dvun-tor maf. I fam yehat ashiv-tor wuh zherka. Kling mokuhlek, kaula sentimentalists. Heh du nam-tor awfully unjust, basil. Sarlah du ne' la' tor console me. Ik nam-tor sem-rik-tor t' du. Du talal me consoled, heh du nam-tor furious. Uf spo' wuh sympathetic person! Du remind me t' wuh var harry var-tor me pa' wuh ac'ruth philanthropist vi spent dah-leh tevun t' ish-veh ha'kiv svi' trying tor prah ein grievance redressed, il ein unjust tor-gav rubitau—i yen-tor exactly ra ish-veh vesh'. T'forti au navau, heh nothing kupi namautau ish-veh disappointment. Au had absolutely nothing tor tor, siyah tev-tor t' _ennui_, heh became wuh wugau misanthrope. Heh isha, t'nash-veh tal-kam hinek basil, kuv du really aitlun tor console me, saven-tor me rather tor yen-tor ra has pavesh-tor, il tor gla-tor ish-veh s' wuh proper tanafluk sfek t' zan-tor. Vesh' ish-veh ri gautier vi nam-tor-tor tor kitau pa' _la consolation des arts_? I vokau picking abru wuh pi' vellum-wein-tor dunap svi' ish-veh studio veh gad heh chancing fi' ik delightful zhit-bal. Muhl, i am ri spo' ik nu'ri sasu du var-tor me t' lu etek vesh' ne' na' marlow teretuhr, wuh nu'ri sasu vi nam-tor-tor tor leralmin ik kin-kur satin kupi console veh na' ek' wuh miseries t' ha'kiv. I ashaya vaksurik vel ik veh mokuhlek esta heh el'rek. Hinek brocades, yar-kur bronzes, lacquer-ar'kadan, skrim-tor ivories, exquisite surroundings, luxury, pomp—tra' nam-tor mau tor nam-tor prah s' ek' aifa. Tonk'peh wuh tanafluk temperament ik au fereik-tor, il na' sovek tav reveal, nam-tor fam dvun weht tor me. Tor shetau wuh spectator t' veh’s sha' ha'kiv, u' harry leralmin-tor, nam-tor tor stron wuh suffering t' ha'kiv. I fai-tor du nam-tor ak'wikmun na' t'nash-veh talking tor du spo' nash. Du ma ri realized uf i ma storik. I vesh' wuh schoolboy lu du fai-tor me. I am wuh sasu i'. I ma uzh shaukaush, uzh nahp, uzh ideas. I am natya, tonk'peh du bolau ri spo' me lehkuh. I am rubai, tonk'peh du bolau kwon-hau-ov nam-tor t'nash-veh t'hy'la. Veling, i am maut tishau t' harry. Tonk'peh i fai-tor ik du nam-tor weh-rom do au nam-tor. Du nam-tor ri stronger—du nam-tor nuh' mau kwes t' ha'kiv—tonk'peh du nam-tor weh-rom. Heh uf kunli etek nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor teretuhr! Don’t trasha me, basil, heh don’t quarrel k' me. I am ra i am. Tra' nam-tor nothing weht tor nam-tor leralmin-tor.” wuh krassu olau strangely dvun-tor. Wuh lad vesh' infinitely tal-kam tor ish-veh, heh ish-veh nafu'es had vesh' wuh lo'uk turning sfek svi' ish-veh tanaf. Au kupi ri lesh wuh idea t' reproaching ish-veh sovek weht. Po' ek', ish-veh indifference vesh' probably goh wuh mood ik would be' dvun maf. Tra' vesh' ni mau svi' ish-veh ik vesh' rom, ni mau svi' ish-veh ik vesh' thol. “muhl, dorian, ” au leralmin-tor na' wu-vath, k' wuh maf abru'teruklar-ru'lut, “i skil-tor’t stariben tor du va'ashiv pa' nash horrible vel, po' tor-gad. I goh sahrafel ish-veh ahm skil-tor’t nam-tor mentioned svi' tersaya k' ish-veh. Wuh inquest nam-tor tor nem-tor shi nash aru. Ma au summoned du?” dorian hutau ish-veh patam, heh wuh glazhau t' il'nai'ga be' dvun-tor abru' ish-veh limuk na' wuh mention t' wuh zhit “inquest.” tra' vesh' vel ni crude heh vulgar pa' kanok-vei t' wuh ves. “au don’t fai-tor t'nash-veh ahm, ” au kilko-tor. “tonk'peh surely she did?” “goh t'nash-veh christian ahm, heh ik i am ved sure she worla mentioned tor sovek veh. She var-tor me wuh'wak ik au vesh' ek' rather curious tor oren-tor vi i vesh', heh ik she invariably var-tor au t'nash-veh ahm vesh' prince sem-rik-tor. Ish-veh vesh' takov t' ish-veh. Du bolau tor me wuh bestan t' sibyl, basil. I dang spo' ki' vel weht t' ish-veh do wuh vokaya t' wuh zamu shok-tor heh ein pushau pathetic zhit.” “i dungi ar'kadan heh tor vel, dorian, kuv ish-veh would sanoi du.
