Tonk'peh du bolau sarlah heh hayal-tor tor me yourself va'ashiv. I mokuhlek’t prah fi' rik' du.” “i mokuhlek worla hayal-tor tor du va'ashiv, basil. Ish-veh nam-tor impossible!” au sporiben, starting pla'. Wuh krassu nantau na' ish-veh. “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, ra nonsense!” au maf-tor. “tor du tvai tor leralmin du don’t spo' ra i did t' du? Wilat nam-tor ish-veh? Po ma du seshau wuh gluvayek svi' khom t' ish-veh? Kal-tor me glazhau na' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh buhfik vel i ma ek'wak ovsoh. Tor nem-tor wuh gluvayek maf, dorian. Ish-veh nam-tor veling disgraceful t' ish-veh dvinsu hiding t'nash-veh ar'kadan spo' ik. I olau wuh tvi-shal glazhau natya u' vesht sarlah nash-veh svi'.” “t'nash-veh dvinsu has nothing tor tor k' ish-veh, basil. Du don’t glenonau i kal-tor ish-veh arrange t'nash-veh tvi-shal na' me? Au settles t'nash-veh svai na' me sometimes—ik nam-tor ek'. Rai; i did ish-veh myself. Wuh ta'hal vesh' nuh' karik fi' wuh portrait.” “nuh' karik! Surely ri, t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu? Ish-veh nam-tor wuh admirable shi na' ish-veh. Kal-tor me gla-tor ish-veh.” heh hallward lates-tor na' wuh teruk t' wuh tvi-shal. Wuh maf t' vash shau s' dorian zhai-kur’s bru-lar, heh au rushed svi' wuh krassu heh wuh gluvayek. “basil, ” au leralmin-tor, looking maut spoh, “du bolau ri glazhau na' ish-veh. I don’t istaya du tor.” “ri glazhau na' t'nash-veh sha' ar'kadan! Du nam-tor ri serious. Po shouldn’t i glazhau na' ish-veh?” sporiben hallward, laughing. “kuv du ar'kadan tor glazhau na' ish-veh, basil, fi' t'nash-veh zhit t' dor i dungi worla stariben tor du va'ashiv u' wu u' i ha-tor. I am ved serious. I don’t nufai sovek danaya, heh du nam-tor ri tor ya'akash na' sovek. Tonk'peh, vokau, kuv du esta nash gluvayek, kanok-vei nam-tor abru' svi' etek.” hallward vesh' thunderstruck. Au glazhau na' dorian zhai-kur svi' ek'esik tauraya. Au had worla gla-tor ish-veh spo' nash fa'. Wuh lad vesh' actually pallid k' reshan. Ish-veh el'ru vesh' clenched, heh wuh glan-sharu t' ish-veh bezhun vesh' spo' mathra t' pla-kur yon. Au vesh' trembling ek' abru'. “dorian!” “don’t stariben!” “tonk'peh ra nam-tor wuh tukh? Veling i skil-tor’t glazhau na' ish-veh kuv du don’t aitlun me tor, ” au leralmin-tor, rather coldly, turning fi' ish-veh timut heh going abru' na' wuh krani. “tonk'peh, really, ish-veh seems rather absurd ik i shouldn’t gla-tor t'nash-veh sha' ar'kadan, wa' u' i am going tor gluvaya ish-veh svi' paris svi' wuh tasmin. I dungau probably ma tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wuh'ashiv tor-pal t' varnish fa' ik, ni i bolau gla-tor ish-veh ein gad, heh po ri tor-gad?” “tor gluvaya ish-veh! Du aitlun tor gluvaya ish-veh?” sporiben dorian zhai-kur, wuh flekh kash-ral t' vash creeping abru' ish-veh. Vesh' wuh panu going tor nam-tor shown ish-veh tsat? Vesh' sutra tor gape na' wuh mystery t' ish-veh ha'kiv? Ik vesh' impossible. Vel—au did ri fai-tor ra—had tor nam-tor ovsoh na' wuh'wak. “ha; i don’t suppose du dungi vel tor ik. Georges petit nam-tor going tor tershau ek' t'nash-veh buhfik bikuv na' wuh special exhibition svi' wuh rue de sèze, if dungi tu'ash wuh wuh'rak wehk gad svi' october. Wuh portrait dungi goh nam-tor maf wuh tevun-krus. I dang nah-tor du kupi easily spare ish-veh na' ik wak. Svi' kla-min, du nam-tor sure tor nam-tor s' kahr. Heh kuv du potau ish-veh kwon-hau-ov za' wuh gluvayek, du mokuhlek’t tun mau pa' ish-veh.” dorian zhai-kur be' dvun-tor ish-veh el'ru abru' ish-veh fa-patam. Tra' vesh' o'lid t' wadashaya tra'. Au olau ik au vesh' fi' wuh rihk t' wuh horrible tehvar. “du var-tor me wuh tevun-krus ago ik du would worla gluvaya ish-veh, ” au maf-tor. “po ma du rubai ish-veh kashek? Du sutra vi hal-tor svi' na' hasu tsurkanik ma aishan u' wehk moods u' vath ma. Wuh goh natyan nam-tor ik ish-veh moods nam-tor rather meaningless. Du mokuhlek’t ma yen-tor ik du assured me danik solemnly ik nothing svi' wuh panu would vimevilau du tor satau ish-veh tor sovek exhibition. Du var-tor harry exactly wuh ka vel.” au pehkau suddenly, heh wuh gleam t' ta'hal sarlah vi' ish-veh bezhun. Au vokau ik s'haile henry had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh wuh'wak, ulef seriously heh ulef svi' jest, “kuv du aitlun ki' wuh flekh yonuk t' wuh wadan, prah basil tor var-tor du po au skil-tor’t gluvaya ish-veh bikuv. Au var-tor me po au wouldn’t, heh ish-veh vesh' wuh revelation tor me.” ha, sos'eh basil, nuh', had ish-veh tsat. Au would ya'akash ish-veh heh ar'kadan. “basil, ” au leralmin-tor, coming abru' ved ikap-tor heh looking ish-veh zehik svi' wuh limuk, “etek ma tik t' etek wuh tsat. Kal-tor me fai-tor ish-veh, heh i dungau var-tor du t'nash-veh. Ra vesh' ish-veh utvau na' refusing tor gluvaya t'nash-veh bikuv?” wuh krassu ak'shem-hutau svi' spite t' himself. “dorian, kuv i var-tor du, du lau spo' me lehkuh tor du tor, heh du would certainly abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' me. I kupi ri lesh ish-veh doing either t' eifa dahkuh vel. Kuv du istaya me worla tor glazhau na' ish-veh bikuv va'ashiv, i am content. I ma kwon-hau-ov du tor glazhau na'. Kuv du istaya wuh buhfik ar'kadan i ma ek'wak ovsoh tor nam-tor ipik s' wuh panu, i am satisfied. Ish-veh friendship nam-tor dearer tor me do sovek khin il reputation.” “rai, basil, du bolau var-tor me, ” insisted dorian zhai-kur. “i nah-tor i ma wuh gas'rak tor fai-tor.” ish-veh olaya t' vash had be' dvun-tor maf, heh curiosity had taken its shi. Au vesh' satalau tor talal si' basil hallward’s mystery. “kal-tor etek hayal-tor ne', dorian, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu, looking troubled. “kal-tor etek hayal-tor ne'. Heh aishan kilko-srashiv me veh deshker. Ma du pubeglanau svi' wuh bikuv vel curious?—vel ik probably palikauk did ri kwul du, tonk'peh ik revealed itself tor du suddenly?” “basil!” maf-tor wuh lad, clutching wuh kar t' ish-veh ku-san k' trembling el'ru heh gazing na' ish-veh k' kwai startled bezhun. “gla-tor nash-veh du did. Don’t stariben. Bek-tor till du zhu-tor ra i ma tor leralmin. Dorian, s' wuh moment i ragel-tor du, ish-veh nafu'es had wuh danik wehtsuri vi-yumuk abru' me. I vesh' abrukhau, soul, shi'nahp, heh tepul, k' du. Du became tor me wuh visible incarnation t' ik unseen tangu t'vi vokaya haunts etek tanafsu spo' wuh exquisite sahr-tor. I worshipped du. I grew kis-ka t' kanok veh tor ik du stariben. I aitlu ki' du ek' tor myself. I vesh' goh kunli lu i vesh' k' du. Lu du vesh' maf s' me, du vesh' fam dvun la' svi' t'nash-veh tanaf. Veling, i worla kal-tor du fai-tor sovek-vel pa' nash. Ish-veh would ma vesh' impossible. Du would ri ma ken-tor ish-veh. I hardly ken-tor ish-veh myself. I goh fai-tor ik i had gla-tor perfection limuk tor limuk, heh ik wuh panu had shetau wonderful tor t'nash-veh bezhun—nuh' wonderful, sos'eh, na' svi' such mad worships tra' nam-tor peril, wuh peril t' losing au, rai lehkuh do wuh peril t' keeping au. Wehk gad heh wehk gad went fi', heh i grew weht heh weht absorbed svi' du. Yi sarlah wuh uzh storaya. I had drawn du u' paris svi' dainty fo-wein, heh u' adonis k' huntsman’s tor-sai heh polished boar-tilek. Crowned k' ras lotus-blossoms du had hayal-tor fi' wuh prow t' adrian’s tus-hali, gazing mes' wuh yar-kur turbid nile. Du had gal-tor abru' wuh fam dvun patra t' ein greek lap-shal heh gla-tor svi' wuh masu’s ralash-fam haul-tukh wuh marvel t' ish-veh sha' limuk. Heh ish-veh had ek' vesh' ra tanaf dang nam-tor—unconscious, tangu, heh remote. Veh gad, wuh fatal gad i sometimes nah-tor, i satalau tor kras wuh wonderful portrait t' du u' du actually nam-tor, ri svi' wuh costume t' tevik ya'shakhuv, tonk'peh svi' ish-veh sha' sai-vel heh svi' ish-veh sha' wak. Whether ish-veh vesh' wuh realism t' wuh method, il wuh mere wonder t' ish-veh sha' nafu'es, thus directly presented tor me rik' mist il veil, i fam yehat var-tor. Tonk'peh i fai-tor ik u' i ar'kada na' ish-veh, kanok wef heh wontin t' kur seemed tor me tor reveal t'nash-veh tsat. I grew kwes ik vath would fai-tor t' t'nash-veh idolatry. I olau, dorian, ik i had var-tor nuh' mau, ik i had shitau nuh' mau t' myself vi' ish-veh. Yi ish-veh vesh' ik i resolved worla tor kal-tor wuh bikuv tor nam-tor gluvau. Du vesh' wuh pi' annoyed; tonk'peh yi du did ri realize ek' ik ish-veh tvai tor me. Harry, tor ik i variben pa' ish-veh, abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' me. Tonk'peh i did ri kashek ik. Lu wuh bikuv vesh' shahtau, heh i hayal-tor sa'awek k' ish-veh, i olau ik i vesh' gas'rak. Muhl, po' wuh zamu gad wuh vel losrak t'nash-veh studio, heh u' ak u' i had prah rid t' wuh intolerable sem t' its la'es, ish-veh seemed tor me ik i had vesh' duhik svi' imagining ik i had gla-tor sovek-vel svi' ish-veh, weht do ik du vesh' extremely rom-looking heh ik i kupi kras. Kauk i' i fam yehat gol'nev olaya ik ish-veh nam-tor wuh lafosh tor nah-tor ik wuh shaukaush veh olau svi' fereikan nam-tor ek'wak really shown svi' wuh ar'kadan veh fereik-tor. Tanaf nam-tor kwon-hau-ov weht o'zawh do etek fancy. Shid heh kur var-tor etek t' shid heh kur—ik nam-tor ek'. Ish-veh k'ashiv seems tor me ik tanaf ip-sut wuh tanafsu irak weht completely do ish-veh ek'wak reveals ish-veh. Heh ni lu i prah nash nufai s' paris, i satalau tor tor ish-veh portrait wuh principal vel svi' t'nash-veh exhibition. Ish-veh worla paresh-tor tor me ik du would klee'fah. Gla-tor nash-veh i' ik du vesh' gas'rak. Wuh bikuv fam yehat nam-tor shown. Du bolau ri nam-tor reshnek k' me, dorian, na' ra i ma var-tor du. U' i leralmin-tor tor harry, wuh'wak, du nam-tor tor tor nam-tor worshipped.” dorian zhai-kur drew wuh wu esh. Wuh kur sarlah pla' tor ish-veh nak, heh wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut mavau pa' ish-veh bru-lar. Wuh peril vesh' abru'. Au vesh' safe na' wuh wak. Wi au kupi ri gol'nev olaya vaik pity na' wuh krassu vi had aishan tor nash flekh confession tor ish-veh, heh wondered kuv au himself would ek'wak nam-tor ni abrukhau k' wuh nafu'es t' wuh t'hy'la. S'haile henry had wuh sem-rik t' hasu maut tehvar-bosh. Tonk'peh ik vesh' ek'. Au vesh' nuh' clever heh nuh' cynical tor nam-tor really tishau t'. Would tra' ek'wak nam-tor ein veh vi would boshaya ish-veh k' wuh flekh idolatry? Vesh' ish-veh t' wuh vel ik ha'kiv had svi' mahr-kel? “ish-veh nam-tor wehtsuri tor me, dorian, ” leralmin-tor hallward, “ik du dang ma gla-tor nash svi' wuh portrait. Did du really gla-tor ish-veh?” “vesht gla-tor nash-veh vel svi' ish-veh, ” au kilko-tor, “vel ik seemed tor me maut curious.” “muhl, du don’t kashek t'nash-veh looking na' wuh vel i'?” dorian hutau ish-veh patam. “du bolau ri ya'akash me ik, basil. I kupi ri possibly kal-tor du lamok svi' khom t' ik bikuv.” “du dungi ein gad, surely?” “worla.” “muhl, sos'eh du nam-tor gas'rak. Heh i' rom-bye, dorian. Du ma vesh' wuh veh person svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv vi has really vi-yumuk t'nash-veh tanaf. Whatever i ma ovsoh ik nam-tor rom, i owe tor du. Ah! Du don’t fai-tor ra ish-veh kodona me tor var-tor du ek' ik i ma var-tor du.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam basil, ” leralmin-tor dorian, “ra ma du var-tor me? Veling ik du olau ik du krol-tor me nuh' mau. Ik nam-tor ri kauk wuh compliment.” “ish-veh vesh' ri intended u' wuh compliment. Ish-veh vesh' wuh confession. I' ik i ma tor ish-veh, vel seems ki' hal-tor s' me. Sos'eh veh dang worla shitau veh’s worship vi' zhit.” “ish-veh vesh' wuh maut disappointing confession.” “po, ra did du gish, dorian? Du didn’t gla-tor sovek-kitok svi' wuh bikuv, did du? Tra' vesh' nothing else tor gla-tor?” “rai; tra' vesh' nothing else tor gla-tor. Po tor du ya'akash? Tonk'peh du mustn’t variben pa' worship. Ish-veh nam-tor duhik. Du heh i nam-tor t'hylara, basil, heh etek bolau kwon-hau-ov hafau ni.” “du ma prah harry, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu sadly. “oh, harry!” maf-tor wuh lad, k' wuh ripple t' laughter. “harry spends ish-veh gad svi' taran ra nam-tor incredible heh ish-veh khru svi' doing ra nam-tor improbable. Aishan wuh wihfelau t' ha'kiv i would spo' tor ras-tukh. Tonk'peh fam dvun i don’t nah-tor i would hal-tor tor harry kuv i vesh' svi' trouble. I would sooner hal-tor tor du, basil.” “du dungi hayal-tor tor me va'ashiv?” “impossible!” “du spoil t'nash-veh ha'kiv u' wuh tanafsu k' refusing, dorian. Rai sasu sarlah mes' dahkuh tangu vel. Zamu sarlah mes' veh.” “i mokuhlek’t danau ish-veh tor du, basil, tonk'peh i bolau worla hayal-tor tor du va'ashiv. Tra' nam-tor vel fatal pa' wuh portrait. Ish-veh has wuh ha'kiv t' its sha'. I dungi sarlah heh ma theris-masu k' du. Ik dungi nam-tor aishan u' vaksurik.” “pleasanter na' du, i am kwes, ” murmured hallward regretfully. “heh i' rom-bye. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor du skil-tor’t kal-tor me glazhau na' wuh bikuv wuh'wak va'ashiv. Tonk'peh ik mokuhlek’t nam-tor gol-tor. I ved ken-tor ra du olau pa' ish-veh.” u' au losrak wuh tvi-shal, dorian zhai-kur abru'teruklar-ru'lut tor himself. Ri donku-tor basil! Uf pi' au fai-tor t' wuh yeht utvau! Heh uf flekh ish-veh vesh' ik, instead t' having vesh' punekwitau tor reveal ish-veh sha' tsat, au had navau, siyah k' pavesh, svi' wresting wuh tsat s' ish-veh t'hy'la! Uf mau ik flekh confession danau tor ish-veh! Wuh krassu’s absurd nunau t' jealousy, ish-veh kwai vaikaya, ish-veh madonik panegyrics, ish-veh curious reticences—au ken-tor au ek' i', heh au olau sorry. Tra' seemed tor ish-veh tor nam-tor vel tragic svi' wuh friendship ni kur-tor k' romance. Au spes-tevan heh estuhl wuh kus-vakh. Wuh portrait bolau nam-tor ipik maf na' ek' kodona-tor. Au kupi ri sahr-tor such wuh risk t' discovery va'ashiv. Ish-veh had vesh' mad t' ish-veh ki' kal-tor wuh vel tor hafau, kauk na' wuh wadan, svi' wuh tvi-shal tor if sovek t' ish-veh t'hylara had access. Chapter x. Lu ish-veh dvinsu svi-tor, au glazhau na' ish-veh steadfastly heh wondered kuv au had nahp t' peering za' wuh gluvayek. Wuh sasu vesh' ved impassive heh bek-tor na' ish-veh zek. Dorian lit wuh cigarette heh lates-tor abru' tor wuh makh heh glanced vi' ish-veh. Au kupi gla-tor wuh haulan t' skilsu’s limuk perfectly. Ish-veh vesh' spo' wuh placid limein t' servility. Tra' vesh' nothing tor nam-tor kwes t', tra'. Wi au nahp ish-veh buhfik tor nam-tor fi' ish-veh klashausu. Speaking maut slowly, au var-tor ish-veh tor var-tor wuh kelek-keeper ik au aitlu tor gla-tor ish-veh, heh yi tor hal-tor tor wuh nentu-maker heh ya'akash ish-veh tor satau dahkuh t' ish-veh sasu pauk na' wuh'wak. Ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik u' wuh sasu losrak wuh tvi-shal ish-veh bezhun czar-tor svi' wuh kharat t' wuh gluvayek. Il vesh' ik goh ish-veh sha' fancy? Po' wuh zamu moments, svi' ish-veh nesh-kur silk sai-vel, k' hinek-fashioned og-elakh mittens fi' ish-veh wrinkled el'ru, mrs. Mor bustled vi' wuh shi'dunap. Au ya'akash ish-veh na' wuh tal-muv t' wuh schoolroom. “wuh hinek schoolroom, mr. Dorian?” she sporiben. “po, ish-veh nam-tor bosh t' grazhiv. I bolau prah ish-veh arranged heh shitau zehik fa' du hal-tor vi' ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor ri nunau na' du tor gla-tor, osu. Ish-veh nam-tor ri, indeed.” “i don’t aitlun ish-veh shitau zehik, mor. I goh aitlun wuh tal-muv.” “muhl, osu, du’ll nam-tor wein-tor k' cobwebs kuv du hal-tor vi' ish-veh. Po, ish-veh hasn’t vesh' tu'ash na' nearly kaukuh tevun—ri opi' ish-veh lordship tev-tor.” au winced na' wuh mention t' ish-veh sa'mekh'al. Au had hateful vokaya t' ish-veh. “ik tor ri tukh, ” au kilko-tor. “i veling aitlun tor gla-tor wuh shi—ik nam-tor ek'. Mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh tal-muv.” “heh la' nam-tor wuh tal-muv, osu, ” leralmin-tor wuh hinek t'sai, going abru' wuh tuhllar t' ish-veh bunch k' tremulously uncertain el'ru. “la' nam-tor wuh tal-muv. I’ll ma ish-veh ska' wuh bunch svi' wuh moment. Tonk'peh du don’t nah-tor t' living abru tra', osu, heh du ni kel'o la'?” “rai, rai, ” au maf-tor petulantly. “nemaiyo, mor. Ik dungi tor.” she svizh-tor na' wuh zamu moments, heh vesh' garrulous abru' ein detail t' wuh household. Au spes-tevan heh var-tor ish-veh tor khartau vel u' she nahp buhfik. She losrak wuh tvi-shal, wreathed svi' abru'teruklar-ru'lut. U' wuh svep a'ing, dorian shitau wuh tal-muv svi' ish-veh abru'lik heh glazhau pauk wuh tvi-shal. Ish-veh bezhun tevan-tor fi' wuh suk, gahv-kur satin coverlet heavily embroidered k' pi-maat-tukh, wuh splendid krus t' tab-ma seventeenth-century venetian ar'kadan ik ish-veh sa'mekh'al had afer-tor svi' wuh convent be' bologna. Ha, ik would dvin-tor tor wrap wuh dreadful vel svi'. Ish-veh had sos'eh dvin-tor k'ashiv u' wuh pall na' wuh tevik. I' ish-veh vesh' tor ip-sut vel ik had wuh corruption t' its sha', weh-rasahkos do wuh corruption t' tevakh itself—vel ik would kosh-ves horrors heh wi would worla tev-tor. Ra wuh worm vesh' tor wuh tevikeh, ish-veh sins would nam-tor tor wuh kras-tor glakuv fi' wuh canvas. Au would mar its vaksur heh yokul maf its takov. Au would defile ish-veh heh tor ish-veh shameful. Heh wi wuh vel would fam dvun ha-tor fi'. Ish-veh would nam-tor kwon-hau-ov alive. Au ak'shem-hutau, heh na' wuh moment au regretted ik au had ri var-tor basil wuh yeht utvau po au had istau tor ip-sut wuh bikuv maf. Basil would ma gol-tor ish-veh tor tehnau s'haile henry’s vi-yumuk, heh wuh fam dvun weht poisonous vi-yumuk ik sarlah s' ish-veh sha' temperament. Wuh ashaya ik au spitau ish-veh—na' ish-veh vesh' really ashaya—had nothing svi' ish-veh ik vesh' ri thol heh intellectual. Ish-veh vesh' ri ik mere tukhik admiration t' vaksur ik nam-tor pukeshta t' wuh kash-ral heh ik tev-tor lu wuh kash-ral zung-tor. Ish-veh vesh' such ashaya u' michelangelo had fainu, heh montaigne, heh winckelmann, heh shakespeare himself. Ha, basil kupi ma korsau ish-veh. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' nuh' tab-ma i'. Wuh vesht kupi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor annihilated. Regret, wafaya, il forgetfulness kupi tor ik. Tonk'peh wuh fa-wak vesh' inevitable. Tra' vesh' shaukaush svi' ish-veh ik would talal ish-veh terrible sek, sahr-tor-tor ik would tor wuh duv t' ish-veh ek'rasah yeht. Au nem-tor abru s' wuh ku-san wuh lo'uk gahv-kur-heh-pi-maat-tukh lef'es ik wein-tor ish-veh, heh, holding ish-veh svi' ish-veh el'ru, be' dvun-tor za' wuh gluvayek. Vesh' wuh limuk fi' wuh canvas viler do fa'? Ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik ish-veh vesh' unchanged, heh wi ish-veh loathing t' ish-veh vesh' intensified. Pi-maat-tukh isachya, pla-kur bezhun, heh she-tor-yon-kur bru-lar—au ek' vesh' tra'. Ish-veh vesh' veling wuh sagluvaya ik had rubitau. Ik vesh' horrible svi' its cruelty. Tcok'at tor ra gla-tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh t' censure il rebuke, uf gan basil’s reproaches pa' sibyl vane had vesh'!—uf gan, heh t' ra pi' khrosahp! Ish-veh sha' soul vesh' looking si' na' ish-veh s' wuh canvas heh calling ish-veh tor judgement. Wuh glazhau t' kusut sarlah mes' ish-veh, heh au flung wuh don-ka pall abru' wuh bikuv. U' au did ni, wuh knock sarlah tor wuh svep. Au be' dvun-tor si' u' ish-veh dvinsu svi-tor. “wuh persons nam-tor la', monsieur.” au olau ik wuh sasu bolau nam-tor prah rid t' na' wuh'wak. Au bolau ri nam-tor kal-tor tor fai-tor wilat wuh bikuv vesh' hasu taken tor. Tra' vesh' vel sly pa' ish-veh, heh au had thoughtful, treacherous bezhun. Sitting ne' na' wuh kitaun-pasu au scribbled wuh pitoh tor s'haile henry, asking ish-veh tor satau ish-veh pauk vel tor telv-tor heh reminding ish-veh ik au vesh' tor ragel-tor na' ohkuh-leh-kau ik khru. “bek-tor na' wuh kilko-srashiv, ” au leralmin-tor, handing ish-veh tor ish-veh, “heh gluvaya wuh sasu svi' la'.” svi' dahkuh il rehkuh minutes tra' vesh' wuh'ashiv knock, heh mr. Hubbard himself, wuh u'thet nentu-maker t' khu'rak audley yut, sarlah svi' k' wuh somewhat rough-looking nu'ri assistant. Mr. Hubbard vesh' wuh florid, yon-kur-whiskered pi' sasu, t'vi admiration na' tanaf vesh' considerably tempered k' wuh inveterate impecuniosity t' danik t' wuh tanafsu vi dealt k' ish-veh. U' wuh tor-go, au worla losrak ish-veh mahr-kel. Au bek-tor na' sutra tor sarlah tor ish-veh. Tonk'peh au kwon-hau-ov tor wuh kaulauf svi' favour t' dorian zhai-kur. Tra' vesh' vel pa' dorian ik sem-rik-tor kanok-veh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh sanosh kauk tor gla-tor ish-veh. “ra mokuhlek i tor na' du, mr. Zhai-kur?” au leralmin-tor, rubbing ish-veh thelik freckled el'ru. “i nahp i would tor myself wuh dor t' coming pauk svi' person. I ma aishan prah wuh vaksur t' wuh nentu, osu. Picked ish-veh abru na' wuh sale. Hinek florentine. Sarlah s' fonthill, i dva-tor. Admirably suited na' wuh religious subject, mr. Zhai-kur.” “i am ni sorry du ma putan-tor yourself wuh trouble t' coming pauk, mr. Hubbard. I dungau certainly eku svi' heh glazhau na' wuh nentu—hi i don’t hal-tor svi' mau na' la' na' religious tanaf—tonk'peh tor-gad i goh aitlun wuh bikuv lesh tor wuh fik t' wuh kelek na' me. Ish-veh nam-tor rather ras, ni i nahp i would ya'akash du tor lend me wuh couple t' ish-veh sasu.” “rai trouble na' ek', mr. Zhai-kur. I am delighted tor nam-tor t' sovek dvin tor du. If nam-tor wuh ar'kadan t' tanaf, osu?” “nash, ” kilko-tor dorian, dvun-tor wuh gluvayek pla'. “mokuhlek du dvun ish-veh, covering heh ek', aishan u' ish-veh nam-tor? I don’t aitlun ish-veh tor prah scratched going upstairs.” “tra' dungi nam-tor rai rihag'es, osu, ” leralmin-tor wuh genial nentu-maker, palikaya, k' wuh mamuk t' ish-veh assistant, tor unhook wuh bikuv s' wuh wu dvesh-tukh naf-elakh k' if ish-veh vesh' suspended. “heh, i', wilat dungau etek lesh ish-veh tor, mr. Zhai-kur?” “i dungi gluvaya du wuh yut, mr. Hubbard, kuv du dungi kindly zahal-tor me. Il sos'eh du had weh-rom hal-tor svi' khom. I am kwes ish-veh nam-tor gas'rak na' wuh fik t' wuh kelek. Etek dungi hal-tor abru k' wuh khom staircase, u' ish-veh nam-tor wider.” au meskarau wuh svep tu'ash na' au, heh au be' dvun-tor si' vi' wuh tvur heh began wuh shen. Wuh elaborate character t' wuh nentu had tor wuh bikuv extremely bulky, heh i' heh yi, svi' spite t' wuh obsequious protests t' mr. Hubbard, vi had wuh yeht tradesman’s spirited ritishaya t' seeing wuh gentleman doing sovek-vel useful, dorian shitau ish-veh el'ru tor ish-veh ni u' tor gol'nev au. “vel t' wuh tus tor lesh, osu, ” hushau wuh pi' sasu lu au pulau wuh fik landing. Heh au psethau ish-veh shiny fa-patam. “i am kwes ish-veh nam-tor rather ras, ” murmured dorian u' au unlocked wuh svep ik tu'ash vi' wuh tvi-shal ik vesh' tor potau na' ish-veh wuh curious tsat t' ish-veh ha'kiv heh ip-sut ish-veh soul s' wuh bezhun t' sasu. Au had ri svi-tor wuh shi na' weht do kehkuh tevun—ri, indeed, opi' au had nam-tor-tor ish-veh wuh'rak u' wuh mavau-tvi-shal lu au vesh' wuh kan, heh yi u' wuh orenau lu au grew somewhat older. Ish-veh vesh' wuh suk, muhl-proportioned tvi-shal, if had vesh' specially torvau k' wuh kim-shah s'haile kelso na' wuh nam-tor-tor t' wuh pi' grandson ik, na' ish-veh flekh likeness tor ish-veh ko-mekh, heh isha na' vath utvau, au had kwon-hau-ov fnu-ven heh aitlu tor potau na' wuh ir. Ish-veh saudau tor dorian ki' tonk'peh pi' rubai. Tra' vesh' wuh masuk' italian _cassone_, k' its fantastically kras-tor gluvau-math heh its tarnished gilt mouldings, svi' if au had ni k'ashiv ipik himself u' wuh sa-kan. Tra' wuh satinwood dunap-nuf boshau k' ish-veh dog-eared schoolbooks. Fi' wuh temok za' ish-veh vesh' hanging wuh ka ragged flemish tapestry wilat wuh spoh-tor sa-te'kru heh ko-te'kru vesh' mavaun chess svi' wuh bah-ker, du' wuh apc'koik t' hawkers fau-tor k', carrying hooded kushel fi' ish-veh gauntleted kar-nik. Uf muhl au vokau ish-veh ek'! Kanok moment t' ish-veh lonely kan-wak sarlah pla' tor ish-veh u' au glazhau pauk. Au recalled wuh stainless purity t' ish-veh boyish ha'kiv, heh ish-veh seemed horrible tor ish-veh ik ish-veh vesh' la' wuh fatal portrait vesh' tor nam-tor ipik maf. Uf pi' au had nahp, svi' eifa tevik gad, t' ek' ik vesh' svi' mahr-kel na' ish-veh! Tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai vath shi svi' wuh kelek ni shar s' prying bezhun u' nash. Au had wuh tal-muv, heh kling else kupi svi-tor ish-veh. Ne'rak its gahv-kur pall, wuh limuk kras-tor fi' wuh canvas kupi tor'ovau bestial, sodden, heh unclean. Ra did ish-veh tukh? Kling kupi gla-tor ish-veh. Au himself would ri gla-tor ish-veh. Po dang au glantau wuh hideous corruption t' ish-veh soul? Au potau ish-veh youth—ik vesh' hiyet. Heh, isha, lau ri ish-veh malat tor'ovau finer, po' ek'? Tra' vesh' rai utvau ik wuh fa-wak dang nam-tor ni bosh t' mesh. Ein ashaya lau sarlah mes' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh purify ish-veh, heh fo-dan ish-veh s' eifa sins ik seemed tor nam-tor already stirring svi' tam'a heh svi' kahm—eifa curious unpictured sins t'vi maut mystery lent au ish-veh subtlety heh ish-veh sem-rik. Sos'eh, ein gad, wuh pi-maat'rer glazhau would ma be' dvun-tor maf s' wuh ug'yon-kur kash-zakar ru'lut, heh au lau gluvaya tor wuh panu basil hallward’s masterpiece. Rai; ik vesh' impossible. Wadan k' wadan, heh wehk gad k' wehk gad, wuh vel fi-tor wuh canvas vesh' growing hinek. Ish-veh lau stron wuh hideousness t' sin, tonk'peh wuh hideousness t' ya'shakhuv vesh' svi' mahr-kel na' ish-veh. Wuh nak would shetau hollow il nemosik. Kin-kur kushel’s ash'ya would creep pauk wuh fading bezhun heh tor au horrible. Wuh isachya would pak-tor its ugel'es, wuh ru'lut would gape il tevan-tor, would nam-tor duhik il gross, u' wuh ru'lut t' hinek sasu nam-tor. Tra' would nam-tor wuh wrinkled drahk, wuh samu, pla-kur-veined el'ru, wuh kuvoran-tor ak'shem, ik au vokau svi' wuh sa'mekh'al vi had vesh' ni harr-krus tor ish-veh svi' ish-veh boyhood. Wuh bikuv had tor nam-tor ip-sut. Tra' vesh' rai gol'nev na' ish-veh. “katau ish-veh svi', mr. Hubbard, sanoi, ” au leralmin-tor, wearily, turning pauk. “i am sorry i potau du ni wu. I vesh' thinking t' vel else.” “kwon-hau-ov glad ki' wuh shom, mr. Zhai-kur, ” kilko-tor wuh nentu-maker, vi vesh' fam dvun gasping na' esh. “wilat dungau etek shitau ish-veh, osu?” “oh, sovek-wilat. La': nash dungi tor. I don’t aitlun ki' ish-veh geldau abru. Aishan galat ish-veh tehnat wuh temok. Itaren.” “lau veh glazhau na' wuh ar'kadan t' tanaf, osu?” dorian palikau. “ish-veh would ri eku'ko du, mr. Hubbard, ” au leralmin-tor, keeping ish-veh bezhun fi' wuh sasu. Au olau pok tor leap fi-tor ish-veh heh fling ish-veh tor wuh solektra kuv au dared tor abertau wuh gorgeous hanging ik ip-sut wuh tsat t' ish-veh ha'kiv. “i shan’t trouble du sovek weht i'. I am mau obliged na' ish-veh kindness svi' coming pauk.” “mokov, mokov, mr. Zhai-kur. Ek'wak pok tor tor sovek-vel na' du, osu.” heh mr. Hubbard tramped downstairs, zahal-tor k' wuh assistant, vi glanced pla' na' dorian k' wuh glazhau t' fusik wonder svi' ish-veh rough uncomely limuk. Au had worla gla-tor sovek veh ni marvellous. Lu wuh ralash t' ish-veh footsteps had tev-tor maf, dorian klacha wuh svep heh shitau wuh tal-muv svi' ish-veh abru'lik. Au olau safe i'. Kling would ek'wak glazhau fi-tor wuh horrible vel. Rai bezhun tonk'peh ish-veh would ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh mesh. Fi' reaching wuh shi'dunap, au afer-tor ik ish-veh vesh' aishan po' kaukuh o’wak-vel heh ik wuh theris-masu had vesh' already katau abru. Fi' wuh pi' pasu t' gu'gelik perfumed lapan bali papuhnkau k' ba'hun'ahb, wuh la' s' t'sai radley, ish-veh guardian’s ko-telsu, wuh takov professional invalid vi had spent wuh preceding karil svi' cairo, vesh' lying wuh pitoh s' s'haile henry, heh be' ish-veh vesh' wuh dunap bound svi' kin-kur dun, wuh wein slightly torn heh wuh rihk soiled. Wuh va'asau t' wuh wuh yadan t' _the st. James’s gazette_ had vesh' shitau fi' wuh theris-masu-tray. Ish-veh vesh' evident ik skilsu had fun-tor. Au wondered kuv au had ragel-tor wuh sasu svi' wuh tvur u' au vesh' leaving wuh kelek heh had wormed s' au ra au had vesh' doing. Au would nam-tor sure tor din-tor wuh bikuv—had rai vet din-tor ish-veh already, du' au had vesh' laying wuh theris-masu-vel. Wuh gluvayek had ri vesh' eku pla', heh wuh blank ret vesh' visible fi' wuh temok. Sos'eh ein mu-yor au lau talal ish-veh creeping upstairs heh trying tor nekwitaya wuh svep t' wuh tvi-shal. Ish-veh vesh' wuh horrible vel ki' wuh zamasu svi' veh’s kelek. Au had puzhu-tor t' don-ka sasu vi had vesh' blackmailed ek' ish-veh ha-tor k' ein dvinsu vi had telv-tor wuh nuhm, il overheard wuh conversation, il picked abru wuh nop k' wuh shi'yavekh, il afer-tor ne'rak wuh trak wuh withered svai il wuh tresahk-tor t' crumpled lace. Au spes-tevan, heh having mukau himself si' ein theris-masu, tu'ash s'haile henry’s pitoh. Ish-veh vesh' veling tor leralmin ik au satau ish-veh pauk wuh khru dun, heh wuh dunap ik lau eku'ko ish-veh, heh ik au would nam-tor na' wuh muhd na' ohkuh-leh-kau. Au tu'ash _the st. James’s_ languidly, heh glazhau k'fai ish-veh. Wuh yon-kur hish-ulidar fi' wuh fifth thalv kum-tor ish-veh bezhun. Ish-veh drew attention tor wuh zahalik paragraph: inquest fi' wuh fundauik-ithop.—wuh inquest vesh' meskarau nash asal na' wuh kus-vakh tavern, hoxton fau-yut, k' mr. Danby, wuh kahkrus tevanu-talsu, fi' wuh ak'shem t' sibyl vane, wuh nu'ri fundauik-ithop recently engaged na' wuh royal theatre, holborn. Wuh verdict t' tevakh k' misadventure vesh' fun-tor. Considerable sympathy vesh' sagluvau na' wuh ko-mekh t' wuh tevik, vi vesh' greatly dau du' wuh giving t' ish-veh sha' evidence, heh ik t' dr. Birrell, vi had tor wuh lehk-mortem linisaya t' wuh tevik. Au kwal-tor, heh tearing wuh dun svi' dahkuh, went mes' wuh tvi-shal heh flung wuh krus maf. Uf watosh ish-veh ek' vesh'! Heh uf horribly yeht ugliness tor vel! Au olau wuh pi' annoyed k' s'haile henry na' having satau ish-veh wuh report. Heh ish-veh vesh' certainly stupid t' ish-veh ki' pu'ulidau ish-veh k' yon-kur hish. Skilsu lau ma telv-tor ish-veh. Wuh sasu fai-tor weht do hiyet eingelsu na' ik. Sos'eh au had telv-tor ish-veh heh had palikau tor suspect vel. Heh, wi, ra did ish-veh tukh? Ra had dorian zhai-kur tor tor k' sibyl vane’s tevakh? Tra' vesh' nothing tor pthak. Dorian zhai-kur had ri pustau ish-veh. Ish-veh bezhun tevan-tor fi' wuh kin-kur dunap ik s'haile henry had satau ish-veh. Ra vesh' ish-veh, au wondered. Au went na' wuh pi', pearl-kur-tor octagonal lamok ik had kwon-hau-ov glazhau tor ish-veh spo' wuh ar'kadan t' ein flekh egyptian bees ik wrought svi' haul-tukh, heh taking abru wuh ral'es, flung himself vi' wuh kar-ku-san heh began tor da-tor abru' wuh mor. Po' wuh zamu minutes au became absorbed. Ish-veh vesh' wuh strangest dunap ik au had ek'wak telv-tor. Ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik svi' exquisite raiment, heh tor wuh delicate ralash t' kolchak, wuh sins t' wuh panu vesh' be' dvun-tor svi' dumb gluvaya fa' ish-veh. Vel ik au had dimly sahr-tor-tor t' vesh' suddenly tor yeht tor ish-veh. Vel t' if au had worla sahr-tor-tor vesh' gradually revealed. Ish-veh vesh' wuh dunap rik' wuh besau heh k' goh veh character, hasu, indeed, veling wuh psychological orenau t' wuh ac'ruth nu'ri parisian vi spent ish-veh ha'kiv trying tor realize svi' wuh nineteenth century ek' wuh shaukaush heh nuk t' nahp ik belonged tor kanok century kaula ish-veh sha', heh tor hau-ov abru, u' ish-veh vesh', svi' himself wuh vuhnauk moods k'fai if wuh panu-tam'a had ek'wak be' dvun-tor, loving na' ish-veh mere artificiality eifa renunciations ik sasu ma unwisely puvutau virtue, u' mau u' eifa malatik rebellions ik kau-bosh sasu fam dvun vutau sin. Wuh style svi' if ish-veh vesh' written vesh' ik curious jewelled style, vivid heh obscure na' wuh'wak, bosh t' _argot_ heh t' archaisms, t' ek'mishupik sagluvaya heh t' elaborate paraphrases, ik characterizes wuh ar'kadan t' ein t' wuh finest tanafsu t' wuh french shi'oren t' _symbolistes_. Tra' vesh' svi' ish-veh metaphors u' monstrous u' orchids heh u' subtle svi' kur. Wuh ha'kiv t' wuh kash-ral vesh' kethelvau svi' wuh zhil t' mystical ven-dol-leralmin. Veh hardly fai-tor na' wak whether veh vesh' telvan wuh spiritual ecstasies t' ein mediæval osu il wuh morbid confessions t' wuh iyik sinner. Ish-veh vesh' wuh poisonous dunap. Wuh ras vil t' incense seemed tor cling pa' its thalv heh tor trouble wuh shi'nahp. Wuh mere cadence t' wuh zhit-bal, wuh subtle monotony t' ish-veh ralash-tanaf, ni bosh u' ish-veh vesh' t' wehkonik refrains heh dvun elaborately ashiv-tor, torvau svi' wuh kashek t' wuh lad, u' au be' dvun-tor s' chapter tor chapter, wuh shid t' reverie, wuh malady t' dreaming, ik tor ish-veh unconscious t' wuh tevan-tor gad heh creeping duv. Cloudless, heh tilau k' veh solitary yel, wuh khaf-tukh-yar-kur igen gleamed k'fai wuh krani. Au telv-tor fi' k' its wan ta'hal till au kupi telv-tor rai weht. Yi, po' ish-veh valet had reminded ish-veh several wak t' wuh lateness t' wuh wadan, au prah abru, heh going vi' wuh thurai tvi-shal, shitau wuh dunap fi' wuh pi' florentine pasu ik kwon-hau-ov lam-tor na' ish-veh bedside heh began sai-vel-tor na' aru-yem. Ish-veh vesh' siyah naukuh o’wak-vel fa' au pulau wuh muhd, wilat au afer-tor s'haile henry sitting sa'awek, svi' wuh asal-tvi-shal, looking maut mau bored. “i am ni sorry, harry, ” au maf-tor, “tonk'peh really ish-veh nam-tor entirely ish-veh lafot. Ik dunap du satau me ni sem-tor me ik i forgot uf wuh wak vesh' going.” “ha, i nahp du would spo' ish-veh, ” kilko-tor ish-veh kasu, rising s' ish-veh ku-san. “i didn’t leralmin i tishau ish-veh, harry. I leralmin-tor ish-veh sem-tor me. Tra' nam-tor wuh lo'uk natyan.” “ah, du ma discovered ik?” murmured s'haile henry. Heh au be' dvun-tor vi' wuh dining-tvi-shal. Chapter xi. Na' tevun, dorian zhai-kur kupi ri elik himself s' wuh vi-yumuk t' nash dunap. Il sos'eh ish-veh would nam-tor weht accurate tor leralmin ik au worla sought tor elik himself s' ish-veh. Au procured s' paris rai lehkuh tor naukuh suk-dun va'asau t' wuh wuh'rak yadan, heh had au bound svi' natya colours, ni ik au lau saikhut ish-veh vuhnauk moods heh wuh rubai fancies t' wuh malat abru' if au seemed, na' wak, ki' siyah entirely pakik tash. Wuh hero, wuh wonderful nu'ri parisian svi' ik wuh romantic heh wuh talik temperaments vesh' ni strangely herish-tor, became tor ish-veh wuh ves t' prefiguring ves t' himself. Heh, indeed, wuh bosh dunap seemed tor ish-veh tor tuhlau wuh var t' ish-veh sha' ha'kiv, written fa' au had ha-tor ish-veh. Svi' veh sfek au vesh' weht fortunate do wuh dunap’s fantastic hero. Au worla fai-tor—worla, indeed, had sovek aishan tor fai-tor—ik somewhat grotesque dread t' haulat, heh polished mokev skonn, heh fam dvun masu if sarlah fi-tor wuh nu'ri parisian ni lehkuh-mal svi' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh vesh' occasioned k' wuh sudden nehaya t' wuh beau ik had wuh'wak, sauyaing, vesh' ni remarkable. Ish-veh vesh' k' wuh siyah pi-maat'rer mak—heh sos'eh svi' nearly kanok mak, u' certainly svi' kanok sanosh, cruelty has its shi—ik au nam-tor-tor tor telv-tor wuh latter krus t' wuh dunap, k' its really tragic, kuv somewhat overemphasized, khrosahp t' wuh sorrow heh despair t' veh vi had himself pakik ra svi' vath, heh wuh panu, au had danik dearly valued. Na' wuh wonderful vaksur ik had ni sem-tor basil hallward, heh wehk vath isha ish-veh, seemed worla tor trasha ish-veh. Kauk eifa vi had puzhu-tor wuh danik ek'rasah vel tehnat ish-veh—heh s' wak tor wak flekh rumours pa' ish-veh nuk t' ha'kiv crept k'fai london heh became wuh chatter t' wuh muhd—kupi ri dva-tor sovek-vel tor ish-veh dishonour lu gla-tor au ish-veh. Au had kwon-hau-ov wuh glazhau t' veh vi had potau himself unspotted s' wuh panu. Sasu vi variben grossly became ralash-fam lu dorian zhai-kur svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. Tra' vesh' vel svi' wuh purity t' ish-veh limuk ik rebuked au. Ish-veh mere la'es seemed tor recall tor au wuh vokaya t' wuh innocence ik au had tarnished. Au wondered uf veh ni sem-rik-tor heh graceful u' au vesh' kupi ma stron-tor wuh kuraya t' wuh ya'shakhuv ik vesh' na' wuh'wak sordid heh sensual. K'ashiv, fi' returning ha-kel s' veh t' eifa mysterious heh prolonged absences ik mazhiv-kur-tor shen tor such flekh conjecture among eifa vi vesh' ish-veh t'hylara, il nahp ik au vesh' ni, au himself would creep upstairs tor wuh klacha tvi-shal, tu'ash wuh svep k' wuh tal-muv ik worla losrak ish-veh i', heh lamok, k' wuh haulat, svi' khom t' wuh portrait ik basil hallward had kras-tor t' ish-veh, looking i' na' wuh ek'rasah heh shakhuvaya limuk fi' wuh canvas, heh i' na' wuh rom nu'ri limuk ik abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor pla' na' ish-veh s' wuh polished makh. Wuh maut sharpness t' wuh contrast nam-tor-tor tor quicken ish-veh kash-ral t' sanosh. Au grew weht heh weht enamoured t' ish-veh sha' vaksur, weht heh weht interested svi' wuh corruption t' ish-veh sha' soul. Au would linisau k' minute tun, heh sometimes k' wuh monstrous heh terrible delight, wuh hideous zehl ik seared wuh wrinkling fa-patam il ukrau pa' wuh ras sensual ru'lut, wondering sometimes if vesh' wuh weht horrible, wuh glat t' sin il wuh glat t' ya'shakhuv. Au would shi ish-veh wan-kur el'ru be' wuh dirik bloated el'ru t' wuh bikuv, heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Au mocked wuh misshapen ak'shem heh wuh failing sikrus. Tra' vesh' moments, indeed, na' mu-yor, lu, lying sleepless svi' ish-veh sha' delicately scented tvi-shal, il svi' wuh sordid tvi-shal t' wuh pi' has-bosh-famed tavern be' wuh kifau if, ne' wuh assumed ahm heh svi' pasut, ish-veh vesh' ish-veh es'merka tor vakavik, au would nah-tor t' wuh ruin au had katau fi-tor ish-veh soul k' wuh pity ik vesh' ek' wuh weht poignant fai'ei ish-veh vesh' purely selfish. Tonk'peh moments such u' aifa vesh' ritsuri. Ik curiosity pa' ha'kiv if s'haile henry had wuh'rak stirred svi' ish-veh, u' au hayal-tor teretuhr svi' wuh bah-ker t' ish-veh t'hy'la, seemed tor increase k' gratification. Wuh weht au fai-tor, wuh weht au aitlu tor fai-tor. Au had mad avon-telik ik grew weht ravenous u' au puyem-tot au. Wi au vesh' ri really reckless, na' sovek tav svi' ish-veh relations tor shila'es. Wuh'wak il dah'wak kanok tevun-krus du' wuh karil, heh fi' tik gad khru du' wuh tevun-yonuk palesh-tor, au would lehm tu'ash tor wuh panu ish-veh vaksurik kelek heh ma wuh danik u'thet ralash-tanafsu t' wuh gad tor sem-rik ish-veh be'hai'la k' wuh wonders t' ish-veh tanaf. Ish-veh pi' aru-yem, svi' wuh settling t' if s'haile henry kwon-hau-ov gol-tor ish-veh, vesh' noted u' mau na' wuh tun-bosh dvel heh placing t' eifa invited, u' na' wuh exquisite zahvan shown svi' wuh decoration t' wuh pasu, k' its subtle symphonic arrangements t' akan svai, heh embroidered sai, heh ek'hinek-vel math t' pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh. Indeed, tra' vesh' wehk, wa' among wuh maut nu'ri sasu, vi gla-tor, il fancied ik gla-tor au, svi' dorian zhai-kur wuh yeht realization t' wuh ves t' if au had k'ashiv sahr-tor-tor svi' eton il oxford gad, wuh ves ik vesh' tor terish-tor vel t' wuh yeht iyula t' wuh scholar k' ek' wuh takov heh distinction heh buhfik manner t' wuh citizen t' wuh panu. Tor au au seemed tor nam-tor t' wuh apc'koik t' eifa ik dante kethelvau u' having sought tor “tor themselves buhfik k' wuh worship t' vaksur.” spo' gautier, au vesh' veh na' ik “wuh visible panu nam-tor.” heh, certainly, tor ish-veh ha'kiv itself vesh' wuh wuh'rak, wuh greatest, t' wuh arts, heh na' ish-veh ek' wuh vath arts seemed tor nam-tor tonk'peh wuh preparation. Fashion, k' if ra nam-tor really fantastic shetau na' wuh moment universal, heh dandyism, if, svi' its sha' yut, nam-tor wuh attempt tor seo'a wuh ek'esik modernity t' vaksur, had, veling, ish-veh sem na' ish-veh. Ish-veh nuk t' sai-vel-tor, heh wuh particular styles ik s' wak tor wak au dau, had ish-veh pu'ulidau vi-yumuk fi' wuh nu'ri exquisites t' wuh mayfair rin'k'n heh pall mall muhd krani, vi va'asau ish-veh svi' kanok-vei ik au did, heh ar'kada tor reproduce wuh ur'kif sem-rik t' ish-veh graceful, hi tor ish-veh goh ulef-serious, fopperies. Na', du' au vesh' tonk'peh nuh' pok tor nar-tor wuh shul ik vesh' siyah iyi nufau tor ish-veh fi' ish-veh coming t' ya'shakhuv, heh afer-tor, indeed, wuh subtle sanosh svi' wuh nahp ik au lau really shetau tor wuh london t' ish-veh sha' gad ra tor imperial neronian rome wuh kitausu t' wuh satyricon wuh'wak had vesh', wi svi' ish-veh inmost khaf-spol au aitlu tor nam-tor vel weht do wuh mere _arbiter elegantiarum_, tor nam-tor consulted fi' wuh sai-vel-tor t' wuh ek'zer, il wuh knotting t' wuh necktie, il wuh spa-tor t' wuh cane. Au sought tor elaborate ein uzh scheme t' ha'kiv ik would ma its reasoned ven-dol-leralmin heh its ordered dvatai, heh talal svi' wuh spiritualizing t' wuh kash-ral its k'lek realization. Wuh worship t' wuh kash-ral has k'ashiv, heh k' mau yeht-gav, vesh' decried, sasu olaya wuh malatik instinct t' vash pa' shaukaush heh kashan ik seem stronger do themselves, heh ik au nam-tor d'wonil t' thresh-tor k' wuh lehkuh highly organized shidau t' nam. Tonk'peh ish-veh saudau tor dorian zhai-kur ik wuh yeht malat t' wuh kash-ral had worla vesh' ken-tor, heh ik au had hafau savage heh aushfa goh fai'ei wuh panu had sought tor starve au vi' nekhaya il tor stau au k' kusut, instead t' aiming na' tor au meilak t' wuh uzh kator-dva, t' if wuh tok-ti instinct na' vaksur vesh' tor nam-tor wuh abrupik noshtra. U' au glazhau pla' fi-tor sasu dvun-tor k'fai vesht-var, au vesh' haunted k' wuh olaya t' pak. Ni mau had vesh' surrendered! Heh tor such pi' lof! Tra' had vesh' mad wilful rejections, monstrous shidau t' shal-torture heh shal-wafaya, t'vi tveshu vesh' pthak heh t'vi result vesh' wuh degradation infinitely weht terrible do ik fancied degradation s' if, svi' ish-veh ignorance, au had sought tor stron; malat, svi' ish-veh wonderful irony, driving si' wuh anchorite tor yem-tor k' wuh kwai animals t' wuh eshikh heh giving tor wuh hermit wuh beasts t' wuh vunai u' ish-veh besu. Ha: tra' vesh' tor nam-tor, u' s'haile henry had prophesied, wuh uzh hedonism ik vesh' tor recreate ha'kiv heh tor korsau ish-veh s' ik harsh uncomely puritanism ik nam-tor having, svi' etwel sha' gad, its curious revival. Ish-veh vesh' ki' its dvin t' wuh kash-tor-vel, certainly, wi ish-veh vesh' worla tor nar-tor sovek wihka il torektra ik would involve wuh sacrifice t' sovek nuk t' passionate veshtaya. Its mokh, indeed, vesh' tor nam-tor veshtaya itself, heh ri wuh savas t' veshtaya, slor il sfith(-) u' au lau nam-tor. T' wuh asceticism ik deadens wuh kash-ral, u' t' wuh vulgar profligacy ik dulls au, ish-veh vesh' tor fai-tor nothing. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' tor saven-tor sasu tor concentrate himself fi-tor wuh moments t' wuh ha'kiv ik nam-tor itself tonk'peh wuh moment. Tra' nam-tor zamu t' etek vi ma ri sometimes wakened fa' gad-keshtan, either po' veh t' eifa dreamless mu-yor ik tor etek siyah enamoured t' tevakh, il veh t' eifa mu-yor t' horror heh misshapen mak, lu k'fai wuh tvi-shal t' wuh shi'nahp fnashtaya phantoms weht terrible do reality itself, heh instinct k' ik vivid ha'kiv ik lurks svi' ek' grotesques, heh ik lends tor gothic tanaf its enduring vitality, nash tanaf hasu, veh lau fancy, wa' wuh tanaf t' eifa t'vi kashkau ma vesh' troubled k' wuh malady t' reverie. Gradually wan-kur ozh creep k'fai wuh curtains, heh au saudau tor tremble. Svi' nesh-kur fantastic shid, dumb duv ukrau vi' wuh teruk t' wuh tvi-shal heh crouch tra'. S'udish, tra' nam-tor wuh stirring t' kushel among wuh mor, il wuh ralash t' sasu going forth tor ish-veh ar'kadan, il wuh spes-tevan heh sob t' wuh salan coming ne' s' wuh kunel heh wandering pauk wuh ralash-fam kelek, u' hi ish-veh ptha tor wake wuh sleepers heh wi bolau bolau vutau forth yuk s' ish-veh gahv-kur tauk. Veil po' veil t' wonil dusky gauze nam-tor abertau, heh k' degrees wuh shidau heh colours t' vel nam-tor restored tor au, heh etek glantau wuh gad-keshtan remaking wuh panu svi' its ek'hinek-vel nel-dath. Wuh wan haulat zaprah ish-veh va'amau ha'kiv. Wuh flameless tapers lamok wilat etek had losrak au, heh be' au ti wuh ulef-tresahk dunap ik etek had vesh' studying, il wuh wired svai ik etek had worn na' wuh rin'k'n, il wuh nuhm ik etek had vesh' kwes tor telv-tor, il ik etek had telv-tor nuh' k'ashiv. Nothing seems tor etek rubai. S' wuh unreal duv t' wuh mu-yor sarlah pla' wuh yeht ha'kiv ik etek had fainu. Etek ma tor resume ish-veh wilat etek had losrak ska', heh tra' vazgau abru' etek wuh terrible kash-ral t' wuh bolayek na' wuh continuance t' tepul svi' wuh ka wearisome pauk t' stereotyped es'merka, il wuh kwai longing, ish-veh lau nam-tor, ik etwel bezhun-wein lau tu'ash ein asal fi-tor wuh panu ik had vesh' refashioned anew svi' wuh mu'khlup'es na' etwel sanosh, wuh panu svi' if vel would ma sluk shid heh colours, heh nam-tor rubai, il ma vath tsat, wuh panu svi' if wuh vesht would ma pi' il rai shi, il rish-tor, na' sovek tav, svi' rai d'wonil shid t' obligation il regret, wuh remembrance kauk t' mak having its bitterness heh wuh vokaya t' sanosh ish-veh kusut. Ish-veh vesh' wuh fereikan t' such panu u' aifa ik seemed tor dorian zhai-kur tor nam-tor wuh yeht vel, il svi' wuh yeht vel, t' ha'kiv; heh svi' ish-veh psthan na' kashan ik would nam-tor na' wuh'wak uzh heh delightful, heh ma ik meilak t' strangeness ik nam-tor ni bolayatik tor romance, au would k'ashiv thanai ac'ruth nuk t' nahp ik au fai-tor tor nam-tor really akansu tor ish-veh malat, abandon himself tor ish-veh subtle vi-yumuk, heh yi, having, u' ish-veh vesh', kum-tor ish-veh kur heh satisfied ish-veh intellectual curiosity, trasha au k' ik curious indifference ik nam-tor ri incompatible k' wuh yeht ardour t' temperament, heh ik, indeed, fupa s' ac'ruth iyik kloshai-talsu, nam-tor k'ashiv wuh nosh t' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' rumoured t' ish-veh wuh'wak ik au vesh' pa' tor hau wuh roman catholic communion, heh certainly wuh roman ho-rah had kwon-hau-ov wuh lo'uk skamaya na' ish-veh. Wuh kanok-gadik sacrifice, weht awful really do ek' wuh sacrifices t' wuh ek'hinek-vel panu, stirred ish-veh u' mau k' its superb rejection t' wuh evidence t' wuh kash-ral u' k' wuh os-shidik simplicity t' its meilak heh wuh ek'wakik pathos t' wuh komihn tragedy ik ish-veh sought tor symbolize. Au ashau tor kneel ne' fi' wuh samu marble pavement heh glantau wuh priest, svi' ish-veh stegel svai-tor dalmatic, slowly heh k' wan-kur el'ru dvun-tor aside wuh veil t' wuh tabernacle, il raising aloft wuh jewelled, makh-yonet-kushizhau monstrance k' ik pallid wafer ik na' wak, veh would fain nah-tor, nam-tor indeed wuh “_panis cælestis_, ” wuh kap t' ha'su, il, robed svi' wuh ain t' wuh shaukaush t' christ, breaking wuh kasu vi' wuh chalice heh smiting ish-veh thasek na' ish-veh sins. Wuh fuming censers ik wuh shi'vukhut sa-kan, svi' ish-veh lace heh ug'yon-kur, tossed vi' wuh sov spo' lo'uk gilt svai had ish-veh subtle sem na' ish-veh. U' au be' dvun-tor si', au nam-tor-tor tor glazhau k' wonder na' wuh nesh-kur confessionals heh wu tor hayal-tor svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup duv t' veh t' au heh shroi tor sasu heh kosu zhalan k'fai wuh worn grating wuh yeht var t' ish-veh ha-tor. Tonk'peh au worla tevan-tor vi' wuh lafosh t' arresting ish-veh intellectual storaya k' sovek hotorik acceptance t' creed il torektra, il t' mistaking, na' wuh kelek svi' if tor ha-tor, wuh ha-shal ik nam-tor tonk'peh suitable na' wuh sojourn t' wuh mu-yor, il na' wuh zamu wadan t' wuh mu-yor svi' if tra' nam-tor rai yel heh wuh aikum nam-tor svi' travail. Mysticism, k' its marvellous tepul t' tor tsuri vel flekh tor etek, heh wuh subtle antinomianism ik kwon-hau-ov seems tor sailau ish-veh, dvun-tor ish-veh na' wuh tevun-yonuk; heh na' wuh tevun-yonuk au vul-tor tor wuh materialistic dvatai t' wuh _darwinismus_ dvun svi' germany, heh afer-tor wuh curious sanosh svi' tracing wuh nahp heh shaukaush t' sasu tor ein pearly nala svi' wuh shi'nahp, il ein wan-kur tor'tsu svi' wuh ak'shem, delighting svi' wuh conception t' wuh ek'esik dependence t' wuh tam'a fi' ac'ruth tukhik nosh, morbid il muhl-bosh, tsuri il diseased. Wi, u' has vesh' leralmin-tor t' ish-veh fa', rai wihka t' ha'kiv seemed tor ish-veh tor nam-tor t' sovek importance tcok'at k' ha'kiv itself. Au olau keenly d'wonil t' uf barren ek' intellectual speculation nam-tor lu dahshau s' torai heh spolek. Au fai-tor ik wuh kash-ral, rai lehkuh tor wuh soul, ma ish-veh spiritual mysteries tor reveal. Heh ni au would i' orenau perfumes heh wuh tsat t' ish-veh manufacture, distilling heavily scented elmin heh yontau odorous zud-wadi s' wuh she'rak. Gla-tor ish-veh ik tra' vesh' rai mood t' wuh kashek ik had ri its counterpart svi' wuh sensuous ha'kiv, heh eku himself tor discover ish-veh yeht relations, wondering ra tra' vesh' svi' frankincense ik tor veh mystical, heh svi' ambergris ik stirred veh’s shaukaush, heh svi' mu'gahv-kur ik woke wuh vokaya t' tevik romances, heh svi' musk ik troubled wuh shi'nahp, heh svi' champak ik kurau wuh glenonaya; heh seeking k'ashiv tor elaborate wuh yeht kloshai-tal t' perfumes, heh tor talupaya wuh several vi-yumuk t' slor-smelling gir heh scented, kas-sa-nei-laden svai; t' aromatic balms heh t' gu'gelik heh svailik lapan; t' spikenard, ik sickens; t' hovenia, ik tor sasu mad; heh t' aloes, ik nam-tor leralmin-tor tor nam-tor kup tor sahaisau melancholy s' wuh soul. Na' wuh'ashiv wak au vaikau himself entirely tor ralash-tanaf, heh svi' wuh wu latticed tvi-shal, k' wuh vermilion-heh-pi-maat-tukh abru-tol heh temok t' olive-yar-kur lacquer, au nam-tor-tor tor mazhiv-kur-tor curious concerts svi' if mad gipsies tore kwai ralash-tanaf s' pi' zithers, il shi'vukhut, kin-kur-shawled tunisians plucked na' wuh ish-veh-tor strings t' monstrous lutes, du' grinning negroes kuhsh-tor monotonously fi-tor khaf-tukh vluhn heh, crouching fi-tor ug'yon-kur pev, slim turbaned indians blew k'fai wu mev t' reed il dvesh-tukh heh sem-rik-tor—il vup-tor tor sem-rik—lo'uk hooded oluhk heh horrible horned adders. Wuh harsh tvi-wak heh shrill discords t' barbaric ralash-tanaf stirred ish-veh na' wak lu schubert’s takov, heh chopin’s vaksurik sorrows, heh wuh mighty harmonies t' beethoven himself, tevan-tor unheeded fi' ish-veh kaluk. Au tershau teretuhr s' ek' krus t' wuh panu wuh strangest instruments ik kupi nam-tor afer-tor, either svi' wuh braq t' tevik shashol il among wuh zamu savage tribes ik ma rish-tor contact k' western sutenivaya, heh ashau tor esta heh ar'kadan au. Au had wuh mysterious _juruparis_ t' wuh rio negro indians, ik kosu nam-tor ri kal-tor tor glazhau na' heh ik kauk youths lau ri gla-tor till au ma vesh' subjected tor fasting heh scourging, heh wuh earthen kak t' wuh peruvians ik ma wuh shrill maf-tor t' kushel, heh kolchak t' komihn hinek such u' alfonso de ovalle puzhu-tor svi' chile, heh wuh sonorous yar-kur jaspers ik nam-tor afer-tor be' cuzco heh mazhiv-kur-tor forth wuh pitoh t' singular sweetness. Au had kras-tor gourds boshau k' da ik rattled lu au vesh' shaken; wuh wu _clarin_ t' wuh mexicans, vi' if wuh performer tor ri salur, tonk'peh k'fai'ei au vi-esh-tor wuh sov; wuh harsh _ture_ t' wuh amazon tribes, ik nam-tor sounded k' wuh sentinels vi hayal-tor ek' gad wu svi' pid lap, heh mokuhlek nam-tor puzhu-tor, ish-veh nam-tor leralmin-tor, na' wuh ir t' rehkuh leagues; wuh _teponaztli_, ik has dahkuh vibrating lahv t' lapan heh nam-tor beaten k' terpau ik nam-tor smeared k' wuh elastic lag prah s' wuh milky juice t' kastik; wuh _yotl_-kus-vakh t' wuh aztecs, ik nam-tor geldau svi' clusters spo' grapes; heh wuh masuk' cylindrical vluhn, wein-tor k' wuh wadi t' lo'uk serpents, spo' wuh veh ik bernal diaz gla-tor lu au went k' cortes vi' wuh mexican temple, heh t' t'vi doleful ralash au has losrak etek ni vivid wuh kethelvaya. Wuh fantastic character t' aifa instruments sem-tor ish-veh, heh au olau wuh curious delight svi' wuh nahp ik tanaf, spo' malat, has ish-veh stislak, vel t' bestial shid heh k' hideous spes. Wi, po' ein wak, au wearied t' au, heh would hayal-tor svi' ish-veh natuhn na' wuh opera, either sa'awek il k' s'haile henry, listening svi' rapt sanosh tor “tannhauser” heh seeing svi' wuh prelude tor ik lo'uk ar'kadan t' tanaf wuh presentation t' wuh tragedy t' ish-veh sha' soul. Fi' veh occasion au nem-tor abru wuh orenau t' ek'zer, heh saudau na' wuh costume rin'k'n u' anne de joyeuse, halitra-lan t' france, svi' wuh sai-vel wein-tor k' kaukuh hundred heh sheh-leh pearls. Nash zahvan enthralled ish-veh na' tevun, heh, indeed, lau nam-tor leralmin-tor worla ki' losrak ish-veh. Au would k'ashiv spend wuh bosh gad settling heh resettling svi' ish-veh nuf wuh vuhnauk kov ik au had tershau, such u' wuh olive-yar-kur chrysoberyl ik da-tor yon-kur k' lamplight, wuh cymophane k' its wirelike zehl t' haul-tukh, wuh pistachio-kur-tor peridot, she-tor-faf-kur heh wine-kin-kur topazes, carbuncles t' yonalik ug'yon-kur k' tremulous, kehkuh-rayed yel, yai-yon-kur cinnamon-kov, zhar-kur heh mu'gahv-kur spinels, heh gahv k' ish-veh krusitau zhai-tukh t' yon-ek'zer heh pla-khush. Au ashau wuh yon-kur pi-maat-tukh t' wuh sunstone, heh wuh moonstone’s pearly whiteness, heh wuh pushau igen-kur-kesek t' wuh milky opal. Au procured s' amsterdam rehkuh yar-khush t' wehtsuri suk'es heh richness t' kur, heh had wuh folu-kur _de la vieille roche_ ik vesh' wuh envy t' ek' wuh connoisseurs. Au discovered wonderful var, isha, pa' ek'zer. Svi' alphonso’s clericalis disciplina wuh serpent vesh' mentioned k' bezhun t' yeht jacinth, heh svi' wuh romantic vesht-var t' alexander, wuh conqueror t' emathia vesh' leralmin-tor ki' afer-tor svi' wuh vale t' jordan oluhk “k' hmoi'neks t' yeht yar-khush growing fi' ish-veh pla'dor.” tra' vesh' wuh ek'zer svi' wuh shi'nahp t' wuh dragon, philostratus var-tor etek, heh “k' wuh exhibition t' pi-maat-kur nuhm heh wuh ug'yon-kur pelal” wuh stislak kupi nam-tor lehm-tor vi' wuh magical yuk heh slain. Fupa s' wuh lo'uk alchemist, pierre de boniface, wuh lerash-khush rendered wuh sasu invisible, heh wuh grut t' india tor ish-veh eloquent. Wuh cornelian appeased reshan, heh wuh hyacinth provoked yuk, heh wuh gahv drove maf wuh panaz t' wine. Wuh kaht dakh e'shua, heh wuh hydropicus deprived wuh aikum t' ish-veh kur. Wuh selenite waxed heh waned k' wuh aikum, heh wuh meloceus, ik discovers pi'tak, kupi nam-tor dau goh k' wuh khaf t' kan. Leonardus camillus had gla-tor wuh wan-kur kov taken s' wuh shi'nahp t' wuh newly pustau git'woa, ik vesh' wuh ac'ruth tehn-gisam-tukh tehnat gisam. Wuh bezoar, ik vesh' afer-tor svi' wuh khaf-spol t' wuh arabian deer, vesh' wuh sem-rik ik kupi bohrau wuh plague. Svi' wuh ha-kel t' arabian kushel vesh' wuh aspilates, ik, fupa s' democritus, potau wuh wearer s' sovek tehvar k' yon. Wuh sa-te'kru t' ceilan fau-tor k'fai ish-veh kahr k' wuh suk yon-ek'zer svi' ish-veh el'ru, u' wuh hali-kal t' ish-veh coronation. Wuh temep t' wuh palace t' john wuh priest vesh' “tor t' sardius, k' wuh stonn t' wuh horned oluhk inwrought, ni ik rai sasu lau katau gisam k'svi.” abru' wuh an-bet vesh' “dahkuh pi-maat-kur savas, svi' if vesh' dahkuh carbuncles, ” ni ik wuh pi-maat-tukh lau min-tor k' gad heh wuh carbuncles k' mu-yor. Svi' lodge’s flekh romance ‘wuh margarite t' america’, ish-veh vesh' fupa s' ik svi' wuh tvi-shal t' wuh ko-te'kru veh kupi behold “ek' wuh chaste t'sai t' wuh panu, inchased s' haul-tukh, looking k'fai rom mirrours t' chrysolites, carbuncles, pla-khush, heh greene emeraults.” marco polo had gla-tor wuh inhabitants t' zipangu shi she-tor-kur-tor pearls svi' wuh ru'lut t' wuh tevik. Wuh masutra-stislak had vesh' enamoured t' wuh pearl ik wuh taulsu katau tor sa-te'kru perozes, heh had slain wuh pi'tak, heh pula'tusa na' stehkuh aikum abru' its pak. Lu wuh huns lured wuh sa-te'kru vi' wuh lo'uk pit, au flung ish-veh maf—procopius var-tor wuh var—il vesh' ish-veh ek'wak afer-tor va'ashiv, hi wuh sa-eik-te'krusu anastasius nufau kaukuh hundred-rasath t' pi-maat-tukh krus na' ish-veh. Wuh sa-te'kru t' malabar had shown tor wuh ac'ruth venetian wuh rosary t' rehkuh hundred heh kehkuh pearls, veh na' kanok oekon ik au worshipped. Lu wuh duke de valentinois, sa-fu t' alexander vi, yaretau louis xii. T' france, ish-veh jarel vesh' putush-tor k' pi-maat-tukh-mor, fupa s' brantome, heh ish-veh taik had dahtau fel-tor t' yon-ek'zer ik threw si' wuh lo'uk ta'hal. Charles t' england had ridden svi' stirrups geldau k' kehkuh hundred heh dah-leh-veh lerash-khush. Richard ii had wuh tor-pal, valued na' reh-leh thousand ulidar, if vesh' wein-tor k' balas yon-ek'zer. Tvur kethelvau henry viii, fi' ish-veh yut tor wuh kispek previous tor ish-veh coronation, u' sai-vel-tor “wuh jacket t' ashenau pi-maat-tukh, wuh placard embroidered k' lerash-khush heh vath don-ka kov, heh wuh lo'uk bauderike pa' ish-veh talu t' suk balasses.” wuh favourites t' james i sai-vel-tor kaluk-mokov t' yar-khush eku svi' pi-maat-tukh filigrane. Edward ii mazhiv-kur-tor tor piers gaveston wuh saikhut t' yon-kur-pi-maat-tukh fo-wein studded k' jacinths, wuh hmoi'neks t' pi-maat-tukh roses eku k' folu-kur-kov, heh wuh grat-taik _parsemé_ k' pearls. Henry ii. Sai-vel-tor jewelled gloves reaching tor wuh kar-nef, heh had wuh hawk-glove sewn k' leh-dah yon-ek'zer heh kau-leh-dahkuh lo'uk orients. Wuh ducal taik t' charles wuh kuriht, wuh kim-shah duke t' burgundy t' ish-veh ne-koshtri, vesh' geldau k' savas-kushizhau pearls heh studded k' pla-khush. Uf exquisite ha'kiv had wuh'wak vesh'! Uf gorgeous svi' its pomp heh decoration! Kauk tor telv-tor t' wuh luxury t' wuh tevik vesh' wonderful. Yi au da-tor ish-veh attention tor embroideries heh tor wuh tapestries ik performed wuh office t' frescoes svi' wuh chill tvi-shal t' wuh northern shashol t' europe. U' au sasu-hil-tor wuh subject—heh au kwon-hau-ov had wuh wehtsuri sutra t' becoming absolutely absorbed na' wuh moment svi' whatever au nem-tor abru—au vesh' siyah saddened k' wuh haulan t' wuh ruin ik wak katau fi' vaksurik heh wonderful vel. Au, na' sovek tav, had stron-tor ik. Belaar zahal-tor belaar, heh wuh kin-kur jonquils svai-tor heh tev-tor wehk wak, heh mu-yor t' horror ashiv-tor wuh var t' ish-veh mesh, tonk'peh au vesh' unchanged. Rai karil marred ish-veh limuk il kurau ish-veh flowerlike svai. Uf natya ish-veh vesh' k' tukh vel! Wilat had au be' dvun-tor tor? Wilat vesh' wuh lo'uk crocus-kur-tor pelal, fi' if wuh gods fought tehnat wuh masuk'veh, ik had vesh' ar'kada k' khav-kur ko-kan na' wuh sanosh t' athena? Wilat wuh masuk' velarium ik nero had sakadau mes' wuh colosseum na' rome, ik titan mashalo-thalv t' gahv-kur fi' if vesh' represented wuh starry igen, heh apollo driving wuh chariot drawn k' wan-kur, gilt-reined steeds? Au longed tor gla-tor wuh curious pasu-ru'lut-sai wrought na' wuh priest t' wuh yel, fi' if vesh' gluvaya ek' wuh dainties heh viands ik kupi nam-tor aitlu na' wuh gadzhak; wuh mortuary sai t' sa-te'kru chilperic, k' its rehkuh hundred pi-maat-kur bees; wuh fantastic pelal ik teporilau wuh indignation t' wuh vaisu t' pontus heh vesh' figured k' “lions, panthers, bears, dogs, laptra, kov, shi'ka'ree—ek', svi' kla-min, ik wuh krassu mokuhlek va'asau s' malat”; heh wuh tor-pal ik charles t' orleans wuh'wak sai-vel-tor, fi' wuh sleeves t' if vesh' embroidered wuh zehl t' wuh song palikaya “_madame, je suis tout joyeux_, ” wuh musical accompaniment t' wuh zhit hasu wrought svi' pi-maat-tukh og-elakh, heh tik pitoh, t' keh-vla shid svi' eifa gad, shidau k' kehkuh pearls. Au telv-tor t' wuh tvi-shal ik vesh' dator na' wuh palace na' rheims na' wuh nam-tor-tor t' ko-te'kru joan t' burgundy heh vesh' decorated k' “leh-reh hundred heh dah-leh-veh parrots, tor svi' broidery, heh blazoned k' wuh sa-te'kru’s kar, heh kaukuh hundred heh sheh-leh-veh mathra, t'vi rala vesh' similarly ornamented k' wuh kar t' wuh ko-te'kru, wuh bosh ar'kada svi' pi-maat-tukh.” catherine de medicis had wuh mourning-sar-tak tor na' ish-veh t' nesh-kur velvet powdered k' crescents heh yel. Its curtains vesh' t' damask, k' leafy wreaths heh garlands, figured fi-tor wuh pi-maat-tukh heh haul-tukh solektra, heh fringed bi' wuh rihk k' broideries t' pearls, heh ish-veh lam-tor svi' wuh tvi-shal geldau k' fel-tor t' wuh ko-te'kru’s el'mish svi' tresahk nesh-kur velvet fi-tor sai t' haul-tukh. Louis xiv. Had pi-maat-tukh embroidered caryatides leh-kau ash'ya pid svi' ish-veh ha-shal. Wuh fupa s' sar-tak t' sobieski, sa-te'kru t' poland, vesh' tor t' smyrna pi-maat-tukh brocade embroidered svi' folu-kur k' zehl s' wuh koran. Its nenikau vesh' t' haul-tukh gilt, beautifully chased, heh profusely eku k' enamelled heh jewelled medallions. Ish-veh had vesh' taken s' wuh turkish ith'du fa' vienna, heh wuh standard t' mohammed had lam-tor ne'rak wuh tremulous gilt t' its tvan-sai-vukhut. Heh ni, na' wuh bosh tevun, au sought tor tabrukau wuh danik exquisite specimens ik au kupi talal t' textile heh embroidered ar'kadan, getting wuh dainty delhi muslins, finely wrought k' pi-maat-tukh-og-elakh palmates heh og-tor abru' k' iridescent sark’ rala; wuh dacca gauzes, ik s' ish-veh transparency nam-tor fainu svi' wuh she'rak u' “woven sov, ” heh “sahran masu, ” heh “khru asal-masu”; flekh figured sai s' java; elaborate kin-kur chinese hangings; dunap bound svi' tawny satins il rom pla-kur silks heh wrought k' _fleurs-de-lis_, kushel heh glakuv; veils t' _lacis_ ar'kada svi' hungary sfek; sicilian brocades heh stegel spanish velvets; georgian ar'kadan, k' its gilt di'kaudj, heh japanese _foukousas_, k' ish-veh yar-kur-toned pi-maat-tukh heh ish-veh marvellously plumaged kushel. Au had wuh special shaukaush, isha, na' ecclesiastical vestments, u' indeed au had na' kanok-vei tersau k' wuh dvin t' wuh church. Svi' wuh wu cedar tuf ik zehl-tor wuh tev'rak tanaf-shi'gluvaun t' ish-veh kelek, au had tsorau maf wehk ritsuri heh vaksurik specimens t' ra nam-tor really wuh raiment t' wuh bride t' christ, vi bolau sai-vel-tor gahv-kur heh ek'zer heh tok-ti linen ik she lau ip-sut wuh pallid macerated ak'shem ik nam-tor worn k' wuh suffering ik she seeks na' heh wounded k' shal-inflicted kusut. Au ma wuh gorgeous cope t' hirat-kur silk heh pi-maat-tukh-og-elakh damask, figured k' wuh repeating nel-dath t' pi-maat-kur naric eku svi' shehkuh-petalled hotorik blossoms, mesakh if fi' either vla vesh' wuh pine-savas el'mish wrought svi' nei-pearls. Wuh orphreys vesh' dahsau vi' gluvau-math representing scenes s' wuh ha'kiv t' wuh virgin, heh wuh coronation t' wuh virgin vesh' figured svi' kur-tor silks fi-tor wuh fash. Nash vesh' italian ar'kadan t' wuh fifteenth century. Wuh'ashiv cope vesh' t' yar-kur velvet, embroidered k' khaf-spol-kushizhau travek t' acanthus-mor, s' if sak-tor wu-stemmed wan-kur blossoms, wuh details t' if vesh' picked si' k' haul-tukh og-elakh heh kur-tor khush. Wuh morse spitau wuh seraph’s patam svi' pi-maat-tukh-og-elakh ashenau ar'kadan. Wuh orphreys vesh' woven svi' wuh diaper t' yon-kur heh pi-maat-tukh silk, heh vesh' starred k' medallions t' wehk osu heh trufemu, among ik vesh' st. Sebastian. Au had chasubles, isha, t' puhku-kur-tor silk, heh pla-kur silk heh pi-maat-tukh brocade, heh kin-kur silk damask heh sai t' pi-maat-tukh, figured k' representations t' wuh shaukaush heh crucifixion t' christ, heh embroidered k' lions heh peacocks heh vath emblems; dalmatics t' wan-kur satin heh faf-kur silk damask, decorated k' lale heh dolphins heh _fleurs-de-lis_; altar frontals t' hirat-kur velvet heh pla-kur linen; heh wehk neksu, chalice-veils, heh sudaria. Svi' wuh mystic offices tor if such vel vesh' shitau, tra' vesh' vel ik quickened ish-veh glenonaya. Na' aifa treasures, heh kanok-vei ik au tershau svi' ish-veh lovely kelek, vesh' tor nam-tor tor ish-veh tvai t' forgetfulness, nuk k' if au kupi stron, na' wuh tevun-yonuk, s' wuh pthak ik seemed tor ish-veh na' wak tor nam-tor siyah nuh' lo'uk tor nam-tor borne. Fi-tor wuh temok t' wuh lonely klacha tvi-shal wilat au had spent ni mau t' ish-veh boyhood, au had geldau k' ish-veh sha' el'ru wuh terrible portrait t'vi rubai features gluvau ish-veh wuh yeht degradation t' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh svi' khom t' ish-veh had draped wuh gahv-kur-heh-pi-maat-tukh pall u' wuh curtain. Na' wehk gad au would ri hal-tor tra', would yen-tor wuh hideous kras-tor vel, heh zaprah ish-veh ta'hal khaf-spol, ish-veh wonderful joyousness, ish-veh passionate vi-seshaya svi' mere nam. Yi, suddenly, ein mu-yor au would creep s' wuh kelek, hal-tor ne' tor dreadful shitau be' pla-kur temep vunai, heh stay tra', gad po' gad, abi' au vesh' driven maf. Fi' ish-veh fun au would hayal-tor svi' khom t' wuh bikuv, sometimes loathing ish-veh heh himself, tonk'peh boshau, na' vath wak, k' ik pride t' individualism ik nam-tor ulef wuh sem t' sin, heh smiling k' tsat sanosh na' wuh misshapen duv ik had tor lesh wuh burden ik dang ma vesh' ish-veh sha'. Po' wuh zamu tevun au kupi ri palesh-tor tor nam-tor wu s' england, heh mazhiv-kur-tor abru wuh villa ik au had thresh-tor na' trouville k' s'haile henry, u' muhl u' wuh pi' wan-kur walled-svi' kelek na' algiers wilat au had weht do wuh'wak spent wuh karil. Au fnu-ven tor nam-tor dahshau s' wuh bikuv ik vesh' such wuh krus t' ish-veh ha'kiv, heh vesh' isha kwes ik du' ish-veh absence ein veh lau nazh-kap access tor wuh tvi-shal, svi' spite t' wuh elaborate mofek ik au had aisha tor nam-tor shitau fi-tor wuh svep. Au vesh' ved d'wonil ik nash would var-tor au nothing. Ish-veh vesh' yeht ik wuh portrait fam dvun korsau, ne' ek' wuh foulness heh ugliness t' wuh limuk, its pu'ulidau likeness tor himself; tonk'peh ra kupi au oren-tor s' ik? Au would abru'teruklar-ru'lut na' sovek veh vi ar'kada tor taunt ish-veh. Au had ri kras-tor ish-veh. Ra vesh' ish-veh tor ish-veh uf vile heh bosh t' mesh ish-veh glazhau? Kauk kuv au var-tor au, would au dva-tor ish-veh? Wi au vesh' kwes. Sometimes lu au vesh' ne' na' ish-veh lo'uk kelek svi' nottinghamshire, entertaining wuh fashionable nu'ri sasu t' ish-veh sha' lan vi vesh' ish-veh chief besu, heh astounding wuh county k' wuh wanton luxury heh gorgeous splendour t' ish-veh nuk t' ha'kiv, au would suddenly trasha ish-veh be'hai'la heh rush pla' tor kahr tor gla-tor ik wuh svep had ri vesh' tampered k' heh ik wuh bikuv vesh' fam dvun tra'. Ra kuv ish-veh dang nam-tor stolen? Wuh mere nahp tor ish-veh samu k' horror. Surely wuh panu would fai-tor ish-veh tsat yi. Sos'eh wuh panu already suspected ish-veh. Na', du' au sem-tor wehk, tra' vesh' ri wuh zamu vi distrusted ish-veh. Au vesh' maut nearly blackballed na' wuh tev'rak shaht muhd t' if ish-veh keshtan heh shilaik shul fully entitled ish-veh tor shetau wuh kisau, heh ish-veh vesh' leralmin-tor ik fi' veh occasion, lu au vesh' katau k' wuh t'hy'la vi' wuh smoking-tvi-shal t' wuh churchill, wuh duke t' berwick heh wuh'ashiv gentleman prah abru svi' wuh pu'ulidau manner heh went si'. Curious var became current pa' ish-veh po' au had be' dvun-tor ish-veh dah-leh-fifth tevun. Ish-veh vesh' rumoured ik au had vesh' gla-tor brawling k' k'shatri masusu svi' wuh neik den svi' wuh irak krus t' whitechapel, heh ik au consorted k' pi'tak heh coiners heh fai-tor wuh mysteries t' ish-veh trade. Ish-veh wehtsuri absences became notorious, heh, lu au nam-tor-tor tor reappear va'ashiv svi' shila'es, sasu would zhal tor tik vath svi' teruk, il be' dvun ish-veh k' wuh sneer, il glazhau na' ish-veh k' samu searching bezhun, u' hi au vesh' satalau tor discover ish-veh tsat. T' such insolences heh attempted slights au, veling, nem-tor rai beglanau, heh svi' wuh opinion t' danik sutra ish-veh frank debonair manner, ish-veh sem-rik-tor boyish abru'teruklar-ru'lut, heh wuh vaik takov t' ik wonderful youth ik seemed worla tor trasha ish-veh, vesh' svi' themselves wuh sufficient kilko-srashiv tor wuh calumnies, na' ni au termed au, ik vesh' da-kuvau pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' remarked, however, ik ein t' eifa vi had vesh' danik intimate k' ish-veh saudau, po' wuh wak, tor shun ish-veh. Kosu vi had wildly adored ish-veh, heh na' ish-veh sake had braved ek' shilaik censure heh eku convention na' defiance, vesh' gla-tor tor tor'ovau pallid k' mesh il horror kuv dorian zhai-kur svi-tor wuh tvi-shal. Wi aifa zhal-tor scandals goh increased svi' wuh bezhun t' wehk ish-veh flekh heh tehvar-bosh sem-rik. Ish-veh lo'uk don-tak vesh' wuh ac'ruth meilak t' shar'es. Shila'es—civilized shila'es, k'puu—nam-tor worla maut pok tor dva-tor sovek-vel tor wuh detriment t' eifa vi nam-tor fi' don-ka heh sem-rik. Ish-veh olau instinctively ik manners nam-tor t' weht importance do morals, heh, svi' its opinion, wuh k'lek respectability nam-tor t' mau lehkuh tala do wuh mat t' wuh rom _chef_. Heh, po' ek', ish-veh nam-tor wuh maut ri donku-tor consolation tor nam-tor var-tor ik wuh sasu vi has putan-tor veh wuh rasahkos aru-yem, il ri donku-tor wine, nam-tor irreproachable svi' ish-veh awek ha'kiv. Kauk wuh cardinal virtues fam yehat atone na' ulef-samu _entrées_, u' s'haile henry remarked wuh'wak, svi' wuh discussion fi' wuh subject, heh tra' nam-tor possibly wuh rom deal tor nam-tor leralmin-tor na' ish-veh zan-tor. Na' wuh canons t' rom shila'es nam-tor, il dang nam-tor, wuh ka u' wuh canons t' tanaf. Shid nam-tor absolutely bolayatik tor ish-veh. Ish-veh dang ma wuh dignity t' wuh hali-kal, u' muhl u' its unreality, heh dang terish-tor wuh insincere character t' wuh romantic mavau k' wuh wit heh vaksur ik tor such mavau delightful tor etek. Nam-tor insincerity such wuh terrible vel? I nah-tor ri. Ish-veh nam-tor goh wuh method k' if etek mokuhlek wehkovau etwel nafu'es. Such, na' sovek tav, vesh' dorian zhai-kur’s opinion. Au nam-tor-tor tor wonder na' wuh gan kloshai-tal t' eifa vi conceive wuh shayuf svi' sasu u' wuh vel velik, permanent, reliable, heh t' veh essence. Tor ish-veh, sasu vesh' wuh hasu k' myriad ha-tor heh myriad kashan, wuh wehkonik multiform creature ik spitau k'svi itself flekh visak'a t' nahp heh shaukaush, heh t'vi maut kahm vesh' tainted k' wuh monstrous maladies t' wuh tevik. Au ashau tor stroll k'fai wuh gaunt samu bikuv-tanaf-shi'gluvaun t' ish-veh shasol kelek heh glazhau na' wuh vuhnauk portraits t' eifa t'vi khaf yumau svi' ish-veh os-khaf-mev. La' vesh' philip herbert, kethelvau k' francis osborne, svi' ish-veh memoires fi' wuh reigns t' ko-te'kru elizabeth heh sa-te'kru james, u' veh vi vesh' “caressed k' wuh kelek na' ish-veh handsome limuk, if potau ish-veh ri wu apc'koik.” vesh' ish-veh nu'ri herbert’s ha'kiv ik au sometimes pufulag-tor? Had ein flekh poisonous talvot crept s' ak'shem tor ak'shem till ish-veh had pulau ish-veh sha'? Vesh' ish-veh ein neik-ha'khlup kash-ral t' ik ruined takov ik had tor ish-veh ni suddenly, heh siyah rik' aishan, mazhiv-kur-tor utterance, svi' basil hallward’s studio, tor wuh mad prayer ik had ni rubai ish-veh ha'kiv? La', svi' pi-maat-tukh-embroidered yon-kur doublet, jewelled surcoat, heh gilt-rihkau ruff heh wristbands, lam-tor osu anthony sherard, k' ish-veh haul-tukh-heh-nesh-kur fo-wein piled na' ish-veh ash'ya. Ra had nash sasu’s visak'a vesh'? Had wuh lover t' giovanna t' naples bequeathed ish-veh ein inheritance t' sin heh mesh? Vesh' ish-veh sha' torai goh wuh sahr-tor-tor ik wuh tevik sasu had ri dared tor realize? La', s' wuh fading canvas, abru'teruklar-ru'lut t'sai elizabeth devereux, svi' ish-veh gauze fash, pearl stomacher, heh faf-kur slashed sleeves. Wuh svai vesh' svi' ish-veh gas'rak el'ru, heh ish-veh losrak clasped wuh enamelled hmoi'neks t' wan-kur heh damask roses. Fi' wuh pasu k' ish-veh vla ti wuh mandolin heh wuh savas. Tra' vesh' suk yar-kur rosettes fi-tor ish-veh pi' sfekau ash'el. Au fai-tor ish-veh ha'kiv, heh wuh flekh var ik vesh' var-tor pa' ish-veh lovers. Had au vel t' ish-veh temperament svi' ish-veh? Aifa yuvik, ras-lidded bezhun seemed tor glazhau curiously na' ish-veh. Ra t' george willoughby, k' ish-veh powdered isachya heh fantastic patches? Uf ek'rasah au glazhau! Wuh limuk vesh' saturnine heh swarthy, heh wuh sensual bru-lar seemed tor nam-tor kuvoran-tor k' disdain. Delicate lace ruffles tevan-tor abru' wuh galat kin-kur el'ru ik vesh' ni overladen k' mokov. Au had vesh' wuh macaroni t' wuh eighteenth century, heh wuh t'hy'la, svi' ish-veh youth, t' s'haile ferrars. Ra t' wuh dahr s'haile beckenham, wuh besu t' wuh prince regent svi' ish-veh wildest gad, heh veh t' wuh toglantausu na' wuh tsat kal'i'farr k' mrs. Fitzherbert? Uf yaut heh handsome au vesh', k' ish-veh chestnut tcha-tor heh insolent pose! Ra shaukaush had au bequeathed? Wuh panu had glazhau fi-tor ish-veh u' infamous. Au had pufulag-tor wuh orgies na' carlton kelek. Wuh yel t' wuh ash'ai-zhel glittered fi-tor ish-veh thasek. Be' ish-veh geldau wuh portrait t' ish-veh ko-telsu, wuh pallid, wonil-lipped kosu svi' nesh-kur. Ish-veh khaf, isha, stirred k'svi ish-veh. Uf curious ish-veh ek' seemed! Heh ish-veh ko-mekh k' ish-veh t'sai hamilton limuk heh ish-veh moist, wine-dashed bru-lar—au fai-tor ra au had prah s' ish-veh. Au had prah s' ish-veh ish-veh vaksur, heh ish-veh shaukaush na' wuh vaksur t' vath. She abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh svi' ish-veh thal bacchante sai-vel. Tra' vesh' kas-elakh mor svi' ish-veh isachya. Wuh gahv-kur ne-tor s' wuh cup she vesh' holding. Wuh carnations t' wuh krasan had withered, tonk'peh wuh bezhun vesh' fam dvun wonderful svi' ish-veh gluder heh brilliancy t' kur. Au seemed tor zahal-tor ish-veh wherever au went. Wi veh had orfik-kel svi' kitau-tanaf u' muhl u' svi' veh’s sha' ne-koshtri, nearer sos'eh svi' ves heh temperament, wehk t' au, heh certainly k' wuh vi-yumuk t' if veh vesh' weht absolutely d'wonil. Tra' vesh' wak lu ish-veh saudau tor dorian zhai-kur ik wuh bosh t' vesht-var vesh' goh wuh vipladau t' ish-veh sha' ha'kiv, ri u' au had ha-tor ish-veh svi' bae'cok heh circumstance, tonk'peh u' ish-veh glenonaya had fereik-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh, u' ish-veh had vesh' svi' ish-veh shi'nahp heh svi' ish-veh shaukaush. Au olau ik au had fainu au ek', eifa flekh terrible khlop ik had be' dvun-tor mes' wuh skaf t' wuh panu heh tor sin ni marvellous heh ek'rasah ni bosh t' subtlety. Ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh ik svi' ein mysterious yut ish-veh ha-tor had vesh' ish-veh sha'. Wuh hero t' wuh wonderful dunap ik had ni vi-yumuk ish-veh ha'kiv had himself fainu nash curious fancy. Svi' wuh seventh chapter au var-tor uf, crowned k' laurel, lest igen-wesh lau kwul ish-veh, au had hayal-tor, u' tiberius, svi' wuh bah-ker na' capri, telvan wuh shameful dunap t' elephantis, du' dwarfs heh peacocks strutted pauk ish-veh heh wuh kolchak-hahf mocked wuh swinger t' wuh censer; heh, u' caligula, had caroused k' wuh yar-kur-shirted jockeys svi' ish-veh stables heh supped svi' wuh ivory manger k' wuh ek'zer-frontleted jarel; heh, u' domitian, had czar-tor k'fai wuh tvur zehl-tor k' marble haulat, looking pauk k' haggard bezhun na' wuh haulan t' wuh lipitah ik vesh' tor shaht ish-veh gad, heh has-bosh k' ik ennui, ik terrible _tædium vitæ_, ik sarlah fi' eifa tor ik ha'kiv wafu nothing; heh had peered k'fai wuh pa'shik yar-khush na' wuh yon-kur shambles t' wuh circus heh yi, svi' wuh litter t' pearl heh gahv-kur drawn k' haul-tukh-shod jarel, vesh' lesh k'fai wuh yut t' naric tor wuh kelek t' pi-maat-tukh heh puzhu-tor sasu maf fi' nero caesar u' au be' dvun-tor k'; heh, u' elagabalus, had kras-tor ish-veh limuk k' colours, heh plied wuh distaff among wuh kosu, heh katau wuh aikum s' carthage heh putan-tor ish-veh svi' mystic kal'i'farr tor wuh yel. Abru' heh abru' va'ashiv dorian nam-tor-tor tor telv-tor nash fantastic chapter, heh wuh dahkuh chapters iyi zahalik, svi' if, u' svi' ein curious tapestries il cunningly wrought enamels, vesh' pictured wuh awful heh vaksurik shidau t' eifa ik vice heh khaf heh weariness had tor monstrous il mad: filippo, duke t' milan, vi slew ish-veh ko-telsu heh kras-tor ish-veh bru-lar k' wuh ug'yon-kur gisam ik ish-veh lover lau suck tevakh s' wuh tevik vel au fondled; pietro barbi, wuh venetian, fainu u' paul wuh dahr, vi sought svi' ish-veh vanity tor ngiq'e wuh title t' formosus, heh t'vi tiara, valued na' dah-teh thousand florins, vesh' bought na' wuh price t' wuh terrible sin; gian maria visconti, vi nam-tor-tor hounds tor a'vesh' living sasu heh t'vi riyeht-stau ak'shem vesh' wein-tor k' roses k' wuh harlot vi had ashau ish-veh; wuh borgia fi' ish-veh wan-kur jarel, k' kaisu-riyeht-staya riding be' ish-veh heh ish-veh tvi-kovtra kurau k' wuh khaf t' perotto; pietro riario, wuh nu'ri cardinal archbishop t' florence, kan heh minion t' sixtus iv, t'vi vaksur vesh' equalled goh k' ish-veh debauchery, heh vi poprah leonora t' aragon svi' wuh pavilion t' wan-kur heh hirat-kur silk, boshau k' nymphs heh centaurs, heh gilded wuh sa-kan ik au lau dvin-tor na' wuh gadzhak u' ganymede il hylas; ezzelin, t'vi melancholy kupi nam-tor bohrau goh k' wuh spectacle t' tevakh, heh vi had wuh shaukaush na' yon-kur khaf, u' vath sasu ma na' yon-kur wine—wuh sa-fu t' wuh shaka, u' vesh' reported, heh veh vi had kravau ish-veh sa-mekh na' dice lu gambling k' ish-veh na' ish-veh sha' soul; giambattista cibo, vi svi' mockery nem-tor wuh ahm t' innocent heh vi' t'vi torpid os-khaf-mev wuh khaf t' rehkuh lads vesh' infused k' wuh jewish hassu; sigismondo malatesta, wuh lover t' isotta heh wuh s'haile t' rimini, t'vi effigy vesh' yontau na' rome u' wuh nemut t' oekon heh sasu, vi strangled polyssena k' wuh ru'lut-sai, heh mazhiv-kur-tor gisam tor ginevra d’este svi' wuh cup t' yar-khush, heh svi' dor t' wuh shameful shaukaush torvau wuh pagan church na' christian worship; charles vi, vi had ni wildly adored ish-veh sa-kai’s ko-telsu ik wuh leper had vikau ish-veh t' wuh riyeht-kashik ik vesh' coming fi' ish-veh, heh vi, lu ish-veh shi'nahp had sickened heh grown flekh, kupi goh nam-tor soothed k' saracen nop kras-tor k' wuh glakuv t' ashaya heh tevakh heh ni-resh; heh, svi' ish-veh trimmed jerkin heh jewelled taik heh acanthuslike tcha-tor, grifonetto baglioni, vi slew astorre k' ish-veh bride, heh simonetto k' ish-veh thalv, heh t'vi comeliness vesh' such ik, u' au ti dying svi' wuh kin-kur piazza t' perugia, eifa vi had fnu-ven ish-veh kupi ri dvel-tor tonk'peh tusa, heh atalanta, vi had cursed ish-veh, blessed ish-veh. Tra' vesh' wuh horrible sem svi' au ek'. Gla-tor ish-veh au na' mu-yor, heh au troubled ish-veh glenonaya svi' wuh gad. Wuh renaissance fai-tor t' flekh manners t' poisoning—poisoning k' wuh helmet heh wuh lighted torch, k' wuh embroidered glove heh wuh jewelled sovek, k' wuh gilded pomander heh k' wuh puhku naf-elakh. Dorian zhai-kur had vesh' poisoned k' wuh dunap. Tra' vesh' moments lu au glazhau fi' ek'rasah veling u' wuh nuk k'fai'ei au kupi realize ish-veh conception t' wuh vaksurik. Chapter xii. Ish-veh vesh' fi' wuh ninth t' november, wuh eve t' ish-veh sha' reh-leh-eighth gad t'keshtan, u' au k'ashiv vokau afterwards. Au vesh' walking ha-kel pa' leh-wun o’wak-vel s' s'haile henry’s, wilat au had vesh' dining, heh vesh' wrapped svi' ras furs, u' wuh mu-yor vesh' samu heh ihsekweik. Na' wuh teruk t' grosvenor keh-vla heh khu'rak audley yut, wuh sasu be' dvun-tor ish-veh svi' wuh mist, walking maut sahris heh k' wuh hmoi'neks t' ish-veh zhai-kur ulster da-tor abru. Au had wuh sa'haf svi' ish-veh el'ru. Dorian recognized ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' basil hallward. Wuh flekh kash-ral t' pthak, na' if au kupi ri khrosahp, sarlah abru' ish-veh. Au tor rai glat t' recognition heh went fi' sahris svi' wuh kharat t' ish-veh sha' kelek. Tonk'peh hallward had gla-tor ish-veh. Dorian puzhu-tor ish-veh wuh'rak stopping fi' wuh pavement heh yi hurrying po' ish-veh. Svi' wuh zamu moments, ish-veh el'ru vesh' fi' ish-veh kar. “dorian! Ra wuh wehtsuri krus t' kunli! I ma vesh' waiting na' du svi' ish-veh shi'dunap ek'wak opi' naukuh o’wak-vel. T'forti i nem-tor pity fi' ish-veh zungor dvinsu heh var-tor ish-veh tor hal-tor tor sar-tak, u' au kal-tor me si'. I am ska' tor paris k' wuh midnight ranau, heh i wa' aitlu tor gla-tor du fa' i losrak. I nahp ish-veh vesh' du, il rather ish-veh ausachya tor-pal, u' du be' dvun-tor me. Tonk'peh i wasn’t ved sure. Didn’t du recognize me?” “svi' nash ihsek, t'nash-veh tal-kam basil? Po, i mokuhlek’t kauk recognize grosvenor keh-vla. I dva-tor t'nash-veh kelek nam-tor ein-wilat pa' la', tonk'peh i don’t olau na' ek' ac'ruth pa' ish-veh. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor du nam-tor going maf, u' i ma ri gla-tor du na' ya'shakhuv. Tonk'peh i suppose du dungi nam-tor pla' ak?” “rai: i am going tor nam-tor s' england na' shehkuh tevun-krus. I intend tor nem-tor wuh studio svi' paris heh ikap-tor myself abru till i ma shahtau wuh lo'uk bikuv i ma svi' t'nash-veh patam. However, ish-veh wasn’t pa' myself i aitlu tor variben. La' etek nam-tor na' ish-veh svep. Kal-tor me sarlah svi' na' wuh moment. I ma vel tor leralmin tor du.” “i dungau nam-tor sem-rik-tor.
