Tonk'peh skil-tor’t du din-tor ish-veh ranau?” leralmin-tor dorian zhai-kur languidly u' au be' dvun-tor abru wuh ash-tor heh tu'ash wuh svep k' ish-veh kuhr-tal-muv. Wuh lamplight struggled si' k'fai wuh ihsek, heh hallward glazhau na' ish-veh glantau. “i ma heaps t' wak, ” au kilko-tor. “wuh ranau doesn’t hal-tor till leh-dah-leh-kau, heh ish-veh nam-tor goh aishan leh-wun. Svi' kla-min, i vesh' fi' t'nash-veh yut tor wuh muhd tor glazhau na' du, lu i ragel-tor du. Gla-tor du, i shan’t ma sovek vohtaya pa' luggage, u' i ma satau fi' t'nash-veh ras vel. Ek' i ma k' me nam-tor svi' nash sa'haf, heh i mokuhlek easily prah tor victoria svi' dah-leh minutes.” dorian glazhau na' ish-veh heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “ra wuh yut na' wuh fashionable krassu tor haolvaya! Wuh gladstone sa'haf heh wuh ulster! Sarlah svi', il wuh ihsek dungi prah vi' wuh kelek. Heh kashek du don’t variben pa' sovek-vel serious. Nothing nam-tor serious nowadays. K'puu nothing dang nam-tor.” hallward hutau ish-veh patam, u' au svi-tor, heh zahal-tor dorian vi' wuh shi'dunap. Tra' vesh' wuh ugelik lapan yon blazing svi' wuh suk tu'ash hearth. Wuh ha'gelek vesh' lit, heh wuh tu'ash dutch haul-tukh tam'a-nuf lam-tor, k' ein siphons t' soda-masu heh suk tresahk-makh tumblers, fi' wuh pi' marqueterie pasu. “gla-tor du ish-veh dvinsu tor me ved na' ha-kel, dorian. Au mazhiv-kur-tor me kanok-vei i aitlu, including ish-veh buhfik pi-maat-tukh-tipped cigarettes. Au nam-tor wuh danik hospitable creature. I spo' ish-veh mau weh-rom do wuh frenchman du nam-tor-tor ki'. Ra has shetau t' wuh frenchman, k' wuh bye?” dorian shrugged ish-veh tipan. “i dva-tor au telik t'sai radley’s maid, heh has afer-tor ish-veh svi' paris u' wuh eingelsu dressmaker. _anglomanie_ nam-tor maut fashionable abru' tra' i', i zhu-tor. Ish-veh seems silly t' wuh french, doesn’t ish-veh? Tonk'peh—tor du fai-tor?—au vesh' mokov wuh rasahkos dvinsu. I worla tishau ish-veh, tonk'peh i had nothing tor complain pa'. Veh k'ashiv glenonau vel ik nam-tor ved absurd. Au vesh' really maut vaikau tor me heh seemed ved sorry lu au went maf. Ma wuh'ashiv brandy-heh-soda? Il would du spo' hock-heh-seltzer? I kwon-hau-ov nem-tor hock-heh-seltzer myself. Tra' nam-tor sure tor nam-tor ein svi' wuh thurai tvi-shal.” “itaren, i skil-tor’t ma sovek-vel weht, ” leralmin-tor wuh krassu, taking ish-veh taik heh tor-pal ska' heh throwing au fi' wuh sa'haf ik au had shitau svi' wuh teruk. “heh i', t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, i aitlun tor stariben tor du seriously. Don’t kwal spo' ik. Du tor ish-veh ni mau weht rihagik na' me.” “ra nam-tor ish-veh ek' pa'?” maf-tor dorian svi' ish-veh petulant yut, flinging himself ne' fi' wuh ku-san. “i rok ish-veh nam-tor ri pa' myself. I am zungor t' myself tor-mu-yor. I dang spo' tor nam-tor somebody else.” “ish-veh nam-tor pa' yourself, ” kilko-tor hallward svi' ish-veh shi'vukhut glu spes, “heh i bolau leralmin ish-veh tor du. I dungau goh potau du ulef wuh wadan.” dorian spes-tevan heh lit wuh cigarette. “ulef wuh wadan!” au murmured. “ish-veh nam-tor ri mau tor ya'akash t' du, dorian, heh ish-veh nam-tor entirely na' ish-veh sha' sake ik i am speaking. I nah-tor ish-veh gas'rak ik du dang fai-tor ik wuh danik dreadful vel nam-tor hasu leralmin-tor tehnat du svi' london.” “i don’t istaya tor fai-tor sovek-vel pa' au. I ashaya scandals pa' vath sutra, tonk'peh scandals pa' myself don’t eku'ko me. Au ma ri prah wuh sem-rik t' novelty.” “au bolau eku'ko du, dorian. Kanok gentleman nam-tor interested svi' ish-veh rom ahm. Du don’t aitlun sutra tor variben t' du u' vel vile heh degraded. Veling, du ma ish-veh shul, heh ish-veh don-tak, heh ek' ik ves t' vel. Tonk'peh shul heh don-tak nam-tor ri kanok-vei. Kashek du, i don’t dva-tor aifa rumours na' ek'. K'puu, i mokuhlek’t dva-tor au lu gla-tor nash-veh du. Sin nam-tor wuh vel ik kitau itself mes' wuh sasu’s limuk. Ish-veh fam yehat nam-tor ip-sut. Sutra variben sometimes t' tsat vices. Tra' nam-tor rai such vel. Kuv wuh wretched sasu has wuh vice, ish-veh gluvau itself svi' wuh zehl t' ish-veh ru'lut, wuh tevan-tor t' ish-veh bezhun-wein, wuh moulding t' ish-veh el'ru kauk. Somebody—i skil-tor’t mention ish-veh ahm, tonk'peh du fai-tor ish-veh—sarlah tor me kim-shah tevun ki' ish-veh portrait ovsoh. I had worla gla-tor ish-veh fa', heh had worla puzhu-tor sovek-vel pa' ish-veh na' wuh wak, hi i ma puzhu-tor wuh rom deal opi'. Au nufau wuh madonik price. I klee'fah ish-veh. Tra' vesh' vel svi' wuh shid t' ish-veh ozh ik i fnu-ven. I fai-tor i' ik i vesh' ved gas'rak svi' ra i fancied pa' ish-veh. Ish-veh ha'kiv nam-tor dreadful. Tonk'peh du, dorian, k' ish-veh pure, ugelik, innocent limuk, heh ish-veh marvellous untroubled youth—i mokuhlek’t dva-tor sovek-vel tehnat du. Heh wi gla-tor nash-veh du maut seldom, heh du worla sarlah ne' tor wuh studio i', heh lu i am maf s' du, heh i zhu-tor ek' aifa hideous vel ik sutra nam-tor zhalan pa' du, i don’t fai-tor ra tor leralmin. Po nam-tor ish-veh, dorian, ik wuh sasu spo' wuh duke t' berwick mor wuh tvi-shal t' wuh muhd lu du svi-tor ish-veh? Po nam-tor ish-veh ik ni wehk gentlemen svi' london dungi neither hal-tor tor ish-veh kelek il invite du tor ish-veh? Du nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor wuh t'hy'la t' s'haile staveley. I ragel-tor ish-veh na' aru-yem kim-shah wehk gad. Ish-veh ahm pavesh-tor tor sarlah abru svi' conversation, svi' tersaya k' wuh miniatures du ma lent tor wuh exhibition na' wuh dudley. Staveley tcha-tor ish-veh bru heh leralmin-tor ik du lau ma wuh danik tanafluk zahv-tor, tonk'peh ik du vesh' wuh sasu ik rai pure-minded ko-kan dang nam-tor kal-tor tor fai-tor, heh ik rai chaste kosu dang hayal-tor svi' wuh ka tvi-shal k'. I reminded ish-veh ik i vesh' wuh t'hy'la t' ish-veh, heh ya'akash ish-veh ra au tvai. Au var-tor me. Au var-tor me gas'rak si' fa' kanok-veh. Ish-veh vesh' horrible! Po nam-tor ish-veh friendship ni fatal tor nu'ri sasu? Tra' vesh' ik wretched sa-kan svi' wuh klashau vi committed suicide. Du vesh' ish-veh lo'uk t'hy'la. Tra' vesh' osu henry ashton, vi had tor trasha england k' wuh tarnished ahm. Du heh au vesh' inseparable. Ra pa' adrian singleton heh ish-veh dreadful shaht? Ra pa' s'haile kent’s goh sa-fu heh ish-veh career? I ragel-tor ish-veh sa-mekh za-gad svi' st. James’s yut. Au seemed pushau k' mesh heh sorrow. Ra pa' wuh nu'ri duke t' perth? Ra wihfelau t' ha'kiv has au prah i'? Ra gentleman would katravahsu k' ish-veh?” “pehkaya, basil. Du nam-tor talking pa' vel t' if du fai-tor nothing, ” leralmin-tor dorian zhai-kur, biting ish-veh bru, heh k' wuh pitoh t' vaik contempt svi' ish-veh spes. “du ya'akash me po berwick mor wuh tvi-shal lu i svi-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor fai'ei i fai-tor kanok-vei pa' ish-veh ha'kiv, ri fai'ei au fai-tor sovek-vel pa' t'nash-veh. K' such khaf u' au has svi' ish-veh os-khaf-mev, uf kupi ish-veh vipladau nam-tor sok'i? Du ya'akash me pa' henry ashton heh nu'ri perth. Did i saven-tor wuh veh ish-veh vices, heh wuh vath ish-veh debauchery? Kuv kent’s silly sa-fu nem-tor ish-veh ko-telsu s' wuh yut, ra nam-tor ik tor me? Kuv adrian singleton kitau ish-veh t'hy'la’s ahm mes' wuh dun, am i ish-veh keeper? I fai-tor uf sutra chatter svi' england. Wuh svitan mohrn sov ish-veh moral prejudices abru' ish-veh gross aru-yem-pasu, heh zhal pa' ra au vutau wuh profligacies t' ish-veh betters svi' zek tor ar'kadan heh pretend ik au nam-tor svi' klon shila'es heh fi' intimate zhil k' wuh sutra au slander. Svi' nash shasol, ish-veh nam-tor hiyet na' wuh sasu tor ma distinction heh shi'nahp na' kanok tsuri lahv tor wag tehnat ish-veh. Heh ra wihfelau t' ha-tor tor aifa sutra, vi pose u' hasu moral, ras-tukh themselves? T'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, du yen-tor ik etek nam-tor svi' wuh salatik solektra t' wuh hypocrite.” “dorian, ” maf-tor hallward, “ik nam-tor ri wuh deshker. England nam-tor rasahkos hiyet i fai-tor, heh eingelsu shila'es nam-tor ek' riyeht. Ik nam-tor wuh utvau po i aitlun du tor nam-tor tok-ti. Du ma ri vesh' tok-ti. Veh has wuh gas'rak tor judge t' wuh sasu k' wuh daya au has abru' ish-veh t'hylara. Ish-veh seem tor pak-tor ek' kash-ral t' dor, t' goodness, t' purity. Du ma boshau au k' wuh ni-resh na' sanosh. Au ma hal-tor ne' vi' wuh gluder. Du pufulag-tor au tra'. Ha: du pufulag-tor au tra', heh wi du mokuhlek abru'teruklar-ru'lut, u' du nam-tor smiling i'. Heh tra' nam-tor weh-rasahkos za'. I fai-tor du heh harry nam-tor inseparable. Surely na' ik utvau, kuv na' rim vath, du dang ri ma tor ish-veh ko-kai’s ahm wuh k'-zhit.” “nem-tor tun, basil. Du hal-tor nuh' irak.” “i bolau stariben, heh du bolau shroi. Du dungau shroi. Lu du ragel-tor t'sai gwendolen, ri wuh esh t' scandal had ek'wak estuhl ish-veh. Nam-tor tra' wuh single tevan kosu svi' london i' vi would yetur k' ish-veh svi' wuh shi'sochya? Po, kauk ish-veh kanu nam-tor ri kal-tor tor ha-tor k' ish-veh. Yi tra' nam-tor vath var—var ik du ma vesh' gla-tor creeping na' gad-keshtan s' dreadful kelek heh slinking svi' pasut vi' wuh foulest dens svi' london. Nam-tor au yeht? Mokuhlek au nam-tor yeht? Lu i wuh'rak puzhu-tor au, i abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. I zhu-tor au i', heh au tor me ak'shem-hutau. Ra pa' ish-veh shasol-kelek heh wuh ha'kiv ik nam-tor pufulag-tor tra'? Dorian, du don’t fai-tor ra nam-tor leralmin-tor pa' du. I skil-tor’t var-tor du ik i don’t aitlun tor preach tor du. I vokau harry taran wuh'wak ik kanok sasu vi da-tor himself vi' wuh amateur curate na' wuh moment kwon-hau-ov began k' taran ik, heh yi proceeded tor shaya ish-veh zhit. I tor aitlun tor preach tor du. I aitlun du tor ras-tukh such wuh ha'kiv u' dungi tor wuh panu respect du. I aitlun du ki' wuh sok'i ahm heh wuh rom vipladau. I aitlun du tor prah rid t' wuh dreadful sutra du katravahsu k'. Don’t shrug ish-veh tipan spo' ik. Don’t nam-tor ni indifferent. Du ma wuh wonderful vi-yumuk. Kal-tor ish-veh nam-tor na' rom, ri na' ek'rasah. Au leralmin ik du corrupt kanok veh k' ik du shetau intimate, heh ik ish-veh nam-tor ved sufficient na' du tor svi-tor wuh kelek na' mesh t' ein ves tor zahal-tor po'. I don’t fai-tor whether ish-veh nam-tor ni il ri. Uf dang i fai-tor? Tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor leralmin-tor t' du. I am var-tor vel ik ish-veh seems impossible tor vet. S'haile gloucester vesh' veh t' t'nash-veh greatest t'hylara na' oxford. Au gluvau me wuh nuhm ik ish-veh ko-telsu had written tor ish-veh lu she vesh' dying sa'awek svi' ish-veh villa na' mentone. Ish-veh ahm vesh' implicated svi' wuh danik terrible confession i ek'wak telv-tor. I var-tor ish-veh ik ish-veh vesh' absurd—ik i fai-tor du thoroughly heh ik du vesh' incapable t' sovek-vel t' wuh ves. Fai-tor du? I wonder tor i fai-tor du? Fa' i kupi kilko-srashiv ik, i dang ma tor gla-tor ish-veh soul.” “tor gla-tor t'nash-veh soul!” muttered dorian zhai-kur, starting abru s' wuh ku-san heh turning siyah wan-kur s' pthak. “ha, ” kilko-tor hallward gravely, heh k' glu-toned sorrow svi' ish-veh spes, “tor gla-tor ish-veh soul. Tonk'peh goh oekon mokuhlek tor ik.” wuh sfith(-) abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' mockery shau s' wuh bru-lar t' wuh younger sasu. “du dungau gla-tor ish-veh yourself, tor-mu-yor!” au maf-tor, seizing wuh ha'gelek s' wuh pasu. “sarlah: ish-veh nam-tor ish-veh sha' handiwork. Po shouldn’t du glazhau na' ish-veh? Du mokuhlek var-tor wuh panu ek' pa' ish-veh afterwards, kuv du dvel-tor. Kling would dva-tor du. Kuv au did dva-tor du, au would spo' me ek' wuh weh-rom na' ish-veh. I fai-tor wuh ya'shakhuv weh-rom do du tor, hi du dungi prate pa' ish-veh ni tediously. Sarlah, i var-tor du. Du ma chattered hiyet pa' corruption. I' du dungau glazhau fi' ish-veh limuk tor limuk.” tra' vesh' wuh ni-resh t' pride svi' kanok zhit au uttered. Au stamped ish-veh ash'ya fi-tor wuh solektra svi' ish-veh boyish insolent manner. Au olau wuh terrible mak na' wuh nahp ik ein veh else vesh' tor thresh ish-veh tsat, heh ik wuh sasu vi had kras-tor wuh portrait ik vesh' wuh tveshu t' ek' ish-veh mesh vesh' tor nam-tor burdened na' wuh shom t' ish-veh ha'kiv k' wuh hideous vokaya t' ra au had ovsoh. “ha, ” au fator, coming closer tor ish-veh heh looking steadfastly vi' ish-veh harr-krus bezhun, “i dungau gluvaya du t'nash-veh soul. Du dungau gla-tor wuh vel ik du fancy goh oekon mokuhlek gla-tor.” hallward palikau pla'. “nash nam-tor blasphemy, dorian!” au maf-tor. “du bolau ri leralmin vel spo' ik. Au nam-tor horrible, heh au don’t tvai sovek-vel.” “du nah-tor ni?” au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor va'ashiv. “i fai-tor ni. U' na' ra i leralmin-tor tor du tor-mu-yor, i leralmin-tor ish-veh na' ish-veh rom. Du fai-tor i ma vesh' kwon-hau-ov wuh stanch t'hy'la tor du.” “don’t esta me. Shaht ra du ma tor leralmin.” wuh kuvoran-tor kahai t' kusut pohshaya mes' wuh krassu’s limuk. Au svizh-tor na' wuh moment, heh wuh kwai olaya t' pity sarlah abru' ish-veh. Po' ek', ra gas'rak had au tor ihv-tor vi' wuh ha'kiv t' dorian zhai-kur? Kuv au had ovsoh wuh tithe t' ra vesh' rumoured pa' ish-veh, uf mau au bolau ma dashau! Yi au straightened himself abru, heh lates-tor abru' tor wuh yon-shi, heh lam-tor tra', looking na' wuh yontau lap-fek k' ish-veh frostlike vitush heh ish-veh throbbing tviyan t' yai. “i am waiting, basil, ” leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri sasu svi' wuh lerash pa'shik spes. Au da-tor pauk. “ra i ma tor leralmin nam-tor nash, ” au maf-tor. “du bolau mazhiv-kur-tor me ein kilko-srashiv tor aifa horrible falun ik nam-tor tor tehnat du. Kuv du var-tor me ik au nam-tor absolutely untrue s' palikaya tor shaht, i dungau dva-tor du. Wafu au, dorian, wafu au! Mokuhlek’t gla-tor du ra i am going k'fai? T'nash-veh oekon! Don’t var-tor me ik du nam-tor rasahkos, heh corrupt, heh shameful.” dorian zhai-kur abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Tra' vesh' wuh tcha t' contempt svi' ish-veh bru-lar. “sarlah upstairs, basil, ” au leralmin-tor quietly. “i potau wuh gad-dunap t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv s' gad tor gad, heh ish-veh worla mor wuh tvi-shal svi' if ish-veh nam-tor written. I dungau gluvaya ish-veh tor du kuv sarlah du k' me.” “dungau-sarlah nash-veh k' du, dorian, kuv du istaya ish-veh. Gla-tor nash-veh i ma din-tor t'nash-veh ranau. Ik tor rai tukh. I mokuhlek hal-tor tor-morrow. Tonk'peh don’t ya'akash me tor telv-tor sovek-vel tor-mu-yor. Ek' i aitlun nam-tor wuh eiktra kilko-srashiv tor t'nash-veh deshker.” “ik dungau nam-tor putan-tor tor du upstairs. I kupi ri mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh la'. Du dungi ri ma tor telv-tor wu.” chapter xiii. Au be' dvun-tor s' wuh tvi-shal heh began wuh shen, basil hallward zahalik ikap-tor za'. Au lates-tor softly, u' sasu tor instinctively na' mu-yor. Wuh ha'gelek vishizhau fantastic duv fi' wuh temok heh staircase. Wuh rising salan tor ein t' wuh krani rattle. Lu au pulau wuh fik landing, dorian eku wuh ha'gelek ne' fi' wuh lan-tol, heh taking si' wuh tal-muv, da-tor ish-veh svi' wuh klachek. “du insist fi' fai-tor, basil?” au ya'akash svi' wuh neik spes. “ha.” “i am delighted, ” au kilko-tor, smiling. Yi au hau, somewhat harshly, “du nam-tor wuh veh sasu svi' wuh panu vi nam-tor entitled tor fai-tor kanok-vei pa' me. Du ma had weht tor tor k' t'nash-veh ha'kiv do du nah-tor”; heh, taking abru wuh ha'gelek, au tu'ash wuh svep heh went svi'. Wuh samu current t' sov be' dvun-tor au, heh wuh ta'hal pohshaya abru na' wuh moment svi' wuh yai t' murky zhar-kur. Au ak'shem-hutau. “ikap-tor wuh svep za' du, ” au zhal-tor, u' au shitau wuh ha'gelek fi' wuh pasu. Hallward glanced pauk ish-veh k' wuh puzzled sagluvaya. Wuh tvi-shal glazhau u' kuv ish-veh had ri vesh' ha-tor svi' na' tevun. Wuh spoh-tor flemish tapestry, wuh curtained bikuv, wuh hinek italian _cassone_, heh wuh siyah herbosh dunap-nuf—ik vesh' ek' ik ish-veh seemed tor tuhlau, isha wuh ku-san heh wuh pasu. U' dorian zhai-kur vesh' ha'gelan wuh ulef-yontau ha'fek ik vesh' standing fi' wuh mantelshelf, gla-tor ish-veh ik wuh bosh shi vesh' wein-tor k' grazhiv heh ik wuh la'y vesh' svi' razh. Wuh aushfa sahr-tor scuffling za' wuh wainscoting. Tra' vesh' wuh damp vil t' mildew. “ni du nah-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor goh oekon vi gla-tor wuh soul, basil? Bes-tor ik curtain pla', heh du dungi gla-tor t'nash-veh.” wuh spes ik stariben vesh' samu heh pi-maat'rer. “du nam-tor mad, dorian, il mavaun wuh krus, ” muttered hallward, frowning. “du skil-tor’t? Yi i bolau tor ish-veh myself, ” leralmin-tor wuh nu'ri sasu, heh au tore wuh curtain s' its fek heh flung ish-veh fi' wuh solektra. Wuh sporun t' horror shau s' wuh krassu’s bru-lar u' gla-tor ish-veh svi' wuh neik-ha'khlup ta'hal wuh hideous limuk fi' wuh canvas grinning na' ish-veh. Tra' vesh' vel svi' its sagluvaya ik boshau ish-veh k' spa'ash heh loathing. Rom heavens! Ish-veh vesh' dorian zhai-kur’s sha' limuk ik au vesh' looking na'! Wuh horror, whatever ish-veh vesh', had ri wi entirely spoiled ik marvellous vaksur. Tra' vesh' fam dvun ein pi-maat-tukh svi' wuh thinning isachya heh ein ug'yon-kur fi' wuh sensual ru'lut. Wuh sodden bezhun had potau vel t' wuh loveliness t' ish-veh pla-kur, wuh thol curves had ri wi completely be' dvun-tor maf s' chiselled han-sharular heh s' plastic drahk. Ha, ish-veh vesh' dorian himself. Tonk'peh vi had ovsoh ish-veh? Au seemed tor recognize ish-veh sha' brushwork, heh wuh nentu vesh' ish-veh sha' design. Wuh idea vesh' monstrous, wi au olau kwes. Au seized wuh lighted ha'fek, heh meskarau ish-veh tor wuh bikuv. Svi' wuh losrak-el'ru teruk vesh' ish-veh sha' ahm, traced svi' wu nuhm t' ugelik vermilion. Ish-veh vesh' ein flalik parody, ein infamous ignoble satire. Au had worla ovsoh ik. Fam dvun, ish-veh vesh' ish-veh sha' bikuv. Au fai-tor ish-veh, heh au olau u' kuv ish-veh khaf had rubai svi' wuh moment s' yon tor sluggish le-suma. Ish-veh sha' bikuv! Ra did ish-veh tvai? Po had ish-veh rubitau? Au da-tor heh glazhau na' dorian zhai-kur k' wuh bezhun t' wuh has-bosh sasu. Ish-veh ru'lut twitched, heh ish-veh parched lahv seemed unable tor articulate. Au be' dvun-tor ish-veh el'ru mes' ish-veh fa-patam. Ish-veh vesh' dank k' clammy wadashaya. Wuh nu'ri sasu vesh' leaning tehnat wuh mantelshelf, watching ish-veh k' ik flekh sagluvaya ish-veh gla-tor fi' wuh limuk t' eifa vi nam-tor absorbed svi' wuh mavau lu ein lo'uk tanafsu nam-tor peran. Tra' vesh' neither yeht sorrow svi' ish-veh il yeht mak. Tra' vesh' veling wuh shaukaush t' wuh spectator, k' sos'eh wuh hanuvaya t' triumph svi' ish-veh bezhun. Au had taken wuh svai s' ish-veh tor-pal, heh vesh' smelling ish-veh, il pretending tor tor ni. “ra tor nash tvai?” maf-tor hallward, na' kim-shah. Ish-veh sha' spes sounded shrill heh curious svi' ish-veh kaluk. “tevun ago, lu i vesh' wuh sa-kan, ” leralmin-tor dorian zhai-kur, crushing wuh svai svi' ish-veh el'ru, “du ragel-tor me, snuhkrol-tor me, heh saven-tor me tor nam-tor vain t' t'nash-veh rom glazhau. Veh gad du puragtau me tor wuh t'hy'la t' ish-veh, vi danau tor me wuh wonder t' youth, heh du shahtau wuh portrait t' me ik revealed tor me wuh wonder t' vaksur. Svi' wuh mad moment ik, kauk i', i don’t fai-tor whether i regret il ri, i tor wuh istaya, sos'eh du would vutau ish-veh wuh prayer.” “i vokau ish-veh! Oh, uf muhl i vokau ish-veh! Rai! Wuh vel nam-tor impossible. Wuh tvi-shal nam-tor damp. Mildew has prah vi' wuh canvas. Wuh kras-tor i nam-tor-tor had ein wretched ek'tukh gisam svi' au. I var-tor du wuh vel nam-tor impossible.” “ah, ra nam-tor impossible?” murmured wuh nu'ri sasu, going abru' tor wuh krani heh leaning ish-veh fa-patam tehnat wuh samu, mist-kurau makh. “du var-tor me du had vashau ish-veh.” “i vesh' riyeht. Ish-veh has vashau me.” “i don’t dva-tor ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh bikuv.” “mokuhlek’t gla-tor du ish-veh tangu svi' ish-veh?” leralmin-tor dorian bitterly. “t'nash-veh tangu, u' du vutau ish-veh.” “u' du puvutau ish-veh.” “tra' vesh' nothing ek'rasah svi' ish-veh, nothing shameful. Du vesh' tor me such wuh tangu u' i dungau worla ragel-tor va'ashiv. Nash nam-tor wuh limuk t' wuh satyr.” “ish-veh nam-tor wuh limuk t' t'nash-veh soul.” “christ! Ra wuh vel i bolau ma worshipped! Ish-veh has wuh bezhun t' wuh e'shua.” “tik t' etek has sha-ka-ri heh bogozh svi' ish-veh, basil, ” maf-tor dorian k' wuh kwai gesture t' despair. Hallward da-tor va'ashiv tor wuh portrait heh gazed na' ish-veh. “t'nash-veh oekon! Kuv ish-veh nam-tor yeht, ” au sporiben, “heh nash nam-tor ra du ma ovsoh k' ish-veh ha'kiv, po, du bolau nam-tor weh-rasahkos kauk do eifa vi variben tehnat du fancy du tor nam-tor!” au meskarau wuh ta'hal abru va'ashiv tor wuh canvas heh linisau ish-veh. Wuh skonn seemed tor nam-tor ved undisturbed heh u' au had losrak ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' s' k'svi, sauyaing, ik wuh foulness heh horror had sarlah. K'fai ein flekh quickening t' tvik ha'kiv wuh leprosies t' sin vesh' slowly eating wuh vel maf. Wuh rotting t' wuh tevikeh svi' wuh watery shi'vukhut vesh' ri ni pthak-bosh. Ish-veh el'ru hutau, heh wuh ha'fek tevan-tor s' its socket fi' wuh lan-tol heh ti tra' sputtering. Au shitau ish-veh ash'ya fi' ish-veh heh shitau ish-veh si'. Yi au flung himself vi' wuh rickety ku-san ik vesh' standing k' wuh pasu heh visolektau ish-veh limuk svi' ish-veh el'ru. “rom oekon, dorian, ra wuh tupa! Ra wuh awful tupa!” tra' vesh' rai kilko-srashiv, tonk'peh au kupi zhu-tor wuh nu'ri sasu sobbing na' wuh krani. “pray, dorian, pray, ” au murmured. “ra nam-tor ish-veh ish-veh vesh' saven-tor tor leralmin svi' veh’s boyhood? ‘ras-tukh etek ri vi' temptation. Forgive etek etwel sins. Pu-tor maf etwel iniquities.’ kal-tor etek leralmin ik teretuhr. Wuh prayer t' ish-veh pride has vesh' kilko-tor. Wuh prayer t' ish-veh repentance dungi nam-tor kilko-tor isha. I worshipped du nuh' mau. I am taflau na' ish-veh. Du worshipped yourself nuh' mau. Etek nam-tor fi' taflau.” dorian zhai-kur da-tor slowly pa' heh glazhau na' ish-veh k' bezhun-masu-ha'khlup-ne-tor bezhun. “ish-veh nam-tor nuh' tab-ma, basil, ” au faltered. “ish-veh nam-tor worla nuh' tab-ma, dorian. Kal-tor etek kneel ne' heh ar'kadan kuv etek fam yehat vokau wuh prayer. Isn’t tra' wuh zehl ein-wilat, ‘hi ish-veh sins nam-tor u' ug'yon-kur, wi i dungi tor au u' wan-kur u' izh’?” “eifa zhit tvai nothing tor me i'.” “hush! Don’t leralmin ik. Du ma ovsoh hiyet ek'rasah svi' ish-veh ha'kiv. T'nash-veh oekon! Don’t gla-tor du ik accursed vel leering na' etek?” dorian zhai-kur glanced na' wuh bikuv, heh suddenly wuh uncontrollable olaya t' hatred na' basil hallward sarlah abru' ish-veh, u' hi ish-veh had vesh' suggested tor ish-veh k' wuh glakuv fi' wuh canvas, zhal-tor vi' ish-veh kaluk k' eifa grinning bru-lar. Wuh mad shaukaush t' wuh shi'kar aushfa stirred k'svi ish-veh, heh au loathed wuh sasu vi vesh' hayal-tor na' wuh pasu, weht do svi' ish-veh bosh ha'kiv au had ek'wak loathed sovek-vel. Au glanced wildly pa'. Vel glimmered fi' wuh fik t' wuh kras-tor tuf ik limuk-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh bezhun tevan-tor fi' ish-veh. Au fai-tor ra ish-veh vesh'. Ish-veh vesh' wuh lipau ik au had katau abru, ein gad fa', tor tresahk wuh krus t' elakh, heh had yen-tor tor nem-tor maf k' ish-veh. Au dvun-tor slowly na' ish-veh, be' dvun-tor hallward u' au did ni. U' ak u' au prah za' ish-veh, au seized ish-veh heh da-tor pauk. Hallward stirred svi' ish-veh ku-san u' kuv au vesh' going tor shen. Au rushed na' ish-veh heh hil-tor wuh lipau vi' wuh lo'uk os-khaf-mev ik nam-tor za' wuh kaluk, crushing wuh sasu’s patam ne' fi' wuh pasu heh stabbing va'ashiv heh va'ashiv. Tra' vesh' wuh stifled groan heh wuh horrible ralash t' ein veh choking k' khaf. Rehkuh wak wuh outstretched kar pohshaya abru convulsively, pral-tor grotesque, stegel-fingered el'ru svi' wuh sov. Au stabbed ish-veh dah'wak weht, tonk'peh wuh sasu did ri dvun. Vel began tor itsk-yumaya fi' wuh lan-tol. Au bek-tor na' wuh moment, fam dvun pressing wuh patam ne'. Yi au threw wuh lipau fi' wuh pasu, heh shroi. Au kupi zhu-tor nothing, tonk'peh wuh thezh, thezh fi' wuh threadbare la'y. Au tu'ash wuh svep heh went si' fi' wuh landing. Wuh kelek vesh' absolutely hizhuk. Kling vesh' pa'. Na' wuh zamu seconds au lam-tor bending abru' wuh balustrade heh peering ne' vi' wuh nesh-kur seething muhl t' mu'khlup'es. Yi au nem-tor si' wuh tal-muv heh fun-tor tor wuh tvi-shal, locking himself svi' u' au did ni. Wuh vel vesh' fam dvun hayal-tor svi' wuh ku-san, straining abru' wuh pasu k' ovalau patam, heh humped pla', heh wu fantastic kar. Had ish-veh ri vesh' na' wuh yon-kur jagged bezhun-masu svi' wuh talu heh wuh clotted nesh-kur patra ik vesh' slowly eikan fi' wuh pasu, veh would ma leralmin-tor ik wuh sasu vesh' veling asleep. Uf sahris ish-veh had ek' vesh' ovsoh! Au olau strangely hayal, heh walking abru' tor wuh krani, tu'ash ish-veh heh ash-tor si' fi' wuh fah-yat. Wuh salan had blown wuh ihsek maf, heh wuh igen vesh' spo' wuh monstrous peacock’s harr, starred k' myriads t' pi-maat-kur bezhun. Au glazhau ne' heh gla-tor wuh policeman going ish-veh rounds heh flashing wuh wu ha-zehl t' ish-veh makh-yonet fi' wuh svep t' wuh ralash-fam kelek. Wuh hirat-kur gla-tor t' wuh prowling hansom gleamed na' wuh teruk heh yi vanished. Wuh kosu svi' wuh fluttering shawl vesh' creeping slowly k' wuh railings, staggering u' she went. I' heh yi she pehkau heh peered pla'. Wuh'wak, she began tor uralau svi' wuh hoarse spes. Wuh policeman strolled abru' heh leralmin-tor vel tor ish-veh. She stumbled maf, laughing. Wuh sfith(-) thorshaya swept mes' wuh keh-vla. Wuh pa-tukh-ha'gelek hanuvau heh became pla-kur, heh wuh leafless lap hutau ish-veh nesh-kur shek-tukh khlup tor heh fro. Au shivered heh went pla', ikapik wuh krani za' ish-veh. Having pulau wuh svep, au da-tor wuh tal-muv heh tu'ash ish-veh. Au did ri kauk glance na' wuh riyeht-stau sasu. Au olau ik wuh tsat t' wuh bosh vel vesh' ri tor realize wuh situation. Wuh t'hy'la vi had kras-tor wuh fatal portrait tor if ek' ish-veh misery had vesh' due had hal-tor s' ish-veh ha'kiv. Ik vesh' hiyet. Yi au vokau wuh ha'gelek. Ish-veh vesh' wuh rather curious veh t' moorish workmanship, tor t' pasik haul-tukh inlaid k' arabesques t' burnished pishek, heh studded k' dirik folu-kur. Sos'eh ish-veh lau nam-tor din-tor k' ish-veh dvinsu, heh deshkau would nam-tor ya'akash. Au hesitated na' wuh moment, yi au da-tor pla' heh nem-tor ish-veh s' wuh pasu. Au kupi ri gol'nev seeing wuh tevik vel. Uf fam dvun ish-veh vesh'! Uf horribly wan-kur wuh wu el'ru glazhau! Ish-veh vesh' spo' wuh dreadful wax glakuv. Having klacha wuh svep za' ish-veh, au crept quietly downstairs. Wuh woodwork creaked heh seemed tor lit'dhae u' kuv svi' kusut. Au pehkau several wak heh bek-tor. Rai: kanok-vei vesh' fam dvun. Ish-veh vesh' goh wuh ralash t' ish-veh sha' footsteps. Lu au pulau wuh shi'dunap, gla-tor ish-veh wuh sa'haf heh tor-pal svi' wuh teruk. Au bolau nam-tor ipik maf ein-wilat. Au unlocked wuh tsat hish-tor ik vesh' svi' wuh wainscoting, wuh hish-tor svi' if au potau ish-veh sha' curious pastau, heh shitau au vi' ish-veh. Au kupi easily yontau au afterwards. Yi au seshau si' ish-veh glantau. Ish-veh vesh' dah-leh minutes tor dahkuh. Au hayal-tor ne' heh began tor nah-tor. Kanok tevun—kanok tevun-krus, siyah—sasu vesh' strangled svi' england na' ra au had ovsoh. Tra' had vesh' wuh ni-resh t' riyeht-staya svi' wuh sov. Ein yon-kur yel had sarlah nuh' beyik wuh terra. Heh wi, ra evidence vesh' tra' tehnat ish-veh? Basil hallward had losrak wuh kelek na' leh-wun. Kling had gla-tor ish-veh sarlah svi' va'ashiv. Danik t' wuh dvinsu vesh' na' selby royal. Ish-veh valet had hal-tor tor sar-tak. Paris! Ha. Ish-veh vesh' tor paris ik basil had hal-tor, heh k' wuh midnight ranau, u' au had intended. K' ish-veh curious reserved es'merka, ish-veh would nam-tor tevun-krus fa' sovek suspicions would nam-tor kastorilau. Tevun-krus! Kanok-vei kupi nam-tor vashau wu fa' yi. Wuh sudden nahp kwul-tor ish-veh. Au shitau fi' ish-veh ausachya tor-pal heh taik heh went si' vi' wuh tvur. Tra' au svizh-tor, khaf-spol wuh vohris ras tread t' wuh policeman fi' wuh pavement s'udish heh seeing wuh kahai t' wuh bull’s-bezhun haul-tor svi' wuh krani. Au bek-tor heh meskarau ish-veh esh. Po' wuh zamu moments au drew pla' wuh kuhr heh trel-tor si', shutting wuh svep maut kogavik za' ish-veh. Yi au began ringing wuh kus-vakh. Svi' pa' kaukuh minutes ish-veh valet saudau, ulef-sai-vel-tor heh looking maut drowsy. “ni'droi'ik nar-tor ki' had tor wake du abru, francis, ” au leralmin-tor, stepping svi'; “tonk'peh i had yen-tor t'nash-veh kuhr-tal-muv. Ra wak nam-tor ish-veh?” “lehkuh minutes vesht dahkuh, osu, ” kilko-tor wuh sasu, looking na' wuh wak-vel heh blinking. “lehkuh minutes vesht dahkuh? Uf horribly tab-ma! Du bolau wake me na' naukuh tor-morrow. I ma ein ar'kadan tor tor.” “ek' gas'rak, osu.” “did sovek veh vutau nash khru?” “mr. Hallward, osu. Au stayed la' till leh-wun, heh yi au went maf tor kum ish-veh ranau.” “oh! Ni'droi'ik nar-tor i didn’t gla-tor ish-veh. Did au trasha sovek skladan?” “rai, osu, kaula ik au would kitau tor du s' paris, kuv au did ri talal du na' wuh muhd.” “ik dungi tor, francis. Don’t yen-tor tor vutau me na' naukuh tor-morrow.” “rai, osu.” wuh sasu shambled ne' wuh tvur svi' ish-veh slippers. Dorian zhai-kur threw ish-veh taik heh tor-pal fi-tor wuh pasu heh be' dvun-tor vi' wuh shi'dunap. Na' wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan au lates-tor abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal, biting ish-veh bru heh thinking. Yi au nem-tor ne' wuh pla-kur dunap s' veh t' wuh nef heh began tor da-tor abru' wuh mor. “alan campbell, 152, hertford yut, mayfair.” ha; ik vesh' wuh sasu au aitlu. Chapter xiv. Na' naukuh o’wak-vel wuh thurai asal ish-veh dvinsu sarlah svi' k' wuh cup t' chocolate fi' wuh tray heh tu'ash wuh fe-wein. Dorian vesh' sleeping ved peacefully, lying fi' ish-veh gas'rak vla, k' veh el'ru ne'rak ish-veh nak. Au glazhau spo' wuh sa-kan vi had vesh' zungor si' k' mavau, il orenau. Wuh sasu had tor esta ish-veh dah'wak fi' wuh tipan fa' au woke, heh u' au tu'ash ish-veh bezhun wuh faint abru'teruklar-ru'lut be' dvun-tor mes' ish-veh bru-lar, u' hi au had vesh' pakik svi' ein delightful sahr-tor. Wi au had ri sahr-tor-tor na' ek'. Ish-veh mu-yor had vesh' untroubled k' sovek glakuv t' sanosh il t' kusut. Tonk'peh youth abru'teruklar-ru'lut rik' sovek utvau. Ish-veh nam-tor veh t' its chiefest sem-rik-tor. Au da-tor pauk, heh leaning fi-tor ish-veh kar-nef, began tor mon-tor ish-veh chocolate. Wuh mellow november yel sarlah streaming vi' wuh tvi-shal. Wuh igen vesh' ugelik, heh tra' vesh' wuh genial warmth svi' wuh sov. Ish-veh vesh' siyah spo' wuh asal svi' lau. Gradually wuh pavek t' wuh preceding mu-yor crept k' ralash-fam, khaf-kurau ash'ya vi' ish-veh shi'nahp heh reconstructed themselves tra' k' terrible distinctness. Au winced na' wuh vokaya t' ek' ik au had dashau, heh na' wuh moment wuh ka curious olaya t' loathing na' basil hallward ik had tor ish-veh stau ish-veh u' au hayal-tor svi' wuh ku-san sarlah pla' tor ish-veh, heh au grew samu k' shaukaush. Wuh tevik sasu vesh' fam dvun sitting tra', nuh', heh svi' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel i'. Uf horrible ik vesh'! Such hideous vel vesh' na' wuh mu'khlup'es, ri na' wuh gad. Au olau ik kuv au brooded fi' ra au had hal-tor k'fai au would sicken il tor'ovau mad. Tra' vesh' sins t'vi sem vesh' weht svi' wuh vokaya do svi' wuh doing t' au, flekh triumphs ik gratified wuh pride weht do wuh shaukaush, heh mazhiv-kur-tor tor wuh kash-tor-vel wuh quickened kash-ral t' mak, weht tor sovek mak au katau, il kupi ek'wak katau, tor wuh kash-ral. Tonk'peh nash vesh' ri veh t' au. Ish-veh vesh' wuh vel tor nam-tor driven si' t' wuh kashek, tor nam-tor drugged k' poppies, tor nam-tor strangled lest ish-veh lau strangle veh itself. Lu wuh ulef-wadan kwul-tor, au be' dvun-tor ish-veh el'ru mes' ish-veh fa-patam, heh yi prah abru hastily heh sai-vel-tor himself k' kauk weht do ish-veh tsuri tun, giving wuh rom deal t' attention tor wuh dvel t' ish-veh necktie heh scarf-pin heh rubai ish-veh mokov weht do wuh'wak. Au spent wuh akarshif isha abru' asal-yem, tasting wuh vuhnauk dishes, talking tor ish-veh valet pa' ein uzh liveries ik au vesh' thinking t' getting tor na' wuh dvinsu na' selby, heh going k'fai ish-veh correspondence. Na' ein t' wuh nuhm, au abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Rehkuh t' au bored ish-veh. Veh au telv-tor several wak abru' heh yi tore abru k' wuh slight glazhau t' il'nai'ga svi' ish-veh limuk. “ik awful vel, wuh kosu’s vokaya!” u' s'haile henry had wuh'wak leralmin-tor. Po' au had mon-tor ish-veh cup t' nesh-kur mon, au psethau ish-veh bru-lar slowly k' wuh ru'lut-sai, motioned tor ish-veh dvinsu tor bek-tor, heh going abru' tor wuh pasu, hayal-tor ne' heh kitau dahkuh nuhm. Veh au shitau svi' ish-veh abru'lik, wuh vath au handed tor wuh valet. “nem-tor nash pauk tor 152, hertford yut, francis, heh kuv mr. Campbell nam-tor s' kahr, prah ish-veh shi'yavekh.” u' ak u' au vesh' sa'awek, au lit wuh cigarette heh began lubestan fi-tor wuh krus t' dun, bestan wuh'rak svai heh bits t' te'koshif, heh yi komihn limuk. Suddenly au remarked ik kanok limuk ik au drew seemed ki' wuh fantastic likeness tor basil hallward. Au kwal-tor, heh getting abru, went abru' tor wuh dunap-nuf heh nem-tor si' wuh ral'es na' hazard. Au vesh' satalau ik au would ri nah-tor pa' ra had pavesh-tor abi' ish-veh became absolutely bolayatik ik au dang tor ni. Lu au had sakadau himself fi' wuh ku-san, au glazhau na' wuh title-thalv t' wuh dunap. Ish-veh vesh' gautier’s “Émaux et nafaiées”, charpentier’s japanese-dun yadan, k' wuh jacquemart etching. Wuh binding vesh' t' citron-yar-kur duf, k' wuh design t' gilt trellis-ar'kadan heh dotted naric. Ish-veh had vesh' putan-tor tor ish-veh k' adrian singleton. U' au da-tor abru' wuh thalv, ish-veh bezhun tevan-tor fi' wuh poem pa' wuh el'ru t' lacenaire, wuh samu kin-kur el'ru “_du supplice encore mal lavée_, ” k' its downy yon-kur isachya heh its “_doigts de faune_.” au glanced na' ish-veh sha' wan-kur taper ozh, shuddering slightly svi' spite t' himself, heh be' dvun-tor fi', till sarlah ish-veh tor eifa lovely stanzas fi-tor venice: sur une gamme chromatique, le sein de perles ruisselant, la vénus de l’adriatique wihfelau de l’eau sa-fu corps she-tor et blanc. Les dômes, sur l’azur des ondes suivant la zhit-bal au pur contour, s’enflent comme des gorges rondes que soulève un soupir d’amour. L’esquif aborde et me dépose, jetant sa-fu amarre au pilier, devant une façade she-tor, sur le marbre d’un escalier. Uf exquisite au vesh'! U' veh telv-tor au, veh seemed tor nam-tor floating ne' wuh yar-kur masu-yut t' wuh faf-kur heh pearl kahr, hayal-tor svi' wuh nesh-kur gondola k' haul-tukh prow heh trailing curtains. Wuh mere zehl glazhau tor ish-veh spo' eifa zehik zehl t' folu-kur-pla-kur ik zahal-tor veh u' veh kwitau si' tor wuh lido. Wuh sudden kahai t' kur reminded ish-veh t' wuh gleam t' wuh opal-heh-kurak-throated kushel ik nuv pauk wuh ha-vol honeycombed campanile, il stalk, k' such stately takov, k'fai wuh neik-ha'khlup, grazhiv-kurau kesek-weizehl. Leaning pla' k' ulef-a'ing bezhun, au potau taran abru' heh abru' tor himself: “devant une façade she-tor, sur le marbre d’un escalier.” wuh bosh t' venice vesh' svi' eifa dahkuh zehl. Au vokau wuh tasmin ik au had be' dvun-tor tra', heh wuh wonderful ashaya ik had stirred ish-veh tor mad delightful follies. Tra' vesh' romance svi' kanok shi. Tonk'peh venice, spo' oxford, had potau wuh za-mesu na' romance, heh, tor wuh yeht romantic, za-mesu vesh' kanok-vei, il siyah kanok-vei. Basil had vesh' k' ish-veh krus t' wuh wak, heh had hal-tor kwai abru' tintoret. Ri donku-tor basil! Ra wuh horrible yut na' wuh sasu tor tev-tor! Au spes-tevan, heh nem-tor abru wuh ral'es va'ashiv, heh ar'kada tor yen-tor. Au telv-tor t' wuh vitem-tor ik hash-tor svi' heh s' wuh pi' _café_ na' smyrna wilat wuh hadjis hayal-tor counting ish-veh puhku o'lid heh wuh turbaned merchants vuzh ish-veh wu tasselled mev heh variben gravely tor tik vath; au telv-tor t' wuh obelisk svi' wuh shi de la concorde ik tusa-tor bezhun-masu t' zasuhl svi' its lonely sunless sashasolaya heh longs tor nam-tor pla' k' wuh fal, lotus-wein-tor nile, wilat tra' nam-tor sphinxes, heh she-tor-yon-kur ibises, heh wan-kur vultures k' gilded spahk, heh crocodiles k' pi' beryl bezhun ik ukrau abru' wuh yar-kur steaming vral; au began tor kesh-travek abru' eifa zehl if, bestan ralash-tanaf s' shok-kurau marble, var-tor t' ik curious sukhlop ik gautier tcok'at tor wuh contralto spes, wuh “_monstre charmant_” ik ku-san svi' wuh khush-zul-kov-tvi-shal t' wuh louvre. Tonk'peh po' wuh wak wuh dunap tevan-tor s' ish-veh el'ru. Au grew nervous, heh wuh horrible nunau t' vash sarlah abru' ish-veh. Ra kuv alan campbell dang nam-tor s' england? Gad would veshaya fa' au kupi sarlah pla'. Sos'eh au lau klee'fah tor sarlah. Ra kupi au tor yi? Kanok moment vesh' t' bolik importance. Au had vesh' lo'uk t'hylara wuh'wak, kaukuh tevun fa'—siyah inseparable, indeed. Yi wuh intimacy had sarlah suddenly tor wuh shaht. Lu au ragel-tor svi' shila'es i', ish-veh vesh' goh dorian zhai-kur vi abru'teruklar-ru'lut: alan campbell worla did. Au vesh' wuh extremely clever nu'ri sasu, hi au had rai yeht appreciation t' wuh visible arts, heh whatever pi' kash-ral t' wuh vaksur t' poetry au ma au had nazh-tor entirely s' dorian. Ish-veh abrupik intellectual shaukaush vesh' na' ek'tal. Na' cambridge au had spent wuh lo'uk deal t' ish-veh wak working svi' wuh ek'tal-zup-shal, heh had taken wuh rom mohrn svi' wuh malatik ek'tal tripos t' ish-veh tevun. Indeed, au vesh' fam dvun vaikau tor wuh orenau t' meil-tal, heh had wuh ek'tal-zup-shal t' ish-veh sha' svi' if au nam-tor-tor tor ikap-tor himself abru ek' gad wu, greatly tor wuh il'nai'ga t' ish-veh ko-mekh, vi had eku ish-veh khaf-spol fi' ish-veh standing na' parliament heh had wuh vague idea ik wuh meil-talsu vesh' wuh person vi tor abru prescriptions. Au vesh' wuh marom ralash-tanafsu, however, u' muhl, heh mavau fi' wuh violin heh wuh piano weh-rom do danik amateurs. Svi' kla-min, ish-veh vesh' ralash-tanaf ik had wuh'rak katau ish-veh heh dorian zhai-kur teretuhr—ralash-tanaf heh ik indefinable skamaya ik dorian seemed tor nam-tor kup tor tusok whenever au istau—heh, indeed, tusok-tor k'ashiv rik' hasu d'wonil t' ish-veh. Au had ragel-tor na' t'sai berkshire’s wuh mu-yor ik rubinstein mavau tra', heh po' ik nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor kwon-hau-ov gla-tor teretuhr na' wuh opera heh wherever rom ralash-tanaf vesh' going fi'. Na' leh-oh tevun-krus ish-veh intimacy palesh-tor. Campbell vesh' kwon-hau-ov either na' selby royal il svi' grosvenor keh-vla. Tor ish-veh, u' tor wehk vath, dorian zhai-kur vesh' wuh ves t' kanok-vei ik nam-tor wonderful heh sem-rik svi' ha'kiv. Whether il ri wuh quarrel had taken shi svi' au kling ek'wak fai-tor. Tonk'peh suddenly sutra remarked ik au scarcely stariben lu au ragel-tor heh ik campbell seemed kwon-hau-ov tor hal-tor maf lehkuh-mal s' sovek party na' if dorian zhai-kur vesh' la'. Au had rubai, nuh'—vesh' strangely melancholy na' wak, saudau siyah tor ritishaya khaf-spol ralash-tanaf, heh would worla himself mavau, giving u' ish-veh tobeg, lu au vesh' puvutau fi-tor, ik au vesh' ni absorbed svi' ek'tal ik au had rai wak losrak svi' if tor practise. Heh nash vesh' certainly yeht. Kanok gad au seemed tor shetau weht interested svi' ha-tal, heh ish-veh ahm saudau wuh'wak il dah'wak svi' ein t' wuh talik reviews svi' tersaya k' ac'ruth curious spolek. Nash vesh' wuh sasu dorian zhai-kur vesh' waiting na'. Kanok dahr au potau glancing na' wuh wak-vel. U' wuh minutes went k' au became horribly pahutau. Na' kim-shah au prah abru heh began tor sahr abru heh ne' wuh tvi-shal, looking spo' wuh vaksurik kraiskau vel. Au nem-tor wu stealthy strides. Ish-veh el'ru vesh' curiously samu. Wuh suspense became unbearable. Wak seemed tor ish-veh tor nam-tor crawling k' ash'ya t' ras-tukh, du' au k' monstrous salan vesh' hasu swept na' wuh jagged rihk t' ein nesh-kur thresh t' precipice. Au fai-tor ra vesh' waiting na' ish-veh tra'; gla-tor ish-veh, indeed, heh, shuddering, plesh-tor k' dank el'ru ish-veh yontau lids u' hi au would ma robbed wuh maut shi'nahp t' glan heh driven wuh bezhun-kal pla' vi' ish-veh tauk. Ish-veh vesh' nam-tor-fam. Wuh shi'nahp had its sha' yem-tukh fi' if ish-veh battened, heh wuh glenonaya, tor grotesque k' vash, kuvoran-tor heh distorted u' wuh living vel k' kusut, tam-tor spo' ein flalik puppet fi' wuh lamok heh wa'limatau k'fai dvun-tor limein. Yi, suddenly, wak pehkau na' ish-veh. Ha: ik glan-fam, vohris-eshan vel ukrau rai weht, heh horrible nahp, wak hasu tevik, raced nimbly fi' svi' khom, heh zaseshau wuh hideous fa-wak s' its shi'vukhut, heh gluvau ish-veh tor ish-veh. Au nantau na' ish-veh. Its maut horror tor ish-veh kov. Na' kim-shah wuh svep tu'ash heh ish-veh dvinsu svi-tor. Au da-tor glazed bezhun fi-tor ish-veh. “mr. Campbell, osu, ” leralmin-tor wuh sasu. Wuh spes-tevan t' vas shau s' ish-veh parched bru-lar, heh wuh kur sarlah pla' tor ish-veh nak. “ya'akash ish-veh tor sarlah svi' na' wuh'wak, francis.” au olau ik au vesh' himself va'ashiv. Ish-veh mood t' cowardice had be' dvun-tor maf. Wuh sasu ovalau heh retired. Svi' wuh zamu moments, alan campbell lates-tor svi', looking maut harr-krus heh rather spoh, ish-veh ritsuri-spoh'es hasu intensified k' ish-veh kastik-kov-nesh-kur isachya heh gu'gelik bezhun-zehl. “alan! Nash nam-tor ves t' du. I nemaiyo na' coming.” “i had intended worla tor svi-tor ish-veh kelek va'ashiv, zhai-kur. Tonk'peh du leralmin-tor ish-veh vesh' wuh tukh t' ha'kiv heh tevakh.” ish-veh spes vesh' lerash heh samu. Au stariben k' vohris deliberation. Tra' vesh' wuh glazhau t' contempt svi' wuh br'xan searching gaze ik au da-tor fi' dorian. Au potau ish-veh el'ru svi' wuh abru'lik t' ish-veh astrakhan tor-pal, heh seemed ri ki' pubeglanau wuh gesture k' if au had vesh' puna-shau. “ha: ish-veh nam-tor wuh tukh t' ha'kiv heh tevakh, alan, heh tor weht do veh person. Hayal-tor ne'.” campbell nem-tor wuh ku-san k' wuh pasu, heh dorian hayal-tor mesyutik tor ish-veh. Wuh dahkuh sasu’s bezhun ragel-tor. Svi' dorian’s tra' vesh' vaik pity. Au fai-tor ik ra au vesh' going tor tor vesh' dreadful. Po' wuh ish-veh-tor moment t' silence, au gal-tor mes' heh leralmin-tor, maut quietly, tonk'peh watching wuh daya t' tik zhit fi-tor wuh limuk t' ish-veh au had satau na', “alan, svi' wuh klacha tvi-shal na' wuh fik t' nash kelek, wuh tvi-shal tor if kling tonk'peh myself has access, wuh tevik sasu nam-tor hayal-tor na' wuh pasu. Au has vesh' tevik lehkuh wadan i'. Don’t stir, heh don’t glazhau na' me spo' ik. Vi wuh sasu nam-tor, po au tev-tor, uf au tev-tor, nam-tor tukh ik ri tor concern du. Ra du ma tor tor nam-tor nash—” “pehkaya, zhai-kur. I don’t aitlun tor fai-tor sovek-vel further. Whether ra du ma var-tor me nam-tor yeht il ri yeht doesn’t concern me. I entirely decline tor nam-tor rish-tor abru svi' ish-veh ha'kiv. Potau ish-veh horrible tsat tor yourself. Au don’t eku'ko me sovek weht.” “alan, au dungi ma tor eku'ko du. Nash-veh dungi ma tor eku'ko du. I am awfully sorry na' du, alan. Tonk'peh i mokuhlek’t gol'nev myself. Du nam-tor wuh veh sasu vi nam-tor kup tor korsau me. I am punekwitau tor katau du vi' wuh tukh. I ma rai option. Alan, du nam-tor talik. Du fai-tor pa' meil-tal heh vel t' ik ves. Du ma tor spolek. Ra du ma prah tor tor nam-tor tor vashau wuh vel ik nam-tor upstairs—tor vashau ish-veh ni ik ri wuh vestige t' ish-veh dungi nam-tor losrak. Kling gla-tor nash person sarlah vi' wuh kelek. Indeed, na' wuh la' moment au nam-tor supposed tor nam-tor svi' paris. Au dungi ri nam-tor din-tor na' tevun-krus. Lu au nam-tor din-tor, tra' bolau nam-tor rai zavikau t' ish-veh afer-tor la'. Du, alan, du bolau rubah ish-veh, heh kanok-vei ik t' ish-veh, vi' wuh handful t' vitush ik i lau scatter svi' wuh sov.” “du nam-tor mad, dorian.” “ah! I vesh' waiting na' du tor vutau me dorian.” “du nam-tor mad, i var-tor du—mad tor glenonau ik i would ashenau wuh ozh tor gol'nev du, mad tor tor nash monstrous confession. I dungi ma nothing tor tor k' nash tukh, whatever ish-veh nam-tor. Tor du nah-tor i am going tor peril t'nash-veh reputation na' du? Ra nam-tor ish-veh tor me ra e'shua’s ar'kadan du nam-tor abru tor?” “ish-veh vesh' suicide, alan.” “i am glad t' ik. Tonk'peh vi drove ish-veh tor ish-veh? Du, i dang fancy.” “tor du fam dvun klee'fah tor tor nash na' me?” “veling i klee'fah. I dungi ma absolutely nothing tor tor k' ish-veh. I don’t tun ra mesh sarlah fi' du. Du nazh ish-veh ek'. I dang ri nam-tor sorry tor gla-tor du disgraced, publicly disgraced. Uf dare du ya'akash me, t' ek' sasu svi' wuh panu, tor rish myself abru svi' nash horror? I dang ma nahp du fai-tor weht pa' sutra’s characters. Ish-veh t'hy'la s'haile henry wotton mokuhlek’t ma saven-tor du mau pa' kloshai-tal, whatever else au has saven-tor du. Nothing dungi vimevilau me tor stir wuh ash tor gol'nev du. Du ma sarlah tor wuh riyeht sasu. Hal-tor tor ein t' ish-veh t'hylara. Don’t sarlah tor me.” “alan, ish-veh vesh' riyeht-staya. I pustau ish-veh. Du don’t fai-tor ra au had tor me dash. Whatever t'nash-veh ha'kiv nam-tor, au had weht tor tor k' wuh tor il wuh marring t' ish-veh do ri donku-tor harry has had. Au lau ri ma intended ish-veh, wuh result vesh' wuh ka.” “riyeht-staya! Rom oekon, dorian, nam-tor ik ra du ma sarlah tor? I dungau ri inform fi-tor du. Ish-veh nam-tor ri t'nash-veh business. Isha, rik' t'nash-veh stirring svi' wuh tukh, du nam-tor ac'ruth tor nam-tor pehkau. Kling ek'wak kugau wuh tr'y'kak rik' doing vel stupid. Tonk'peh i dungi ma nothing tor tor k' ish-veh.” “du bolau ma vel tor tor k' ish-veh. Bek-tor, bek-tor wuh moment; shroi tor me. Goh shroi, alan. Ek' i ya'akash t' du nam-tor tor perform wuh ac'ruth talik spolek. Du hal-tor tor shi'has heh tevik-kelek, heh wuh horrors ik du tor tra' don’t dau du. Kuv svi' ein hideous dissecting-tvi-shal il rasvilik ek'tal-zup-shal du afer-tor nash sasu lying fi' wuh leaden pasu k' yon-kur gutters scooped si' svi' ish-veh na' wuh khaf tor yumaya k'fai, du would veling glazhau fi-tor ish-veh u' wuh admirable subject. Du would ri da-tor wuh isachya. Du would ri dva-tor ik du vesh' doing sovek-vel riyeht. Fi' wuh contrary, du would probably olau ik du vesh' benefiting wuh komihn ne-koshtri, il increasing wuh hau-ov t' fai-tukh svi' wuh panu, il gratifying intellectual curiosity, il vel t' ik ves. Ra i aitlun du tor tor nam-tor goh ra du ma k'ashiv ovsoh fa'. Indeed, tor vashau wuh ak'shem bolau nam-tor irak lehkuh horrible do ra du nam-tor accustomed tor ar'kadan na'. Heh, vokau, ish-veh nam-tor wuh goh krus t' evidence tehnat me. Kuv ish-veh nam-tor discovered, i am pakik; heh ish-veh nam-tor sure tor nam-tor discovered vita du gol'nev me.” “i ma rai aitlun tor gol'nev du. Du yen-tor ik. I am veling indifferent tor wuh bosh vel. Ish-veh has nothing tor tor k' me.” “alan, i entreat du. Nah-tor t' wuh shul i am svi'. Aishan fa' du sarlah i siyah fainted k' vash. Du lau fai-tor vash yourself ein gad. Rai! Don’t nah-tor t' ik. Glazhau na' wuh tukh purely s' wuh talik sfek t' zan-tor. Du don’t inquire wilat wuh tevik vel fi' if du spolek sarlah s'. Don’t inquire i'. I ma var-tor du nuh' mau u' ish-veh nam-tor. Tonk'peh i eit'jae t' du tor tor nash. Etek vesh' t'hylara wuh'wak, alan.” “don’t stariben pa' eifa gad, dorian—au nam-tor tevik.” “wuh tevik svizh-tor sometimes. Wuh sasu upstairs dungi ri hal-tor maf. Au nam-tor sitting na' wuh pasu k' ovalau patam heh outstretched kar. Alan! Alan! Kuv du don’t sarlah tor t'nash-veh assistance, i am ruined. Po, au dungi geldau me, alan! Don’t du ken-tor? Au dungi geldau me na' ra i ma ovsoh.” “tra' nam-tor rai rom svi' prolonging nash scene. I absolutely klee'fah tor tor sovek-vel svi' wuh tukh. Ish-veh nam-tor kae-amp t' du tor ya'akash me.” “du klee'fah?” “ha.” “i entreat du, alan.” “ish-veh nam-tor nam-tor-fam.” wuh ka glazhau t' pity sarlah vi' dorian zhai-kur’s bezhun. Yi au sakadau si' ish-veh el'ru, nem-tor wuh krus t' dun, heh kitau vel fi' ish-veh. Au telv-tor ish-veh abru' dah'wak, hesha ish-veh carefully, heh kwitau ish-veh mes' wuh pasu. Having ovsoh nash, au prah abru heh went abru' tor wuh krani. Campbell glazhau na' ish-veh svi' ak'wikmun, heh yi nem-tor abru wuh dun, heh tu'ash ish-veh. U' au telv-tor ish-veh, ish-veh limuk became ghastly spoh heh au tevan-tor pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san. Wuh horrible kash-ral t' has-mar sarlah abru' ish-veh. Au olau u' kuv ish-veh khaf-spol vesh' beating itself tor tevakh svi' ein herbosh hollow. Po' dahkuh il rehkuh minutes t' terrible silence, dorian da-tor pauk heh sarlah heh lam-tor za' ish-veh, putting ish-veh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh tipan. “i am ni sorry na' du, alan, ” au murmured, “tonk'peh du trasha me rai alternative. I ma wuh nuhm written already. La' ish-veh nam-tor. Gla-tor du wuh shi'yavekh. Kuv du don’t gol'nev me, i bolau satau ish-veh. Kuv du don’t gol'nev me, i dungi satau ish-veh. Du fai-tor ra wuh result dungi nam-tor. Tonk'peh du nam-tor going tor gol'nev me. Ish-veh nam-tor impossible na' du tor klee'fah i'. I ar'kada tor spare du. Du dungi tor me wuh yeht-gav tor nafai-tor ik. Du vesh' harr-krus, harsh, offensive. Du skasau me u' rai sasu has ek'wak dared tor skasau me—rai living sasu, na' sovek tav. I spitau ish-veh ek'. I' ish-veh nam-tor na' me tor dictate zhil.” campbell visolektau ish-veh limuk svi' ish-veh el'ru, heh wuh ak'shem-hutau be' dvun-tor k'fai ish-veh. “ha, ish-veh nam-tor t'nash-veh da-tor tor dictate zhil, alan. Du fai-tor ra au nam-tor. Wuh vel nam-tor ved velik. Sarlah, don’t ar'kadan yourself vi' nash tau. Wuh vel has tor nam-tor ovsoh. Limuk ish-veh, heh tor ish-veh.” wuh groan shau s' campbell’s bru-lar heh au shivered ek' abru'. Wuh ticking t' wuh wak-vel fi' wuh mantelpiece seemed tor ish-veh tor nam-tor dividing wak vi' dahshauk galu t' agony, tik t' if vesh' nuh' terrible tor nam-tor borne. Au olau u' kuv wuh shek-tukh mokov vesh' hasu slowly tightened pauk ish-veh fa-patam, u' kuv wuh disgrace k' if au vesh' threatened had already sarlah fi-tor ish-veh. Wuh el'ru fi-tor ish-veh tipan rasathau spo' wuh el'ru t' ras-tukh. Ish-veh vesh' intolerable. Ish-veh seemed tor plesh-tor ish-veh. “sarlah, alan, du bolau klopau na' wuh'wak.” “i fam yehat tor ish-veh, ” au leralmin-tor, mechanically, u' hi zhit kupi rubitau vel. “du bolau. Du ma rai dvel. Don’t vohtaya.” au hesitated wuh moment. “nam-tor tra' wuh yon svi' wuh tvi-shal upstairs?” “ha, tra' nam-tor wuh pa-tukh-yon k' slah-tukh.” “i dungau ma tor hal-tor ha-kel heh prah ein vel s' wuh ek'tal-zup-shal.” “rai, alan, du bolau ri trasha wuh kelek. Kitau si' fi' wuh thalv t' notepaper ra du aitlun heh t'nash-veh dvinsu dungi nem-tor wuh cab heh katau wuh vel pla' tor du.” campbell scrawled wuh zamu zehl, blotted au, heh addressed wuh envelope tor ish-veh assistant. Dorian nem-tor wuh pitoh abru heh telv-tor ish-veh carefully. Yi au rang wuh kus-vakh heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor ish-veh valet, k' zek tor fun u' ak u' tor-yehat heh tor katau wuh vel k' ish-veh. U' wuh tvur svep ikap-tor, campbell palikau nervously, heh having prah abru s' wuh ku-san, went abru' tor wuh vuzh-mev-krus. Au vesh' shivering k' wuh ves t' ague. Na' nearly dah-leh minutes, neither t' wuh sasu stariben. Wuh hash-tor buzzed noisily pa' wuh tvi-shal, heh wuh ticking t' wuh wak-vel vesh' spo' wuh kuhsh-tor t' wuh mah-vel. U' wuh kusek kwul-tor veh, campbell da-tor pauk, heh looking na' dorian zhai-kur, gla-tor ik ish-veh bezhun vesh' boshau k' bezhun-masu. Tra' vesh' vel svi' wuh purity heh refinement t' ik maf limuk ik seemed tor enrage ish-veh. “du nam-tor infamous, absolutely infamous!” au muttered. “hush, alan. Du ma korsau t'nash-veh ha'kiv, ” leralmin-tor dorian. “ish-veh ha'kiv? Rom heavens! Ra wuh ha'kiv ik nam-tor! Du ma hal-tor s' corruption tor corruption, heh i' du ma culminated svi' tr'y'kak. Svi' doing ra i am going tor tor—ra du nekwitaya me tor tor—ish-veh nam-tor ri t' ish-veh ha'kiv ik i am thinking.” “ah, alan, ” murmured dorian k' wuh spes-tevan, “i istaya du had wuh thousandth krus t' wuh pity na' me ik i ma na' du.” au da-tor maf u' au stariben heh lam-tor looking si' na' wuh bah-ker. Campbell tor rai kilko-srashiv. Po' pa' lehkuh minutes wuh knock sarlah tor wuh svep, heh wuh dvinsu svi-tor, carrying wuh suk mahogany tuf t' meli-tukh, k' wuh wu pakuv t' pishek heh taluhk-tukh raf-elakh heh dahkuh rather curiously kushizhau shek-tukh stek. “dungau i trasha wuh vel la', osu?” au ya'akash campbell. “ha, ” leralmin-tor dorian. “heh i am kwes, francis, ik i ma wuh'ashiv skrol na' du. Ra nam-tor wuh ahm t' wuh sasu na' richmond vi tanilau selby k' orchids?” “lerashau, osu.” “ha—lerashau. Du bolau hal-tor ne' tor richmond na' wuh'wak, gla-tor lerashau personally, heh var-tor ish-veh tor satau dah'wak u' wehk orchids u' i ordered, heh ki' u' zamu wan-kur ones u' tor-yehat. Svi' kla-min, i don’t aitlun sovek wan-kur ones. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh lovely gad, francis, heh richmond nam-tor wuh maut takov shi—vathru i wouldn’t ertau du pa' ish-veh.” “rai trouble, osu. Na' ra wak dungau i nam-tor pla'?” dorian glazhau na' campbell. “uf wu dungi ish-veh spolek nem-tor, alan?” au leralmin-tor svi' wuh hayal indifferent spes. Wuh la'es t' wuh wuh person svi' wuh tvi-shal seemed tor mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh wehtsuri courage. Campbell kwal-tor heh zeshau ish-veh bru. “ish-veh dungi nem-tor pa' kaukuh wadan, ” au kilko-tor. “ish-veh dungi nam-tor wak hiyet, yi, kuv du nam-tor pla' na' ulef-vesht stehkuh, francis. Il stay: aishan trasha t'nash-veh vel si' na' sai-vel-tor. Du mokuhlek ma wuh khru tor yourself. I am ri dining na' ha-kel, ni i dungau ri aitlun du.” “nemaiyo, osu, ” leralmin-tor wuh sasu, leaving wuh tvi-shal. “i', alan, tra' nam-tor ri wuh moment tor nam-tor pakik. Uf ras nash tuf nam-tor! I’ll nem-tor ish-veh na' du. Du katau wuh vath vel.” au stariben rapidly heh svi' wuh authoritative manner. Campbell olau abrukhau k' ish-veh. Au losrak wuh tvi-shal teretuhr. Lu au pulau wuh fik landing, dorian nem-tor si' wuh tal-muv heh da-tor ish-veh svi' wuh klachek. Yi au pehkau, heh wuh troubled glazhau sarlah vi' ish-veh bezhun. Au ak'shem-hutau. “i don’t nah-tor i mokuhlek hal-tor svi', alan, ” au murmured. “ish-veh nam-tor nothing tor me. I don’t require du, ” leralmin-tor campbell coldly. Dorian ulef tu'ash wuh svep. U' au did ni, gla-tor ish-veh wuh limuk t' ish-veh portrait leering svi' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel. Fi' wuh lan-tol svi' khom t' ish-veh wuh torn curtain vesh' lying. Au vokau ik wuh mu-yor fa' au had yen-tor, na' wuh wuh'rak wak svi' ish-veh ha'kiv, tor ip-sut wuh fatal canvas, heh vesh' pa' tor rush fa'rak, lu au drew pla' k' wuh ak'shem-hutau. Ra vesh' ik loathsome yon-kur asal-masu ik gleamed, masupik heh glistening, fi' veh t' wuh el'ru, u' hi wuh canvas had wadashau khaf? Uf horrible ish-veh vesh'!—weht horrible, ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh na' wuh moment, do wuh ralash-fam vel ik au fai-tor vesh' sakadau mes' wuh pasu, wuh vel t'vi grotesque misshapen duv fi' wuh gla-tor la'y gluvau ish-veh ik ish-veh had ri stirred, tonk'peh vesh' fam dvun tra', u' au had losrak ish-veh. Au heaved wuh glu esh, tu'ash wuh svep wuh pi' wider, heh k' ulef-a'ing bezhun heh averted patam, lates-tor sahris svi', satalau ik au would ri glazhau kauk wuh'wak fi-tor wuh tevik sasu. Yi, stooping ne' heh taking abru wuh pi-maat-tukh-heh-gahv-kur hanging, au flung ish-veh gas'rak abru' wuh bikuv. Tra' au pehkau, olaya kwes tor da-tor pauk, heh ish-veh bezhun teslau themselves fi' wuh intricacies t' wuh nel-dath fa' ish-veh. Au puzhu-tor campbell bringing svi' wuh ras tuf, heh wuh irons, heh wuh vath vel ik au had required na' ish-veh dreadful ar'kadan. Au began tor wonder kuv au heh basil hallward had ek'wak ragel-tor, heh, kuv ni, ra au had nahp t' tik vath. “trasha me i', ” leralmin-tor wuh harr-krus spes za' ish-veh. Au da-tor heh hurried si', aishan d'wonil ik wuh tevik sasu had vesh' kwit pla' vi' wuh ku-san heh ik campbell vesh' gazing vi' wuh glistening kin-kur limuk. U' au vesh' going downstairs, au puzhu-tor wuh tal-muv hasu da-tor svi' wuh klachek. Ish-veh vesh' wu po' stehkuh lu campbell sarlah pla' vi' wuh shi'dunap. Au vesh' spoh, tonk'peh absolutely hayal. “i ma ovsoh ra du ya'akash me tor tor, ” au muttered. “heh i', rom-bye. Kal-tor etek worla gla-tor tik vath va'ashiv.” “du ma korsau me s' ruin, alan. I fam yehat yen-tor ik, ” leralmin-tor dorian veling. U' ak u' campbell had losrak, au went upstairs. Tra' vesh' wuh horrible fnish-tor t' nitric sash svi' wuh tvi-shal. Tonk'peh wuh vel ik had vesh' sitting na' wuh pasu vesh' hal-tor. Chapter xv. Ik khru, na' ohkuh-reh-leh, exquisitely sai-vel-tor heh sai-vel-tor wuh suk gonaf-razh t' parma mu'gahv-kur, dorian zhai-kur vesh' ushered vi' t'sai narborough’s bestan-tvi-shal k' bowing dvinsu. Ish-veh fa-patam vesh' throbbing k' maddened tor'tsu, heh au olau wildly teporilau, tonk'peh ish-veh manner u' au keh'sei abru' ish-veh hostess’s el'ru vesh' u' hagik heh graceful u' ek'wak. Sos'eh veh worla seems ni mau na' veh’s ease u' lu veh has tor mavau wuh krus. Certainly kling looking na' dorian zhai-kur ik mu-yor kupi ma pudva-tor ik au had be' dvun-tor k'fai wuh tragedy u' horrible u' sovek tragedy t' etwel ya'shakhuv. Eifa finely kushizhau ozh kupi worla ma clutched wuh lipau na' sin, il eifa smiling bru-lar ma lit'dhae fi' oekon heh goodness. Au himself kupi ri gol'nev wondering na' wuh hayal t' ish-veh demeanour, heh na' wuh moment olau keenly wuh terrible sanosh t' wuh dahtau ha'kiv. Ish-veh vesh' wuh pi' party, prah abru rather svi' wuh brax k' t'sai narborough, vi vesh' wuh maut clever kosu k' ra s'haile henry nam-tor-tor tor kethelvau u' wuh hafau t' really remarkable ugliness. She had skan-tor wuh marom ko-telsu tor veh t' etwel danik tedious kevet-dutar, heh having visolektau ish-veh sa-telsu properly svi' wuh marble mausoleum, if she had herself designed, heh telik ska' ish-veh daughters tor ein don-ka, rather shakhupik sasu, she vaikau herself i' tor wuh pleasures t' french glenokitau-tanaf, french cookery, heh french _esprit_ lu she kupi prah ish-veh. Dorian vesh' veh t' ish-veh especial favourites, heh she kwon-hau-ov var-tor ish-veh ik she vesh' extremely glad she had ri ragel-tor ish-veh svi' lehkuh-mal ha'kiv. “i fai-tor, t'nash-veh tal-kam, i dang ma tevan-tor madly svi' ashaya k' du, ” she nam-tor-tor tor leralmin, “heh lehm-tor t'nash-veh bonnet gas'rak abru' wuh mills na' ish-veh sake. Ish-veh nam-tor danik fortunate ik du vesh' ri nahp t' na' wuh wak. U' ish-veh vesh', etwel bonnets vesh' ni unbecoming, heh wuh mills vesh' ni occupied svi' trying tor ashenau wuh salan, ik i worla had kauk wuh flirtation k' anybody. However, ik vesh' ek' narborough’s lafot. Au vesh' dreadfully pen-sighted, heh tra' nam-tor rai sanosh svi' taking svi' wuh sa-telsu vi worla gla-tor sovek-vel.” ish-veh be'hai'la nash khru vesh' rather tedious. Wuh kla-min vesh', u' she danau tor dorian, za' wuh maut shabby sovek, veh t' ish-veh telik daughters had sarlah abru ved suddenly tor stay k' ish-veh, heh, tor tor tukh weh-rasahkos, had actually katau ish-veh sa-telsu k' ish-veh. “i nah-tor ish-veh nam-tor danik unkind t' ish-veh, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” she zhal-tor. “veling i hal-tor heh stay k' au kanok belaar po' sarlah nash-veh s' homburg, tonk'peh yi wuh hinek kosu spo' me bolau ma sluk sov sometimes, heh isha, i really wake au abru. Du don’t fai-tor ra wuh nam au ras-tukh ne' tra'. Ish-veh nam-tor pure unadulterated shasol ha'kiv. Au prah abru lehkuh-mal, fai'ei au ma ni mau tor tor, heh hal-tor tor sar-tak lehkuh-mal, fai'ei au ma ni pi' tor nah-tor pa'. Tra' has ri vesh' wuh scandal svi' wuh neighbourhood opi' wuh wak t' ko-te'kru elizabeth, heh consequently au ek' tevan asleep po' aru-yem. Du shan’t hayal-tor thurai either t' au. Du dungau hayal-tor k' me heh amuse me.” dorian murmured wuh graceful compliment heh glazhau pauk wuh tvi-shal. Ha: ish-veh vesh' certainly wuh tedious party. Dahkuh t' wuh sutra au had worla gla-tor fa', heh wuh vath consisted t' ernest harrowden, veh t' eifa svitan-aged mediocrities ni tsuri svi' london muhd vi ma rai nemut, tonk'peh nam-tor thoroughly ritishau k' ish-veh t'hylara; t'sai ruxton, wuh overdressed kosu t' keh-leh-stehkuh, k' wuh hooked han, vi vesh' kwon-hau-ov trying tor prah herself compromised, tonk'peh vesh' ni peculiarly eiktra ik tor ish-veh lo'uk disappointment kling would ek'wak dva-tor sovek-vel tehnat ish-veh; mrs. Erlynne, wuh pushing kling, k' wuh delightful lisp heh venetian-yon-kur isachya; t'sai alice chapman, ish-veh hostess’s ko-fu, wuh dowdy pasik ko-kan, k' veh t' eifa noshtra british limuk ik, wuh'wak gla-tor, nam-tor worla vokau; heh ish-veh sa-telsu, wuh yon-kur-cheeked, wan-kur-whiskered creature vi, spo' ni wehk t' ish-veh mohrn, vesh' ne' wuh impression ik inordinate joviality mokuhlek atone na' wuh entire fam t' ideas. Au vesh' rather sorry au had sarlah, till t'sai narborough, looking na' wuh lo'uk ormolu gilt wak-vel ik sprawled svi' gaudy curves fi' wuh kihsh-kur-draped mantelshelf, sporiben: “uf horrid t' henry wotton tor nam-tor ni tab-ma! I satau pauk tor ish-veh nash asal fi' pavesh heh au ugau faithfully ri tor disappoint me.” ish-veh vesh' ein consolation ik harry vesh' tor nam-tor tra', heh lu wuh svep tu'ash heh au puzhu-tor ish-veh vohris musical spes lending sem-rik tor ein insincere apology, au ceased tor olau bored. Tonk'peh na' aru-yem au kupi ri yokul sovek-vel. Math po' math went maf untasted. T'sai narborough potau scolding ish-veh na' ra she puvutau “wuh viltah tor ri donku-tor adolphe, vi fereik-tor wuh _menu_ specially na' du, ” heh i' heh yi s'haile henry glazhau mes' na' ish-veh, wondering na' ish-veh silence heh abstracted manner. S' wak tor wak wuh butler boshau ish-veh makh k' champagne. Au drank eagerly, heh ish-veh mag seemed tor increase. “dorian, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry na' kim-shah, u' wuh _chaud-froid_ vesh' hasu handed pauk, “ra nam-tor wuh tukh k' du tor-mu-yor? Du nam-tor ved si' t' wihfelau.” “i dva-tor au nam-tor svi' ashaya, ” maf-tor t'sai narborough, “heh ik au nam-tor kwes tor var-tor me na' pthak i dang nam-tor kis-ka. Au nam-tor ved gas'rak. I certainly dang.” “tal-kam t'sai narborough, ” murmured dorian, smiling, “i ma ri vesh' svi' ashaya na' wuh bosh wehk gad—ri, svi' kla-min, opi' madame de ferrol losrak kahr.” “uf du sasu mokuhlek tevan svi' ashaya k' ik kosu!” sporiben wuh hinek t'sai. “i really fam yehat ken-tor ish-veh.” “ish-veh nam-tor veling fai'ei she vokau du lu du vesh' wuh pi' ko-kan, t'sai narborough, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “she nam-tor wuh veh naf svi' etek heh ish-veh pen pelal.” “she tor ri vokau t'nash-veh pen pelal na' ek', s'haile henry. Tonk'peh i vokau ish-veh maut muhl na' vienna reh-leh tevun ago, heh uf _décolletée_ she vesh' yi.” “she nam-tor fam dvun _décolletée_, ” au kilko-tor, taking wuh olive svi' ish-veh wu ozh; “heh lu she nam-tor svi' wuh maut klon gown she glazhau spo' wuh _édition de luxe_ t' wuh rasahkos french dunap. She nam-tor really wonderful, heh bosh t' ak'wikmun. Ish-veh tsoh na' skan affection nam-tor wehtsuri. Lu ish-veh wuh sa-telsu tev-tor, ish-veh isachya da-tor ved pi-maat-tukh s' tushat.” “uf mokuhlek du, harry!” maf-tor dorian. “ish-veh nam-tor wuh danik romantic danaya, ” abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor wuh hostess. “tonk'peh ish-veh wuh sa-telsu, s'haile henry! Du don’t tvai tor leralmin ferrol nam-tor wuh fourth?” “certainly, t'sai narborough.” “i don’t dva-tor wuh zhit t' ish-veh.” “muhl, ya'akash mr. Zhai-kur. Au nam-tor veh t' ish-veh danik intimate t'hylara.” “nam-tor ish-veh yeht, mr. Zhai-kur?” “she assures me ni, t'sai narborough, ” leralmin-tor dorian. “i ya'akash ish-veh whether, spo' marguerite de navarre, she had ish-veh khaf-spol embalmed heh geldau na' ish-veh girdle. She var-tor me she didn’t, fai'ei rim t' au had had sovek khaf-spol na' ek'.” “kehkuh sa-telsu! Fi-tor t'nash-veh zhit ik nam-tor _trop de zêle_.” “_trop d’audace_, i var-tor ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor dorian. “oh! She nam-tor audacious hiyet na' sovek-vel, t'nash-veh tal-kam. Heh ra nam-tor ferrol spo'? I don’t fai-tor ish-veh.” “wuh sa-telsu t' maut vaksurik kosu belong tor wuh criminal mohrn, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, mon-tor ish-veh wine. T'sai narborough kwul ish-veh k' ish-veh sovek. “s'haile henry, i am mokov ak'wikmun ik wuh panu leralmin-tor ik du nam-tor extremely wicked.” “tonk'peh ra panu leralmin-tor ik?” ya'akash s'haile henry, elevating ish-veh bezhun-zehl. “ish-veh mokuhlek goh nam-tor wuh thurai panu. Nash panu heh i nam-tor fi' marom zhil.” “kanok-veh i fai-tor leralmin-tor du nam-tor maut wicked, ” maf-tor wuh hinek t'sai, shaking ish-veh patam. S'haile henry glazhau serious na' ein moments. “ish-veh nam-tor perfectly monstrous, ” au leralmin-tor, na' kim-shah, “wuh yut sutra hal-tor pa' nowadays taran vel tehnat veh za' veh’s pla' ik nam-tor absolutely heh entirely yeht.” “isn’t au incorrigible?” maf-tor dorian, leaning fa'rak svi' ish-veh ku-san. “i rok ni, ” leralmin-tor ish-veh hostess, laughing. “tonk'peh really, kuv du ek' worship madame de ferrol svi' nash ridiculous yut, i dungau ma tor marry va'ashiv ni u' tor nam-tor svi' wuh fashion.” “du dungi worla marry va'ashiv, t'sai narborough, ” shau svi' s'haile henry. “du vesh' irak nuh' kunli. Lu wuh kosu marries va'ashiv, ish-veh nam-tor fai'ei she detested ish-veh wuh'rak sa-telsu. Lu wuh sasu marries va'ashiv, ish-veh nam-tor fai'ei au adored ish-veh wuh'rak ko-telsu. Kosu ar'kadan ish-veh kunli; sasu risk ish-veh.” “narborough wasn’t buhfik, ” maf-tor wuh hinek t'sai. “kuv au had vesh', du would ri ma ashau ish-veh, t'nash-veh tal-kam t'sai, ” vesh' wuh rejoinder. “kosu ashaya etek na' etwel lafot. Kuv etek ma hiyet t' au, au dungi forgive etek kanok-vei, kauk etwel intellects. Du dungi worla ya'akash me tor aru-yem va'ashiv po' taran nash, i am kwes, t'sai narborough, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor ved yeht.” “veling ish-veh nam-tor yeht, s'haile henry. Kuv etek kosu did ri ashaya du na' ish-veh lafot, wilat would du ek' nam-tor? Ri veh t' du would ek'wak nam-tor telik. Du would nam-tor wuh eku t' unfortunate bachelors. Ri, however, ik ik would rubitau du mau. Nowadays ek' wuh telik sasu ha-tor spo' bachelors, heh ek' wuh bachelors spo' telik sasu.” “_fin de siêcle_, ” murmured s'haile henry. “_fin du globe_, ” kilko-tor ish-veh hostess. “i istaya ish-veh vesh' _fin du globe_, ” leralmin-tor dorian k' wuh spes-tevan. “ha'kiv nam-tor wuh lo'uk disappointment.” “ah, t'nash-veh tal-kam, ” maf-tor t'sai narborough, putting fi' ish-veh gloves, “don’t var-tor me ik du ma saguhsh-tor ha'kiv. Lu wuh sasu leralmin-tor ish-veh fai-tor ik ha'kiv has saguhsh-tor ish-veh. S'haile henry nam-tor maut wicked, heh i sometimes istaya ik i had vesh'; tonk'peh du nam-tor tor tor nam-tor rom—du glazhau ni rom. I bolau talal du wuh nice ko-telsu. S'haile henry, don’t du nah-tor ik mr. Zhai-kur dang prah telik?” “i am kwon-hau-ov telling ish-veh ni, t'sai narborough, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry k' wuh kes-wun. “muhl, etek bolau glazhau si' na' wuh suitable match na' ish-veh. I dungau hal-tor k'fai debrett carefully tor-mu-yor heh bes-tor si' wuh feim t' ek' wuh eligible nu'ri t'sai.” “k' ish-veh ya'shakhuv, t'sai narborough?” ya'akash dorian. “veling, k' ish-veh ya'shakhuv, slightly ver-tor. Tonk'peh nothing bolau nam-tor ovsoh svi' wuh brax. I aitlun ish-veh tor nam-tor ra _the asal post_ calls wuh suitable alliance, heh i aitlun du fi' tor nam-tor kunli.” “ra nonsense sutra variben pa' kunli kal'i'farr!” sporiben s'haile henry. “wuh sasu mokuhlek nam-tor kunli k' sovek kosu, u' wu u' au tor ri ashaya ish-veh.” “ah! Ra wuh cynic du nam-tor!” maf-tor wuh hinek t'sai, pushing pla' ish-veh ku-san heh nodding tor t'sai ruxton. “du bolau sarlah heh aru-yokul k' me ak va'ashiv. Du nam-tor really wuh admirable tonic, mau weh-rom do ra osu andrew prescribes na' me. Du bolau var-tor me ra sutra du would spo' tor ragel-tor, hi. I aitlun ish-veh tor nam-tor wuh delightful hohnaya.” “i spo' sasu vi ma wuh fa-wak heh kosu vi ma wuh vesht, ” au kilko-tor. “il tor du nah-tor ik would tor ish-veh wuh petticoat party?” “i pthak ni, ” she leralmin-tor, laughing, u' she lam-tor abru. “wuh thousand pardons, t'nash-veh tal-kam t'sai ruxton, ” she hau, “i didn’t gla-tor du hadn’t shahtau ish-veh cigarette.” “worla kashek, t'sai narborough. I vuzh wuh lo'uk deal nuh' mau. I am going tor grei myself, na' wuh fa-wak.” “pray don’t, t'sai ruxton, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “moderation nam-tor wuh fatal vel. Hiyet nam-tor u' rasahkos u' wuh yem. Weht do hiyet nam-tor u' rom u' wuh gadzhak.” t'sai ruxton glanced na' ish-veh curiously. “du bolau sarlah heh danau ik tor me ein aru, s'haile henry. Ish-veh sounds wuh sem-rik wihka, ” she murmured, u' she swept s' wuh tvi-shal. “i', kashek du don’t stay nuh' wu abru' ish-veh politics heh scandal, ” maf-tor t'sai narborough s' wuh svep. “kuv du tor, etek nam-tor sure tor squabble upstairs.” wuh sasu abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor, heh mr. Chapman prah abru solemnly s' wuh ash'ya t' wuh pasu heh sarlah abru tor wuh fik. Dorian zhai-kur rubai ish-veh ku-san heh went heh hayal-tor k' s'haile henry. Mr. Chapman began tor variben svi' wuh ral spes pa' wuh situation svi' wuh kelek t' commons. Au guffawed na' ish-veh adversaries. Wuh zhit _doctrinaire_—zhit bosh t' vash tor wuh british kashek—reappeared s' wak tor wak svi' ish-veh thorshaya. Wuh alliterative prefix dvin-tor u' wuh fanet t' oratory. Au abertau wuh union jack fi' wuh kov-suk'fek t' nahp. Wuh inherited stupidity t' wuh ne-koshtri—ralash eingelsu tsuri kash-ral au jovially termed ish-veh—vesh' shown tor nam-tor wuh proper bulwark na' shila'es. Wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut curved s'haile henry’s bru-lar, heh au da-tor pauk heh glazhau na' dorian. “nam-tor du weh-rom, t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu?” au ya'akash. “du seemed rather s' wihfelau na' aru-yem.” “i am ved muhl, harry. I am zungor. Ik nam-tor ek'.” “du vesh' sem-rik-tor kim-shah mu-yor. Wuh pi' duchess nam-tor ved vaikau tor du. She var-tor me she nam-tor going ne' tor selby.” “she has ugau tor sarlah fi' wuh twentieth.” “nam-tor monmouth tor nam-tor tra', nuh'?” “oh, ha, harry.” “au bores me dreadfully, siyah u' mau u' au bores ish-veh. She nam-tor maut clever, nuh' clever na' wuh kosu. She fam-tor wuh indefinable sem-rik t' kobat'es. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh ash'ya t' krizhiv ik tor wuh pi-maat-tukh t' wuh glakuv taluhk. Ish-veh ash'ya nam-tor maut takov, tonk'peh au nam-tor ri ash'ya t' krizhiv. Wan-kur porcelain ash'ya, kuv du spo'. Au ma vesh' k'fai wuh yon, heh ra yon tor ri vashau, ish-veh lerashau. She has had veshtau.” “uf wu has she vesh' telik?” ya'akash dorian. “wuh ek'wak'es, she var-tor me. I dva-tor, fupa s' wuh peerage, ish-veh nam-tor lehkuh tevun, tonk'peh lehkuh tevun k' monmouth bolau ma vesh' spo' ek'wak'es, k' wak lehm-tor svi'. Vi else nam-tor coming?” “oh, wuh willoughbys, s'haile rugby heh ish-veh ko-telsu, etwel hostess, geoffrey clouston, wuh tsuri eku. I ma ya'akash s'haile grotrian.” “i spo' ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “wuh lo'uk wehk sutra don’t, tonk'peh i talal ish-veh sem-rik-tor. Au atones na' hasu occasionally somewhat overdressed k' hasu kwon-hau-ov absolutely abru'-educated. Au nam-tor wuh maut iyik ves.” “i don’t fai-tor kuv au dungi nam-tor kup tor sarlah, harry. Au lau ma tor hal-tor tor monte carlo k' ish-veh sa-mekh.” “ah! Ra wuh nuisance sutra’s sutra nam-tor! Ar'kadan heh tor ish-veh sarlah. K' wuh yut, dorian, du sahr-tor ska' maut lehkuh-mal kim-shah mu-yor. Du losrak fa' leh-wun. Ra did du tor afterwards? Did du hal-tor zehik ha-kel?” dorian glanced na' ish-veh hurriedly heh kwal-tor. “rai, harry, ” au leralmin-tor na' kim-shah, “i did ri prah ha-kel till nearly rehkuh.” “did du hal-tor tor wuh muhd?” “ha, ” au kilko-tor. Yi au zeshau ish-veh bru. “rai, i don’t tvai ik. I didn’t hal-tor tor wuh muhd. I lates-tor pa'. I yen-tor ra i did. Uf inquisitive du nam-tor, harry! Du kwon-hau-ov aitlun tor fai-tor ra veh has vesh' doing. I kwon-hau-ov aitlun tor yen-tor ra i ma vesh' doing. Vesht sarlah nash-veh svi' na' ulef-vesht dahkuh, kuv du istaya tor fai-tor wuh faikaik wak. I had losrak t'nash-veh kuhr-tal-muv na' ha-kel, heh t'nash-veh dvinsu had tor kal-tor me svi'. Kuv du aitlun sovek corroborative evidence fi' wuh subject, du mokuhlek ya'akash ish-veh.” s'haile henry shrugged ish-veh tipan. “t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, u' kuv i tun-tor! Kal-tor etek hal-tor abru tor wuh bestan-tvi-shal. Rai sherry, nemaiyo, mr. Chapman. Vel has pavesh-tor tor du, dorian. Var-tor me ra ish-veh nam-tor. Du nam-tor ri yourself tor-mu-yor.” “don’t kashek me, harry. I am irritable, heh s' temper. Dungau-sarlah nash-veh pauk heh gla-tor du tor-morrow, il thurai gad. Tor t'nash-veh tobeg-tor tor t'sai narborough. I shan’t hal-tor upstairs. I dungau hal-tor ha-kel. I bolau hal-tor ha-kel.” “ek' gas'rak, dorian. I dare leralmin dungau gla-tor nash-veh du tor-morrow na' theris-masu-wak. Wuh duchess nam-tor coming.” “i dungi ar'kadan tor nam-tor tra', harry, ” au leralmin-tor, leaving wuh tvi-shal. U' au drove pla' tor ish-veh sha' kelek, au vesh' d'wonil ik wuh kash-ral t' vash au nahp au had strangled had sarlah pla' tor ish-veh. S'haile henry’s casual questioning had tor ish-veh pak-tor ish-veh tor'tsu na' wuh moment, heh au aitlu ish-veh tor'tsu fam dvun. Vel ik vesh' tehvar-bosh had tor nam-tor vashau. Au winced. Au fnu-ven wuh idea t' kauk touching au. Wi ish-veh had tor nam-tor ovsoh. Au realized ik, heh lu au had klacha wuh svep t' ish-veh shi'dunap, au tu'ash wuh tsat hish-tor vi' if au had kwit basil hallward’s tor-pal heh sa'haf. Wuh masuk' yon vesh' blazing. Au piled wuh'ashiv lap-fek fi' ish-veh. Wuh fnish-tor t' wuh singeing sai-vel heh yontau duf vesh' horrible. Ish-veh nem-tor ish-veh rehkuh-ha-shal t' wuh wadan tor consume kanok-vei. Na' wuh shaht au olau faint heh has-bosh, heh having lit ein algerian pastilles svi' wuh tilau khaf-tukh fas-nentu, au bathed ish-veh el'ru heh fa-patam k' wuh samuyau musk-scented sfith-masu. Suddenly au palikau. Ish-veh bezhun grew strangely ugelik, heh au gnawed nervously na' ish-veh underlip. Svi' dahkuh t' wuh krani lam-tor wuh suk florentine tsorayek, tor s' ebony heh inlaid k' ivory heh pla-kur lapis. Au glantau ish-veh u' hi ish-veh vesh' wuh vel ik kupi sem-tor heh tor kwes, u' hi ish-veh meskarau vel ik au longed na' heh wi siyah loathed. Ish-veh esh quickened. Wuh mad craving sarlah abru' ish-veh. Au lit wuh cigarette heh yi threw ish-veh maf. Ish-veh bezhun-wein tevan-tor till wuh wu fringed lashes siyah estuhl ish-veh nak. Tonk'peh au fam dvun glantau wuh tsorayek. Na' kim-shah au prah abru s' wuh ku-san fi' if au had vesh' lying, went abru' tor ish-veh, heh having unlocked ish-veh, estuhl ein ipik sikar. Wuh triangular zish-nef be' dvun-tor slowly si'. Ish-veh ozh dvun-tor instinctively na' ish-veh, spis-tor svi', heh a'ing fi' vel. Ish-veh vesh' wuh pi' chinese natuhn t' nesh-kur heh pi-maat-tukh-grazhiv lacquer, elaborately wrought, wuh vla patterned k' curved pral, heh wuh silken elakh geldau k' pauk khush heh tasselled svi' plaited mokev og-elakh. Au tu'ash ish-veh. Svi'udish vesh' wuh yar-kur paste, waxy svi' lustre, wuh vil curiously ras heh persistent. Au hesitated na' ein moments, k' wuh strangely immobile abru'teruklar-ru'lut fi-tor ish-veh limuk. Yi shivering, hi wuh igen-tukh t' wuh tvi-shal vesh' terribly fal, au drew himself abru heh glanced na' wuh wak-vel. Ish-veh vesh' dah-leh minutes tor leh-dah. Au shitau wuh natuhn pla', shutting wuh tsorayek svep u' au did ni, heh went vi' ish-veh shi'yuk. U' midnight vesh' striking krish-tukh salur fi-tor wuh dusky sov, dorian zhai-kur, sai-vel-tor commonly, heh k' wuh muffler wrapped pauk ish-veh drahk, crept quietly s' ish-veh kelek. Svi' tel-tor yut au afer-tor wuh hansom k' wuh rom jarel. Au hailed ish-veh heh svi' wuh neik spes mazhiv-kur-tor wuh yetursu wuh shi'yavekh. Wuh sasu hutau ish-veh patam. “ish-veh nam-tor nuh' irak na' me, ” au muttered. “la' nam-tor wuh sovereign na' du, ” leralmin-tor dorian. “du dungau ma wuh'ashiv kuv du yetur sahris.” “ek' gas'rak, osu, ” kilko-tor wuh sasu, “du dungi nam-tor tra' svi' wuh wadan, ” heh po' ish-veh panavau had prah svi' au da-tor ish-veh jarel pauk heh drove rapidly na' wuh pilash. Chapter xvi. Wuh samu sov-masu began tor tevan, heh wuh blurred yut-ha'gelek glazhau ghastly svi' wuh dripping mist. Wuh tsuri-kelek vesh' aishan ikapik, heh neik-ha'khlup sasu heh kosu vesh' clustering svi' pushau travek pauk ish-veh svep. S' ein t' wuh mofek sarlah wuh ralash t' horrible laughter. Svi' vath, drunkards brawled heh shei. Lying pla' svi' wuh hansom, k' ish-veh taik seshau abru' ish-veh fa-patam, dorian zhai-kur glantau k' listless bezhun wuh sordid mesh t' wuh lo'uk kahr, heh i' heh yi au ashiv-tor tor himself wuh zhit ik s'haile henry had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh fi' wuh wuh'rak gad au had ragel-tor, “tor bohrau wuh soul k' tvai t' wuh kash-ral, heh wuh kash-ral k' tvai t' wuh soul.” ha, ik vesh' wuh tsat. Au had k'ashiv ar'kada ish-veh, heh would ar'kadan ish-veh va'ashiv i'. Tra' vesh' opium dens wilat veh kupi mahr-tor oblivion, dens t' horror wilat wuh vokaya t' hinek sins kupi nam-tor vashau k' wuh ni-resh t' sins ik vesh' uzh. Wuh aikum geldau neik svi' wuh igen spo' wuh kin-kur grat. S' wak tor wak wuh masuk' misshapen wan sakadau wuh wu kar mes' heh ip-sut ish-veh. Wuh pa-tukh-ha'gelek grew fewer, heh wuh yut weht wonil heh gloomy. Wuh'wak wuh sasu pakik ish-veh yut heh had tor yetur pla' ulef wuh mile. Wuh zhis she-tor s' wuh jarel u' ish-veh splashed abru wuh pi'muzh. Wuh sidewindows t' wuh hansom vesh' clogged k' wuh zhai-kur-flannel mist. “tor bohrau wuh soul k' tvai t' wuh kash-ral, heh wuh kash-ral k' tvai t' wuh soul!” uf wuh zhit rang svi' ish-veh kaluk! Ish-veh soul, certainly, vesh' has-bosh tor tevakh. Vesh' ish-veh yeht ik wuh kash-ral kupi bohrau ish-veh? Innocent khaf had vesh' ne-tor. Ra kupi atone na' ik? Ah! Na' ik tra' vesh' rai atonement; tonk'peh hi thrap-fam'es nufau vesh' impossible, forgetfulness vesh' tor-yehat fam dvun, heh au vesh' satalau tor yen-tor, tor stamp wuh vel si', tor plesh-tor ish-veh u' veh would plesh-tor wuh adder ik had rakusau veh. Indeed, ra gas'rak had basil ki' spoken tor ish-veh u' au had ovsoh? Vi had tor ish-veh wuh judge abru' vath? Au had leralmin-tor vel ik vesh' dreadful, horrible, ri tor nam-tor palesh-tor. Fi' heh fi' plodded wuh hansom, going slower, ish-veh seemed tor ish-veh, na' tik ash. Au kwit abru wuh pash heh puvutau tor wuh sasu tor yetur faster. Wuh hideous avon na' opium began tor gnaw na' ish-veh. Ish-veh drahk yontau heh ish-veh delicate el'ru twitched nervously teretuhr. Au kwul-tor na' wuh jarel madly k' ish-veh terpau. Wuh yetursu abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor heh whipped abru. Au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor svi' kilko-srashiv, heh wuh sasu vesh' ralash-fam. Wuh yut seemed interminable, heh wuh yut spo' wuh nesh-kur vis t' ein sprawling a'lazb. Wuh monotony became unbearable, heh u' wuh mist thickened, au olau kwes. Yi au be' dvun-tor k' lonely brickfields. Wuh ihsek vesh' lighter la', heh au kupi gla-tor wuh flekh, mashek-kushizhau kilns k' ish-veh zhar-kur, fanlike lahv t' yon. Wuh dog barked u' au went k', heh irak maf svi' wuh mu'khlup'es ein wandering masutra-gull shei. Wuh jarel stumbled svi' wuh rut, yi swerved aside heh shau vi' wuh ausahr. Po' ein wak au losrak wuh krizhiv fau-yut heh rattled va'ashiv abru' rough-paven yut. Danik t' wuh krani vesh' gu'gelik, tonk'peh i' heh yi fantastic duv vesh' silhouetted tehnat ein lamplit glan-fam. Au glantau au curiously. Au dvun-tor spo' monstrous marionettes heh tor gestures spo' ha-tor vel. Au fnu-ven au. Wuh pasik reshan vesh' svi' ish-veh khaf-spol. U' au da-tor wuh teruk, wuh kosu saul-tor vel na' au s' wuh tu'ash svep, heh dahkuh sasu sahr-tor po' wuh hansom na' pa' wuh hundred ker. Wuh yetursu kuhsh-tor na' au k' ish-veh wonil-zehl. Ish-veh nam-tor leralmin-tor ik shaukaush tor veh nah-tor svi' wuh da-kuv.
