Certainly k' hideous ashivaya wuh bitten bru-lar t' dorian zhai-kur kushizhau heh reshaped eifa subtle zhit ik dealt k' soul heh kash-ral, till au had afer-tor svi' au wuh bosh sagluvaya, u' ish-veh vesh', t' ish-veh mood, heh justified, k' intellectual messaya, shaukaush ik rik' such justification would fam dvun ma abrukhau ish-veh temper. S' nala tor nala t' ish-veh shi'nahp crept wuh veh nahp; heh wuh kwai aitlun tor ha-tor, danik terrible t' ek' sasu’s yeht-avon, quickened vi' nekwitaya tik trembling tor'tsu heh slah. Ugliness ik had wuh'wak vesh' hateful tor ish-veh fai'ei ish-veh tor vel yeht, became tal-kam tor ish-veh i' na' ik maut utvau. Ugliness vesh' wuh veh reality. Wuh dirik brawl, wuh loathsome den, wuh crude khrash t' disordered ha'kiv, wuh maut vileness t' pi'tak heh vrekasht, vesh' weht vivid, svi' ish-veh intense actuality t' impression, do ek' wuh gracious shid t' tanaf, wuh dreamy duv t' song. Au vesh' ra au bolau na' forgetfulness. Svi' rehkuh gad au would nam-tor elik. Suddenly wuh sasu drew abru k' wuh hutau na' wuh fik t' wuh gu'gelik lane. Abru' wuh neik kamu heh jagged vuzh-mev-tuh t' wuh kelek she-tor wuh nesh-kur mashalo-thalv-lap t' ships. Wreaths t' wan-kur mist clung spo' ghostly masu-halovau tor wuh ker. “ein-wilat pa' la', osu, ain’t ish-veh?” au ya'akash huskily k'fai wuh pash. Dorian palikau heh peered pauk. “nash dungi tor, ” au kilko-tor, heh having prah si' hastily heh putan-tor wuh yetursu wuh hayaik panavau au had ugau ish-veh, au lates-tor sahris svi' wuh kharat t' wuh quay. La' heh tra' wuh makh-yonet gleamed na' wuh harr-krus t' ein masuk' merchantman. Wuh ta'hal hutau heh splintered svi' wuh pi'muzh. Wuh yon-kur glare sarlah s' wuh outward-bound steamer ik vesh' coaling. Wuh slimy pavement glazhau spo' wuh masupik mackintosh. Au hurried fi' na' wuh losrak, glancing pla' i' heh yi tor gla-tor kuv au vesh' hasu zahal-tor. Svi' pa' stehkuh il ohkuh minutes au pulau wuh pi' shabby kelek ik vesh' wedged svi' svi' dahkuh gaunt zhuk-om. Svi' veh t' wuh fik-krani lam-tor wuh ha'gelek. Au pehkau heh mazhiv-kur-tor wuh peculiar knock. Po' wuh pi' wak au puzhu-tor ash-tor svi' wuh tvur heh wuh naf-elakh hasu unhooked. Wuh svep tu'ash quietly, heh au went svi' rik' taran wuh zhit tor wuh squat misshapen khlop ik flattened itself vi' wuh duv u' au be' dvun-tor. Na' wuh shaht t' wuh tvur geldau wuh tattered yar-kur curtain ik swayed heh hutau svi' wuh gusty salan if had zahal-tor ish-veh svi' s' wuh yut. Au zaseshau ish-veh aside heh svi-tor wuh wu neik tvi-shal if glazhau u' kuv ish-veh had wuh'wak vesh' wuh wuh-tav taman-saloon. Shrill flaring pa-tukh-jets, pasik heh distorted svi' wuh hash-tor-blown haulat ik limuk-tor au, vesh' ranged pauk wuh temok. Greasy haulek t' ribbed zhai-tukh backed au, tor quivering mathra t' ta'hal. Wuh lan-tol vesh' wein-tor k' ochre-kur-tor sawdust, sahr-tor la' heh tra' vi' vral, heh kurau k' gu'gelik mokov t' ne-tor liquor. Ein malays vesh' crouching k' wuh pi' yonol-tukh stove, mavaun k' hinek tumek heh showing ish-veh wan-kur zud u' au chattered. Svi' veh teruk, k' ish-veh patam visolektau svi' ish-veh kar, wuh masusu sprawled abru' wuh pasu, heh k' wuh tawdrily kras-tor mofek ik sahr-tor mes' veh ovsotik vla lam-tor dahkuh haggard kosu, mocking wuh hinek sasu vi vesh' brushing wuh sleeves t' ish-veh tor-pal k' wuh sagluvaya t' spa'ash. “au nah-tor au’s prah yon-kur ants fi' ish-veh, ” abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor veh t' au, u' dorian be' dvun-tor k'. Wuh sasu glazhau na' ish-veh svi' vash heh began tor whimper. Na' wuh shaht t' wuh tvi-shal tra' vesh' wuh pi' staircase, leading tor wuh mu'glau tvi-shal. U' dorian hurried abru its rehkuh rickety ash-tor, wuh ras vil t' opium ragel-tor ish-veh. Au heaved wuh glu esh, heh ish-veh han-sharular quivered k' sanosh. Lu au svi-tor, wuh nu'ri sasu k' mos kin-kur isachya, vi vesh' bending abru' wuh ha'gelek ha'gelan wuh wu wonil mev, glazhau abru na' ish-veh heh nodded svi' wuh hesitating manner. “du la', adrian?” muttered dorian. “wilat else dang i nam-tor?” au kilko-tor, listlessly. “rim t' wuh chaps dungi stariben tor me i'.” “i nahp du had losrak england.” “darlington nam-tor ri going tor tor sovek-vel. T'nash-veh sa-kai vlitau wuh dun na' kim-shah. George doesn’t stariben tor me either. I don’t tun, ” au hau k' wuh spes-tevan. “u' wu u' veh has nash tukh, veh doesn’t aitlun t'hylara. I nah-tor i ma had nuh' wehk t'hylara.” dorian winced heh glazhau pauk na' wuh grotesque vel ik ti svi' such fantastic postures fi' wuh ragged yuk-vel. Wuh kuvoran-tor sikrus, wuh gaping ru'lut, wuh staring lustreless bezhun, sem-tor ish-veh. Au fai-tor svi' ra flekh heavens au vesh' suffering, heh ra pasik hells vesh' teaching au wuh tsat t' ein uzh mak. Au vesh' weh-rom ska' do au vesh'. Au vesh' prisoned svi' nahp. Vokaya, spo' wuh horrible malady, vesh' eating ish-veh soul maf. S' wak tor wak au seemed tor gla-tor wuh bezhun t' basil hallward looking na' ish-veh. Wi au olau au kupi ri stay. Wuh la'es t' adrian singleton troubled ish-veh. Au aitlu tor nam-tor wilat kling would fai-tor vi au vesh'. Au aitlu tor stron s' himself. “i am going fi' tor wuh vath shi, ” au leralmin-tor po' wuh svizh. “fi' wuh kif?” “ha.” “ik mad-aushfa nam-tor sure tor nam-tor tra'. Au skil-tor’t ma ish-veh svi' nash shi i'.” dorian shrugged ish-veh tipan. “i am has-bosh t' kosu vi ashaya veh. Kosu vi fnu-ven veh nam-tor mau weht eku'ki. Isha, wuh tukh nam-tor weh-rom.” “mau wuh ka.” “i spo' ish-veh weh-rom. Sarlah heh ma vel tor mon. I bolau ma vel.” “i don’t aitlun sovek-vel, ” murmured wuh nu'ri sasu. “worla kashek.” adrian singleton she-tor abru wearily heh zahal-tor dorian tor wuh mofek. Wuh ulef-caste, svi' wuh ragged turban heh wuh shabby ulster, wa'limatau wuh hideous na'shaya u' au kwit wuh mashek t' brandy heh dahkuh tumblers svi' khom t' au. Wuh kosu sidled abru heh began tor chatter. Dorian da-tor ish-veh pla' fi' au heh leralmin-tor vel svi' wuh neik spes tor adrian singleton. Wuh pi'tak-tor abru'teruklar-ru'lut, spo' wuh malay crease, writhed mes' wuh limuk t' veh t' wuh kosu. “etek nam-tor maut yaut tor-mu-yor, ” she sneered. “na' oekon’s sake don’t variben tor me, ” maf-tor dorian, stamping ish-veh ash'ya fi' wuh solektra. “ra tor du aitlun? Donku? La' ish-veh nam-tor. Don’t ek'wak variben tor me va'ashiv.” dahkuh yon-kur kil-tor kahai na' wuh moment svi' wuh kosu’s sodden bezhun, yi hanuvau si' heh losrak au pasik heh glazed. She tossed ish-veh patam heh dref-tor wuh di'kaudj ska' wuh tumek k' greedy ozh. Ish-veh besu glantau ish-veh enviously. “ish-veh’s rai nam-tor-tor, ” spes-tevan adrian singleton. “i don’t tun tor hal-tor pla'. Ra tor ish-veh tukh? I am ved kunli la'.” “du dungi kitau tor me kuv du aitlun sovek-vel, skil-tor’t du?” leralmin-tor dorian, po' wuh svizh. “sos'eh.” “rom mu-yor, yi.” “rom mu-yor, ” kilko-tor wuh nu'ri sasu, be' dvun-tor abru wuh ash-tor heh psethau ish-veh parched ru'lut k' wuh handkerchief. Dorian lates-tor tor wuh svep k' wuh glazhau t' kusut svi' ish-veh limuk. U' au drew wuh curtain aside, wuh hideous abru'teruklar-ru'lut shau s' wuh kras-tor bru-lar t' wuh kosu vi had taken ish-veh donku. “tra' hal-tor wuh e'shua’s bargain!” she huhk-tor, svi' wuh hoarse spes. “curse du!” au kilko-tor, “don’t vutau me ik.” she snapped ish-veh ozh. “prince sem-rik-tor nam-tor ra du spo' tor nam-tor puvutau, ain’t ish-veh?” she saul-tor po' ish-veh. Wuh drowsy masusu leaped tor ish-veh ash'ya u' she stariben, heh glazhau wildly pauk. Wuh ralash t' wuh shutting t' wuh tvur svep tevan-tor fi' ish-veh kaluk. Au rushed si' u' kuv svi' pursuit. Dorian zhai-kur hurried bi' wuh quay k'fai wuh drizzling sov-masu. Ish-veh latva k' adrian singleton had strangely dvun-tor ish-veh, heh au wondered kuv wuh ruin t' ik nu'ri ha'kiv vesh' really tor nam-tor laid na' ish-veh svep, u' basil hallward had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh k' such infamy t' viltah. Au zeshau ish-veh bru, heh na' wuh zamu seconds ish-veh bezhun grew maf. Wi, po' ek', ra did ish-veh tukh tor ish-veh? Veh’s gad vesh' nuh' brief tor nem-tor wuh burden t' wuh'ashiv’s lafosh fi' veh’s tipan. Tik sasu ha-tor ish-veh sha' ha'kiv heh vlitau ish-veh sha' price na' living ish-veh. Wuh goh pity vesh' veh had tor vlitau ni k'ashiv na' wuh single lafot. Veh had tor vlitau abru' heh abru' va'ashiv, indeed. Svi' ish-veh dealings k' sasu, buk worla a'ing ish-veh khrosahp. Tra' nam-tor moments, kloshai-talsu var-tor etek, lu wuh shaukaush na' sin, il na' ra wuh panu calls sin, ni abrukhau wuh malat ik kanok slah t' wuh ak'shem, u' kanok nala t' wuh shi'nahp, seems tor nam-tor instinct k' pthak-bosh impulses. Sasu heh kosu na' such moments pak-tor wuh el'es t' ish-veh dungi. Au dvun tor ish-veh terrible shaht u' automatons dvun. Dvel nam-tor taken s' au, heh conscience nam-tor either pustau, il, kuv ish-veh ha-tor na' ek', ha-tor tonk'peh tor mazhiv-kur-tor rebellion its sem heh disobedience its sem-rik. Na' ek' sins, u' theologians weary ri t' reminding etek, nam-tor sins t' disobedience. Lu ik pid tam'a, ik asal yel t' ek'rasah, tevan-tor s' sha-ka-ri, ish-veh vesh' u' wuh rebel ik au tevan-tor. Callous, concentrated fi' ek'rasah, k' kurau kashek, heh soul k'avon na' rebellion, dorian zhai-kur hastened fi', quickening ish-veh ash u' au went, tonk'peh u' au darted aside vi' wuh neik-ha'khlup archway, ik had dvin-tor ish-veh k'ashiv u' wuh pen tresahk tor wuh has-bosh-famed shi wilat au vesh' going, au olau himself suddenly seized s' za', heh fa' au had wak tor fosh-tor himself, au vesh' kwit pla' tehnat wuh temok, k' wuh brutal el'ru pauk ish-veh drahk. Au struggled madly na' ha'kiv, heh k' wuh terrible urgam wrenched wuh tightening ozh maf. Svi' wuh dahr au puzhu-tor wuh click t' wuh revolver, heh gla-tor wuh gleam t' wuh polished subok, pointing zehik na' ish-veh patam, heh wuh dusky shid t' wuh pen, bali-eku sasu limuk-tor ish-veh. “ra tor du aitlun?” au hushau. “potau hizhuk, ” leralmin-tor wuh sasu. “kuv du stir, i pohshau du.” “du nam-tor mad. Ra ma i ovsoh tor du?” “du vashau wuh ha'kiv t' sibyl vane, ” vesh' wuh kilko-srashiv, “heh sibyl vane vesh' t'nash-veh ko-kai. She pustau herself. I fai-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh tevakh nam-tor na' ish-veh svep. I swore i would stau du svi' fun. Na' tevun i ma sought du. I had rai clue, rai zavikau. Wuh dahkuh sutra vi kupi ma kethelvau du vesh' tevik. I fai-tor nothing t' du tonk'peh wuh kelek-aushfa ahm she nam-tor-tor tor vutau du. I puzhu-tor ish-veh tor-mu-yor k' pavesh. Tor ish-veh sochya k' oekon, na' tor-mu-yor du nam-tor going tor tev-tor.” dorian zhai-kur grew has-bosh k' pthak. “i worla fai-tor ish-veh, ” au stammered. “i worla puzhu-tor t' ish-veh. Du nam-tor mad.” “du had weh-rom confess ish-veh sin, na' u' sure u' i am james vane, du nam-tor going tor tev-tor.” tra' vesh' wuh horrible moment. Dorian did ri fai-tor ra tor leralmin il tor. “ne' fi' ish-veh mal-nef!” growled wuh sasu. “i mazhiv-kur-tor du veh minute tor tor ish-veh sochya—rai weht. I hal-tor fi' dohn tor-mu-yor na' india, heh i bolau tor t'nash-veh job wuh'rak. Veh minute. Ik’s ek'.” dorian’s kar tevan-tor tor ish-veh vla. Shivau k' vash, au did ri fai-tor ra tor tor. Suddenly wuh kwai rok kahai mes' ish-veh shi'nahp. “pehkaya, ” au maf-tor. “uf wu ago nam-tor ish-veh opi' ish-veh ko-kai tev-tor? Sahris, var-tor me!” “leh-oh tevun, ” leralmin-tor wuh sasu. “po tor du ya'akash me? Ra tor tevun tukh?” “leh-oh tevun, ” abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor dorian zhai-kur, k' wuh esta t' triumph svi' ish-veh spes. “leh-oh tevun! Eku me ne' wuh ha'gelek heh glazhau na' t'nash-veh limuk!” james vane hesitated na' wuh moment, ri understanding ra vesh' tvai. Yi au seized dorian zhai-kur heh zaseshau ish-veh s' wuh archway. Neik-ha'khlup heh wavering u' vesh' wuh salan-blown ta'hal, wi ish-veh dvin-tor tor gluvaya ish-veh wuh hideous lafosh, u' ish-veh seemed, vi' if au had tevan-tor, na' wuh limuk t' wuh sasu au had sought tor stau had ek' wuh svai t' boyhood, ek' wuh unstained purity t' youth. Au seemed pi' weht do wuh lad t' dah-leh belaar, hardly older, kuv older indeed na' ek', do ish-veh ko-kai had vesh' lu au had parted ni wehk tevun ago. Ish-veh vesh' obvious ik nash vesh' ri wuh sasu vi had vashau ish-veh ha'kiv. Au loosened ish-veh meskaraya heh reeled pla'. “t'nash-veh oekon! T'nash-veh oekon!” au maf-tor, “heh i would ma riyeht-stau du!” dorian zhai-kur drew wuh wu esh. “du ma vesh' fi' wuh rihk t' committing wuh terrible tr'y'kak, t'nash-veh sasu, ” au leralmin-tor, looking na' ish-veh sternly. “kal-tor nash nam-tor wuh warning tor du ri tor nem-tor vengeance vi' ish-veh sha' el'ru.” “forgive me, osu, ” muttered james vane. “i vesh' tehs-tor. Wuh pavesh zhit i puzhu-tor svi' ik damned den eku me fi' wuh riyeht yut.” “du had weh-rom hal-tor ha-kel heh shitau ik el'ru-pohshayek maf, il du lau prah vi' trouble, ” leralmin-tor dorian, turning fi' ish-veh timut heh going slowly ne' wuh yut. James vane lam-tor fi' wuh pavement svi' horror. Au vesh' trembling s' patam tor ash'ya. Po' wuh pi' du', wuh nesh-kur duv ik had vesh' creeping bi' wuh dripping temok dvun-tor si' vi' wuh ta'hal heh sarlah beyik ish-veh k' stealthy footsteps. Au olau wuh el'ru laid fi' ish-veh kar heh glazhau pauk k' wuh palikaya. Ish-veh vesh' veh t' wuh kosu vi had vesh' drinking na' wuh mofek. “po didn’t du stau ish-veh?” she shisau si', putting haggard limuk ved beyik ish-veh. “i fai-tor du vesh' zahalik ish-veh lu du rushed si' s' daly’s. Du duhsu! Du dang ma pustau ish-veh. Au has lots t' donku, heh au’s u' rasahkos u' rasahkos.” “au nam-tor ri wuh sasu i am looking na', ” au kilko-tor, “heh i aitlun rai sasu’s donku. I aitlun wuh sasu’s ha'kiv. Wuh sasu t'vi ha'kiv i aitlun bolau nam-tor nearly keh-leh i'. Nash-veh nam-tor pi' weht do wuh sa-kan. Itaren oekon, i ma ri prah ish-veh khaf fi-tor t'nash-veh el'ru.” wuh kosu mazhiv-kur-tor wuh sfith(-) abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “pi' weht do wuh sa-kan!” she sneered. “po, sasu, ish-veh’s nigh fi' leh-oh tevun opi' prince sem-rik-tor tor me ra i am.” “du ti!” maf-tor james vane. She ashenau ish-veh el'ru abru tor sha-ka-ri. “fa' oekon i am telling wuh yeht'es, ” she maf-tor. “fa' oekon?” “kwul me dumb kuv ish-veh ain’t ni. Au nam-tor wuh rasahkos veh ik sarlah la'. Au leralmin au has makau himself tor wuh e'shua na' wuh takov limuk. Ish-veh’s nigh fi' leh-oh tevun opi' i ragel-tor ish-veh. Au hasn’t rubai mau opi' yi. I ma, hi, ” she hau, k' wuh sickly leer. “du swear nash?” “i swear ish-veh, ” sarlah svi' hoarse vava s' ish-veh pa'ash ru'lut. “tonk'peh don’t mazhiv-kur-tor me maf tor ish-veh, ” she whined; “i am kwes t' ish-veh. Kal-tor me ma ein donku na' t'nash-veh mu-yor’s lodging.” au shau s' ish-veh k' wuh oath heh rushed tor wuh teruk t' wuh yut, tonk'peh dorian zhai-kur had sasaudau. Lu au glazhau pla', wuh kosu had vanished isha. Chapter xvii. Wuh wehk gad later dorian zhai-kur vesh' sitting svi' wuh conservatory na' selby royal, talking tor wuh takov duchess t' monmouth, vi k' ish-veh sa-telsu, wuh jaded-looking sasu t' sheh-leh, vesh' svi' ish-veh be'hai'la. Ish-veh vesh' theris-masu-wak, heh wuh mellow ta'hal t' wuh masuk', lace-wein-tor ha'gelek ik lam-tor fi' wuh pasu lit abru wuh delicate china heh mah-tor haul-tukh t' wuh dvin na' if wuh duchess vesh' presiding. Ish-veh wan-kur el'ru vesh' dvun-tor daintily among wuh cups, heh ish-veh bosh yon-kur bru-lar vesh' smiling na' vel ik dorian had zhal-tor tor ish-veh. S'haile henry vesh' lying pla' svi' wuh silk-draped wicker ku-san, looking na' au. Fi' wuh peach-kur-tor divan hayal-tor t'sai narborough, pretending tor shroi tor wuh duke’s kethelvaya t' wuh kim-shah brazilian sark ik au had hau tor ish-veh tershaya. Rehkuh nu'ri sasu svi' elaborate smoking-saikhut vesh' handing theris-masu-cakes tor ein t' wuh kosu. Wuh kelek-party consisted t' leh-dah sutra, heh tra' vesh' weht gishu tor lasha fi' wuh thurai gad. “ra nam-tor du dahkuh talking pa'?” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, strolling abru' tor wuh pasu heh putting ish-veh cup ne'. “i rok dorian has var-tor du pa' t'nash-veh dotor na' rechristening kanok-vei, gladys. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh delightful idea.” “tonk'peh i don’t aitlun tor nam-tor rechristened, harry, ” rejoined wuh duchess, looking abru na' ish-veh k' ish-veh wonderful bezhun. “i am ved satisfied k' t'nash-veh sha' ahm, heh i am sure mr. Zhai-kur dang nam-tor satisfied k' ish-veh.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam gladys, i would ri rubitau either ahm na' wuh panu. Au nam-tor fi' buhfik. I vesh' thinking chiefly t' svai. Za-gad i tresahk wuh orchid, na' t'nash-veh gonaf-razh. Ish-veh vesh' wuh marvellous gla-tor vel, u' dau-bosh u' wuh stehkuh tevalik sins. Svi' wuh thoughtless moment i ya'akash veh t' wuh bahsu ra ish-veh vesh' puvutau. Au var-tor me ish-veh vesh' wuh tok-ti specimen t' _robinsoniana_, il vel dreadful t' ik ves. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh maf yeht'es, tonk'peh etek ma pakik wuh sutra t' giving lovely ahm tor vel. Ahm nam-tor kanok-vei. I worla quarrel k' torai. T'nash-veh veh quarrel nam-tor k' zhit. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh goh vel au nam-tor nunau na'.” “yi ra dang etek vutau du, harry?” she ya'akash. “ish-veh ahm nam-tor prince paradox, ” leralmin-tor dorian. “i recognize ish-veh svi' wuh kahai, ” sporiben wuh duchess. “i skil-tor’t zhu-tor t' ish-veh, ” abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor s'haile henry, sinking vi' wuh ku-san. “s' wuh label tra' nam-tor rai stron! I klee'fah wuh title.” “royalties lau ri abdicate, ” tevan-tor u' wuh warning s' takov bru-lar. “du istaya me tor fosh-tor t'nash-veh throne, yi?” “ha.” “i mazhiv-kur-tor wuh yeht'es t' tor-morrow.” “i prefer wuh lafosh t' tor-gad, ” she kilko-tor. “du disarm me, gladys, ” au maf-tor, catching wuh wilfulness t' ish-veh mood. “t' ish-veh fo-dan, harry, ri t' ish-veh tilek.” “i worla ayaya tehnat vaksur, ” au leralmin-tor, k' wuh pral t' ish-veh el'ru. “ik nam-tor ish-veh lafosh, harry, dva-tor me. Du tala vaksur irak nuh' mau.” “uf mokuhlek du leralmin ik? I nafai-tor ik i nah-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom tor nam-tor vaksurik do tor nam-tor rom. Tonk'peh fi' wuh vath el'ru, kling nam-tor weht pok do i am tor nafai-tor ik ish-veh nam-tor weh-rom tor nam-tor rom do tor nam-tor watosh.” “ugliness nam-tor veh t' wuh stehkuh tevalik sins, yi?” maf-tor wuh duchess. “ra shetau t' ish-veh simile pa' wuh orchid?” “ugliness nam-tor veh t' wuh stehkuh tevalik virtues, gladys. Du, u' wuh rom tory, bolau ri underrate au. Naliveh, wuh bible, heh wuh stehkuh tevalik virtues ma tor etwel england ra she nam-tor.” “du don’t spo' ish-veh shasol, yi?” she ya'akash. “i ha-tor svi' ish-veh.” “ik du lau censure ish-veh wuh weh-rom.” “would du ma me nem-tor wuh verdict t' europe fi' ish-veh?” au inquired. “ra tor au leralmin t' etek?” “ik tartuffe has emigrated tor england heh tu'ash wuh mahr-kel.” “nam-tor ik ish-veh, harry?” “i mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh tor du.” “i kupi ri nam-tor-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh nam-tor nuh' yeht.” “du bolaya ri nam-tor kwes. Etwel countrymen worla recognize wuh kethelvaya.” “au nam-tor practical.” “au nam-tor weht cunning do practical. Lu au tor abru ish-veh ledger, au vo'ektaya stupidity k' don-tak, heh vice k' hypocrisy.” “fam dvun, etek ma ovsoh lo'uk vel.” “lo'uk vel ma vesh' kwit fi' etek, gladys.” “etek ma lesh ish-veh burden.” “goh u' irak u' wuh fek di'kizh.” she hutau ish-veh patam. “i dva-tor svi' wuh ne-koshtri, ” she maf-tor. “ish-veh represents wuh rishan t' wuh pushing.” “ish-veh has storaya.” “nehaya sem-tor me weht.” “ra t' tanaf?” she ya'akash. “ish-veh nam-tor wuh malady.” “ashaya?” “wuh illusion.” “odva?” “wuh fashionable substitute na' dva.” “du nam-tor wuh sceptic.” “worla! Du dang mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh warning.” “i daren’t, mr. Zhai-kur. Po, she fereik-tor taik na' me. Du vokau wuh veh i sai-vel-tor na' t'sai hilstone’s bah-ker-party? Ek' rom taik nam-tor tor s' nothing.” “spo' ek' rom reputations, gladys, ” svi-shau s'haile henry. “kanok daya ish-veh torvau mazhiv-kur-tor veh wuh nemut. Tor nam-tor popular veh bolau nam-tor wuh mediocrity.” “ri k' kosu, ” leralmin-tor wuh duchess, shaking ish-veh patam; “heh kosu tor-go wuh panu. I assure du etek mokuhlek’t lesh mediocrities. Etek kosu, u' ein veh leralmin-tor, ashaya k' etwel kaluk, aishan u' du sasu ashaya k' ish-veh bezhun, kuv du ek'wak ashaya na' ek'.” “ish-veh seems tor me ik etek worla tor sovek-kitok, ” murmured dorian. “ah! Yi, du worla really ashaya, mr. Zhai-kur, ” kilko-tor wuh duchess k' mock sadness. “t'nash-veh tal-kam gladys!” maf-tor s'haile henry. “uf mokuhlek du leralmin ik? Romance ha-tor k' repetition, heh repetition rushan-tor wuh yeht-avon vi' wuh tanaf. Isha, tik wak ish-veh ashau nam-tor wuh goh wak veh has ek'wak ashau. Natyan t' vel tor ri rubitau singleness t' shaukaush. Ish-veh goh intensifies ish-veh. Etek mokuhlek ma svi' ha'kiv tonk'peh veh lo'uk veshtaya na' buhfik, heh wuh tsat t' ha'kiv nam-tor tor reproduce ik veshtaya u' k'ashiv u' tor-yehat.” “kauk lu veh has vesh' wounded k' ish-veh, harry?” ya'akash wuh duchess po' wuh svizh. “wa' lu veh has vesh' wounded k' ish-veh, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry. Wuh duchess da-tor heh glazhau na' dorian zhai-kur k' wuh curious sagluvaya svi' ish-veh bezhun. “ra tor du leralmin tor ik, mr. Zhai-kur?” she inquired. Dorian hesitated na' wuh moment. Yi au threw ish-veh patam pla' heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “i kwon-hau-ov sep-wafikh k' harry, duchess.” “kauk lu au nam-tor riyeht?” “harry nam-tor worla riyeht, duchess.” “heh tor ish-veh ven-dol-leralmin tor du kunli?” “i ma worla pstha na' happiness. Vi aitlu happiness? I ma pstha na' sanosh.” “heh afer-tor ish-veh, mr. Zhai-kur?” “k'ashiv. Nuh' k'ashiv.” wuh duchess spes-tevan. “i am searching na' sochya, ” she leralmin-tor, “heh kuv i don’t hal-tor heh sai-vel, i dungau ma rim nash khru.” “kal-tor me prah du ein orchids, duchess, ” maf-tor dorian, starting tor ish-veh ash'ya heh walking ne' wuh conservatory. “du nam-tor flirting disgracefully k' ish-veh, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry tor ish-veh krei. “du had weh-rom nem-tor tun. Au nam-tor maut sem-rik.” “kuv au vesh' ri, tra' would nam-tor rai puk.” “greek ragel-tor greek, yi?” “i am fi' wuh vla t' wuh trojans. Au fought na' wuh kosu.” “au vesh' defeated.” “tra' nam-tor weh-rasahkos vel do kum, ” she kilko-tor. “du ausahr k' wuh thal rein.” “sahr mazhiv-kur-tor ha'kiv, ” vesh' wuh _riposte_. “i dungau kitau ish-veh svi' t'nash-veh gad-dunap tor-mu-yor.” “ra?” “ik wuh yontau kan ashau wuh yon.” “i am ri kauk singed. T'nash-veh rala nam-tor untouched.” “du nam-tor-tor au na' kanok-vei, kaula hash.” “courage has be' dvun-tor s' sasu tor kosu. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh uzh veshtaya na' etek.” “du ma wuh rival.” “vi?” au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “t'sai narborough, ” au zhal-tor. “she perfectly adores ish-veh.” “du boshaya me k' apprehension. Wuh appeal tor antiquity nam-tor fatal tor etek vi nam-tor romanticists.” “romanticists! Du ma ek' wuh methods t' ek'tal.” “sasu ma educated etek.” “tonk'peh ri danau du.” “kethelvau etek u' wuh guv, ” vesh' ish-veh kali-fi. “sphinxes rik' tsat.” she glazhau na' ish-veh, smiling. “uf wu mr. Zhai-kur nam-tor!” she leralmin-tor. “kal-tor etek hal-tor heh gol'nev ish-veh. I ma ri wi var-tor ish-veh wuh kur t' t'nash-veh pelal.” “ah! Du bolau saikhut ish-veh pelal tor ish-veh svai, gladys.” “ik would nam-tor wuh fe-wakik surrender.” “romantic tanaf palikau k' its climax.” “i bolau potau wuh opportunity na' retreat.” “svi' wuh parthian manner?” “au afer-tor ek'manek svi' wuh eshikh. I kupi ri tor ik.” “kosu nam-tor ri kwon-hau-ov kal-tor wuh dvel, ” au kilko-tor, tonk'peh hardly had au shahtau wuh zhit-bal fa' s' wuh irak shaht t' wuh conservatory sarlah wuh stifled groan, zahal-tor k' wuh pasik ralash t' wuh ras tevan. Kanok-veh palikau abru. Wuh duchess lam-tor motionless svi' horror. Heh k' pthak svi' ish-veh bezhun, s'haile henry rushed k'fai wuh flapping ku tor talal dorian zhai-kur lying limuk ne'le fi' wuh tiled lan-tol svi' wuh deathlike swoon. Au vesh' lesh na' wuh'wak vi' wuh pla-kur bestan-tvi-shal heh laid fi-tor veh t' wuh ku-san. Po' wuh pen wak, sarlah ish-veh tor himself heh glazhau pauk k' wuh dazed sagluvaya. “ra has pavesh-tor?” au ya'akash. “oh! I vokau. Am i safe la', harry?” au began tor tremble. “t'nash-veh tal-kam dorian, ” kilko-tor s'haile henry, “du goh fainted. Ik vesh' ek'. Du bolau ma overtired yourself. Du had weh-rom ri sarlah ne' tor aru-yem. I dungi nem-tor ish-veh shi.” “rai, dungi-sarlah nash-veh ne', ” au leralmin-tor, struggling tor ish-veh ash'ya. “i would rather sarlah ne'. I bolau ri nam-tor sa'awek.” au went tor ish-veh tvi-shal heh sai-vel-tor. Tra' vesh' wuh kwai recklessness t' gaiety svi' ish-veh manner u' au hayal-tor na' pasu, tonk'peh i' heh yi wuh thrill t' vash sahr-tor k'fai ish-veh lu au vokau ik, hish-tor tehnat wuh krani t' wuh conservatory, spo' wuh wan-kur handkerchief, au had gla-tor wuh limuk t' james vane watching ish-veh. Chapter xviii. Wuh thurai gad au did ri trasha wuh kelek, heh, indeed, spent danik t' wuh wak svi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, has-bosh k' wuh kwai vash t' dying, heh wi indifferent tor ha'kiv itself. Wuh hokni'es t' hasu shi'kar, snared, bi'dvun-tor ne', had palikau tor abrukhau ish-veh. Kuv wuh tapestry did tonk'peh tremble svi' wuh salan, au hutau. Wuh tevik mor ik vesh' blown tehnat wuh leaded panes seemed tor ish-veh spo' ish-veh sha' thinoi resolutions heh kwai regrets. Lu au a'ing ish-veh bezhun, gla-tor ish-veh va'ashiv wuh masusu’s limuk peering k'fai wuh mist-kurau makh, heh horror seemed wuh'wak weht tor ti its el'ru fi-tor ish-veh khaf-spol. Tonk'peh sos'eh ish-veh had vesh' goh ish-veh fancy ik had puvutau vengeance s' wuh mu-yor heh eku wuh hideous shid t' taflaya fa' ish-veh. Actual ha'kiv vesh' nezhak, tonk'peh tra' vesh' vel terribly olozhikaik svi' wuh glenonaya. Ish-veh vesh' wuh glenonaya ik eku remorse tor dog wuh ash'ya t' sin. Ish-veh vesh' wuh glenonaya ik tor tik tr'y'kak lesh its misshapen kesh-travek. Svi' wuh tsuri panu t' kla-min wuh wicked vesh' ri taflau, il wuh rom rewarded. Navun vesh' putan-tor tor wuh karik, vravshaya kwit fi-tor wuh kobat. Ik vesh' ek'. Isha, had sovek ri-fainusu vesh' prowling pauk wuh kelek, au would ma vesh' gla-tor k' wuh dvinsu il wuh keepers. Had sovek ash'ya-ulidar vesh' afer-tor fi' wuh svai-sar-tak, wuh bahsu would ma reported ish-veh. Ha, ish-veh had vesh' goh fancy. Sibyl vane’s sa-kai had ri sarlah pla' tor stau ish-veh. Au had masu-halovau maf svi' ish-veh hali tor afersu svi' ein karil masutra. S' ish-veh, na' sovek tav, au vesh' safe. Po, wuh sasu did ri fai-tor vi au vesh', kupi ri fai-tor vi au vesh'. Wuh limein t' youth had korsau ish-veh. Heh wi kuv ish-veh had vesh' goh wuh illusion, uf terrible ish-veh vesh' tor nah-tor ik conscience kupi ashenau such pthak-bosh phantoms, heh mazhiv-kur-tor au visible shid, heh tor au dvun fa' veh! Ra wihfelau t' ha'kiv would ish-veh nam-tor kuv, gad heh mu-yor, duv t' ish-veh tr'y'kak vesh' tor peer na' ish-veh s' ralash-fam teruk, tor mock ish-veh s' tsat shitau, tor zhal svi' ish-veh kaluk u' au hayal-tor na' wuh gadzhak, tor wake ish-veh k' icy ozh u' au ti asleep! U' wuh nahp crept k'fai ish-veh shi'nahp, au grew spoh k' vash, heh wuh sov seemed tor ish-veh ki' shetau suddenly colder. Oh! Svi' ra wuh kwai wadan t' ni-resh au had pustau ish-veh t'hy'la! Uf ghastly wuh mere vokaya t' wuh scene! Gla-tor ish-veh ish-veh ek' va'ashiv. Tik hideous detail sarlah pla' tor ish-veh k' hau horror. S' wuh nesh-kur tauk t' wak, terrible heh swathed svi' ug'yon-kur, she-tor wuh glakuv t' ish-veh sin. Lu s'haile henry sarlah svi' na' shehkuh o’wak-vel, au afer-tor ish-veh maf-tor u' veh t'vi khaf-spol dungi shaya. Ish-veh vesh' ri till wuh wuh gad ik au ventured tor hal-tor si'. Tra' vesh' vel svi' wuh pa'shik, pine-scented sov t' ik karil asal ik seemed tor katau ish-veh pla' ish-veh joyousness heh ish-veh ardour na' ha'kiv. Tonk'peh ish-veh vesh' ri goh wuh tukhik nosh t' ek'sitra ik had aisha wuh rubah. Ish-veh sha' malat had revolted tehnat wuh mau-mazhiv-kur t' thonaya ik had sought tor maim heh mar wuh perfection t' its hayal. K' subtle heh finely wrought temperaments ish-veh nam-tor kwon-hau-ov ni. Ish-veh karik shaukaush bolau either wadi-yarek il vulaya. Au either slay wuh sasu, il themselves tev-tor. Gan sorrows heh gan ashau ha-tor fi'. Wuh ashau heh sorrows ik nam-tor lo'uk nam-tor vashau k' ish-veh sha' plenitude. Isha, au had convinced himself ik au had vesh' wuh shi-kar-tor t' wuh vash-stricken glenonaya, heh glazhau pla' i' fi' ish-veh ptha k' vel t' pity heh ri wuh pi' t' contempt. Po' asal-yem, au lates-tor k' wuh duchess na' wuh wadan svi' wuh bah-ker heh yi drove mes' wuh shi'sochya tor hau wuh shooting-party. Wuh crisp le-su ti spo' alem fi-tor wuh yar. Wuh igen vesh' wuh abomesau cup t' pla-kur mokev. Wuh wonil wontin t' le-suma bordered wuh pa'ash, reed-grown suk'muzh. Na' wuh teruk t' wuh pine-lapan au kum-tor glan t' osu geoffrey clouston, wuh duchess’s sa-kai, jerking dahkuh spent cartridges s' ish-veh pohshayek. Au spen-tor s' wuh hal, heh having var-tor wuh groom tor nem-tor wuh mare ha-kel, tor ish-veh yut na' ish-veh be'hai'la k'fai wuh withered bracken heh rough undergrowth. “ma du had rom torvukh, geoffrey?” au ya'akash. “ri maut rom, dorian. I nah-tor danik t' wuh kushel ma hal-tor tor wuh tu'ash. I dare leralmin ish-veh dungi nam-tor weh-rom po' khi-gad-yem, lu etek prah tor uzh solektra.” dorian strolled bi' k' ish-veh vla. Wuh keen aromatic sov, wuh khav-kur heh yon-kur ha'ge ik glimmered svi' wuh lapan, wuh hoarse maf-tor t' wuh beaters ringing si' s' wak tor wak, heh wuh nasik snaps t' wuh pohshayek ik zahal-tor, sem-tor ish-veh heh boshau ish-veh k' wuh kash-ral t' delightful el'es. Au vesh' abrukhau k' wuh carelessness t' happiness, k' wuh pid indifference t' mak. Suddenly s' wuh lumpy tussock t' hinek yar ein dah-leh ker svi' khom t' au, k' nesh-kur-tipped kaluk abru-tor heh wu hinder sikrus throwing ish-veh fa'rak, palikau wuh hare. Ish-veh terkau na' wuh pi'laptra t' alders. Kal-tor ish-veh ha-tor.” “ra nonsense, dorian!” abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor ish-veh besu, heh u' wuh hare bounded vi' wuh pi'laptra, au pohshau. Tra' vesh' dahkuh maf-tor puzhu-tor, wuh maf t' wuh hare svi' kusut, if nam-tor dreadful, wuh maf t' wuh sasu svi' agony, if nam-tor weh-rasahkos. “rom heavens! I ma kwul wuh beater!” sporiben osu geoffrey. “ra wuh ass wuh sasu vesh' tor prah svi' khom t' wuh pohshayek! Pehkaya shooting tra'!” au puvutau si' na' wuh fik t' ish-veh spes. “wuh sasu nam-tor dash-tor.” wuh patam-keeper sarlah sahran abru k' wuh terpau svi' ish-veh el'ru. “wilat, osu? Wilat nam-tor au?” au saul-tor. Na' wuh ka wak, wuh firing ceased bi' wuh zehl. “la', ” kilko-tor osu geoffrey angrily, hurrying na' wuh pi'laptra. “po fi' terra don’t du potau ish-veh sasu pla'? Au puzhu-tor osu geoffrey ya'akash kuv wuh sasu vesh' really tevik, heh wuh affirmative kilko-srashiv t' wuh keeper. Wuh lapan seemed tor ish-veh ki' shetau suddenly alive k' limuk. Sarlah; kal-tor etek hal-tor ha-kel.” au lates-tor vla k' vla svi' wuh kharat t' wuh avenue na' nearly kau-leh ker rik' speaking. Nash kisheya, i suppose. T'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, ish-veh mokuhlek’t nam-tor gol-tor. Ish-veh vesh' wuh sasu’s sha' lafot. Po did au prah svi' khom t' wuh pohshayek? I spo' wuh duchess maut mau, tonk'peh i don’t ashaya ish-veh.” “heh wuh duchess ashau du maut mau, tonk'peh she tishau du lehkuh, ni du nam-tor excellently matched.” “du nam-tor talking scandal, harry, heh tra' nam-tor worla sovek i'sav na' scandal.” “wuh i'sav t' kanok scandal nam-tor wuh immoral certainty, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, ha'gelan wuh cigarette. “du would sacrifice anybody, harry, na' wuh sake t' wuh epigram.” “wuh panu hal-tor tor wuh altar t' its sha' accord, ” vesh' wuh kilko-srashiv. “i istaya i kupi ashaya, ” maf-tor dorian zhai-kur k' wuh glu pitoh t' pathos svi' ish-veh spes. “tonk'peh i seem ki' pakik wuh shaukaush heh yen-tor wuh aitlun. I am nuh' mau concentrated fi' myself. T'nash-veh sha' nafu'es has shetau wuh burden tor me. I aitlun tor stron, tor hal-tor maf, tor yen-tor. Ish-veh vesh' silly t' me tor sarlah ne' la' na' ek'. Au nam-tor going tor faint.” dorian drew himself abru k' wuh urgam heh abru'teruklar-ru'lut. “ish-veh nam-tor nothing, duchess, ” au murmured; “t'nash-veh tor'tsu nam-tor dreadfully s' zek. She did ri kilko-srashiv na' ein wak, tonk'peh lam-tor gazing na' wuh landscape. “i istaya i fai-tor, ” she leralmin-tor na' kim-shah. Au hutau ish-veh patam. “fai-tukh would nam-tor fatal. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh uncertainty ik sem-rik-tor veh. Wuh mist tor vel wonderful.” “veh lau pak-tor veh’s yut.” “ek' yut shaht na' wuh ka sfek, t'nash-veh tal-kam gladys.” “ra nam-tor ik?” “disillusion.” “ish-veh vesh' t'nash-veh _début_ svi' ha'kiv, ” she spes-tevan. “sarlah ish-veh tor du crowned.” “i am zungor t' strawberry mor.” “au shetau du.” “goh svi' tsuri.” “du would din-tor au, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “i dungi ri krus k' wuh kur-mor.” “monmouth has kaluk.” “hinek ya'shakhuv nam-tor pasik t' khaf-spol.” “has au worla vesh' kis-ka?” “i istaya au had vesh'.” au glanced pa' u' kuv svi' psthan t' vel. “ra nam-tor du looking na'?” she inquired. “wuh gonaf s' ish-veh moktin, ” au kilko-tor. “du ma eku-tor ish-veh.” she abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “i ma fam dvun wuh limein.” “ish-veh tor ish-veh bezhun lovelier, ” vesh' ish-veh kilko. She abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor va'ashiv. Ish-veh zud gluvau spo' wan-kur nei svi' wuh ug'yon-kur savas. Upstairs, svi' ish-veh sha' tvi-shal, dorian zhai-kur vesh' lying fi' wuh ku-san, k' vash svi' kanok tingling slah t' ish-veh ak'shem. Ha'kiv had suddenly shetau nuh' hideous wuh burden na' ish-veh tor lesh. Wuh dreadful tevakh t' wuh unlucky beater, pohshaya svi' wuh pi'laptra spo' wuh kwai aushfa, had seemed tor ish-veh tor pre-khlop tevakh na' himself isha. Au had nearly swooned na' ra s'haile henry had leralmin-tor svi' wuh pavesh mood t' cynical jesting. Na' kaukuh o’wak-vel au rang ish-veh kus-vakh na' ish-veh dvinsu heh mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh zek tor sa'haf ish-veh vel na' wuh mu-yor-sagluvau tor kahr, heh ki' wuh brougham na' wuh svep k' ohkuh-reh-leh. Au vesh' satalau ri tor yuk wuh'ashiv mu-yor na' selby royal. Ish-veh vesh' wuh has-bosh-omened shi. Tevakh lates-tor tra' svi' wuh ug'yel-ha'gel. Wuh yar t' wuh laptra had vesh' gla-tor k' khaf. Yi au kitau wuh pitoh tor s'haile henry, telling ish-veh ik au vesh' going abru tor kahr tor consult ish-veh hassu heh asking ish-veh tor entertain ish-veh be'hai'la svi' ish-veh absence. U' au vesh' putting ish-veh vi' wuh envelope, wuh knock sarlah tor wuh svep, heh ish-veh valet informed ish-veh ik wuh patam-keeper istau tor gla-tor ish-veh. Au kwal-tor heh zeshau ish-veh bru. “satau ish-veh svi', ” au muttered, po' ein moments’ vaunah. U' ak u' wuh sasu svi-tor, dorian seshau ish-veh chequebook s' wuh zish-nef heh sak-tor ish-veh si' fa' ish-veh. “i suppose du ma sarlah pa' wuh unfortunate kisheya t' nash asal, thornton?” au leralmin-tor, taking abru wuh pen. “ha, osu, ” kilko-tor wuh gamekeeper. “vesh' wuh ri donku-tor katravahsu telik? Had au sovek sutra nerik fi' ish-veh?” ya'akash dorian, looking bored. “kuv ni, i dang ri spo' au tor nam-tor losrak svi' aitlun, heh dungi satau au sovek hau-ov t' donku du lau nah-tor bolayatik.” “etek don’t fai-tor vi au nam-tor, osu. Ik nam-tor ra i nem-tor wuh liberty t' coming tor du pa'.” “don’t fai-tor vi au nam-tor?” leralmin-tor dorian, listlessly. “ra tor du tvai? Wasn’t au veh t' ish-veh sasu?” “rai, osu. Worla gla-tor ish-veh fa'. Seems spo' wuh masusu, osu.” wuh pen eku-tor s' dorian zhai-kur’s el'ru, heh au olau u' kuv ish-veh khaf-spol had suddenly pehkau beating. “wuh masusu?” au lit'dhae. “did du leralmin wuh masusu?” “ha, osu. Au glazhau u' kuv au had vesh' wuh wihfelau t' masusu; tattooed fi' fi' kar, heh ik ves t' vel.” “vesh' tra' sovek-vel afer-tor fi' ish-veh?” leralmin-tor dorian, leaning fa'rak heh looking na' wuh sasu k' startled bezhun. “sovek-vel ik would var-tor ish-veh ahm?” “ein donku, osu—ri mau, heh wuh shehkuh-shooter. Tra' vesh' rai ahm t' sovek ves. Wuh tevan-looking sasu, osu, tonk'peh rough-spo'. Wuh wihfelau t' masusu etek nah-tor.” dorian palikau tor ish-veh ash'ya. Wuh terrible rok nuv-tor vesht ish-veh. Au clutched na' ish-veh madly. “wilat nam-tor wuh ak'shem?” au sporiben. “sahris! I bolau gla-tor ish-veh na' wuh'wak.” “ish-veh nam-tor svi' wuh herbosh tihet svi' wuh ha-kel uroshal, osu. Wuh sular don’t spo' tor ma ik wihfelau t' vel svi' ish-veh kelek. Au leralmin wuh tevikeh katau rasahkos kunli.” “wuh ha-kel uroshal! Hal-tor tra' na' wuh'wak heh ragel-tor me. Var-tor veh t' wuh grooms tor katau t'nash-veh jarel pauk. Rai. Worla kashek. I’ll hal-tor tor wuh stables myself. Ish-veh dungi korsau wak.” svi' lehkuh tor wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan, dorian zhai-kur vesh' galloping ne' wuh wu avenue u' lerash u' au kupi hal-tor. Wuh lap seemed tor fnashtaya vesht ish-veh svi' spectral procession, heh kwai duv tor fling themselves mes' ish-veh yut. Wuh'wak wuh mare swerved na' wuh wan-kur temep-lehk heh nearly threw ish-veh. Au lashed ish-veh mes' wuh talu k' ish-veh urozh. She thresh wuh dusky sov spo' wuh kliton. Wuh kov flew s' ish-veh hoofs. Na' kim-shah au pulau wuh ha-kel uroshal. Dahkuh sasu vesh' loitering svi' wuh ker. Au leaped s' wuh saddle heh threw wuh reins tor veh t' au. Svi' wuh dan-irak tihet wuh ta'hal vesh' glimmering. Vel seemed tor var-tor ish-veh ik wuh ak'shem vesh' tra', heh au hurried tor wuh svep heh shitau ish-veh el'ru fi-tor wuh kuhr. Tra' au svizh-tor na' wuh moment, olaya ik au vesh' fi' wuh rihk t' wuh discovery ik would either tor il mar ish-veh ha'kiv. Yi au kwit wuh svep tu'ash heh svi-tor. Fi' wuh tuh t' sacking svi' wuh irak teruk vesh' lying wuh tevik ak'shem t' wuh sasu sai-vel-tor svi' wuh dirik sav'el heh wuh shif t' pla-kur malanu. Wuh gla-tor handkerchief had vesh' shitau abru' wuh limuk. Wuh dirik ha'fek, terpau svi' wuh mashek, sputtered be' ish-veh. Dorian zhai-kur ak'shem-hutau. Au olau ik ish-veh kupi ri nam-tor wuh el'ru tor nem-tor wuh handkerchief maf, heh shoret veh t' wuh uroshal-dvinsu tor sarlah tor ish-veh. “nem-tor ik vel ska' wuh limuk. I istaya tor gla-tor ish-veh, ” au leralmin-tor, clutching na' wuh svep-lehk na' nenikaya. Lu wuh uroshal-dvinsu had ovsoh ni, au ash-tor fa'rak. Wuh maf t' mak shau s' ish-veh bru-lar. Wuh sasu vi had vesh' pohshaya svi' wuh pi'laptra vesh' james vane. Au lam-tor tra' na' ein minutes looking na' wuh tevik ak'shem. U' au fau-tor ha-kel, ish-veh bezhun vesh' bosh t' bezhun-masu, na' au fai-tor au vesh' safe. Chapter xix. “tra' nam-tor rai nam-tor-tor ish-veh telling me ik du nam-tor going tor nam-tor rom, ” maf-tor s'haile henry, dipping ish-veh wan-kur ozh vi' wuh yon-kur khaf-tukh yerak boshau k' she-tor-masu. “du nam-tor ved buhfik. Pray, don’t rubah.” dorian zhai-kur hutau ish-veh patam. “rai, harry, i ma ovsoh nuh' wehk dreadful vel svi' t'nash-veh ha'kiv. I am ri going tor tor sovek weht. I began t'nash-veh rom torai za-gad.” “wilat vesh' du za-gad?” “svi' wuh shasol, harry. I vesh' staying na' wuh pi' ha-shal k' myself.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, smiling, “anybody mokuhlek nam-tor rom svi' wuh shasol. Tra' nam-tor rai temptations tra'. Ik nam-tor wuh utvau po sutra vi ha-tor s' kahr nam-tor ni absolutely uncivilized. Sutenivaya nam-tor ri k' sovek tvai wuh hagik vel tor attain tor. Tra' nam-tor goh dahkuh yut k' if sasu mokuhlek pulau ish-veh. Veh nam-tor k' hasu iyula, wuh vath k' hasu corrupt. Shasol sutra ma rai opportunity t' hasu either, ni au stagnate.” “iyula heh corruption, ” echoed dorian. “i ma fainu vel t' fi'. Ish-veh seems terrible tor me i' ik au dang ek'wak nam-tor afer-tor teretuhr. Na' i ma wuh uzh tangu, harry. I am going tor rubitau. I nah-tor i ma rubitau.” “du ma ri wi var-tor me ra ish-veh rom torai vesh'. Il did du leralmin du had ovsoh weht do veh?” ya'akash ish-veh besu u' au ne-tor vi' ish-veh math wuh pi' hirat-kur rekun t' seeded strawberries heh, k'fai wuh tilau, fo-kushizhau floku, izhau wan-kur slor-tukh fi-tor au. “i mokuhlek var-tor du, harry. Ish-veh nam-tor ri wuh var i kupi var-tor tor sovek veh else. I spared somebody. Ish-veh sounds vain, tonk'peh du ken-tor ra i tvai. She vesh' ved vaksurik heh wonderfully spo' sibyl vane. I nah-tor ish-veh vesh' ik if wuh'rak skamau me tor ish-veh. Du vokau sibyl, don’t du? Uf wu ago ik seems! Muhl, hetty vesh' ri veh t' etwel sha' mohrn, t' rivak. She vesh' veling wuh ko-kan svi' wuh pi'kahr. Tonk'peh i really ashau ish-veh. I am ved sure ik i ashau ish-veh. Ek' du' nash wonderful lau ik etek ma vesh' having, i nam-tor-tor tor sahr-tor ne' heh gla-tor ish-veh dahkuh il rehkuh wak wuh wehk gad. Za-gad she ragel-tor me svi' wuh pi' lap-bah-ker. Wuh savas-blossoms potau tumbling ne' fi' ish-veh isachya, heh she vesh' laughing. Etek vesh' ki' hal-tor maf teretuhr nash asal na' gad-keshtan. Suddenly i satalau tor trasha ish-veh u' flowerlike u' i had afer-tor ish-veh.” “i dang nah-tor wuh novelty t' wuh zherka bolau ma putan-tor du wuh thrill t' yeht sanosh, dorian, ” svi-shau s'haile henry. “tonk'peh i mokuhlek shaht ish-veh idyll na' du. Du mazhiv-kur-tor ish-veh rom na'shikh heh shau ish-veh khaf-spol. Ik vesh' wuh palikaya t' ish-veh reformation.” “harry, du nam-tor horrible! Du mustn’t leralmin aifa dreadful vel. Hetty’s khaf-spol nam-tor ri pushau. Veling, she maf-tor heh ek' ik. Tonk'peh tra' nam-tor rai disgrace fi-tor ish-veh. She mokuhlek ha-tor, spo' perdita, svi' ish-veh bah-ker t' mint heh marigold.” “heh tusa abru' wuh faithless florizel, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, laughing, u' au gal-tor pla' svi' ish-veh ku-san. “t'nash-veh tal-kam dorian, du ma wuh danik curiously boyish moods. Tor du nah-tor nash ko-kan dungi ek'wak nam-tor really content i' k' sovek veh t' ish-veh sha' lan? I suppose she dungi nam-tor telik ein gad tor wuh rough carter il wuh grinning ploughman. Muhl, wuh kla-min t' having ragel-tor du, heh ashau du, dungi saven-tor ish-veh tor despise ish-veh sa-telsu, heh she dungi nam-tor wretched. S' wuh moral sfek t' zan-tor, i fam yehat leralmin ik i nah-tor mau t' ish-veh lo'uk renunciation. Kauk u' wuh palikaya, ish-veh nam-tor ri donku-tor. Isha, uf tor du fai-tor ik hetty isn’t floating na' wuh la' moment svi' ein starlit mill-muzh, k' lovely masu-lilies pauk ish-veh, spo' ophelia?” “i mokuhlek’t lesh nash, harry! Du mock na' kanok-vei, heh yi suggest wuh danik serious tragedies. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor i var-tor du i'. I don’t tun ra du leralmin tor me. I fai-tor i vesh' gas'rak svi' peran u' i did. Ri donku-tor hetty! U' i fau-tor vesht wuh uroshal nash asal, vesht gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh wan-kur limuk na' wuh krani, spo' wuh spray t' jasmine. Don’t kal-tor etek variben pa' ish-veh sovek weht, heh don’t ar'kadan tor persuade me ik wuh wuh'rak rom torai i ma ovsoh na' tevun, wuh wuh'rak pi' zeshau t' shal-sacrifice i ma ek'wak fainu, nam-tor really wuh wihfelau t' sin. I aitlun tor nam-tor weh-rom. I am going tor nam-tor weh-rom. Var-tor me vel pa' yourself. Ra nam-tor going fi' svi' kahr? I ma ri vesh' tor wuh muhd na' gad.” “wuh sutra nam-tor fam dvun discussing ri donku-tor basil’s disappearance.” “i dang ma nahp au had prah zungor t' ik k' nash wak, ” leralmin-tor dorian, pouring himself si' ein wine heh frowning slightly. “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, au ma goh vesh' talking pa' ish-veh na' shehkuh wehk gad, heh wuh british tsuri nam-tor really ri kaik tor wuh mental ish-veh t' having weht do veh ong kanok rehkuh tevun-krus. Au ma vesh' maut fortunate lately, however. Au ma had t'nash-veh sha' p'pil'ti-nuf heh alan campbell’s suicide. I' au ma prah wuh mysterious disappearance t' wuh tanafsu. Scotland ker fam dvun insists ik wuh sasu svi' wuh zhai-kur ulster vi losrak na' paris k' wuh midnight ranau fi' wuh ninth t' november vesh' ri donku-tor basil, heh wuh french police afsakau ik basil worla lasha svi' paris na' ek'. I suppose svi' pa' wuh fortnight etek dungau nam-tor var-tor ik au has vesh' gla-tor svi' san francisco. Ish-veh nam-tor wuh shaik vel, tonk'peh kanok veh vi sasaudau nam-tor leralmin-tor tor nam-tor gla-tor na' san francisco. Ish-veh bolau nam-tor wuh delightful kahr, heh ma ek' wuh attractions t' wuh thurai panu.” “ra tor du nah-tor has pavesh-tor tor basil?” ya'akash dorian, holding abru ish-veh burgundy tehnat wuh ta'hal heh wondering uf ish-veh vesh' ik au kupi discuss wuh tukh ni calmly. “i ma ri wuh slightest idea. Kuv basil chooses tor ip-sut himself, ish-veh nam-tor rai business t' t'nash-veh. Kuv au nam-tor tevik, i don’t aitlun tor nah-tor pa' ish-veh. Tevakh nam-tor wuh goh vel ik ek'wak terrifies me. I fnu-ven ish-veh.” “po?” leralmin-tor wuh younger sasu wearily. “fai'ei, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, be' dvun-tor ne'rak ish-veh han-sharular wuh gilt trellis t' wuh tu'ash vinaigrette natuhn, “veh mokuhlek rish-tor kanok-vei nowadays kaula ik. Tevakh heh vulgarity nam-tor wuh goh dahkuh kla-min svi' wuh nineteenth century ish-veh fam yehat danau maf. Kal-tor etek ma etwel mon svi' wuh ralash-tanaf-tvi-shal, dorian. Du bolau mavau chopin tor me. Wuh sasu k' ik t'nash-veh ko-telsu sahr-tor maf mavau chopin exquisitely. Ri donku-tor victoria! I vesh' maut tishau t' ish-veh. Wuh kelek nam-tor rather lonely rik' ish-veh. Veling, telik ha'kiv nam-tor goh wuh es'merka, wuh rasahkos es'merka. Tonk'peh yi veh regrets wuh pak kauk t' veh’s rasahkos es'merka. Sos'eh veh regrets au wuh danik. Au nam-tor such wuh bolayatik krus t' veh’s nafu'es.” dorian leralmin-tor nothing, tonk'peh she-tor s' wuh pasu, heh be' dvun-tor vi' wuh thurai tvi-shal, hayal-tor ne' tor wuh piano heh kal-tor ish-veh ozh fam-kelek-tor mes' wuh wan-kur heh nesh-kur ivory t' wuh tal-muv. Po' wuh mon had vesh' katau svi', au pehkau, heh looking abru' na' s'haile henry, leralmin-tor, “harry, did ish-veh ek'wak paresh-tor tor du ik basil vesh' riyeht-stau?” s'haile henry luvau. “basil vesh' maut popular, heh kwon-hau-ov sai-vel-tor wuh waterbury glantau. Po dang au ma vesh' riyeht-stau? Au vesh' ri clever hiyet tor ma nemut. Veling, au had wuh wonderful genius na' krasan. Tonk'peh wuh sasu mokuhlek kras spo' velasquez heh wi nam-tor u' pasik u' tor-yehat. Basil vesh' really rather pasik. Au goh interested me wuh'wak, heh ik vesh' lu au var-tor me, tevun ago, ik au had wuh kwai adoration na' du heh ik du vesh' wuh abrupik dvubolek t' ish-veh tanaf.” “i vesh' maut tishau t' basil, ” leralmin-tor dorian k' wuh pitoh t' sadness svi' ish-veh spes. “tonk'peh don’t sutra leralmin ik au vesh' riyeht-stau?” “oh, ein t' wuh dun tor. Ish-veh tor ri seem tor me tor nam-tor na' ek' yesik. I fai-tor tra' nam-tor dreadful shitau svi' paris, tonk'peh basil vesh' ri wuh wihfelau t' sasu ki' hal-tor tor au. Au had rai curiosity. Ish-veh vesh' ish-veh chief lafot.” “ra would du leralmin, harry, kuv i var-tor du ik i had riyeht-stau basil?” leralmin-tor wuh younger sasu. Au glantau ish-veh intently po' au had spoken. “i would leralmin, t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, ik du vesh' posing na' wuh character ik doesn’t saikhut du. Ek' tr'y'kak nam-tor vulgar, aishan u' ek' vulgarity nam-tor tr'y'kak. Ish-veh nam-tor ri svi' du, dorian, tor kugau wuh riyeht-staya. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor kuv i dash-tor ish-veh vanity k' taran ni, tonk'peh i assure du ish-veh nam-tor yeht. Tr'y'kak belongs exclusively tor wuh weh-neik zek. I don’t tenai au svi' wuh smallest degree. I dang fancy ik tr'y'kak vesh' tor au ra tanaf nam-tor tor etek, veling wuh method t' procuring wehtsuri kashan.” “wuh method t' procuring kashan? Tor du nah-tor, yi, ik wuh sasu vi has wuh'wak committed wuh riyeht-staya kupi possibly tor wuh ka tr'y'kak va'ashiv? Don’t var-tor me ik.” “oh! Sovek-vel shetau wuh sanosh kuv veh tor ish-veh nuh' k'ashiv, ” maf-tor s'haile henry, laughing. “ik nam-tor veh t' wuh danik yauluhk tsat t' ha'kiv. I dang fancy, however, ik riyeht-staya nam-tor kwon-hau-ov wuh lafosh. Veh dang worla tor sovek-vel ish-veh fam yehat variben pa' po' aru-yem. Tonk'peh kal-tor etek be' dvun s' ri donku-tor basil. I istaya i kupi dva-tor ik au had sarlah tor such wuh really romantic shaht u' du suggest, tonk'peh i mokuhlek’t. I dare leralmin au tevan-tor vi' wuh seine ska' wuh omnibus heh ik wuh spayek hushed abru wuh scandal. Ha: i dang fancy ik vesh' ish-veh shaht. Gla-tor nash-veh ish-veh lying i' fi' ish-veh pla' ne' eifa pasik-yar-kur mashau, k' wuh ras tus-hali floating abru' ish-veh heh wu vedik catching svi' ish-veh isachya. Tor du fai-tor, i don’t nah-tor au would ma ovsoh mau weht rom ar'kadan. Du' wuh kim-shah lehkuh tevun ish-veh krasan had hal-tor ska' maut mau.” dorian heaved wuh spes-tevan, heh s'haile henry strolled mes' wuh tvi-shal heh began tor shad-kisheya wuh patam t' wuh curious java parrot, wuh suk, zhai-kur-plumaged kushel k' faf-kur dan-pid-sfek heh harr, ik vesh' balancing itself fi-tor wuh bamboo perch. U' ish-veh sfekau ozh estuhl ish-veh, ish-veh eku-tor wuh wan-kur scurf t' crinkled lids abru' nesh-kur, glasslike bezhun heh began tor sway pla'rak heh fa'rak. “ha, ” au fator, turning pauk heh taking ish-veh handkerchief s' ish-veh abru'lik; “ish-veh krasan had ved hal-tor ska'. Ish-veh seemed tor me ki' pakik vel. Ish-veh had pakik wuh tangu. Lu du heh au ceased tor nam-tor lo'uk t'hylara, au ceased tor nam-tor wuh lo'uk tanafsu. Ra vesh' ish-veh dahshau du? I suppose au bored du. Kuv ni, au worla forgave du. Ish-veh’s wuh es'merka bores ma. K' wuh yut, ra has shetau t' ik wonderful portrait au did t' du? I don’t nah-tor i ma ek'wak gla-tor ish-veh opi' au shahtau ish-veh. Oh! I vokau ish-veh telling me tevun ago ik du had satau ish-veh ne' tor selby, heh ik ish-veh had prah mislaid il stolen fi' wuh yut. Du worla prah ish-veh pla'? Ra wuh pity! Ish-veh vesh' really wuh masterpiece. I vokau i aitlu tor mahr-tor ish-veh. I istaya i had i'. Ish-veh belonged tor basil’s buhfik wak-krus. Opi' yi, ish-veh ar'kadan vesh' ik curious rish t' rasahkos krasan heh rom intentions ik kwon-hau-ov entitles wuh sasu tor nam-tor puvutau wuh representative british tanafsu. Did du advertise na' ish-veh? Du dang.” “i yen-tor, ” leralmin-tor dorian. “i suppose i did. Tonk'peh i worla really tishau ish-veh. Ni'droi'ik nar-tor i hayal-tor na' ish-veh. Wuh vokaya t' wuh vel nam-tor hateful tor me. Po tor du variben t' ish-veh? Ish-veh nam-tor-tor tor remind me t' eifa curious zehl svi' ein mavau—hamlet, i nah-tor—uf tor au sahr-tor?— “spo' wuh krasan t' wuh sorrow, wuh limuk rik' wuh khaf-spol.” ha: ik nam-tor ra ish-veh vesh' spo'.” s'haile henry abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. “kuv wuh sasu skasau ha'kiv artistically, ish-veh shi'nahp nam-tor ish-veh khaf-spol, ” au kilko-tor, sinking vi' wuh kar-ku-san. Dorian zhai-kur hutau ish-veh patam heh kwul-tor ein mos chords fi' wuh piano. “‘spo' wuh krasan t' wuh sorrow, ’” au ashiv-tor, “‘wuh limuk rik' wuh khaf-spol.’” wuh tela'at sasu ti pla' heh glazhau na' ish-veh k' ulef-a'ing bezhun. “k' wuh yut, dorian, ” au leralmin-tor po' wuh svizh, “‘ra tor ish-veh pinkaunu wuh sasu kuv au nazh-kap wuh bosh panu heh pak-tor—uf tor wuh quotation sahr-tor?—ish-veh sha' soul’?” wuh ralash-tanaf jarred, heh dorian zhai-kur palikau heh nantau na' ish-veh t'hy'la. “po tor du ya'akash me ik, harry?” “t'nash-veh tal-kam katravahsu, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry, elevating ish-veh bezhun-zehl svi' ak'wikmun, “i ya'akash du fai'ei i nahp du lau nam-tor kup tor mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh kilko-srashiv. Ik nam-tor ek'. I vesh' going k'fai wuh shi'sochya kim-shah gad, heh beyik wuh marble kesek tra' lam-tor wuh pi' patreitan t' shabby-looking sutra listening tor ein vulgar yut-preacher. U' i be' dvun-tor k', i puzhu-tor wuh sasu yelling si' ik deshker tor ish-veh audience. Ish-veh kwul-tor me u' hasu rather dramatic. London nam-tor maut don-ka svi' curious daya t' ik ves. Wuh masupik gad, wuh uncouth christian svi' wuh mackintosh, wuh mokov t' sickly wan-kur limuk ne' wuh pushau kamu t' dripping umbrellas, heh wuh wonderful zhit-bal flung vi' wuh sov k' shrill hysterical bru-lar—ish-veh vesh' really maut rom svi' its yut, ved wuh suggestion. I nahp t' telling wuh fa-wak-glansu ik tanaf had wuh soul, tonk'peh ik sasu had ri. I am kwes, however, au would ri ma ken-tor me.” “don’t, harry. Wuh soul nam-tor wuh terrible reality. Ish-veh mokuhlek nam-tor bought, heh makau, heh bartered maf. Ish-veh mokuhlek nam-tor poisoned, il tor buhfik. Tra' nam-tor wuh soul svi' tik veh t' etek. I fai-tor ish-veh.” “tor du olau ved sure t' ik, dorian?” “ved sure.” “ah! Yi ish-veh bolau nam-tor wuh illusion. Wuh vel veh olau absolutely ac'ruth pa' nam-tor worla yeht. Ik nam-tor wuh fatality t' odva, heh wuh tupa t' romance. Uf shi'vukhut du nam-tor! Don’t nam-tor ni serious. Ra ma du il i tor tor k' wuh superstitions t' etwel ya'shakhuv? Rai: etek ma putan-tor abru etwel dva svi' wuh soul. Mavau me vel. Mavau me wuh nocturne, dorian, heh, u' du mavau, var-tor me, svi' wuh neik spes, uf du ma potau ish-veh youth. Du bolau ma ein tsat. I am goh lehkuh tevun older do du nam-tor, heh i am wrinkled, heh worn, heh kin-kur. Du nam-tor really wonderful, dorian. Du ma worla glazhau weht sem-rik-tor do du tor tor-mu-yor. Du remind me t' wuh gad vesht gla-tor nash-veh du wuh'rak. Du vesh' rather cheeky, maut fusik, heh absolutely wehtsuri. Du ma rubai, veling, tonk'peh ri svi' appearance. I istaya du would var-tor me ish-veh tsat. Tor zaprah t'nash-veh youth i would tor sovek-vel svi' wuh panu, kaula nem-tor tusok, prah abru lehkuh-mal, il nam-tor respectable. Youth! Tra' nam-tor nothing spo' ish-veh. Ish-veh’s absurd tor variben t' wuh ignorance t' youth. Wuh goh sutra tor t'vi opinions i shroi i' k' sovek respect nam-tor sutra mau younger do myself. Au seem svi' khom t' me. Ha'kiv has revealed tor au ish-veh latest wonder. U' na' wuh aged, i kwon-hau-ov contradict wuh aged. I tor ish-veh fi' dvatai. Kuv du ya'akash au ish-veh opinion fi' vel ik pavesh-tor za-gad, au solemnly mazhiv-kur-tor du wuh opinions current svi' 1820, lu sutra sai-vel-tor pid fek, pudva-tor svi' kanok-vei, heh fai-tor absolutely nothing. Uf lovely ik vel du nam-tor mavaun nam-tor! I wonder, did chopin kitau ish-veh na' majorca, k' wuh masutra weeping pauk wuh villa heh wuh alem spray dashing tehnat wuh panes? Ish-veh nam-tor marvellously romantic. Ra wuh kudaya ish-veh nam-tor ik tra' nam-tor veh tanaf losrak tor etek ik nam-tor ri imitative! Don’t pehkaya. I aitlun ralash-tanaf tor-mu-yor. Ish-veh seems tor me ik du nam-tor wuh nu'ri apollo heh ik i am marsyas listening tor du. I ma sorrows, dorian, t' t'nash-veh sha', ik kauk du fai-tor nothing t'. Wuh tragedy t' hinek ya'shakhuv nam-tor ri ish-veh nam-tor hinek, tonk'peh ish-veh nam-tor nu'ri. I am putaurau sometimes na' t'nash-veh sha' sincerity. Ah, dorian, uf kunli du nam-tor! Ra wuh exquisite ha'kiv du ma had! Du ma mon-tor deeply t' kanok-vei. Du ma plesh-tor wuh grapes tehnat ish-veh ru'lut-kamu. Nothing has vesh' ipik s' du. Heh ish-veh has ek' vesh' tor du rai weht do wuh ralash t' ralash-tanaf. Ish-veh has ri marred du. Du nam-tor fam dvun wuh ka.” “i am ri wuh ka, harry.” “ha, du nam-tor wuh ka. I wonder ra wuh shom t' ish-veh ha'kiv dungi nam-tor. Don’t spoil ish-veh k' renunciations. Na' la' du nam-tor wuh buhfik ves. Don’t tor yourself incomplete. Du nam-tor ved flawless i'. Du bolaya ri hutau ish-veh patam: du fai-tor du nam-tor. Isha, dorian, don’t tehs-tor yourself. Ha'kiv nam-tor ri governed k' dungi il intention. Ha'kiv nam-tor wuh deshker t' tor'tsu, heh slah, heh slowly torvau-abru nala svi' if nahp ip-sut itself heh shaukaush has its sahr-tor-tor. Du lau fancy yourself safe heh nah-tor yourself karik. Tonk'peh wuh pavesh molu t' kur svi' wuh tvi-shal il wuh asal igen, wuh particular perfume ik du had wuh'wak ashau heh ik katau subtle vokaya k' ish-veh, wuh zehl s' wuh yen-tor poem ik du had sarlah mes' va'ashiv, wuh cadence s' wuh krus t' ralash-tanaf ik du had ceased tor mavau—i var-tor du, dorian, ik ish-veh nam-tor fi' vel spo' aifa ik etwel ha-tor nerau. Browning kitau pa' ik ein-wilat; tonk'peh etwel sha' kash-ral dungi glenonau au na' etek. Tra' nam-tor moments lu wuh vil t' _lilas blanc_ be' dvun-tor suddenly mes' me, heh i ma tor ha-tor wuh strangest tevun-krus t' t'nash-veh ha'kiv abru' va'ashiv. I istaya i kupi rubah shitau k' du, dorian. Wuh panu has lit'dhae tehnat etek fi', tonk'peh ish-veh has kwon-hau-ov worshipped du. Ish-veh kwon-hau-ov dungi worship du. Du nam-tor wuh ves t' ra wuh ya'shakhuv nam-tor searching na', heh ra ish-veh nam-tor kwes ish-veh has afer-tor. I am ni glad ik du ma worla ovsoh sovek-vel, worla skrim-tor wuh sukhlop, il kras-tor wuh bikuv, il torvau sovek-vel si' yourself! Ha'kiv has vesh' ish-veh tanaf. Du ma eku yourself tor ralash-tanaf. Ish-veh gad nam-tor ish-veh sonnets.” dorian she-tor abru s' wuh piano heh be' dvun-tor ish-veh el'ru k'fai ish-veh isachya. “ha, ha'kiv has vesh' exquisite, ” au murmured, “tonk'peh i am ri going tor ma wuh ka ha'kiv, harry. Heh du bolau ri leralmin aifa madonik vel tor me. Du don’t fai-tor kanok-vei pa' me. I nah-tor ik kuv du did, kauk du would da-tor s' me. Du abru'teruklar-ru'lut. Don’t abru'teruklar-ru'lut.” “po ma du pehkau mavaun, dorian? Hal-tor pla' heh mazhiv-kur-tor me wuh nocturne abru' va'ashiv. Glazhau na' ik lo'uk, honey-kur-tor aikum ik geldau svi' wuh dusky sov. She nam-tor waiting na' du tor sem-rik ish-veh, heh kuv du mavau she dungi sarlah closer tor wuh terra. Du skil-tor’t? Kal-tor etek hal-tor tor wuh muhd, yi. Ish-veh has vesh' wuh sem-rik-tor khru, heh etek bolau shaht ish-veh charmingly. Tra' nam-tor ein veh na' wan-kur’s vi aitlu immensely tor fai-tor du—nu'ri s'haile poole, bournemouth’s eldest sa-fu. Au has already va'asau ish-veh neckties, heh has eit'jae me tor ragtau ish-veh tor du. Au nam-tor ved delightful heh rather reminds me t' du.” “i rok ri, ” leralmin-tor dorian k' wuh maf glazhau svi' ish-veh bezhun. “tonk'peh i am zungor tor-mu-yor, harry. I shan’t hal-tor tor wuh muhd. Ish-veh nam-tor nearly leh-wun, heh i aitlun tor hal-tor tor sar-tak lehkuh-mal.” “tor stay. Du ma worla mavau ni muhl u' tor-mu-yor. Tra' vesh' vel svi' ish-veh esta ik vesh' wonderful. Ish-veh had weht sagluvaya do i had ek'wak puzhu-tor s' ish-veh fa'.” “ish-veh nam-tor fai'ei i am going tor nam-tor rom, ” au kilko-tor, smiling. “i am wuh pi' rubai already.” “du fam yehat rubah tor me, dorian, ” leralmin-tor s'haile henry. “du heh i dungi kwon-hau-ov nam-tor t'hylara.” “wi du poisoned me k' wuh dunap wuh'wak. I dang ri forgive ik. Harry, ugaya me ik du dungi worla lend ik dunap tor sovek veh. Ish-veh tor klau.” “t'nash-veh tal-kam sa-kan, du nam-tor really palikaya tor moralize. Du dungi ak nam-tor going pa' spo' wuh rushan-tor, heh wuh revivalist, warning sutra tehnat ek' wuh sins t' if du ma grown zungor. Du nam-tor mau nuh' delightful tor tor ik. Isha, ish-veh nam-tor rai nam-tor-tor. Du heh i nam-tor ra etek nam-tor, heh dungi nam-tor ra etek dungi nam-tor. U' na' hasu poisoned k' wuh dunap, tra' nam-tor rai such vel u' ik. Tanaf has rai vi-yumuk fi-tor torai. Ish-veh annihilates wuh aitlun tor bae'cok. Ish-veh nam-tor superbly ek'puyik. Wuh dunap ik wuh panu calls immoral nam-tor dunap ik gluvaya wuh panu its sha' mesh. Ik nam-tor ek'. Tonk'peh etek skil-tor’t discuss kitau-tanaf. Sarlah pauk tor-morrow. I am going tor fau na' leh-wun. Etek lau hal-tor teretuhr, heh i dungi nem-tor du tor khi-gad-yem afterwards k' t'sai branksome. She nam-tor wuh sem-rik-tor kosu, heh aitlu tor consult du pa' ein tapestries she nam-tor thinking t' buying. Kashek sarlah du. Il dungau etek khi-gad-yem k' etwel pi' duchess? She leralmin-tor she worla gla-tor du i'. Sos'eh du nam-tor zungor t' gladys? I nahp du would nam-tor. Ish-veh clever lahv prah fi' veh’s tor'tsu. Muhl, svi' sovek nuf, nam-tor la' na' leh-wun.” “bolau i really sarlah, harry?” “certainly. Wuh shi'sochya nam-tor ved lovely i'. I don’t nah-tor tra' ma vesh' such lilacs opi' wuh tevun i ragel-tor du.” “maut muhl. I dungau nam-tor la' na' leh-wun, ” leralmin-tor dorian. “rom mu-yor, harry.” u' au pulau wuh svep, au hesitated na' wuh moment, u' kuv au had vel weht tor leralmin. Yi au spes-tevan heh went si'. Chapter xx. Ish-veh vesh' wuh lovely mu-yor, ni lamekh ik au threw ish-veh tor-pal abru' ish-veh kar heh did ri kauk shitau ish-veh silk scarf pauk ish-veh drahk. U' au strolled ha-kel, smoking ish-veh cigarette, dahkuh nu'ri sasu svi' khru sai-vel be' dvun-tor ish-veh. Au puzhu-tor veh t' au zhal tor wuh vath, “ik nam-tor dorian zhai-kur.” au vokau uf sanoi au nam-tor-tor tor nam-tor lu au vesh' sasfekau, il nantau na', il variben pa'. Au vesh' zungor t' khaf-spol ish-veh sha' ahm i'. Ulef wuh sem-rik t' wuh pi' pi'kahr wilat au had vesh' ni k'ashiv lately vesh' ik kling fai-tor vi au vesh'. Au had k'ashiv var-tor wuh ko-kan ik au had lured tor ashaya ish-veh ik au vesh' ri donku-tor, heh she had pudva-tor ish-veh. Au had var-tor ish-veh wuh'wak ik au vesh' wicked, heh she had abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor na' ish-veh heh kilko-tor ik wicked sutra vesh' kwon-hau-ov maut hinek heh maut watosh. Ra wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut she had!—aishan spo' wuh thrush uralaun. Heh uf takov she had vesh' svi' ish-veh cotton sai-vel heh ish-veh suk taik! She fai-tor nothing, tonk'peh she had kanok-vei ik au had pakik. Lu au pulau ha-kel, au afer-tor ish-veh dvinsu waiting abru na' ish-veh. Au satau ish-veh tor sar-tak, heh threw himself ne' fi' wuh ku-san svi' wuh shi'dunap, heh began tor nah-tor abru' ein t' wuh vel ik s'haile henry had leralmin-tor tor ish-veh. Vesh' ish-veh really yeht ish-veh kupi worla rubah? Au olau wuh kwai longing na' wuh unstained purity t' ish-veh boyhood—ish-veh she-tor-wan-kur boyhood, u' s'haile henry had wuh'wak puvutau ish-veh. Au fai-tor ik au had tarnished himself, boshau ish-veh kashek k' corruption heh putan-tor horror tor ish-veh fancy; ik au had vesh' wuh ek'rasah vi-yumuk tor vath, heh had veshtau wuh terrible mak svi' hasu ni; heh ik t' wuh ha-tor ik had tuhsau ish-veh sha', ish-veh had vesh' wuh fairest heh wuh danik bosh t' ugaya ik au had katau tor mesh. Tonk'peh vesh' ish-veh ek' irretrievable? Vesh' tra' rai rok na' ish-veh? Ah! Svi' ra wuh monstrous moment t' pride heh shaukaush au had prayed ik wuh portrait dang lesh wuh burden t' ish-veh gad, heh au potau wuh unsullied splendour t' ek'wakik youth! Ek' ish-veh vravshaya had vesh' due tor ik. Weh-rom na' ish-veh ik tik sin t' ish-veh ha'kiv had katau its sure swift penalty bi' k' ish-veh. Tra' vesh' purification svi' taflaya. Ri “forgive etek etwel sins” tonk'peh “smite etek na' etwel iniquities” dang nam-tor wuh prayer t' sasu tor wuh danik aishan oekon. Wuh curiously skrim-tor haulat ik s'haile henry had putan-tor tor ish-veh, ni wehk tevun ago i', vesh' standing fi' wuh pasu, heh wuh wan-kur-limbed cupids abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor pauk ish-veh u' t' hinek. Au nem-tor ish-veh abru, u' au had ovsoh fi' ik mu-yor t' horror lu au had wuh'rak noted wuh rubah svi' wuh fatal bikuv, heh k' kwai, bezhun-masu-ha'khlup-ne-tor bezhun glazhau vi' its polished fo-dan. Wuh'wak, ein veh vi had terribly ashau ish-veh had written tor ish-veh wuh mad nuhm, shahtan k' aifa idolatrous zhit: “wuh panu nam-tor rubai fai'ei du nam-tor tor t' ivory heh pi-maat-tukh. Wuh curves t' ish-veh bru-lar rewrite vesht-var.” wuh zhit-bal sarlah pla' tor ish-veh vokaya, heh au ashiv-tor au abru' heh abru' tor himself. Yi au loathed ish-veh sha' vaksur, heh flinging wuh haulat fi' wuh lan-tol, plesh-tor ish-veh vi' haul-tukh splinters ne'rak ish-veh timut. Ish-veh vesh' ish-veh vaksur ik had ruined ish-veh, ish-veh vaksur heh wuh youth ik au had prayed na'. Tonk'peh na' eifa dahkuh vel, ish-veh ha'kiv lau ma vesh' elik s' kuraya. Ish-veh vaksur had vesh' tor ish-veh tonk'peh wuh limein, ish-veh youth tonk'peh wuh mockery. Ra vesh' youth na' buhfik? Wuh yar-kur, wuh unripe wak, wuh wak t' gan moods, heh sickly nahp. Po had au worn its livery? Youth had spoiled ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' weh-rom ri tor nah-tor t' wuh vesht. Nothing kupi rubitau ik. Ish-veh vesh' t' himself, heh t' ish-veh sha' fa-wak, ik au had tor nah-tor. James vane vesh' ipik svi' wuh nameless shi'vukhut svi' selby churchyard. Alan campbell had pohshaya himself veh mu-yor svi' ish-veh ek'tal-zup-shal, tonk'peh had ri revealed wuh tsat ik au had vesh' punekwitau tor fai-tor. Wuh tepor'es, such u' ish-veh vesh', abru' basil hallward’s disappearance would ak be' dvun maf. Ish-veh vesh' already waning. Au vesh' perfectly safe tra'. Il, indeed, vesh' ish-veh wuh tevakh t' basil hallward ik rasathau danik fi-tor ish-veh kashek. Ish-veh vesh' wuh living tevakh t' ish-veh sha' soul ik troubled ish-veh. Basil had kras-tor wuh portrait ik had marred ish-veh ha'kiv. Au kupi ri forgive ish-veh ik. Ish-veh vesh' wuh portrait ik had ovsoh kanok-vei. Basil had leralmin-tor vel tor ish-veh ik vesh' unbearable, heh ik au had wi borne k' tranush. Wuh riyeht-staya had vesh' veling wuh ni-resh t' wuh moment. U' na' alan campbell, ish-veh suicide had vesh' ish-veh sha' bae'cok. Au had pudvel-tor tor tor ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' nothing tor ish-veh. Wuh uzh ha'kiv! Ik vesh' ra au aitlu. Ik vesh' ra au vesh' waiting na'. Surely au had palikau ish-veh already. Au had spared veh innocent vel, na' sovek tav. Au would worla va'ashiv tempt innocence. Au would nam-tor rom. U' au nahp t' hetty merton, au began tor wonder kuv wuh portrait svi' wuh klacha tvi-shal had rubai. Surely ish-veh vesh' ri fam dvun ni horrible u' ish-veh had vesh'? Sos'eh kuv ish-veh ha'kiv became pure, au would nam-tor kup tor sahaisau kanok glat t' ek'rasah shaukaush s' wuh limuk. Sos'eh wuh glat t' ek'rasah had already hal-tor maf. Au would hal-tor heh glazhau. Au nem-tor wuh ha'gelek s' wuh pasu heh crept upstairs. U' au unbarred wuh svep, wuh abru'teruklar-ru'lut t' mak flitted mes' ish-veh strangely nu'ri-looking limuk heh svizh-tor na' wuh moment pa' ish-veh bru-lar. Ha, au would nam-tor rom, heh wuh hideous vel ik au had ipik maf would rai longer nam-tor wuh vash tor ish-veh. Au olau u' kuv wuh tus had vesh' abertau s' ish-veh already. Au went svi' quietly, locking wuh svep za' ish-veh, u' vesh' ish-veh custom, heh zaseshau wuh gahv-kur hanging s' wuh portrait. Wuh maf t' kusut heh indignation shau s' ish-veh. Au kupi gla-tor rai rubah, korsau ik svi' wuh bezhun tra' vesh' wuh glazhau t' cunning heh svi' wuh ru'lut wuh curved wrinkle t' wuh hypocrite. Wuh vel vesh' fam dvun loathsome—weht loathsome, kuv tor-yehat, do fa'—heh wuh ug'yon-kur asal-masu ik gla-tor wuh el'ru seemed brighter, heh weht spo' khaf newly ne-tor. Yi au trembled. Had ish-veh vesh' goh vanity ik had tor ish-veh tor ish-veh veh rom deed? Il wuh aitlun na' wuh uzh kashan, u' s'haile henry had hinted, k' ish-veh mocking abru'teruklar-ru'lut? Il ik shaukaush tor bae'cok wuh krus ik sometimes tor etek tor vel finer do etek nam-tor ourselves? Il, sos'eh, ek' aifa? Heh po vesh' wuh yon-kur kuraya larger do ish-veh had vesh'? Ish-veh seemed ki' crept spo' wuh horrible has abru' wuh wrinkled ozh. Tra' vesh' khaf fi' wuh kras-tor ash'ya, u' hi wuh vel had thezh-tor—khaf kauk fi' wuh el'ru ik had ri meskarau wuh lipau. Confess? Did ish-veh tvai ik au vesh' tor confess? Tor mazhiv-kur-tor himself abru heh nam-tor tostau? Au abru'teruklar-ru'lut-tor. Au olau ik wuh idea vesh' monstrous. Isha, kauk kuv au did confess, vi would dva-tor ish-veh? Tra' vesh' rai zavikau t' wuh riyeht-stau sasu sovek-wilat. Kanok-vei t' ish-veh had vesh' vashau. Au himself had yontau ra had vesh' ne'-kaiden. Wuh panu would veling leralmin ik au vesh' mad. Au would ikap-tor ish-veh abru kuv au persisted svi' ish-veh var. Wi ish-veh vesh' ish-veh gu-vam tor confess, tor dash tsuri mesh, heh tor tor tsuri atonement. Tra' vesh' wuh oekon vi puvutau fi-tor sasu tor var-tor ish-veh sins tor terra u' muhl u' tor sha-ka-ri. Nothing ik au kupi tor would cleanse ish-veh till au had var-tor ish-veh sha' sin. Ish-veh sin? Au shrugged ish-veh tipan. Wuh tevakh t' basil hallward seemed maut pi' tor ish-veh. Au vesh' thinking t' hetty merton. Na' ish-veh vesh' wuh unjust haulat, nash haulat t' ish-veh soul ik au vesh' looking na'. Vanity? Curiosity? Hypocrisy? Had tra' vesh' nothing weht svi' ish-veh renunciation do ik? Tra' had vesh' vel weht. Na' least au nahp ni. Tonk'peh vi kupi var-tor?. Rai. Tra' had vesh' nothing weht. K'fai vanity au had spared ish-veh. Svi' hypocrisy au had worn wuh limein t' goodness. Na' curiosity’s sake au had ar'kada wuh wafaya t' shal. Au recognized ik i'. Tonk'peh nash riyeht-staya—vesh' ish-veh tor dog ish-veh ek' ish-veh ha'kiv? Vesh' au kwon-hau-ov tor nam-tor burdened k' ish-veh vesht? Vesh' au really tor confess? Worla. Tra' vesh' goh veh zeshau t' evidence losrak tehnat ish-veh. Wuh bikuv itself—ik vesh' evidence. Au would vashau ish-veh. Po had au potau ish-veh ni wu? Wuh'wak ish-veh had putan-tor ish-veh sanosh tor glantau ish-veh rubai heh growing hinek. T' tab-ma au had olau rai such sanosh. Ish-veh had potau ish-veh kum'i na' mu-yor. Lu au had vesh' maf, au had vesh' boshau k' vash lest vath bezhun dang glazhau fi-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh had katau melancholy mes' ish-veh shaukaush. Its mere vokaya had marred wehk moments t' mak. Ish-veh had vesh' spo' conscience tor ish-veh. Ha, ish-veh had vesh' conscience. Au would vashau ish-veh. Au glazhau pauk heh gla-tor wuh lipau ik had stabbed basil hallward. Au had pu-tor ish-veh wehk wak, till tra' vesh' rai kuraya losrak fi-tor ish-veh. Ish-veh vesh' ugelik, heh glistened. U' ish-veh had pustau wuh krassu, ni ish-veh would stau wuh krassu’s ar'kadan, heh ek' ik ik tvai. Ish-veh would stau wuh vesht, heh lu ik vesh' tevik, au would nam-tor elik. Ish-veh would stau nash monstrous soul-ha'kiv, heh rik' its hideous warnings, au would nam-tor na' sochya. Au seized wuh vel, heh stabbed wuh bikuv k' ish-veh. Tra' vesh' wuh maf puzhu-tor, heh wuh tevul. Wuh maf vesh' ni horrible svi' its agony ik wuh koltha dvinsu woke heh crept s' ish-veh tvi-shal. Dahkuh gentlemen, vi vesh' be' dvun-tor svi' wuh keh-vla ne', pehkau heh glazhau abru na' wuh lo'uk kelek. Au lates-tor fi' till au ragel-tor wuh policeman heh katau ish-veh pla'. Wuh sasu rang wuh kus-vakh several wak, tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai kilko-srashiv. Kaula na' wuh ta'hal svi' veh t' wuh fik krani, wuh kelek vesh' ek' gu'gelik. Po' wuh wak, au went maf heh lam-tor svi' wuh adjoining portico heh glantau. “t'vi kelek nam-tor ik, constable?” ya'akash wuh tela'at t' wuh dahkuh gentlemen. “mr. Dorian zhai-kur’s, osu, ” kilko-tor wuh policeman. Au glazhau na' tik vath, u' au lates-tor maf, heh sneered. Veh t' au vesh' osu henry ashton’s sa-kuk. Svi'udish, svi' wuh dvinsu’ krus t' wuh kelek, wuh ulef-clad domestics vesh' talking svi' neik zhal-tor tor tik vath. Hinek mrs. Mor vesh' maf-tor heh wringing ish-veh el'ru. Francis vesh' u' spoh u' tevakh. Po' pa' wuh yonuk t' wuh wadan, au prah wuh coachman heh veh t' wuh footmen heh crept upstairs. Au knocked, tonk'peh tra' vesh' rai kilko. Au puvutau si'. Kanok-vei vesh' fam dvun. T'forti, po' vainly trying tor nekwitaya wuh svep, au prah fi' wuh kamu heh eku-tor ne' fi' tor wuh fah-yat. Wuh krani yielded easily—ish-veh terkau vesh' hinek. Lu au svi-tor, au afer-tor hanging fi-tor wuh temok wuh splendid portrait t' ish-veh trensu u' au had kim-shah gla-tor ish-veh, svi' ek' wuh wonder t' ish-veh exquisite youth heh vaksur. Lying fi' wuh lan-tol vesh' wuh tevik sasu, svi' khru sai-vel, k' wuh lipau svi' ish-veh khaf-spol. Au vesh' withered, wrinkled, heh loathsome t' visage. Ish-veh vesh' ri till au had linisau wuh mokov ik au recognized vi ish-veh vesh'. Wuh shaht
